ge, Ya꞉suwa꞉lo꞉ tamin amilo꞉ mo꞉mo꞉da wido꞉wo꞉lo꞉, dimido꞉wo꞉lo꞉, a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ Hebenelo꞉ a꞉ma꞉la꞉do꞉ ane a꞉no꞉, Lug ne tamin amio꞉ gemo꞉ sa꞉sa꞉liga꞉fo꞉. Godeya꞉yo꞉ Ya꞉suwo꞉ Hebene halonamio꞉ semo꞉ tililia꞉ ha꞉naki, Eyo꞉ Enedo꞉ iliga꞉felema꞉no꞉ kaluwo꞉ da꞉fea꞉sa꞉ga꞉, imo꞉wo꞉ asuluma꞉no꞉ to nowo꞉ Mamaya꞉ halaido꞉ a꞉ma꞉yo꞉ sio꞉.
<range>
Ya꞉suwo꞉ sowa꞉sa꞉ga꞉, mela꞉no꞉wo꞉ a꞉dia꞉sa꞉ga꞉ dasilakiyo꞉, Enedo꞉ iliga꞉felema꞉no꞉ kaluwo꞉ e hendele dasilia꞉ga꞉ mela꞉no꞉wo꞉ di a꞉la꞉ tili asuluma꞉ki, E ho꞉leno꞉ do꞉la꞉fo꞉ fa꞉la꞉da꞉ino꞉ i o꞉lia꞉ sia꞉len. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉yo꞉ Eyo꞉ Godeya꞉ ene kaluka꞉isale ko꞉lo꞉ bo꞉fo꞉lab man a꞉no꞉ wida꞉len.
Ya꞉suwa꞉yo꞉ egele silikiyo꞉, imo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Gio꞉ Ya꞉lusalemo꞉ semo꞉ ta꞉fo꞉ ha꞉nakiyo꞉, Dowa꞉lo꞉ boba kelego꞉ gimo꞉lo꞉ dimia꞉no꞉ dinali sio꞉ a꞉no꞉, niyo꞉ gimo꞉wo꞉ tamin amio꞉ sio꞉ ko꞉lo꞉, giliyo꞉ a꞉no꞉ dia꞉ni yasita꞉bi.
Yona꞉yo꞉ ho꞉n deya to꞉lola꞉len ko꞉sega, Godeya꞉yo꞉ gio꞉ Ene Mamaleya꞉ to꞉loma꞉no꞉wo꞉, ho꞉len a꞉la꞉se ko꞉na꞉ma dowab.”
A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ iyo꞉ kegea꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Ya꞉sumo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉dabuba꞉ba꞉, “Alan, Isolael kaluka꞉isaleyo꞉ halale alitakiyo꞉, inin amio꞉ misa꞉ kalu nowo꞉ fa꞉la꞉dota꞉ga꞉, wa꞉ka bo꞉fo꞉melea꞉ki, giyo꞉ o꞉go꞉ o꞉li dimidama꞉no꞉wele?”
A꞉la꞉dabuba꞉dabiki, Ya꞉suwa꞉yo꞉ a꞉ma꞉la꞉yo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Kelego꞉ fa꞉la꞉doma꞉no꞉ ho꞉len a꞉no꞉ Dowa꞉ Ene da꞉feyo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ gio꞉ mada mo꞉asulo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉lab.
Ko꞉sega Mamaya꞉yo꞉ gio꞉ go꞉lu alitalikiyo꞉, gio꞉ halaido꞉wo꞉ dia꞉sa꞉ga꞉ ami, Ni towo꞉ Ya꞉lusalemo꞉lo꞉ Yudiayo꞉lo꞉, Samalia hen a꞉namio꞉ wida꞉sa꞉ga꞉, a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉yo꞉ henfelo꞉ we tambo wida꞉li sia꞉mela꞉ib” a꞉la꞉sio꞉.
To a꞉no꞉ sa꞉la꞉sa꞉ga꞉ eletakiyo꞉, Ya꞉suwo꞉ halona ha꞉nabiki, iyo꞉ alolo bo꞉fo꞉leno꞉, E kola꞉ go꞉lulabiki, iliyo꞉ wa꞉kabiyo꞉ mo꞉ba꞉ba꞉.
Ya꞉suwo꞉ akina o꞉ha꞉na꞉labiki, iyo꞉ a꞉no꞉ alolo bo꞉fo꞉li elen ami, kalu a꞉la꞉ nowo꞉, helebeso꞉g ho꞉lo꞉ ka sa꞉ga꞉lela꞉ ko꞉lo꞉, wigibole a꞉naka handalota꞉ga꞉, ili aniba kagayo꞉.
Kalu a꞉la꞉ma꞉yo꞉ imo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Ga꞉lili kalu gio꞉, madali akin amio꞉ alolo bo꞉fo꞉leko꞉ mo꞉wo꞉ ha꞉? Ya꞉su gi o꞉lia꞉lo꞉ elen ko꞉lo꞉ Godeya꞉ Hebenelo꞉ tilia꞉gane a꞉no꞉, E a꞉ma꞉la꞉ yalikiyo꞉, E Hebenelo꞉ ha꞉nabikilo꞉ ba꞉dab o꞉leaum a꞉ma꞉la꞉yo꞉lo꞉ a꞉la꞉ka mia꞉ib.”
Olif misio꞉ a꞉no꞉ Ya꞉lusalem o꞉lia꞉yo꞉ ko꞉na꞉ma ko꞉lo꞉, iyo꞉ Olif misio꞉wo꞉ ta꞉ta꞉sa꞉ga꞉, a꞉ma꞉la꞉ Ya꞉lusalem ane.
Iyo꞉ Ya꞉lusalem fa꞉la꞉dowa꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, ilo꞉ sa꞉sen galale wa꞉l amio꞉ a꞉na tiane. Kalu i a꞉namilo꞉ seno꞉ we, Bida, Yon, Yemes, Andulu, Filib, Tomas, Batolomiyu, Madiyu, Yemes Alofiusa꞉ inso꞉, Saimon Sa꞉la꞉t kalu, a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ Yuda꞉s, Yemesa꞉ inso꞉.
Kalu i a꞉ma꞉yo꞉ asulo꞉wo꞉ imilise dota꞉ga꞉, Godemo꞉ dulugu sa꞉la꞉len. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ Ya꞉su ano, Malia, o꞉lia꞉ ka꞉isale nolo꞉lo꞉, a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ Ya꞉su ao i nolo꞉lo꞉ i o꞉lia꞉ siliki, dulugu sa꞉la꞉len.
Ho꞉len a꞉namio꞉ Ya꞉su amilo꞉ tilidabu kaluka꞉isale agelo꞉wo꞉, do꞉la꞉lowo꞉wo꞉ do꞉la꞉fo꞉ a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ do꞉la꞉fo꞉ a꞉la꞉. Iyo꞉ kegeneliabiki, Bidayo꞉ usa dasilia꞉ga꞉ kagafo꞉liki, towo꞉ imo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉,
“Nao i, Yuda꞉s e ni o꞉lia꞉ sia꞉likilo꞉, nili nanogdo꞉ dia꞉seno꞉ nowo꞉ e. Mo꞉luwo꞉ Mamaya꞉yo꞉ emo꞉ dinali sa꞉labikiyo꞉, Debidi eyo꞉ Godeya꞉ bugo꞉ amio꞉, Yuda꞉s eyo꞉ Ya꞉suwo꞉ teledoma꞉ib a꞉la꞉bo꞉, Debidi e sa꞉sa꞉li alifa꞉. A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ o꞉g wenamio꞉, hendele fa꞉la꞉dowab.” Bida eyo꞉ imo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉.
<range>
Yuda꞉s eyo꞉ mogago꞉wo꞉ dimida꞉sa꞉ga꞉, mole elo꞉ di a꞉ma꞉yo꞉, hen nowo꞉ kilili. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ Yuda꞉s e hen a꞉na ha꞉na꞉sa꞉ga꞉, sulufo꞉ tindakiyo꞉, kufo꞉ elo꞉wo꞉ a꞉no꞉ gasedaki, gono꞉ ha꞉la꞉ya sugusulia꞉ handalowo꞉.
Ya꞉lusa꞉lem kaluka꞉isaleyo꞉ tambo dabu ko꞉lo꞉ iliyo꞉ hen a꞉no꞉ ene to wikilakiyo꞉, Akedama a꞉la꞉sio꞉. To a꞉no꞉ ha꞉go꞉ we, ho꞉bo꞉lo꞉ tulo꞉ hen.
Bida eyo꞉ towo꞉ wa꞉ka a꞉kudu sa꞉laki, “Gisalo꞉ bugo꞉ amio꞉ a꞉la꞉ dinali sio꞉, ‘Hen elo꞉ a꞉namio꞉ kelego꞉wo꞉ aundo꞉ma doma꞉ib ko꞉lo꞉, kalu imilig nowo꞉lo꞉ a꞉namio꞉ mada mo꞉doma꞉ib.’ A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ Gisalo꞉ bugo꞉ amio꞉ to nowo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, ‘Kalu noma꞉yo꞉ nanog elo꞉ dia꞉sen a꞉no꞉ o꞉lika dia꞉ib.’
A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ kalu imilig nowo꞉ ni o꞉lia꞉ gasayaki, Ya꞉su a꞉ma꞉la꞉do꞉ dasi a꞉no꞉ eyo꞉ walama꞉ki, niliyo꞉ da꞉fema꞉nigo꞉l. Kalu a꞉no꞉ negeledo꞉ Ya꞉su o꞉lia꞉lo꞉ sia꞉sen a꞉no꞉, Yon elo꞉ ho꞉n amio꞉ to꞉lolo꞉ a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ mio꞉wo꞉, Ya꞉su elo꞉ Hebenelo꞉ a꞉ma꞉la꞉ anelo꞉ ba꞉ba꞉ a꞉no꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ da꞉fema꞉no꞉” Bida a꞉la꞉sio꞉.
<range>
A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ iliyo꞉ kalu wiyo꞉ a꞉la꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ salifa꞉. Nowo꞉ Yosa꞉b Basabas a꞉la꞉do꞉ sa꞉la꞉sen a꞉no꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ sio꞉. Ene wiyo꞉ nowo꞉ Yustus. Kalu nowo꞉ Matias.
Wi a꞉la꞉ a꞉no꞉ salitakiyo꞉, iliyo꞉ Godemo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉ dulugu sio꞉, “Alan Giyo꞉, nili kufa꞉ uso꞉ ba꞉da꞉sen ko꞉lo꞉ a꞉la꞉ we nowo꞉ Giyo꞉ da꞉feyo꞉lalega, Giyo꞉ nimo꞉wo꞉ walama.
Yuda꞉s e nanog enedo꞉wo꞉ ta꞉ta꞉sa꞉ga꞉, hen elo꞉ ego꞉le, enedo꞉ a꞉na doma꞉ni ane ko꞉lo꞉ kalu a꞉no꞉ e nanogo꞉ dia꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Iliga꞉felo꞉ kalu doma꞉ki, Giyo꞉ nimo꞉wo꞉ walama.”
Iliyo꞉ a꞉la꞉ dulugu sa꞉la꞉sa꞉ga꞉ ami, iyo꞉ wi imilig nowo꞉ fa꞉la꞉doma꞉ki, a꞉la꞉ma꞉ wiyo꞉ ibuwa sa꞉sa꞉la꞉sa꞉ga꞉, a꞉na hea꞉sa꞉ga꞉ ba꞉ba꞉ amio꞉, Matiasa꞉ wiyo꞉ di ko꞉lo꞉ e Iliga꞉felo꞉ kalu kugu a꞉no꞉ e ko꞉lo꞉ dowo꞉.
Bentekos ho꞉len a꞉no꞉ fa꞉la꞉dowabiki, tilidabu kaluka꞉isaleyo꞉ sagala꞉liki, a usa kegeo꞉.
Iyo꞉ a꞉na sen amio꞉, wigibo a꞉naka fo alano꞉, fufa alano꞉ o꞉ngo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ halona a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ a uso꞉ tambo wa꞉lifo꞉.
Iliyo꞉ kelego꞉ nowo꞉, de wa꞉sowayo꞉ eano꞉ o꞉ngo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ ba꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉, de ean o꞉ngo꞉ma꞉yo꞉ kaluka꞉isale tambo gogo alifela꞉i ane.
I a꞉no꞉ tambo amio꞉ Mamayo꞉ ililitabiki, imo꞉wo꞉ asulo꞉wo꞉ dimiaki, halaido꞉wo꞉ dia꞉sa꞉ga꞉, to ko꞉li ko꞉lilo꞉wo꞉ a꞉na mo꞉mo꞉da sio꞉.
Ho꞉len a꞉namio꞉ Yuwa꞉ mando꞉ kudu ha꞉nan kalu nolo꞉ hen ko꞉li ko꞉lilo꞉wa a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ ya꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Ya꞉lusalem a꞉na sen.
Iyo꞉ fo alan a꞉no꞉ da꞉da꞉ga꞉yo꞉ tambo kegea꞉sa꞉ga꞉ ami, Iliga꞉felo꞉ kalu iliyo꞉ to sa꞉lakiyo꞉, kalu kegeo꞉ i a꞉ma꞉ towo꞉ sa꞉labiki, iyo꞉ iligaki kele asulu tandeo꞉.
Iyo꞉ molo asulaki a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Kalu i we Ga꞉lili kalule ko꞉sega o꞉go꞉ ililo꞉ to sa꞉labo꞉, niliyo꞉ nini to a꞉da꞉dab we, mo꞉wo꞉ o꞉bele?
<range>
Nio꞉ heno꞉ ko꞉li ko꞉lilo꞉wa a꞉la꞉ga꞉ga꞉ mio꞉. Nolo꞉ Patia, Midia, Elam. Nowo꞉ Yudia, Kabadosia, Pontus, Esia, Filigia, Bafilia, Isib, a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ Libia hen anibamilo꞉ Salini amisa꞉n a꞉namilo꞉ sa꞉seno꞉ a꞉no꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ mio꞉, a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ nolo꞉ Lom a꞉na a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ ya꞉sio꞉.
<range>
Ni us amio꞉, nolo꞉ Yu kalu, nolo꞉ Yu kaluma ko꞉sega, Yu kalu ililo꞉ tilidabu o꞉leaum, iyo꞉lo꞉ a꞉la꞉tilidabu. Nolo꞉ Kilit kalu, nolo꞉ Alebia kalu, ko꞉sega ililo꞉ Godeya꞉lo꞉ molo ha꞉na꞉no꞉ to widab a꞉no꞉, niliyo꞉ ninin towa꞉ do꞉do꞉l” a꞉la꞉sio꞉.
Iyo꞉ moda꞉sa꞉ga꞉, kele asulaki egelebo꞉ a꞉la꞉dabu ba꞉ba꞉, “We o꞉bo꞉ngo꞉ fa꞉la꞉dowabele?”
Ko꞉sega kalu nolba꞉ya꞉ dio꞉ge sa꞉laki, “Kalu we wain ho꞉n na꞉sa꞉ga꞉ dafolakigab” a꞉la꞉sio꞉.
Bida e, iliga꞉felan kalu kelena꞉la꞉fo꞉ nol o꞉lia꞉ dasila꞉sa꞉ga꞉ kagafo꞉liki, Bida eyo꞉ kaluka꞉isale kegeo꞉ imo꞉wo꞉ towo꞉ halale widakiyo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Yu kalu o꞉lia꞉ Ya꞉lusalemdo꞉ sa꞉sen kalu gio꞉, niyo꞉ mo꞉wo꞉ dinafa fanda sa꞉ma꞉nigo꞉l ko꞉lo꞉ gio꞉ dabuma.
Gili asulakiyo꞉ kalu i we dafolab a꞉la꞉asulab ko꞉sega, o꞉go꞉ ofa꞉si agato꞉wa dowab ko꞉lo꞉ kalu i we mada mo꞉dafolab.
O꞉ngo꞉ma! Kalu i we, dinali sa꞉lan kalu Yoel, elo꞉ dinali sio꞉ o꞉leaum dimidab. Yoel eyo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉,
“‘Godeya꞉yo꞉ sa꞉lakiyo꞉, “Elema꞉no꞉ ho꞉leno꞉ ko꞉na꞉ma dowalikiyo꞉, Ni Mamayo꞉ kaluka꞉isale tambomo꞉ ko꞉go꞉lu alifelema꞉no꞉ ko꞉lo꞉, Gi so꞉wa iyo꞉lo꞉, ga꞉la꞉la꞉yo꞉lo꞉, dinali sa꞉lan kaluwa꞉lo꞉ widan o꞉ngo꞉ doma꞉ib. So꞉wa iliyo꞉ ho꞉le ba꞉ba꞉ib, a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉, kalu anaso꞉ imo꞉wo꞉ ofowo꞉ walalifelema꞉ib.
Ho꞉len a꞉namio꞉, madali nanogdo꞉ dian kaluka꞉isale i a꞉namio꞉lo꞉ Ni Mamayo꞉ ko꞉go꞉lu alifelema꞉no꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ iyo꞉lo꞉ dinali sa꞉lan kaluwa꞉lo꞉ widan o꞉ngo꞉ doma꞉ib.
Niyo꞉ akin halonamio꞉ molo ha꞉na꞉no꞉wo꞉ dimidama꞉no꞉. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ henfelo꞉ wiyo꞉lo꞉ a꞉la꞉dimidama꞉no꞉. Ho꞉bo꞉ o꞉lia꞉ de o꞉lia꞉ a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ de ho꞉mo꞉n alan fa꞉la꞉doma꞉ki dimidama꞉no꞉.
Alana꞉ ho꞉len nafaleyo꞉ o꞉semo꞉fa꞉la꞉dowalikiyo꞉, ofo꞉ sololiaki, eleyo꞉ ho꞉bo꞉ o꞉ngo꞉ doma꞉ib.
Ho꞉len a꞉namio꞉ kaluka꞉isale abeyo꞉ Godeya꞉lo꞉ asuwa꞉foma꞉kilo꞉ tolo꞉ dulugu sa꞉la꞉lab a꞉no꞉, iyo꞉ wa꞉lo꞉ mo꞉diaki, ga꞉li mesea꞉ki ta꞉fa꞉no꞉.”’
“Isolael kalu gio꞉, ni towa꞉ dabuma. Nasa꞉la꞉d kalu Ya꞉su, elo꞉ molo ha꞉na꞉no꞉ gilo꞉ amio꞉ dimido꞉ a꞉no꞉, giliyo꞉ ba꞉ba꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ E hendele Godeya꞉ da꞉fea꞉sa꞉ga꞉ iliga꞉fo꞉lo꞉b a꞉la꞉asuluma꞉ki go꞉.
Godeya꞉yo꞉ Ya꞉suwo꞉ gili dagiya꞉ difa꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ giliyo꞉ E mogago꞉ kalu nolbo꞉ i malana aluma꞉kilo꞉ ta꞉fo꞉ a꞉no꞉, gili sa꞉ndan o꞉ngo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ giliyo꞉ a꞉la꞉dimidama꞉ib a꞉la꞉liki, Godeya꞉yo꞉ mo꞉lu da꞉fefa꞉.
Ko꞉sega Godeya꞉yo꞉ Ya꞉suwo꞉ soma꞉no꞉ nagalo꞉loba꞉da꞉yo꞉ ga꞉li sili alitaki, Eyo꞉ mela꞉no꞉wo꞉ a꞉dimiabiki, Ya꞉su e a꞉ma꞉la꞉yo꞉ a꞉na dasi. Mo꞉wo꞉ sowana꞉ halaido꞉ a꞉ma꞉yo꞉ Ya꞉suwo꞉ mada mo꞉ta꞉li.
Taminde amio꞉ Debidiya꞉yo꞉ Ya꞉su amilo꞉ fa꞉la꞉doma꞉ibo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ asulaki, towo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “‘Ho꞉leno꞉ tambowo꞉ Alan E ne o꞉lia꞉ elena ba꞉ba꞉. E ni dagi ililiba iliki, ni asuwa꞉fa꞉ib ko꞉lo꞉ ne mada mo꞉tagima꞉no꞉.
A꞉la꞉go꞉ko꞉lo꞉ ne sagalo꞉ siliki, niyo꞉ towo꞉ mada sagalo꞉le sa꞉la꞉lo꞉l. Ne sowalikiyo꞉, Giyo꞉ ne dane ane hen a꞉namio꞉ mo꞉ta꞉fa꞉ib. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ gilo꞉ da꞉feyo꞉ kalu a꞉no꞉ hesema꞉kiyo꞉ mo꞉ta꞉fa꞉ib. A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ ne to a꞉no꞉ fanda asulaki, mada mo꞉keleasuluma꞉no꞉.
<range>
Giyo꞉ ne mela꞉no꞉lo꞉ dia꞉no꞉ tog a꞉no꞉ wido꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ ne Ge o꞉lia꞉ silikiyo꞉, mada sagalo꞉wo꞉ alan doma꞉no꞉.’
“Ni nao i, to a꞉no꞉ Debidi eyo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ niyo꞉ o꞉go꞉ gimo꞉wo꞉ fanda so꞉lo꞉l. Mo꞉luwo꞉ nili ma꞉mu Debidi e sowabiki daido꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ elo꞉ daido꞉ hen a꞉no꞉ nilo꞉ sab anib wena a꞉lab.
E dinali sa꞉lan kalu ko꞉lo꞉ Debidiya꞉ e ma꞉mu amilo꞉ kalu so꞉wa fa꞉la꞉dowab a꞉ma꞉yo꞉, tif amio꞉ e misa꞉ kalu dowaki, hen elo꞉ a꞉no꞉ bo꞉fo꞉mela꞉ib a꞉la꞉liki, Godeya꞉lo꞉ dinali sio꞉ a꞉no꞉, eyo꞉ asulo꞉.
A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ Debidi eyo꞉ Godeya꞉lo꞉ dimidama꞉ib a꞉no꞉ e tamin amio꞉ asulakiyo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, ‘E sowalikiyo꞉, dane ane hen a꞉namio꞉ mo꞉ta꞉fa꞉ib a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ ene do꞉mo꞉wo꞉ mo꞉hesema꞉ib.’ Debidi eyo꞉ to a꞉no꞉ sa꞉lakiyo꞉, Gode elo꞉ da꞉feyo꞉ kalu a꞉ma꞉la꞉do꞉ dasima꞉ib a꞉no꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ sio꞉.
Gode Eyo꞉ Ya꞉su E mela꞉no꞉wo꞉ a꞉ma꞉la꞉ dimia꞉sa꞉ga꞉lo꞉ dasi alifa꞉ a꞉no꞉, nio꞉ tambo ninin siya꞉ ba꞉ba꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ so꞉lo꞉l.
Godeya꞉yo꞉ Ya꞉suwo꞉ wabudakiyo꞉, ene wiyo꞉ dulugu sa꞉laki, Ya꞉su e Godeya꞉ dagi ililiba mesea꞉ki ta꞉fo꞉. Do Godeya꞉lo꞉ dinali sio꞉ aumbo꞉ dimidakiyo꞉, Ya꞉sumo꞉wo꞉ Mamayo꞉ dimi ko꞉lo꞉ gilido꞉ o꞉go꞉do꞉ ba꞉dab o꞉lia꞉ da꞉dab o꞉lia꞉ a꞉no꞉, Eyo꞉ ni amio꞉ ko꞉go꞉lu alifelab.
Debidi e Hebeneyo꞉ halona mo꞉ane ko꞉sega eyo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “‘Godeya꞉yo꞉ ni Alanbo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, Niyo꞉ gis kalu gilo꞉wo꞉ gi ha꞉g amio꞉ semo꞉ dia꞉talikiyo꞉, ge ni dagi ililiba siliki, ne o꞉lia꞉ bo꞉fo꞉lubi.’
<range>
“A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ Isolael kaluka꞉isale gio꞉ tambo dinafa asuluma. Gilido꞉ Ya꞉su ko꞉lo꞉ i malana amilo꞉ sana so꞉no꞉ a꞉no꞉, Yesuwo꞉ Godeya꞉ Enedo꞉ Da꞉feyo꞉ Kalu doma꞉ki ta꞉fo꞉. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ Kalu Alan doma꞉ki da꞉feyo꞉wo꞉ e” Bida eyo꞉ towo꞉ a꞉la꞉wido꞉.
Kaluka꞉isaleyo꞉ to Bida elo꞉ widab a꞉no꞉ da꞉dakiyo꞉, iyo꞉ to a꞉ma꞉yo꞉ himuwa olabiki, iliyo꞉ Bidayo꞉ a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ Iliga꞉felo꞉ kalu nol o꞉lia꞉mo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉dabuba꞉ba꞉, “Ni nao i, niliyo꞉ waga dimidama꞉no꞉wele?”
A꞉la꞉dabuba꞉dabiki, Bida eyo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Man mogago꞉ gilido꞉ ena꞉li ena꞉li a꞉la꞉do꞉ dimida꞉leno꞉ ta꞉taki, asugo꞉ nodola꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, Ya꞉su Kelisowa꞉ wiya ho꞉na to꞉loma. A꞉la꞉dimidalikiyo꞉ Godeya꞉yo꞉ gilo꞉ mogago꞉ dimida꞉leno꞉ hala꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Eyo꞉ Ene Mamayo꞉ boba dimia꞉ib.
Godeya꞉lo꞉ tamin dinali sio꞉ a꞉no꞉ gimo꞉wo꞉lo꞉, gi so꞉wa i o꞉mo꞉wo꞉lo꞉, kaluka꞉isale ko꞉na꞉lo꞉ a꞉lab o꞉mo꞉wo꞉lo꞉ a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ kaluka꞉isale abeyo꞉ Gode Alan Elo꞉ amilo꞉ mena꞉kilo꞉ ho꞉idab o꞉mo꞉ tambo sio꞉.” Bida eyo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉.
Bida eyo꞉ imo꞉wo꞉ towo꞉ ko꞉li ko꞉lilo꞉ wida꞉sa꞉ga꞉, hagugo꞉ towo꞉lo꞉ imo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Kaluka꞉isale o꞉gdo꞉ mogago꞉lo꞉ dimida꞉likilo꞉ sab we wa꞉dema꞉ib ko꞉lo꞉ gio꞉lo꞉ Godeya꞉yo꞉ wa꞉deabena꞉ki, dinafa dowa꞉bi” a꞉la꞉sio꞉.
A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ kaluka꞉isale Bidaya꞉ to sa꞉labdo꞉ tilidabu a꞉no꞉, iyo꞉ ho꞉na to꞉lofelo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ ho꞉len a꞉namilo꞉ ho꞉gi tilidabu kaluka꞉isale agelo꞉wo꞉, dausa꞉no꞉ otalen ko꞉lo꞉ fa꞉la꞉dowo꞉. (3,000)
Ho꞉gi tilidabu kaluka꞉isale iliyo꞉ Iliga꞉felo꞉ kaluwa꞉lo꞉ widab a꞉no꞉ tilida꞉dakiyo꞉, egele dowa꞉sen. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ ma꞉no꞉wo꞉ ua sagana꞉likiyo꞉, Yesuwa꞉ asulo꞉ ma꞉no꞉wo꞉lo꞉ ua nakiyo꞉, Godemo꞉ dulugu sa꞉la꞉sen. Iyo꞉ a꞉no꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ dimidakiyo꞉, halaido꞉ dimida꞉len.
Iliga꞉felo꞉ kaluwa꞉yo꞉ molo ha꞉na꞉no꞉wo꞉ dimidabiki, kaluka꞉isaleyo꞉ tambo a꞉no꞉ ba꞉dakiyo꞉ molo tandeakiyo꞉, Gode wiyo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ wabudo꞉.
Tilidabu kaluka꞉isale iyo꞉ asulo꞉ imilise dowaki, kelego꞉ da꞉lab ilido꞉ a꞉no꞉ tambo ua dia꞉mela꞉no꞉ a꞉la꞉liki ta꞉fo꞉.
A꞉la꞉go꞉ko꞉lo꞉ kalu nolba꞉yo꞉ ene hen o꞉lia꞉ kelego꞉ o꞉lia꞉yo꞉ nowo꞉mbo꞉ kililia꞉sa꞉ga꞉, mole diab a꞉no꞉ kalu hebe da꞉lab o꞉mo꞉ sa꞉ga꞉liki ane.
Ho꞉leno꞉ tambowo꞉ iyo꞉ asulo꞉wo꞉ imilig dia꞉taki, Godeya꞉ malilo꞉ aya kegea꞉sen. Iyo꞉ Yesu asulo꞉ ma꞉no꞉ naki o꞉lia꞉ ma꞉no꞉le nakiyo꞉lo꞉, noma꞉ aya kegea꞉liki a꞉lakiyo꞉, iyo꞉ mo꞉kanulu naki, ma꞉no꞉wo꞉ tambowo꞉ sagala꞉liki na꞉sen.
Iliyo꞉ Godeyo꞉ wabuda꞉len a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ kaluka꞉isale tambowa꞉yo꞉ iyo꞉ nafa dowab a꞉la꞉asulo꞉. Ho꞉leno꞉ tambowo꞉ Godeya꞉yo꞉ tilidabu kalu ho꞉gi nolo꞉ i a꞉na gasalita꞉sen.
Ho꞉len no amio꞉, dulugu sa꞉la꞉seno꞉ ofa꞉siyo꞉ asola dowabiki, Bida o꞉lia꞉ Yon o꞉lia꞉yo꞉ Godeya꞉ malilo꞉ aya ha꞉na꞉ni ane.
Godeya꞉ malilo꞉ a amilo꞉ tog nowo꞉ “Gesego꞉” a꞉la꞉sa꞉la꞉sen ko꞉lo꞉ a꞉la꞉yo꞉ tog a꞉na ha꞉nakiyo꞉, giligo꞉ sen kalu nowo꞉ tog aniba sena ba꞉ba꞉. Kalu a꞉no꞉ anowa꞉ e sa꞉la꞉liakiyo꞉, e giligo꞉ o꞉ngo꞉ sa꞉la꞉li ko꞉lo꞉, kaluka꞉isaleyo꞉ aya ha꞉na꞉lab o꞉mo꞉wo꞉ moleyo꞉ ha꞉iya꞉melea꞉ki, ho꞉leno꞉ tambo kalu nolba꞉yo꞉ e ga꞉lilia꞉ga꞉, Tog Gesego꞉ a꞉na tagai ta꞉lila꞉sen.
Giliga꞉sen kalu a꞉no꞉ Bida o꞉lia꞉ Yon o꞉lia꞉yo꞉ fa꞉la꞉dowabiki ba꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, a꞉la꞉mo꞉wo꞉ moleyo꞉ ha꞉iyo꞉.
A꞉la꞉ma꞉yo꞉ e ko꞉lo꞉ sikudu ba꞉daki, Bida eyo꞉ emo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Na꞉no꞉ bo꞉ba!”
Eyo꞉ mole dia꞉no꞉ a꞉la꞉asulaki, a꞉la꞉yo꞉ a꞉na sikudu ba꞉ba꞉.
Ko꞉sega Bida eyo꞉ emo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Ne mole imilig nowo꞉ mada aundo꞉ma ko꞉sega, nilo꞉ da꞉labo꞉ we gemo꞉ dimia꞉nigo꞉l. Nasa꞉la꞉d kalu, Ya꞉su Kelisowa꞉ wi halaido꞉ a꞉ma꞉yo꞉, ge dasilia꞉ga꞉ hamana!”
Bida eyo꞉ a꞉la꞉sa꞉la꞉sa꞉ga꞉, e dasilima꞉ki, dagi ililiba꞉ gasiliabiki, wigibo a꞉naka kalu a꞉ma꞉ gib o꞉lia꞉ gibo꞉ kagoman o꞉lia꞉ halaido꞉ dowabiki, ho꞉lu ya꞉ba꞉sa꞉ga꞉, e a꞉na ane. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ egele Godeya꞉ malilo꞉ a usa tiha꞉nakiyo꞉, e sagala꞉liki, ho꞉lu yabala꞉liki a꞉la꞉i siaki, Godeyo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ wabulu sa꞉la꞉li ane.
<range>
Kaluka꞉isale tambowa꞉yo꞉ e ha꞉na꞉ga꞉ ha꞉nakiyo꞉, Godeya꞉ wiyo꞉ wabuda꞉i ha꞉nabiki ba꞉ba꞉ ko꞉lo꞉, iliyo꞉ e giliga꞉sen kalu Tog Gesego꞉wa silikilo꞉ molelo꞉ ha꞉iya꞉sen o꞉mo꞉lo꞉b a꞉la꞉asulaki, iliyo꞉ e falele alifa꞉lo꞉b a꞉la꞉asula꞉sa꞉ga꞉, iyo꞉ iligakiyo꞉ molo asulo꞉.
<range>
Iyo꞉ Godeya꞉ Malilo꞉ aya, “Solomona꞉ Isagen” a꞉la꞉do꞉ sa꞉la꞉sen a꞉na siliki, kalu a꞉no꞉ Bida o꞉lia꞉ Yon o꞉lia꞉ya ta꞉li dofo꞉labiki, kaluka꞉isaleyo꞉ molo tanda꞉sa꞉ga꞉, ilo꞉wa nai da꞉laido꞉.
Bida e kaluka꞉isale kegeab a꞉no꞉ ba꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, imo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Isolael kalu gio꞉, dimidab we ba꞉dakiyo꞉, waga molo tandeaya? Nanin halaido꞉wa꞉yo꞉ kalu we mo꞉falelo꞉ a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ na꞉no꞉ Godeya꞉ siwa꞉l amio꞉lo꞉ digalo꞉ kalu ko꞉lo꞉ we a꞉na dimido꞉lba. A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ giliyo꞉ na꞉n ba꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉ moda꞉so꞉bo.
Nili ma꞉mu A꞉bla꞉hamo꞉, Aisego꞉, Yekobo꞉ i a꞉ma꞉ Godeya꞉yo꞉ wi alano꞉ Ene Nanogdo꞉ dian kalu, Ya꞉sumo꞉ dimi. Ko꞉sega kalu a꞉no꞉ giliyo꞉ gamani kalumo꞉ sanama꞉ki dimia꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Bailata eyo꞉ e ga꞉li hamana꞉ki ta꞉fa꞉no꞉ asulab, ko꞉sega gio꞉ Bailatdo꞉wa silikiyo꞉, e gola ba꞉ba꞉.
Ya꞉su e mada malilo꞉ digalo꞉ kalu ko꞉sega giliyo꞉ e gola ba꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉, kalu noldo꞉ yasala꞉sen a꞉no꞉ Bailatbo꞉wo꞉ ga꞉li fagegefoma a꞉la꞉sa꞉laki, giliyo꞉ kaluka꞉isalemo꞉lo꞉ mela꞉no꞉lo꞉ dimia꞉sen kalu a꞉no꞉ sana sowo꞉. Ko꞉sega Godeya꞉yo꞉ e a꞉ma꞉la꞉ dasi alitabiki, nio꞉ tambo ba꞉ba꞉.
<range>
A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ kalu gilo꞉ ba꞉da꞉sen we, e Ya꞉suwa꞉ wiya tilida꞉dakiyo꞉, ene tilidabu a꞉ma꞉yo꞉ e falele alifa꞉. Ya꞉suwa꞉ wi o꞉lia꞉ tilidabu eya a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ mio꞉ o꞉lia꞉ma꞉yo꞉ e falele alifa꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ o꞉go꞉ e ga꞉li sabiki, gio꞉ tambo ba꞉dab.
“Nao i, gi o꞉lia꞉ gili misa꞉ kalu o꞉lia꞉ma꞉lo꞉ Ya꞉sumo꞉lo꞉ dimido꞉ a꞉no꞉ gio꞉ babale dofo꞉liki dimido꞉, niyo꞉ a꞉la꞉asulo꞉.
Mo꞉luwo꞉ Godeya꞉yo꞉ enedo꞉ dinali sa꞉lan kaluwa꞉ sama꞉ki, towo꞉ imo꞉wo꞉ tambo dimiakiyo꞉, Enedo꞉ da꞉feyo꞉ kalu a꞉no꞉ odo꞉ sia꞉la꞉ga꞉ soma꞉ib a꞉la꞉saefa꞉ ko꞉lo꞉, o꞉go꞉ Godeya꞉yo꞉ a꞉la꞉ka dimidama꞉ki ta꞉fo꞉.
A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ Godeya꞉yo꞉ gili mogago꞉ dimida꞉sen a꞉no꞉ hala꞉ma꞉ki, gio꞉ mogago꞉wo꞉ ta꞉ta꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Godelo꞉loba꞉da꞉ nodoma. Godeya꞉yo꞉ Enedo꞉ da꞉feyo꞉ kalu, Ya꞉su E a꞉ma꞉la꞉ iliga꞉talikiyo꞉, Alan a꞉no꞉ gi o꞉lia꞉ siliki, ha꞉salo꞉ mesa꞉no꞉ ho꞉len nafale gimo꞉wo꞉ dimina꞉ki, gio꞉ asugo꞉ nodoma.
<range>
O꞉go꞉ Ya꞉su E Hebeneya ilikiyo꞉, Godeya꞉lo꞉ kelego꞉wo꞉ tambo ho꞉gi fa꞉la꞉doma꞉nigab ho꞉len a꞉no꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ yasisab. Ho꞉len a꞉no꞉ tamin amio꞉ Godeya꞉yo꞉ Enedo꞉ dinali sa꞉lan kaluwa꞉ sama꞉ki, towo꞉ imo꞉ salifa꞉.
Tamin amio꞉ Moses eyo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, ‘Gode Alana꞉yo꞉ ne ko꞉lo꞉ gimo꞉lo꞉ iliga꞉fo꞉ aumbo꞉, dinali sa꞉lan kalu noma꞉yo꞉ gimo꞉wo꞉ sama꞉kiyo꞉, Isolael kalu go꞉no꞉na a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ iliga꞉fa꞉ib ko꞉lo꞉, giliyo꞉ to elo꞉ sa꞉labo꞉ tilida꞉da꞉bi.
Kalu abeyo꞉ dinali sa꞉lan kaluwa꞉ to sa꞉lab a꞉no꞉ mo꞉tilida꞉dalikiyo꞉, Godeya꞉yo꞉ aloba꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉ yasala꞉ma꞉ib.’ Moses eyo꞉ a꞉la꞉saefa꞉.
“Tamina Godeya꞉ dinali sa꞉lan kalu, Samuel eya mo꞉mo꞉data꞉ga꞉lo꞉ mio꞉wo꞉, o꞉go꞉do꞉ fa꞉la꞉dowab we iliyo꞉ a꞉no꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ tambo sio꞉.
Gi ma꞉mu imo꞉lo꞉ dinali sa꞉lan kalu tamin amilo꞉ sio꞉ a꞉no꞉, giliyo꞉lo꞉ a꞉no꞉ko꞉ dia꞉ib. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ Godeya꞉yo꞉ A꞉bla꞉ham o꞉lia꞉ e ma꞉mui o꞉lia꞉mo꞉wo꞉ towo꞉ saitakiyo꞉, ‘Gilo꞉ so꞉wa sa꞉la꞉la꞉i ha꞉nab i a꞉na a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉yo꞉, henfelo꞉ amilo꞉ so꞉lo꞉ mesa꞉ib a꞉no꞉ tambo halaido꞉ mesea꞉ki ta꞉fa꞉no꞉.’ To saefa꞉ a꞉no꞉ gimo꞉wo꞉lo꞉ sio꞉.
A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ gio꞉ man mogago꞉ dimida꞉seno꞉ ta꞉ta꞉sa꞉ga꞉, halaido꞉wo꞉ dimina꞉ki, Godeya꞉ Ene nanogdo꞉ dian kaluwo꞉ da꞉fea꞉sa꞉ga꞉, gilo꞉wa tamina iliga꞉fo꞉.”
Bida o꞉lia꞉ Yon o꞉lia꞉yo꞉ kaluka꞉isalemo꞉wo꞉ o꞉wida꞉lena, Godeya꞉ Malilo꞉ alo꞉ bo꞉fo꞉lowan misa꞉ kalu o꞉lia꞉ Godemo꞉lo꞉ boba so꞉mia꞉sen kalu i o꞉lia꞉, Sadusi kaluwo꞉ iyo꞉ tambo ya꞉ga꞉ a꞉la꞉lo꞉wa fa꞉la꞉dowo꞉.
A꞉la꞉ma꞉yo꞉ kaluka꞉isalemo꞉wo꞉ Ya꞉su E dasi ko꞉lo꞉ kaluka꞉isale nolo꞉ o꞉li dasima꞉ib a꞉la꞉likilo꞉ wida꞉lab a꞉no꞉ kalu i a꞉no꞉ da꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉ mada mo꞉beo꞉.
A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ iliyo꞉ kalu a꞉la꞉ a꞉no꞉ mo꞉walilima꞉ni ta꞉li ko꞉sega, ofo꞉ tinabiki, iliyo꞉ ali mo꞉walilima꞉no꞉ a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ a꞉la꞉yo꞉ dibolo a usa disalifa꞉.
Ko꞉sega a꞉la꞉ma꞉lo꞉ to wida꞉lab a꞉namio꞉, kaluka꞉isale modo꞉wo꞉ da꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉ tilidabu ko꞉lo꞉ kalu agelo꞉wo꞉ dausa꞉no꞉ bila꞉fo꞉ (5,000.)
Kea꞉fo Yu kogodo꞉ kalu o꞉lia꞉ elelo꞉ asulo꞉ kalu o꞉lia꞉ Yu misa꞉ kalu iyo꞉ tambo Ya꞉lusalem a꞉na kegea꞉sa꞉ga꞉, bobalo꞉ so꞉mia꞉sen misa꞉ kalu, Anas o꞉lia꞉ ene eso꞉lo꞉ nolo꞉lo꞉ a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ Kaiafaso꞉lo꞉, Yono꞉lo꞉, Alegsandayo꞉lo꞉, i a꞉no꞉ tambo Ya꞉lusalem a꞉na kegeo꞉.
<range>
Iliyo꞉ a꞉la꞉yo꞉ tililia꞉ga꞉ ilo꞉ a꞉lab us a꞉na ta꞉taki, a꞉la꞉mo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉dabuba꞉ba꞉, “Gaindo꞉ dimido꞉ a꞉no꞉, halaido꞉wo꞉ o꞉ba dia꞉sa꞉ga꞉ dimido꞉wo꞉? Abe wi a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ dimido꞉wo꞉?”
A꞉la꞉dabuba꞉dabiki, Bida e, Godeya꞉ Mamayo꞉ wa꞉lifo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ eyo꞉ towo꞉ imo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Yu misa꞉ kalu o꞉lia꞉ kogodo꞉ kalu gio꞉ dabuma.
Naindo꞉ giligo꞉ sen kalu ko꞉lo꞉ asuwa꞉takilo꞉, falele alifa꞉ a꞉no꞉ da꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉, giliyo꞉ o꞉go꞉ na꞉no꞉ a꞉na mo꞉walilab ko꞉lo꞉ giyo꞉lo꞉ Isolael kaluwo꞉lo꞉ tambo asuluma꞉ki, niyo꞉ walama꞉no꞉. Kalu giligo꞉ sen ko꞉lo꞉ falela꞉sa꞉ga꞉lo꞉ kagayab we, Nasa꞉la꞉d kalu, Ya꞉su Kelisowa꞉ wi halaido꞉ a꞉ma꞉yo꞉ mada falele alifa꞉. Giliyo꞉ Ya꞉su E, i malana sana sowo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ Godeya꞉yo꞉ E a꞉ma꞉la꞉ a꞉dasi alifa꞉.
<range>
Godeya꞉ bugo꞉wa sa꞉lakiyo꞉, ‘U ko꞉lo꞉ alo꞉ diana꞉lo꞉ sandifo꞉ a꞉no꞉ o꞉go꞉ u a꞉no꞉ alo꞉ halaido꞉lo꞉ ta꞉li mesa꞉no꞉ dowab’ ko꞉lo꞉ u a꞉no꞉ Ya꞉su E.
Kaluka꞉isale gasilima꞉kilo꞉, Godeya꞉lo꞉ henfelo꞉ wenamilo꞉ iliga꞉fo꞉ kalu nowo꞉ mada aundo꞉ma. Ya꞉su imilise Eyo꞉sa kaluka꞉isaleyo꞉ asuwa꞉taki, a꞉ma꞉la꞉ gasilia꞉ib” Bida eyo꞉ imo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉.
Iliyo꞉ a꞉la꞉yo꞉ mo꞉sugululo꞉ a꞉la꞉asulo꞉ ko꞉sega towo꞉ halaido꞉ sa꞉lab a꞉no꞉ da꞉dakiyo꞉, molo asulo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ iliyo꞉ kalu a꞉la꞉ we tamin amio꞉ Ya꞉su o꞉lia꞉lo꞉ sia꞉leno꞉ o꞉mo꞉lo꞉b a꞉la꞉bo꞉ a꞉na asulo꞉.
Ko꞉sega giligo꞉ kalu ko꞉lo꞉ falelo꞉ a꞉no꞉ a꞉la꞉ o꞉lia꞉lo꞉ kagayab a꞉no꞉ iliyo꞉ ba꞉ba꞉ ko꞉lo꞉, iliyo꞉ to halaido꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉mo꞉wo꞉ mo꞉sio꞉.
A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ iliyo꞉ a꞉la꞉yo꞉ ha꞉la꞉ya o꞉hamana a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉, egelebo꞉ towo꞉ a꞉la꞉nenelo꞉, “Niliyo꞉ kalu a꞉la꞉ o꞉mo꞉wo꞉ waga dimidama꞉no꞉wele? A꞉la꞉ma꞉lo꞉ molo ha꞉na꞉no꞉ dimido꞉ a꞉no꞉ Ya꞉lusalem kaluka꞉isaleyo꞉ tambo o꞉ma asululi ko꞉lo꞉ niliyo꞉ ‘we hendelema’ a꞉la꞉bo꞉ mo꞉sa꞉ma꞉no꞉.
<range>
Ko꞉sega a꞉la꞉ma꞉lo꞉ dimido꞉ a꞉no꞉ kaluka꞉isale nolo꞉ da꞉daba꞉na꞉ki, a꞉la꞉mo꞉wo꞉ towo꞉ halaido꞉ a꞉la꞉sa꞉ma꞉no꞉, ‘Ga꞉go꞉ Ya꞉suwa꞉ wi amilo꞉ wa꞉kabiyo꞉ wida꞉so꞉bo!’ a꞉la꞉ka sa꞉ma꞉nigo꞉l.”
Iliyo꞉ a꞉la꞉nenela꞉sa꞉ga꞉ dotakiyo꞉, a꞉la꞉yo꞉ a꞉ma꞉la꞉ mena꞉ki ho꞉lelia꞉ga꞉, a꞉la꞉mo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Gaino꞉ Ya꞉suwa꞉ wi sa꞉lakiyo꞉ wa꞉kabiyo꞉ mada wida꞉so꞉bo,” a꞉la꞉liki iliyo꞉ halaido꞉ sio꞉.
Ko꞉sega Bida o꞉lia꞉ Yon dia꞉ma꞉yo꞉ a꞉ma꞉la꞉yo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Na꞉no꞉ gili towo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ kudu ha꞉na꞉no꞉ kibo꞉bowo꞉, Godeya꞉ towo꞉ mo꞉kuduha꞉na꞉no꞉ domabe ko꞉lo꞉ ginino꞉ dinafa alobana ba꞉da꞉bi.
Mo꞉wo꞉ naindo꞉ ba꞉ba꞉yo꞉ a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ dabu a꞉no꞉ mada tambo wida꞉mela꞉no꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ mo꞉ka꞉ma꞉no꞉.”
A꞉la꞉ma꞉yo꞉ a꞉la꞉sa꞉labiki, iliyo꞉ a꞉la꞉mo꞉wo꞉ towo꞉ wa꞉ka halaido꞉ sa꞉la꞉sa꞉ga꞉, a꞉la꞉yo꞉ ga꞉li iliga꞉fo꞉. Mo꞉wo꞉ Ya꞉lusalem kaluka꞉isale ililo꞉ ba꞉ba꞉ a꞉no꞉ Godeyo꞉ wabudabiki, Yu misa꞉ kaluwa꞉yo꞉ a꞉la꞉ falasila꞉ma꞉no꞉wo꞉ mo꞉dowo꞉.
Mo꞉wo꞉ giligo꞉ sen kalu e, donayo꞉ do꞉la꞉fo꞉ fa꞉la꞉da꞉in dota꞉sa꞉ga꞉, a꞉na falelo꞉.
A꞉la꞉yo꞉ ga꞉li iliga꞉tab amio꞉, tilidabu kaluka꞉isalelo꞉ saba ha꞉na꞉sa꞉ga꞉, bobalo꞉ so꞉mia꞉sen misa꞉ kalu o꞉lia꞉ Yu ko꞉go꞉do꞉ kalu o꞉lia꞉ma꞉lo꞉ sio꞉ a꞉no꞉ a꞉la꞉ma꞉yo꞉ imo꞉wo꞉ tambo malolo꞉ me.
Iliyo꞉ a꞉no꞉ da꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, tambo kegea꞉sa꞉ga꞉ Godemo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉dulugu sio꞉, “Wiso꞉ Alan, Ge akino꞉lo꞉, henfelo꞉wo꞉lo꞉, ho꞉no꞉lo꞉ a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ kelego꞉ tambo usamilo꞉ a꞉lab a꞉no꞉, tambo Gi dimido꞉.
Nili ma꞉mu Debidi e Gi nanogdo꞉ dian kalu ko꞉lo꞉ Godeya꞉ Mamaya꞉ ene halaido꞉ emo꞉ dimiabiki, Gi to we a꞉na sa꞉sa꞉lo꞉, “‘Henfelo꞉ kaluka꞉isaleyo꞉ waga mada kulufa꞉yabele? Iliyo꞉ Gode o꞉lia꞉ madalilo꞉ babuma꞉no꞉ saitab we, waga nenelabele?
Henfelo꞉ amilo꞉ misa꞉ kaluwo꞉ kegea꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Gode o꞉lia꞉ Enedo꞉ Da꞉feyo꞉ Kalu o꞉lia꞉yo꞉ babuma꞉ni dimidaliab.’
Go꞉no꞉n towo꞉ bugo꞉ amio꞉ a꞉la꞉sa꞉sa꞉lo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ o꞉g a꞉namio꞉ Helot o꞉lia꞉ Bontius Bailat o꞉lia꞉ Yuma kalu o꞉lia꞉ Isolael kalu o꞉lia꞉yo꞉ Ya꞉lusalem wena kegea꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Ya꞉su, Gili nanogdo꞉ digalelo꞉ dian kalu e sana soma꞉no꞉wo꞉ togo꞉ kedo꞉. Ya꞉su E Go꞉no꞉n Da꞉feyo꞉ Kalu ko꞉lo꞉ ililo꞉ kegeasa꞉ga꞉lo꞉ dimido꞉ a꞉no꞉ tambo, mo꞉luwo꞉ Go꞉no꞉n asulo꞉ o꞉lia꞉ Go꞉no꞉n halaido꞉ o꞉lia꞉ma꞉ saefa꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ fa꞉la꞉dowo꞉.
<range>
A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ Alan Ge, Yu misa꞉ kalu ililo꞉ nimo꞉lo꞉ to halaido꞉ sio꞉ a꞉no꞉ asulaki, go꞉no꞉n nanog dian kalu nio꞉ Gi towo꞉ halaido꞉ walama꞉ki, asuwa꞉ta꞉biyo꞉.
Gode go꞉no꞉n halaido꞉wa꞉ widakiyo꞉, gi nanog dian kalu, Ya꞉suwa꞉ wiya ilikiyo꞉, kaluka꞉isaleyo꞉ falele alifelaki, molo ha꞉na꞉no꞉ nolo꞉ dimida꞉lubi.”
Iliyo꞉ dulugu sa꞉la꞉sa꞉ga꞉ dotabiki, a ilo꞉ sen a꞉no꞉ ida꞉la꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Mamayo꞉ i amio꞉ wa꞉litabiki, iyo꞉ mo꞉tagilaki, Godeya꞉ towo꞉ halaido꞉ mo꞉mo꞉da wido꞉.
Tilidabu kaluka꞉isaleyo꞉ asulo꞉ imilise dota꞉ga꞉, iyo꞉ “kelego꞉ we na꞉no꞉” a꞉la꞉bo꞉ mo꞉asulaki, tambowo꞉ ua a꞉no꞉ dowo꞉.
Iliga꞉felo꞉ kalu iliyo꞉ a꞉la꞉widaki, “Alan Ya꞉su E hendele a꞉ma꞉la꞉ dasilia꞉ga꞉, mela꞉no꞉ a꞉labka꞉!” a꞉la꞉likilo꞉ towo꞉ halaido꞉ wida꞉len ko꞉lo꞉ Godeya꞉yo꞉ Ene kelego꞉ nafaleyo꞉ iya kogolu alifa꞉.
I usamio꞉ kalu imilig nowo꞉ ma꞉no꞉wo꞉, kelego꞉wo꞉ aundo꞉malo꞉ mo꞉dowo꞉. Mo꞉wo꞉ kalu imilig nowo꞉ kelego꞉lo꞉ma dowalikiyo꞉, kalu noma꞉yo꞉ ba꞉da꞉ga꞉, ene hen o꞉lia꞉ a o꞉lia꞉ kililia꞉sa꞉ga꞉, mole a꞉no꞉ Iliga꞉felo꞉ kalu o꞉mo꞉ dimi ko꞉lo꞉ iliyo꞉ aloba꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉, kelego꞉wo꞉ hebe da꞉lab kalu i o꞉mo꞉ dimia꞉i ane.
<range>
A꞉la꞉gabiki kalu imilig nowo꞉ ene wiyo꞉ Yosa꞉b eyo꞉ a꞉la꞉dimido꞉. Ene mo꞉mio꞉wo꞉ Libai ko꞉lo꞉ hen elo꞉wo꞉ Saibulus. Iliga꞉felo꞉ kalu i a꞉ma꞉yo꞉ ene wi ho꞉gi nowo꞉, Banabas wikilo꞉. Ene wi a꞉ma꞉ ha꞉go꞉ we, nowo꞉ sagala꞉ma꞉kilo꞉ asuwa꞉ta꞉sen kalu.
Banabas eyo꞉ hen heb enedo꞉wo꞉ kililia꞉sa꞉ga꞉, moleyo꞉ dia꞉ya꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Iliga꞉felo꞉ kalu i o꞉mo꞉ dimi.
Ko꞉sega, kalu a꞉namilo꞉ seno꞉ nowo꞉ ene wiyo꞉ Ananaias, a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ ene inga, Safaila ko꞉lo꞉ sen. A꞉la꞉ma꞉yo꞉lo꞉ hen heb inido꞉wo꞉ kililia꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, Ananaias eyo꞉ mole hebo꞉ ene kanulu difa꞉. A꞉la꞉do꞉ gab a꞉no꞉ ingaya꞉yo꞉lo꞉ o꞉li gabolo꞉b a꞉la꞉asulo꞉. Ananaias eyo꞉ mole heb nolo꞉ Iliga꞉felo꞉ kalulo꞉wa dia꞉ha꞉na꞉ga꞉ dimi.
<range>
Emo꞉ dimiabiki, Bida eyo꞉ emo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Ananaias, asulo꞉ gilo꞉wo꞉ Setene bo꞉fo꞉melea꞉ki, fogo꞉ dimi ko꞉lo꞉, giyo꞉ Godeya꞉ Mamayo꞉ a꞉na dikili sa꞉lakiyo꞉, moleyo꞉ hebo꞉ go꞉no꞉ndo꞉ kanulu difa꞉ a꞉no꞉, waga asulaki dimido꞉wo꞉?
Giyo꞉ heno꞉ semo꞉kilili amio꞉, hen a꞉no꞉ hendele ga꞉no꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ kililia꞉sa꞉ga꞉ mole di a꞉no꞉ ga꞉lo꞉ asulab aumbo꞉ o꞉li dimidama꞉no꞉ dowo꞉. A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉, giyo꞉ dikilima꞉no꞉ a꞉la꞉likiyo꞉ waga asulaki sa꞉laya? Madalilo꞉ sa꞉lako꞉, giyo꞉ kaluwo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ dikidaba. Godeyo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ dikili sa꞉lab.”
Ananaias e to a꞉no꞉ da꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉, elo꞉ elen a꞉naka, sulufo꞉ tina꞉sa꞉ga꞉ sowo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉, kalu nolo꞉ to a꞉no꞉ da꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, tagio꞉ alan dowo꞉.
Ananaias e sowabiki, kalu so꞉wa nolo꞉ ya꞉ga꞉, so꞉ga꞉ mela꞉sa꞉ga꞉, dia꞉ha꞉na꞉ga꞉ a꞉na daido꞉.
A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ ofa꞉si otalen ta꞉ta꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, ingayo꞉ Ananaias sowo꞉wo꞉ mo꞉da꞉daki, elo꞉ Bidalo꞉wa mio꞉.
A꞉na fa꞉la꞉dowabiki, Bidaya꞉ emo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉dabuba꞉ba꞉, “Mole gaindo di a꞉no꞉, tambo yomo꞉?” A꞉la꞉sa꞉labiki, Safaila eyo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “A꞉, moleyo꞉ tambo dia꞉mio꞉ yom.”
A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ Bida eyo꞉ emo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Ga꞉go꞉ towo꞉ imilise saeta꞉ga꞉yo꞉, Godeya꞉ Mamayo꞉ da꞉fe ba꞉ba꞉nikiyo꞉, Emo꞉wo꞉ waga dikili sa꞉laya? Ge kalulo꞉ daida꞉len kalu i a꞉no꞉ tog amilo꞉ o꞉yayom ko꞉lo꞉ gelo꞉ a꞉na dia꞉ha꞉na꞉sa꞉ga꞉ dalima꞉nigab.”
Safaila e to a꞉no꞉ko꞉ da꞉dabiki, e sulufo꞉ tina꞉sa꞉ga꞉ sowo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ kalu so꞉wa i a꞉no꞉ ya꞉ga꞉yo꞉, e sowo꞉lo꞉bi ba꞉da꞉ga꞉, iliyo꞉ e dia꞉ha꞉na꞉ga꞉ indo daido꞉ anib a꞉na dalialifa꞉.
Tilidabu kaluka꞉isale tambo olia꞉ kalu nol a꞉namio꞉ sen a꞉no꞉lia꞉yo꞉, malolo꞉ a꞉no꞉ da꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉, iyo꞉ tambo tagi alan dowo꞉.
Iliga꞉felo꞉ kalu iliyo꞉ molo ha꞉na꞉no꞉ ko꞉li ko꞉lilo꞉wo꞉ amisa꞉n us a꞉na dimida꞉len. Tilidabu kaluka꞉isale iyo꞉ ua, Solomona꞉ Isagen a꞉na kegea꞉sen.
Ha꞉la꞉ kaluka꞉isale nol a꞉ma꞉yo꞉ iyo꞉ mada nafale a꞉la꞉asulo꞉ ko꞉sega ha꞉la꞉ kaluka꞉isale i a꞉no꞉ tagilaki, i o꞉lia꞉ mo꞉ gasa kegea꞉sen.
Ko꞉sega ho꞉leno꞉ tambowo꞉, kaluka꞉isale modo꞉ nolo꞉ Alano꞉ tilida꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉, tamin tilidabu kaluka꞉isale i o꞉lia꞉yo꞉ ua gasaya꞉len.
Amisa꞉n kaluka꞉isaleyo꞉ Iliga꞉felo꞉ kalu ililo꞉ molo ha꞉na꞉no꞉ dimida꞉lab a꞉no꞉ ba꞉ba꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ ili asulakiyo꞉ Bidayo꞉ ha꞉nab amio꞉ mama elo꞉ma꞉yo꞉ walaf kalu ka꞉isale iyo꞉ galalalikiyo꞉ falelema꞉ib a꞉la꞉asula꞉sa꞉ga꞉, iliyo꞉ i a꞉no꞉ ga꞉lilia꞉ ya꞉ga꞉, nolo꞉ wo꞉ba, nolo꞉ geondo꞉ wa꞉la alima꞉ki, tog anib a꞉na ta꞉felo꞉.
A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ kaluka꞉isale modo꞉, Ya꞉lusalem anib amilo꞉ kandayo꞉ i a꞉no꞉ kegeo꞉. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ iyo꞉ walafdo꞉ kaluka꞉isale o꞉lia꞉ kalu mama mogago꞉lo꞉ dosdo꞉ o꞉lia꞉yo꞉ tililia꞉ga꞉, Iliga꞉felo꞉ kalulowa yabiki, i a꞉no꞉ tambo falele alifelo꞉.
Bobalo꞉ so꞉mia꞉sen misa꞉ kalu o꞉lia꞉ ene mili, Sadusi kalu o꞉lia꞉ma꞉yo꞉ iliga꞉felo꞉ kalu ilo꞉lo꞉ dimidab a꞉no꞉ ba꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉, iliyo꞉ iliga꞉felo꞉ kalumo꞉wo꞉ mo꞉beaki eteyo꞉wo꞉ alan fa꞉la꞉dowo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ iliyo꞉ iliga꞉felo꞉ kalu i a꞉no꞉ ta꞉lia꞉sa꞉ga꞉, mogago꞉ kalu o꞉lia꞉ dibolo a usa disa꞉.
<range>
Ko꞉sega o꞉g nulu a꞉namio꞉, Godeya꞉ ma꞉mul kaluwa꞉yo꞉ dibolo a a꞉no꞉, togo꞉ koda꞉sa꞉ga꞉, iyo꞉ ha꞉la꞉ya tilili ya꞉ga꞉ handalowakiyo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Gio꞉ ha꞉na꞉sa꞉ga꞉ Godeya꞉ malilo꞉ a usa kagafo꞉liki, gililo꞉ mela꞉no꞉ ho꞉gi di a꞉no꞉ kaluka꞉isalemo꞉wo꞉ tambo wida꞉lubi” eyo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉.
<range>
Elo꞉ sio꞉ o꞉leaum iliyo꞉ a꞉la꞉dimidaki, kea꞉fo nulu ofo꞉ yabikiyo꞉, iyo꞉ Godeya꞉ malilo꞉ aya tina꞉sa꞉ga꞉, a꞉na mo꞉mo꞉da wido꞉. O꞉g kea꞉fo nulu a꞉nami, bobalo꞉ so꞉mia꞉sen misa꞉ kalu o꞉lia꞉ e o꞉lia꞉lo꞉ elen kalu o꞉lia꞉ma꞉yo꞉, Yu amilo꞉ Kanisolo dosdo꞉wo꞉ a꞉na kegeo꞉. Isolael misa꞉ kalu tambo a꞉na kegea꞉sa꞉ga꞉, iliyo꞉ iliga꞉felo꞉ kaluwo꞉ tililia꞉ mena꞉ki dibololo꞉ sab a꞉na to saga꞉fo꞉.
Ko꞉sega dibolo alo꞉ bo꞉fo꞉lowan kaluwo꞉ aya ha꞉na꞉sa꞉ga꞉ ba꞉ba꞉ amio꞉, Iliga꞉felo꞉ kalu i a꞉no꞉ a꞉namilo꞉ mo꞉sena ba꞉ba꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ iyo꞉ a꞉ma꞉la꞉ ha꞉na꞉sa꞉ga꞉ misa꞉ kalumo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Nio꞉ dibolo aya fa꞉la꞉dowaki ba꞉ba꞉ amio꞉, togo꞉ tambo uludo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉, dibolo alo꞉ bo꞉fo꞉lowan kaluwo꞉ toga꞉me amio꞉ o꞉li yasila꞉len ko꞉sega, nio꞉ dibolo a usamio꞉, kalu i a꞉no꞉ mada aundo꞉ma elena ba꞉ba꞉.”
<range>
Bobalo꞉ so꞉mia꞉sen misa꞉ kalu i o꞉lia꞉ Godeya꞉ malilo꞉ alo꞉ bo꞉fo꞉lowan misa꞉ kalu o꞉lia꞉ma꞉yo꞉ to a꞉no꞉ da꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉, iyo꞉ molo asulakiyo꞉, o꞉b ko꞉lo꞉ fa꞉la꞉doma꞉nigabele a꞉la꞉liki modo꞉.
Iyo꞉ a꞉la꞉asula꞉li elen ami, kalu imilise nowo꞉ ya꞉ga꞉, imo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Dabuma. Kalu gililo꞉ dibolo ayamilo꞉ disa꞉ a꞉no꞉, Godeya꞉ malilo꞉ aya kagafo꞉liki, kaluka꞉isalemo꞉wo꞉ towo꞉ a꞉na wida꞉lab” a꞉la꞉sio꞉.
A꞉la꞉sa꞉labiki, Godeya꞉ malilo꞉ alo꞉ bo꞉fo꞉lowan misa꞉ kalu o꞉lia꞉ dibolo alo꞉ bo꞉fo꞉lowan i o꞉lia꞉yo꞉ ha꞉na꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Iliga꞉felo꞉ kalu i a꞉no꞉ a꞉ma꞉la꞉ tililia꞉ mio꞉. Kaluka꞉isale i a꞉namilo꞉ sab a꞉ma꞉yo꞉ bo꞉fo꞉lowan kalu iyo꞉ uwa꞉yo꞉ agodoma꞉ib a꞉la꞉asula꞉sa꞉ga꞉, iyo꞉ tagilaki, iliga꞉felo꞉ kalu a꞉no꞉ mo꞉yami tandeaki, ha꞉sa tilia꞉mio꞉.
Dibolo alo꞉ bo꞉fo꞉lowan kaluwa꞉yo꞉ Iliga꞉felo꞉ kalu iyo꞉ tilili ya꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Yuwa꞉ kanisolo kalulo꞉wa ta꞉fo꞉liki, bobalo꞉ so꞉mia꞉sen misa꞉ kalu eyo꞉ imo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Niliyo꞉ tamin amio꞉ gimo꞉wo꞉ ‘kalu wa꞉ma꞉ wi amio꞉ kaluka꞉isalemo꞉wo꞉ wida꞉so꞉boka꞉’ a꞉la꞉bo꞉ towo꞉ halaido꞉ saefa꞉ ko꞉sega giliyo꞉ Ya꞉lusalem kaluka꞉isalemo꞉wo꞉ tambo towo꞉ wida꞉li ha꞉nab ko꞉lo꞉ giliyo꞉ kaluka꞉isalemo꞉wo꞉ ‘kalu we nili sanasowo꞉ka꞉’ a꞉la꞉li diga꞉li sa꞉la꞉lab” a꞉la꞉sio꞉.
<range>
To a꞉no꞉ da꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Bida o꞉lia꞉ Iliga꞉felo꞉ kalu i nol a꞉ma꞉yo꞉ towo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Niliyo꞉ kaluwa꞉ towo꞉ mo꞉kudu ha꞉na꞉no꞉ ko꞉sega, Godeya꞉ Ene toleyo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ mada kudu ha꞉na꞉no꞉.
Giliyo꞉ Ya꞉suwo꞉ i malana alula꞉sa꞉ga꞉ sana sowo꞉ ko꞉sega, nili ma꞉muwa꞉ Godeya꞉yo꞉ E a꞉ma꞉la꞉ dasi alifa꞉ ko꞉lo꞉lab.
Isolael kaluka꞉isaleya꞉yo꞉ asugo꞉ nodola꞉sa꞉ga꞉, ililo꞉ mogago꞉ dimida꞉seno꞉ hama꞉ki, Godeya꞉yo꞉ Ya꞉suwo꞉ iwalu dia꞉takiyo꞉, ene dagi ililiba ta꞉fo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ Ya꞉su E misa꞉ kalu dowaki, Eyo꞉ kaluka꞉isaleyo꞉ a꞉ma꞉la꞉ gasilia꞉no꞉ dowo꞉.
A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ Godeya꞉yo꞉ kaluka꞉isaleyo꞉ E tolo꞉ kuduha꞉na꞉sen imo꞉wo꞉ Ene Mamayo꞉ dimi ko꞉lo꞉, Godeya꞉lo꞉ dimido꞉ a꞉no꞉ tambo ni o꞉lia꞉ Godeya꞉ Mama o꞉lia꞉ma꞉yo꞉ ba꞉ba꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ a꞉no꞉ wido꞉l”
Iliyo꞉ Bida elo꞉ to sa꞉lab a꞉no꞉ da꞉dakiyo꞉, kulufa꞉yo꞉wo꞉ alan dowa꞉sa꞉ga꞉, iyo꞉ yasalema꞉no꞉ asulo꞉.
Ko꞉sega Fa꞉lisi kalu nowo꞉, ene wiyo꞉ Gamaliel, e elelo꞉ asulo꞉ kalu ko꞉lo꞉ Yu kaluka꞉isale iyo꞉ man elo꞉wo꞉ nafale ba꞉da꞉sen. O꞉g a꞉namio꞉ Gamaliel e, misa꞉ kalu o꞉lia꞉ sen ko꞉lo꞉, e dasila꞉sa꞉ga꞉, kalu nolbo꞉wo꞉ “Iliga꞉felo꞉ kaluwo꞉ ha꞉la꞉ya o꞉tililia꞉ hamana” a꞉la꞉sa꞉la꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Yu misa꞉ kalu imo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Isolael kalu giliyo꞉, kelego꞉ nowo꞉ kalu i wemo꞉wo꞉ dimidama꞉no꞉lalega, giliyo꞉ dinafa asula꞉bi.
<range>
Mo꞉wo꞉ o꞉semo꞉amalela꞉ amio꞉, kalu nowo꞉ Teudas e babuma꞉niki, kalu alan o꞉ngo꞉ dasilabiyo꞉, kalu do꞉la꞉lowo꞉wo꞉ do꞉la꞉fo꞉ fa꞉la꞉da꞉in e kudu ane. Ko꞉sega e sana sowabikiyo꞉, kalu elo꞉ kudu ane a꞉no꞉ tambo dalale ane ko꞉lo꞉ elo꞉ dimidama꞉no꞉ asulo꞉ a꞉no꞉ madali wala꞉.
A꞉ma꞉ fa꞉s amio꞉, wilo꞉ sa꞉sa꞉lan ho꞉leno꞉ dowabikiyo꞉, Yuda꞉s, Ga꞉lili kalu eyo꞉lo꞉ dasila꞉sa꞉ga꞉, eyo꞉ kalu nolo꞉ hala tilia꞉gane ko꞉sega e sana sowabiki, kalu elo꞉ kudu ane a꞉no꞉ tambo dalale ane.
A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ o꞉gdo꞉ fa꞉la꞉dowab we gio꞉ asula꞉bi. Ililo꞉ dimidab we, inin asulo꞉wa fa꞉la꞉dowa꞉sa꞉ga꞉ dimidabo꞉lalega, ililo꞉ dimidama꞉no꞉ asulab a꞉no꞉ madali walema꞉ib. Ko꞉sega nanog a꞉no꞉ Godelo꞉wa a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ mio꞉lalega, giliyo꞉ ililo꞉ nanog diab a꞉no꞉ mada mo꞉ka꞉ma꞉ib. Giliyo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ ka꞉ma꞉no꞉ susialega, gio꞉ Gode o꞉lia꞉ bubaki auma꞉ib. A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ giliyo꞉ mogago꞉ imili nowo꞉ i o꞉lia꞉yo꞉ mo꞉dimidaki, iyo꞉ ga꞉li melea꞉ki ta꞉ta꞉bi.”
<range>
Gamaliel eyo꞉ a꞉la꞉sa꞉labiki, Yu misa꞉ kalu iliyo꞉ elo꞉ to sa꞉lab a꞉no꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ kudu ane. Iliyo꞉ Iliga꞉felo꞉ kaluwo꞉ a꞉ma꞉la꞉ tilia꞉a꞉sa꞉ga꞉ dotabiki, dibolo alo꞉ bo꞉fo꞉lowan kaluwa꞉yo꞉ iyo꞉ sanama꞉ki a꞉na sio꞉ ko꞉lo꞉, sa꞉nda꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉ Iliga꞉felo꞉ kalu imo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Giliyo꞉ Ya꞉suwa꞉ wi sa꞉lakiyo꞉, wa꞉kabiyo꞉ mada wida꞉so꞉bo.” Imo꞉wo꞉ towo꞉ a꞉la꞉ halale sa꞉la꞉sa꞉ga꞉, iliga꞉fo꞉.
A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ iyo꞉ Yu misa꞉ kalu kegeo꞉ a꞉no꞉ ta꞉ta꞉sa꞉ga꞉ ha꞉nakiyo꞉, Godeya꞉yo꞉ iyo꞉ Ya꞉suwa꞉ wiya a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉lo꞉ sendelowo꞉wo꞉ o꞉li diab a꞉la꞉do꞉ asulab a꞉no꞉, iyo꞉ sagala꞉liki ane.
A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ Godeya꞉ malilo꞉ ayamio꞉lo꞉, kaluka꞉isaleya꞉ ayamio꞉lo꞉ Godeya꞉ Ene to nafa widakiyo꞉, Ya꞉su E, Godeya꞉ Enedo꞉ Da꞉feyo꞉ kaluwo꞉ E a꞉la꞉liki iliyo꞉ ho꞉leno꞉ tambo wida꞉li sia꞉liki mo꞉edo꞉.
Ho꞉len a꞉namio꞉ Gode amilo꞉ tilidabu kaluwo꞉ modo꞉ fa꞉la꞉dosdo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ i us a꞉namio꞉ Gilik tolo꞉ sa꞉lan kaluwa꞉yo꞉, Alam tolo꞉ sa꞉lan kalumo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Giliyo꞉ ma꞉no꞉ sagakiyo꞉, ka꞉isale sa꞉ba꞉lo꞉ nilido꞉ a꞉lab a꞉no꞉ mo꞉mia꞉sen” a꞉la꞉sa꞉laki, iyo꞉ towa꞉yo꞉ kego꞉.
A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ Iliga꞉felo꞉ kalu kugula꞉fo꞉ a꞉ma꞉yo꞉, tilidabu kaluwo꞉ tambo ho꞉le kegea꞉sa꞉ga꞉, imo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Nio꞉ nanog diakiyo꞉, Godeya꞉ to walama꞉no꞉wo꞉ kadetaki, ma꞉no꞉ sagama꞉no꞉ dowalega mogago꞉ doma꞉ib.
A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ giliyo꞉ kalu dom a꞉la꞉fo꞉wo꞉ da꞉fea꞉sa꞉ga꞉, niliyo꞉ nanog we imo꞉ dima꞉ki dimia꞉no꞉. Kalu gililo꞉ da꞉feab a꞉no꞉, iyo꞉ asulo꞉wo꞉ alan, Godeya꞉ Mamalo꞉ wa꞉lifo꞉ a꞉lab a꞉no꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ da꞉fea꞉bi.
Giliyo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ a꞉la꞉dimidalikiyo꞉, ho꞉leno꞉ tambowo꞉ niliyo꞉ Godemo꞉ dulugu sa꞉la꞉liki, Ene towo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ walasa꞉la꞉li mesa꞉no꞉.”
Iliyo꞉ a꞉la꞉sa꞉labiki, tilidabu kaluka꞉isale iliyo꞉ to sa꞉lab a꞉no꞉ da꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉ tambo sagalaki, iliyo꞉ kalu nolo꞉ da꞉feyo꞉. Da꞉feyo꞉ kaluwo꞉ nowo꞉ Sitifen. E tilidabu alan a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ Godeya꞉ Mamayo꞉ e amio꞉ wa꞉lifo꞉. Da꞉feyo꞉ kalu nowo꞉ we, Filib, Bolokolus, Nikanol, Timon, Balmenas, a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ nowo꞉ Nikolas, e Antio꞉g amisa꞉n kalu ko꞉lo꞉ e tamin amio꞉ Yu kaluwa꞉lo꞉ tilidabu a꞉no꞉ elo꞉ kudu ane.
Tilidabu kalu iyo꞉ doma꞉la꞉fo꞉ a꞉no꞉ da꞉fea꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Iliga꞉felo꞉ kalulo꞉wa tililia꞉ga꞉, Iliga꞉felo꞉ kaluwa꞉yo꞉ iyo꞉ Godemo꞉ dulugu sa꞉la꞉sa꞉ga꞉, dagiyo꞉ ili misa꞉ wa꞉la difa꞉.
A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ Godeya꞉ towo꞉ da꞉da꞉i ha꞉nakiyo꞉, Ya꞉lusalem amisa꞉n amio꞉, tilidabu kaluka꞉isaleyo꞉ modo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ fa꞉la꞉dowo꞉. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ Godemo꞉lo꞉ bobalo꞉ so꞉mia꞉sen kalu nolo꞉lo꞉ modo꞉ tilidabu.
Godeya꞉yo꞉ Sitifen e asuwa꞉taki, halaido꞉ emo꞉wo꞉ dimi ko꞉lo꞉ Sitifen eyo꞉ kaluka꞉isale siwa꞉l amio꞉ molo ha꞉na꞉no꞉wo꞉ ko꞉li ko꞉lilo꞉ dimido꞉.
Ko꞉sega Yu kalu nolba꞉yo꞉ e o꞉lia꞉yo꞉ towa꞉yo꞉ kego꞉. Kalu i a꞉ma꞉ tolo꞉ wida꞉sen a wiyo꞉ we “Kalu ga꞉li ha꞉na꞉sen A” a꞉la꞉sa꞉la꞉sen. Kalu i a꞉no꞉ nolo꞉ Sailini amisa꞉n o꞉lia꞉ Alegsandia amisa꞉na a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ mio꞉. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ nolo꞉, Silisia hen o꞉lia꞉ Esia hen a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ mio꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ iyo꞉ Sitifen o꞉lia꞉yo꞉ towa꞉yo꞉ kego꞉.
Ko꞉sega Godeya꞉ Mamaya꞉yo꞉ Sitifen emo꞉wo꞉ asulo꞉ nafa dimia꞉len ko꞉lo꞉ kalu i e o꞉lia꞉lo꞉ towa꞉lo꞉ kegab a꞉no꞉ mo꞉tiniaki, iyo꞉ wana dowo꞉.
A꞉la꞉gabiki, iliyo꞉ towo꞉ wo꞉no꞉le sa꞉la꞉li siya꞉likiyo꞉, “Sitifen eyo꞉ Gode o꞉lia꞉ Moses o꞉lia꞉mo꞉wo꞉ dio꞉ge sa꞉lab a꞉la꞉bo꞉ niliyo꞉ dabulo꞉bo꞉ka꞉” a꞉la꞉bo꞉ kalu nolbo꞉wo꞉ towo꞉ sama꞉ki, salifa꞉la꞉li ane.
Iliyo꞉ kaluka꞉isale o꞉lia꞉ ko꞉go꞉do꞉ kaluwo꞉ o꞉lia꞉ elelo꞉ asulo꞉ kalu o꞉lia꞉ma꞉ asulo꞉wo꞉ digidalifa꞉la꞉liki ane ko꞉lo꞉ iliyo꞉ Sitifen e ta꞉lia꞉sa꞉ga꞉ mo꞉walilima꞉ni, Yu amilo꞉ Kanisolo kalulo꞉wa tililigane.
A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ e mo꞉walilakiyo꞉, Sitifen elo꞉ mo꞉dimido꞉lo꞉ sa꞉ma꞉no꞉ kaluwo꞉ tililia꞉ga꞉ ta꞉taki, iliyo꞉ madali towo꞉ a꞉na sa꞉laki, “Sitifen eyo꞉ Moses ele saefa꞉yo꞉ a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ gulugulula꞉sen a malilo꞉wo꞉ dio꞉ge sa꞉la꞉lab.
Kalu wema꞉yo꞉ ‘Ya꞉su, Nasa꞉la꞉d kalu a꞉ma꞉yo꞉ Godeya꞉ Malilo꞉ a we bidilaki, Mosesa꞉ ele man ko꞉lo꞉ nimo꞉lo꞉ dimi a꞉no꞉ togonolema꞉ib’ a꞉la꞉wida꞉labiki dabu” a꞉la꞉sio꞉.
Kalu elo꞉ mo꞉walila꞉likilo꞉ sen i tambo a꞉ma꞉yo꞉, Sitifena꞉ wo꞉lokan sikudu ba꞉ba꞉ amio꞉, wo꞉lokan elo꞉ a꞉no꞉ ma꞉mul kaluwa꞉lo꞉wo꞉ o꞉ngo꞉lo꞉biki ba꞉ba꞉.
Sitifen e mo꞉walila꞉la꞉ga꞉ dotabikiyo꞉, bobalo꞉ so꞉mia꞉sen misa꞉ kalu a꞉ma꞉yo꞉ emo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉dabuba꞉ba꞉, “To gemo꞉lo꞉ mo꞉walilakilo꞉ sa꞉lab we hendeleyo꞉?”
To elo꞉ dabu ba꞉dab a꞉na, a꞉ma꞉la꞉ sa꞉lakiyo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Nao i, do i, gio꞉ dabuma! Nili ma꞉mu A꞉bla꞉ham eyo꞉ Halan amisa꞉n semo꞉ ane amio꞉, Mesobotemia hena sen amio꞉, halaido꞉ Gode a꞉no꞉ elo꞉wa fa꞉la꞉dowakiyo꞉, emo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, ‘Ge go꞉no꞉n mo꞉mio꞉ o꞉lia꞉, go꞉no꞉n hen o꞉lia꞉ ta꞉taki, hen ko꞉li nilo꞉ gemo꞉lo꞉ walama꞉no꞉ a꞉no꞉, ge a꞉na mesa꞉no꞉ hamana.’
<range>
A꞉la꞉sa꞉labikiyo꞉, A꞉bla꞉ham e Kaldean hen a꞉no꞉ kata꞉ta꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Halan amisa꞉n a꞉na ha꞉na꞉sa꞉ga꞉ sen. A꞉na sen ami, iyayo꞉ sowabikiyo꞉, Godeya꞉yo꞉ e a꞉na a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ tililia꞉ga꞉, o꞉go꞉do꞉ gilo꞉ sab hen wena tililia꞉mio꞉.
Ho꞉len a꞉namio꞉, emo꞉wo꞉ ene hendeyo꞉ mo꞉dimiaki, ha꞉lugo꞉wo꞉lo꞉ emo꞉wo꞉ bo꞉fo꞉melea꞉kiyo꞉ mo꞉dimi. Ko꞉sega Godeya꞉ emo꞉ dinali sa꞉laki a꞉la꞉sio꞉, ‘Niyo꞉ hen we tambo ge o꞉lia꞉ gilo꞉ so꞉wa sa꞉la꞉la꞉i ha꞉nab o꞉lia꞉mo꞉wo꞉ dimia꞉no꞉.’ A꞉bla꞉ham e so꞉walo꞉ma dowo꞉ ko꞉sega Godeya꞉yo꞉ emo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉dinali salifa꞉.
Godeya꞉ emo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, ‘Gi so꞉wa sa꞉la꞉la꞉i ha꞉nab a꞉no꞉ ini heno꞉ ta꞉ta꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Isib hena mageso꞉ sia꞉lalikiyo꞉, da꞉ibo꞉ so꞉wa dowaki dikidima꞉ib ko꞉lo꞉ iyo꞉ hen a꞉namio꞉ donayo꞉ 400 a꞉la꞉fo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ mesa꞉ib.
Ko꞉sega Niyo꞉ ilo꞉ da꞉ibo꞉ so꞉wa mesea꞉kilo꞉ ta꞉fo꞉ kalu a꞉no꞉ Isib ego꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ iyo꞉ falasila꞉ma꞉no꞉ a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ tif amio꞉ Niyo꞉ gi so꞉wa sa꞉la꞉la꞉i ha꞉nab i a꞉no꞉ a꞉ma꞉la꞉ tililia꞉ga꞉, hen wena siliki, Nemo꞉wo꞉ gulugulula꞉ma꞉ib.’ Godeya꞉yo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉
A꞉la꞉ dinali sio꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ dinali sio꞉ a꞉no꞉ hendele widakiyo꞉, e do꞉go꞉fo꞉ hege gedema꞉ib a꞉la꞉sio꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ A꞉bla꞉ham eyo꞉ Aisego꞉ sa꞉la꞉liakiyo꞉, ho꞉len ola꞉fo꞉wo꞉ ta꞉ta꞉ga꞉yo꞉, do꞉go꞉fo꞉ hege gede alifa꞉. A꞉la꞉go꞉ko꞉lo꞉ tif amio꞉ Aisego꞉ Yekobo꞉ sa꞉la꞉li a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ Yekobo꞉ so꞉wa kugula꞉fo꞉ sa꞉la꞉li ko꞉lo꞉ so꞉wa a꞉ma꞉yo꞉ Isolael kaluka꞉isale so꞉lo꞉wo꞉ kugula꞉fo꞉ fa꞉la꞉do alifa꞉.
“Nili ma꞉mu, Yekoba꞉ insisa꞉i nolba꞉yo꞉ Yosa꞉bo꞉wo꞉ keleasula꞉sa꞉ga꞉, e Isib kaluwa꞉ da꞉ibo꞉ kalu doma꞉ki, moleya꞉ kilili. Ko꞉sega Godeya꞉yo꞉ Yosa꞉b e hida꞉yo꞉ ba꞉dab a꞉namio꞉, e o꞉lia꞉ dofo꞉liki asufa꞉ ko꞉loemo꞉wo꞉ asulo꞉ alan dimiabiki, Isib misa꞉ kalu, Felo꞉wa꞉ siwa꞉l amio꞉ Yosa꞉b ene mano꞉ nafa ba꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Felo꞉ e sagalaki, Isib hen o꞉lia꞉ ene a o꞉lia꞉yo꞉ Yosa꞉b emo꞉ bo꞉fo꞉melea꞉ki ta꞉fo꞉.
<range>
“A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ Isib hen o꞉lia꞉ Kenan hen a꞉namio꞉, maiyo꞉wo꞉ alan fa꞉la꞉dowaki, hida꞉yo꞉ alan dowo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉, ni ma꞉muwa꞉yo꞉ ma꞉no꞉ ma꞉no꞉wo꞉ aundo꞉ma dowo꞉.
A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ Yekob eyo꞉ Isib hen amio꞉ ma꞉no꞉wo꞉ da꞉laka꞉ a꞉la꞉sa꞉labi da꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉, eyo꞉ nili ma꞉mu iyo꞉ tamin ami a꞉na iliga꞉fo꞉.
Iyo꞉ andeb ane amio꞉, Yosa꞉b e ao imo꞉wo꞉ eneno꞉ a꞉na wida꞉sa꞉ga꞉ dowabiki, Felo e Yosa꞉ba꞉ so꞉lo꞉wo꞉ welo꞉b a꞉la꞉bo꞉ a꞉na asulo꞉.
A꞉ma꞉ fa꞉s amio꞉, Yosa꞉b eyo꞉ ene iya Yekob o꞉lia꞉ so꞉lo꞉ o꞉lia꞉yo꞉ elo꞉wa tambo mena꞉ki saga꞉fo꞉. To saga꞉fo꞉ a꞉no꞉ da꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Yekobo꞉ Isib ane ko꞉lo꞉ Yekoba꞉ so꞉lo꞉ Isib a꞉lab a꞉no꞉lia꞉ agelo꞉wo꞉ do꞉la꞉fo꞉ dom a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ bila꞉fo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ fa꞉la꞉dowo꞉. Yekob o꞉lia꞉ ene sowayo꞉lo꞉ a꞉naka sowo꞉.
<range>
Tif amio꞉ ini ki a꞉no꞉ a꞉ma꞉la꞉ dia꞉ya꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Sekem hen a꞉namio꞉, Hamol insisa꞉ma꞉ heno꞉ A꞉bla꞉hama꞉ tamina moleya꞉ kilili ko꞉lo꞉ ini kiyo꞉ a꞉na daido꞉.
“Godeya꞉yo꞉ A꞉bla꞉hambo꞉lo꞉ dinali sio꞉ ho꞉leno꞉ ko꞉na꞉ma fa꞉la꞉dowabiki, Isib a꞉namio꞉ Isolael kaluwo꞉ mada modo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ fa꞉la꞉dowo꞉.
A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ Isib amio꞉ misa꞉ kalu ho꞉gi fa꞉la꞉dowakiyo꞉, eyo꞉ Yosa꞉bo꞉ mo꞉fanda asulo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ eyo꞉ ni ma꞉mu imo꞉wo꞉ dikida꞉sa꞉ga꞉ hida꞉yo꞉wo꞉ alan dimi. A꞉la꞉gabiki, eyo꞉ inin so꞉wa ho꞉gi sa꞉la꞉la꞉iyo꞉ ka soma꞉ki, ha꞉la꞉ya sandifelema꞉no꞉ a꞉la꞉saefa꞉.
<range>
“Ho꞉len a꞉namio꞉, Moseso꞉ a꞉na sa꞉la꞉li. E mada gesego꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ ele otalen dowabiki, iyaya꞉ aya siliki bo꞉fo꞉len.
A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ e ha꞉la꞉ya ta꞉fo꞉lena, Isib misa꞉ kaluwa꞉ ida꞉ya꞉ ta꞉ulia꞉ga꞉, ene so꞉wayo꞉ aumta꞉ga꞉ fofo꞉.
A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ Isib kalu ili mano꞉ Moses emo꞉wo꞉ tambo walali ko꞉lo꞉ Moses e to sa꞉lan o꞉lia꞉ man dimidan o꞉lia꞉yo꞉ halaido꞉ di kalu ko꞉lo꞉ kagayo꞉.
“Moses e donayo꞉ do꞉la꞉fo꞉ fa꞉la꞉da꞉in ta꞉ga꞉ga꞉ dowabiki, Isolael kaluka꞉isale, ene ao i a꞉no꞉ ba꞉ba꞉ ha꞉na꞉no꞉ asulo꞉.
E a꞉na elen amio꞉, Isib kaluwa꞉yo꞉ Isolael kaluwo꞉ mogagi dikidi sa꞉ndabiki ba꞉ba꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ eyo꞉ asuwa꞉takiyo꞉, Isib kalu a꞉no꞉ wediakiyo꞉, e sanaifa꞉.
Moses eyo꞉ wediabikiyo꞉, ene ao i a꞉ma꞉ asulakiyo꞉ e Godelo꞉ asuwa꞉foma꞉ki iliga꞉fo꞉lo꞉ kalu a꞉la꞉bo꞉ asuluma꞉ki dimido꞉ ko꞉sega iliyo꞉ a꞉la꞉gabolo꞉b a꞉la꞉do꞉ mo꞉asulo꞉.
Ho꞉len no amio꞉, Moses e Isolael kalu a꞉la꞉ nowo꞉ buba꞉lena ba꞉ba꞉. E ba꞉da꞉ga꞉, a꞉la꞉yo꞉ ha꞉fo꞉ disa꞉ma꞉ki sagale alitakiyo꞉, towo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, ‘Gao gaino꞉, waga bubadi?’
Ko꞉sega kalu nolo꞉ sa꞉nda꞉likilo꞉ ha꞉nab a꞉ma꞉yo꞉, Moses e kanilaki, Mosesbo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, ‘Nio gi bo꞉fo꞉liki mo꞉walila꞉lubika꞉ a꞉la꞉bo꞉, abe saefa꞉yo꞉?
Alilo꞉ Isib kalu nowo꞉ gilo꞉ so꞉no꞉ aumbo꞉, o꞉go꞉lo꞉ nelo꞉ gi sanaifa꞉nigaya?’
To sa꞉lab a꞉no꞉ da꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Moses e nai ha꞉na꞉ga꞉, Isib heno꞉ ta꞉ta꞉ga꞉, Midian hen a꞉na ha꞉na꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, e mio꞉ kalu silikiyo꞉, so꞉wayo꞉ a꞉la꞉ sa꞉la꞉li.
“Moses e donayo꞉ do꞉la꞉fo꞉ fa꞉la꞉da꞉ino꞉ gulula꞉sa꞉ga꞉ ilikiyo꞉, e kalalili hen, Sainai misio꞉ anib doba꞉da꞉ sia꞉lena, i abol ko꞉lo꞉ nudula꞉ a꞉nami, delo꞉ wa꞉sowala꞉lab us a꞉na ma꞉mul kaluwo꞉ a꞉na elena, Moses e ba꞉ba꞉.
Moses eyo꞉ ba꞉da꞉ga꞉yo꞉, e moda꞉sa꞉ga꞉, e ma꞉uwa꞉ya ba꞉ba꞉ni ha꞉nabiki, Gode Alan e towo꞉ a꞉na dabu.
Godeya꞉yo꞉ Moses emo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, ‘Ne gi ma꞉mu A꞉bla꞉hamo꞉, Aisego꞉, Yekobo꞉ i a꞉ma꞉ Godeyo꞉ Ne.’ A꞉la꞉sa꞉labiki, Moses e tagilaki bibi sado꞉geta꞉ga꞉, e mo꞉sikudu ba꞉ba꞉.
“A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ Godeya꞉yo꞉ emo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, ‘Hen gelo꞉ kagafo꞉lab we mada malilo꞉ hen ko꞉lo꞉ gi gido꞉fo꞉ amilo꞉ budi sa꞉ga꞉lo꞉ko꞉, dugulema!
Kaluka꞉isale nilo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ Isib hen ami silikilo꞉ hida꞉yo꞉ ililo꞉ diab a꞉no꞉ Ne ba꞉ba꞉. Ne ililo꞉ ya꞉la꞉lab a꞉no꞉ da꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Ne iyo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ sili alifa꞉ni mio꞉. A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ ge mena. Niyo꞉ ge a꞉ma꞉la꞉ Isib iliga꞉fa꞉nigo꞉l.’ Godeya꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉.”
A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ Sitifen eyo꞉ to nolo꞉ a꞉kudu sio꞉, “Moses ko꞉lo꞉ o꞉gdo꞉ Godelo꞉ Isibdo꞉ iliga꞉fa꞉nigab a꞉no꞉, tamin amilo꞉ Isolael kaluka꞉isaleya꞉lo꞉ e gola ba꞉dakiyo꞉, emo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, ‘Nio꞉ gi bo꞉fo꞉liki mo꞉walila꞉bika꞉ a꞉la꞉bo꞉, abe saefa꞉yo꞉?’ a꞉la꞉do꞉ sa꞉labikilo꞉ aneyo꞉ o꞉m. A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ Godeya꞉yo꞉ ma꞉mul kalu ilo꞉wa a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ Mosesdo꞉ amilo꞉ fa꞉la꞉dowo꞉ a꞉ma꞉liki, Moses eyo꞉ Isolael kaluka꞉isaleyo꞉ sili dofo꞉liki bo꞉fo꞉melea꞉ki, iliga꞉fo꞉.
A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ Moses eyo꞉ Isibdo꞉ seno꞉ e sililia꞉ga꞉ handaloma꞉nikiyo꞉, eyo꞉ molo ha꞉na꞉no꞉wo꞉ modo꞉ dimido꞉. Isib hen amio꞉ a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ ho꞉n genelo꞉ amio꞉lo꞉, a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ Isolael kaluka꞉isaleyo꞉ dona do꞉la꞉fo꞉ fa꞉la꞉da꞉in kalalili hen usa sia꞉likiyo꞉lo꞉, e tililia꞉ ha꞉naliki, molo ha꞉na꞉no꞉wo꞉ dimido꞉.
“Moses a꞉ma꞉yo꞉ Isolael kaluka꞉isalemo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, ‘Godeya꞉yo꞉ ne ko꞉lo꞉ gimo꞉lo꞉ iliga꞉fo꞉ aumbo꞉, dinali sa꞉lan kalu nowo꞉, gi us a꞉na a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ iliga꞉fa꞉ib.’
Isolael kaluka꞉isaleyo꞉ kalalili hena siliki kegea꞉len amio꞉ Moseso꞉ i o꞉lia꞉ elen. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ ni ma꞉mui Isolael i o꞉lia꞉ elen amio꞉, e misio꞉ Sainai fa꞉la꞉dowamio꞉, ma꞉mul kalu e o꞉lia꞉ tola꞉. A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ eyo꞉ to mela꞉no꞉lo꞉ a꞉lab a꞉no꞉ da꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉, nimo꞉ malolo꞉ mena꞉ki di.
“Ko꞉sega nili ma꞉mu iya꞉yo꞉ Mosesa꞉ towo꞉ mo꞉kuduhanaki, iliyo꞉ Moses e gola ba꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉, asulo꞉ inido꞉wo꞉ a꞉ma꞉la꞉ Isib ane.
A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ iliyo꞉ A꞉lonbo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, ‘Moses nililo꞉ Isib a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ tililia꞉mio꞉ we, e amio꞉ o꞉b fa꞉la꞉dowabele babalab ko꞉lo꞉ giyo꞉ gode nolo꞉ nilo꞉ tililia꞉ga꞉lo꞉ taminfo꞉ ha꞉na꞉no꞉wo꞉ dimida꞉bi’ a꞉la꞉sio꞉.
Ho꞉len a꞉namio꞉ iliyo꞉ madali godeyo꞉, kao inso꞉ o꞉ngo꞉ a꞉na dimida꞉sa꞉ga꞉ ta꞉fo꞉liki, iliyo꞉ o꞉mo꞉ boba somiaki gulugulula꞉len. Iliyo꞉ ini dagiya꞉lo꞉ dimido꞉ gode a꞉no꞉ wabudakiyo꞉, ma꞉no꞉wo꞉ naki sagalo꞉ alan dowo꞉.
Iliyo꞉ a꞉la꞉dimidabikiyo꞉, Godeya꞉yo꞉ iyo꞉ gola ba꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉, iyo꞉ ofo꞉, tamino꞉ eleyo꞉ a꞉no꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ wabuluma꞉ki ta꞉fo꞉. Dinali sa꞉lan kaluwa꞉ bugo꞉ amio꞉ a꞉la꞉sa꞉sa꞉lo꞉, “‘Isolael kaluka꞉isale gio꞉, kalalili hen amio꞉ dona do꞉la꞉fo꞉ fa꞉la꞉da꞉in a꞉namio꞉ no꞉wo꞉ sa꞉nda꞉sa꞉ga꞉lo꞉ so꞉kugulu mian a꞉no꞉ dimi. Ko꞉sega giliyo꞉ ne wabudakiyo꞉, hendelelo꞉ mo꞉dimi.
Gio꞉ gulugululan helebeso꞉g a dia꞉likilo꞉ sia꞉len a꞉no꞉ madali gode Molog eno꞉ a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ madali gode tamin ko꞉lo꞉ wabudab a꞉no꞉ Lafan eno꞉. Gini dagiya꞉ madali gode a꞉no꞉ dimida꞉sa꞉, o꞉mo꞉wo꞉ wabulu sio꞉. A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ Niyo꞉ gini hende amio꞉ a꞉ma꞉la꞉yo꞉ mo꞉mena꞉ki, Babalon heno꞉ tiginita꞉ga꞉ ko꞉na꞉ ta꞉foma꞉ki ta꞉fa꞉no꞉.’ Dinali sa꞉lan kaluwa꞉yo꞉ a꞉la꞉sa꞉sa꞉lo꞉.
“Nili ma꞉muwa꞉yo꞉ helebeso꞉g a a꞉no꞉ Godeyo꞉ a꞉labka꞉ a꞉la꞉widakiyo꞉, kalalili hen a꞉namio꞉ dia꞉liki sia꞉len. Helebeso꞉g a a꞉no꞉ dia꞉no꞉wo꞉, Godeya꞉yo꞉ Mosesbo꞉ wido꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ iyo꞉ a꞉la꞉dimido꞉.
Tif amio꞉ ni ma꞉mu i a꞉ma꞉ ene so꞉wayo꞉ helebeso꞉g a a꞉no꞉ dimi ko꞉lo꞉ iyo꞉ dia꞉li ha꞉na꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, Yosua e tililia꞉ ha꞉nakiyo꞉, iyo꞉ Godeya꞉ halaido꞉ o꞉lia꞉ma꞉yo꞉, ha꞉la꞉ kalu hen a꞉namilo꞉ sano꞉ o꞉luga꞉felesa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, helebeso꞉g a a꞉no꞉ a꞉na dialifa꞉. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ a a꞉no꞉ hen a꞉na a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉lo꞉ dowa꞉mio꞉wo꞉, Isolael misa꞉ Debidi ho꞉len a꞉na edo꞉.
Godeya꞉yo꞉ Debidi e sagale alifa꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ Debidi eyo꞉ a ho꞉gi nowo꞉ Yekoba꞉ Gode mesea꞉ki dia꞉niki, Godemo꞉wo꞉ dabu ba꞉ba꞉.
Ko꞉sega Godeya꞉ a a꞉no꞉ inso꞉ Solomona꞉ di.
“Ko꞉sega Gode Iwalulo꞉ A꞉labo꞉ E henfelo꞉ kaluwa꞉lo꞉ a dimido꞉ usamio꞉ mo꞉san. Dinali sa꞉lan kaluwa꞉yo꞉, Godeya꞉ towo꞉ sa꞉lakiyo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉,
“‘Hebenelo꞉ halo nelo꞉ mesa꞉no꞉ i fofodo꞉wo꞉ o꞉m, a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ henfelo꞉ we Ni gido꞉fo꞉lo꞉ wa꞉lo꞉fo꞉mela꞉no꞉wo꞉ o꞉m. A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ a Nilo꞉ mesa꞉no꞉ o꞉li o꞉ngo꞉wo꞉ gio꞉ waga dia꞉no꞉wo꞉? Nelo꞉ mesa꞉no꞉wo꞉ ayo꞉ mada mo꞉dialifa꞉ib.
Mo꞉wo꞉ kelego꞉ we No꞉no꞉n tambo dimido꞉.’ Godeya꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉.”
Sitifen eyo꞉ to kudu sa꞉la꞉kiyo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Asulo꞉ gililo꞉wo꞉ halaido꞉ dowa꞉sa꞉ga꞉, ka꞉la꞉no꞉ kali ko꞉lo꞉ gio꞉ ha꞉la꞉ kaluwo꞉ o꞉ngo꞉ dowo꞉. Godeya꞉ Mamaya꞉lo꞉ gimo꞉lo꞉ sa꞉lab a꞉no꞉, giliyo꞉ gola ba꞉da꞉sen. Giliyo꞉ ge ma꞉mu ima꞉lo꞉ man dimida꞉sen aumb dimida꞉lab.
Gi ma꞉mu iyo꞉ Godeya꞉lo꞉ dinali sa꞉lan kaluwo꞉ tambo mo꞉beaki, imo꞉wo꞉ hida꞉yo꞉wo꞉ dimia꞉sen. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ tamin amio꞉ dinali sa꞉lan kalu nolba꞉yo꞉ widakiyo꞉, Godeya꞉ Ene Digalo꞉ Kaluwo꞉ mia꞉ib a꞉la꞉do꞉ sio꞉ i a꞉no꞉lo꞉, iliyo꞉ sana sowa꞉sen. A꞉la꞉go꞉ko꞉lo꞉ o꞉go꞉ kalu a꞉no꞉ mio꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ giliyo꞉ E tele dowa꞉sa꞉ga꞉, sana sowo꞉.
Godeya꞉ ma꞉mula꞉ kaluwa꞉yo꞉ Ene eleyo꞉ gininbo꞉wo꞉ dimi ko꞉sega giliyo꞉ mo꞉kudu ane.” Sitifen eyo꞉ towo꞉ a꞉la꞉wido꞉.
A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ Yu misa꞉ kaluwa꞉yo꞉ Sitifena꞉ to a꞉no꞉ da꞉da꞉ga꞉yo꞉, mada beso꞉ galita꞉ga꞉, emo꞉wo꞉ kulufa꞉yo꞉wo꞉ alan dowo꞉.
Ko꞉sega Sitifen e Godeya꞉ Mamayo꞉ e amio꞉ wa꞉lifo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉, eyo꞉ Hebene alolo ba꞉ba꞉ amio꞉, Godeya꞉ Ene halaido꞉ malilo꞉wo꞉ ba꞉da꞉ga꞉yo꞉, Ya꞉suwo꞉ Godeya꞉ ene dagi ililiba kagayabi ba꞉ba꞉.
A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ eyo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Gio꞉ bo꞉ba! Ne Hebeneyo꞉ kolaitabiki ba꞉ba꞉ amio꞉, Kalule Dowo꞉ E Godeya꞉ ene dagi ililiba kagayabiki bo꞉do꞉l.”
Iyo꞉ to꞉ a꞉no꞉ da꞉dakiyo꞉, ka꞉la꞉no꞉ ka꞉la꞉sa꞉ga꞉, e halalelaki, iyo꞉ tambo elo꞉wa nai ha꞉na꞉ga꞉, e ta꞉lia꞉sa꞉ga꞉, amisa꞉n ha꞉laya susululia꞉ga꞉, uwa꞉ agodo꞉. Iliyo꞉ a꞉la꞉dimidabikiyo꞉, Sitifen elo꞉ mo꞉dimido꞉lo꞉ dikili sio꞉ kalu a꞉ma꞉yo꞉ helebeso꞉go꞉ wa꞉l amilo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉wo꞉ ho꞉go꞉fela꞉sa꞉ga꞉, kalu so꞉wa So꞉l a꞉ma꞉ gido꞉fo꞉ aniba difa꞉.
<range>
Iliyo꞉ uwa꞉ agodabikiyo꞉, Sitifen eyo꞉ Godemo꞉ dulugu sa꞉lakiyo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Ya꞉su Alan, Giyo꞉ ni mama mela꞉no꞉wo꞉ dima.”
A꞉la꞉sa꞉la꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, e tululalilaki, gulalu siliki, towo꞉ halaido꞉ sa꞉laki, “Alan Giyo꞉, mogago꞉ ililo꞉ dimidab we, ga꞉lilaki wedia꞉so꞉bo.” Sitifen e to a꞉no꞉ sa꞉la꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, e ha꞉fo꞉wo꞉ siliga꞉ta꞉ga꞉ sowo꞉.
Ililo꞉ Sitifen sana sowab a꞉no꞉, So꞉l eyo꞉ o꞉li dimidab a꞉la꞉asulo꞉. O꞉g ho꞉len a꞉namio꞉ gisa꞉yo꞉ Ya꞉lusalem Keliso kaluka꞉isalemo꞉wo꞉ hida꞉yo꞉ nolo꞉ modo꞉ mo꞉mo꞉dabiki, tilidabu kaluka꞉isale iyo꞉ dalalelia꞉ga꞉, Yudia hen o꞉lia꞉ Samalia hen o꞉lia꞉ a꞉na ane. Ko꞉sega iliga꞉felo꞉ kalu iyo꞉ mo꞉dalaidaki, Ya꞉lusalem a꞉naka sen.
A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ Godeya꞉ towo꞉ kuduha꞉na꞉sen kalu nolba꞉yo꞉ Sitifena꞉ ene do꞉mo꞉wo꞉ dia꞉sa꞉ga꞉, dali alita꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, iyo꞉ ya꞉foda꞉li ha꞉na꞉sio꞉.
Ko꞉sega So꞉l eyo꞉ Ya꞉su kuduha꞉nab a꞉no꞉ kata꞉foma꞉ki dikidiakiyo꞉, eyo꞉ tilidabu kaluwa꞉ aka ha꞉na꞉ga꞉, iyo꞉ tililia꞉ga꞉, dibolo aya to꞉lolo꞉.
A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ kaluka꞉isale ilo꞉ dalalilia꞉ga꞉lo꞉ ha꞉nab a꞉namio꞉, Godeya꞉ mano꞉ wida꞉i ane.
Filibo꞉ Samalia amisa꞉n a꞉na tina꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Godeya꞉lo꞉ Da꞉feyo꞉ Kalu Ya꞉suwo꞉ weka꞉ a꞉la꞉liki fanda wido꞉.
Kaluka꞉isale kegeo꞉ a꞉namilo꞉ sen a꞉ma꞉yo꞉ Filiba꞉ to widakilo꞉ molo ha꞉na꞉no꞉ dimidab a꞉no꞉ ba꞉dakiyo꞉, iliyo꞉ elo꞉ to sa꞉lab a꞉no꞉ dinafa dabu.
Filib eyo꞉ kaluka꞉isale amio꞉ mama mogago꞉ dosdo꞉ a꞉no꞉ e o꞉luga꞉felabi ha꞉na꞉siakiyo꞉, iyo꞉ ganafoda꞉liki ane. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ giliga꞉sen kaluka꞉isale o꞉lia꞉ kogoneli kalukeisale o꞉lia꞉ yo꞉ modo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ falele alifelo꞉.
A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ Samalia amisa꞉n kaluka꞉isaleyo꞉ sagalo꞉wo꞉ mada alan fa꞉la꞉dowo꞉.
Amisa꞉n a꞉namio꞉ kalu imilise nowo꞉ ene wiyo꞉ Saimon ko꞉lo꞉ a꞉na sen. Eyo꞉ fofa ko꞉li ko꞉lilo꞉ dimida꞉labiki, amisa꞉n kaluka꞉isaleyo꞉ molo asula꞉len. E ene wiyo꞉ duluda꞉liki, misa꞉ kaluwo꞉lo꞉, wa꞉feyo꞉ kaluwo꞉lo꞉ tambo elo꞉ to sa꞉lab a꞉no꞉ tilida꞉dakiyo꞉, “Halaido꞉ Alano꞉ Godeya꞉lo꞉wa a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉lo꞉ mio꞉ a꞉no꞉ e amio꞉ a꞉lab” a꞉la꞉sio꞉.
<range>
Saimon eyo꞉ fofa man a꞉no꞉ imo꞉wo꞉ ko꞉li ko꞉lilo꞉ wida꞉li ha꞉na꞉labiki, iyo꞉ molo asulaki elo꞉ to sa꞉lab a꞉no꞉ iligi dabu.
Ko꞉sega Filib eyo꞉ Godeya꞉ ene kaluka꞉isale ko꞉lo꞉ bo꞉fo꞉lab man nafa o꞉lia꞉, Ya꞉su Kelisowa꞉ wi a꞉no꞉lia꞉yo꞉ wido꞉ amio꞉, kaluka꞉isaleyo꞉ tilida꞉dabiki, iyo꞉ ho꞉na to꞉lolo꞉.
A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ Saimon elo꞉ tilida꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉ dowabi, ho꞉na to꞉lolo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ e Filib o꞉lia꞉ kudu sia꞉la꞉ga꞉, Filib elo꞉ molo ha꞉na꞉no꞉ dimidab a꞉no꞉ ba꞉da꞉ga꞉yo꞉, e molo asulo꞉.
Iliga꞉felo꞉ kalu Ya꞉lusalemdo꞉ sen a꞉ma꞉yo꞉, Samalia kaluka꞉isaleyo꞉ Godeya꞉ mano꞉ tilidabu a꞉la꞉ dabu ko꞉lo꞉, iliyo꞉ Bida o꞉lia꞉ Yon dia꞉yo꞉ ilo꞉ a꞉na iliga꞉fo꞉.
A꞉la꞉yo꞉ fa꞉la꞉dowa꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, i a꞉no꞉ Godeya꞉ Mamayo꞉ dima꞉ki, Godemo꞉wo꞉ dulugu sio꞉.
Mo꞉wo꞉ iyo꞉ Ya꞉suwa꞉ wi amio꞉ ho꞉na to꞉lolo꞉ ko꞉sega, Godeya꞉ Mamayo꞉ i amio꞉ semo꞉ mio꞉.
A꞉la꞉go꞉ko꞉lo꞉ Bida o꞉lia꞉ Yon dia꞉ma꞉yo꞉ dagiyo꞉ kaluka꞉isale amio꞉ golabiki, iyo꞉ Godeya꞉ Mamayo꞉ a꞉na di.
Iliga꞉felo꞉ kaluwa꞉lo꞉ dagiya꞉ golab amio꞉ Mama ko꞉lo꞉ diab a꞉no꞉ ba꞉da꞉ga꞉yo꞉, Saimon eyo꞉ a꞉la꞉ a꞉no꞉ moleya꞉ kililia꞉no꞉ asulaki, a꞉la꞉mo꞉wo꞉ dabu ba꞉ba꞉, “Gaindo꞉ man dimidab ko꞉ aumbo꞉, niyo꞉lo꞉ dagiya꞉yo꞉ kalu nolo꞉ golalikiyo꞉ Mamayo꞉lo꞉ dima꞉ki, halaido꞉ gaindo꞉ ko꞉ nelo꞉ dia꞉niki kililia꞉nigo꞉l.”
<range>
Ko꞉sega Bida eyo꞉ a꞉ma꞉la꞉bo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Godeya꞉ boba kelego꞉ we gi moleya꞉ kililia꞉no꞉ a꞉la꞉liki asulab ko꞉lo꞉ go꞉no꞉n o꞉lia꞉ mole gilo꞉ a꞉no꞉lia꞉yo꞉ de hena soma꞉ni ha꞉na꞉bi.
Gi asulo꞉wo꞉ Godeya꞉ siwa꞉l amio꞉ digalo꞉leyo꞉ mo꞉a꞉lab ko꞉lo꞉ nanog naindo꞉ dio꞉l we, ge o꞉lia꞉ mada mo꞉lido꞉.
Mogago꞉ gilo꞉ dimido꞉ a꞉no꞉ ta꞉ta꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Godemo꞉ foga꞉le sama. Giyo꞉ a꞉la꞉dimidalikiyo꞉, asulo꞉ gilo꞉ amio꞉ kele asulo꞉ a꞉no꞉ ga꞉lila꞉ma꞉ibele a꞉la꞉asulo꞉l.
Mo꞉wo꞉ ge meselo꞉wo꞉ alan dowaki, man mogago꞉ ko꞉lilo꞉ a꞉ma꞉yo꞉ ge meleya꞉fo꞉lab.”
A꞉la꞉sa꞉labiki, Saimon eyo꞉ a꞉ma꞉la꞉bo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Kelego꞉ gaindo꞉ sa꞉lab a꞉no꞉ ne amio꞉ fa꞉la꞉dowaba꞉na꞉kiyo꞉, ne mada gaino꞉ Godemo꞉ dulugu sama.”
A꞉la꞉ma꞉yo꞉ Alana꞉ to o꞉lia꞉ a꞉la꞉mo꞉lo꞉ dimido꞉wo꞉ o꞉lia꞉yo꞉ malolo꞉ mia꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, a꞉ma꞉la꞉ Ya꞉lusalem ha꞉nakiyo꞉, Samalia amisa꞉n nol amio꞉lo꞉ to nafale a꞉no꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ wida꞉li ane.
A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ Godeya꞉ ma꞉mul kaluwa꞉yo꞉ Filibo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Ge dimidalia꞉ga꞉, kalalili hen a꞉namio꞉, tog nowo꞉ Ya꞉lusalem a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ Gasa amisa꞉n a꞉na ha꞉na꞉sen a꞉lab ko꞉lo꞉ ge a꞉na tiha꞉na꞉bi.”
A꞉la꞉sa꞉labiki, Filib e tog a꞉na ha꞉na꞉lena, Itiobia kalu nowo꞉ a꞉na yabiki ba꞉ba꞉. Kalu a꞉ma꞉ ito꞉wo꞉ dugula꞉. Kalu a꞉no꞉ Itiobiaya꞉ misa꞉ ka꞉isale, Kandasiya꞉ ene nanogdo꞉ dian kalu alan nowo꞉ e. E Kandasiya꞉ moleyo꞉ a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ kelego꞉ nafalelo꞉ tambo bo꞉fo꞉lowano꞉ e. E Godeyo꞉ wabuluma꞉niki, Ya꞉lusalem ane ko꞉lo꞉ a꞉ma꞉la꞉ ya꞉lena ba꞉ba꞉.
E hos amilo꞉ i fofodo꞉ wa꞉la siliki, dinali sa꞉lan kalu, Aisaya bugo꞉ a꞉no꞉ halale agela꞉liki mio꞉ ko꞉lo꞉, Godeya꞉ Mamaya꞉yo꞉ Filibo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Ge elo꞉ yab anidoba꞉da꞉, e o꞉lia꞉ ha꞉na꞉ga꞉ ha꞉nani hamana.”
<range>
A꞉la꞉sa꞉labiki, Filib e nai ha꞉na꞉sa꞉ga꞉, i fofodo꞉ ha꞉nab anib a꞉na fa꞉la꞉dowakiyo꞉, kalu a꞉ma꞉lo꞉ dinali sa꞉lan Aisaya bugo꞉ agela꞉i ha꞉nab a꞉no꞉, e dabu. A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ Filib eyo꞉ kalu o꞉mo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉dabuba꞉ba꞉, “To gilo꞉ agelo꞉ a꞉no꞉, ge ha꞉go꞉ fanda asulaya?”
A꞉la꞉dabuba꞉dabiki, kalu a꞉ma꞉yo꞉ a꞉ma꞉la꞉bo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Kalu noma꞉yo꞉ nemo꞉wo꞉ mo꞉fanda sa꞉lalega, ne mada mo꞉fanda asuluma꞉ib.” A꞉la꞉sata꞉ga꞉, Filibo꞉ elo꞉ sab i fofodo꞉ anib wa꞉l a꞉na mesa꞉ mena a꞉la꞉sio꞉.
Godeya꞉ to elo꞉ agelo꞉wo꞉ we, “Sibi sa꞉ma꞉nikilo꞉ tililia꞉gane o꞉ngo꞉ E tililia꞉mio꞉. Sibi inso꞉ a꞉no꞉ fo꞉no꞉ gedeab amilo꞉ mo꞉ganagiliyo꞉wo꞉ o꞉ngo꞉ dowo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ e mego꞉fo꞉ mo꞉tagali.
E sendelowalitaki, mo꞉digale mo꞉walilo꞉. E ma꞉mu iyo꞉ weka꞉ a꞉la꞉bo꞉ mo꞉malolo꞉mia꞉ib, Mo꞉wo꞉ e henfelo꞉ wenamio꞉ mela꞉no꞉wo꞉ nolba꞉yo꞉ sanale.”
Itiobia kaluwa꞉yo꞉ a꞉na agela꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, Filibo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉dabuba꞉ba꞉, “Dinali sa꞉lan a꞉la꞉do꞉ sa꞉lab we, o꞉b ko꞉lo꞉ sa꞉laigabele? Eneno꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ sa꞉labele? O꞉ kalu nowo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ sa꞉labele?”
A꞉la꞉dabuba꞉dabiki, Filib eyo꞉ Godeya꞉ to a꞉no꞉ mo꞉mo꞉da widakiyo꞉, Ya꞉suwa꞉ to nafa a꞉no꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ wido꞉.
A꞉la꞉yo꞉ toga ha꞉na꞉la꞉ga꞉, hondo꞉wa fa꞉la꞉dowaki, Itiobia kaluwa꞉yo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Bo꞉ba! Ho꞉no꞉ we ko꞉lo꞉, gio꞉ ne ho꞉na to꞉loma꞉no꞉wo꞉ o꞉liyo꞉?”
Filib eyo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Ge asulo꞉wo꞉ amio꞉ hendele tilida꞉dalega, ge ho꞉n amio꞉ o꞉li to꞉loma꞉nigo꞉l.” A꞉la꞉sa꞉labiki, Itiobia kalu eyo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Ya꞉su E Godeya꞉ Inso꞉ a꞉la꞉bo꞉ ne tili asulo꞉l.”
A꞉la꞉sa꞉la꞉sa꞉ga꞉ e i fofodo꞉ a꞉no꞉ kagafoma꞉ki sio꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ kagayabikiyo꞉, a꞉la꞉yo꞉ ho꞉na tina꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Filib eyo꞉ kalu a꞉no꞉ ho꞉na to꞉lolo꞉.
A꞉la꞉yo꞉ ho꞉na a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ ha꞉laya fa꞉la꞉dowabikiyo꞉, Godeya꞉ Mamaya꞉yo꞉ Filibo꞉ wigibole a꞉naka dia꞉gane ko꞉lo꞉ Itiobia kalu eyo꞉ wa꞉kabiyo꞉ mada mo꞉ba꞉dabiki, e sagala꞉liki ane.
Ko꞉sega Filib e wigibo Asdot amisa꞉n a꞉naka handalowo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉, e Ya꞉suwa꞉ to nafayo꞉ wida꞉liki, amisa꞉n nolo꞉ ililita꞉ga꞉ aneyo꞉, Sesalia amisa꞉n a꞉na fa꞉la꞉dowo꞉.
O꞉g ho꞉len a꞉namio꞉ So꞉l eyo꞉ Alan amilo꞉ tilidabu kaluka꞉isaleyo꞉ yasalema꞉no꞉ a꞉la꞉li towo꞉ sa꞉la꞉li sia꞉len. E mo꞉fo꞉so꞉ dia꞉no꞉ a꞉la꞉liki, bobalo꞉ so꞉mia꞉sen misa꞉ kalu elo꞉wa dabu ba꞉ba꞉ni ane.
So꞉l e Damaskas amisa꞉na ha꞉na꞉no꞉ asulabiki, e a꞉na ha꞉na꞉ga꞉yo꞉, Alana꞉ Mando꞉ kuduha꞉nab kaluka꞉isale a꞉no꞉ ba꞉dalega, iyo꞉ ta꞉lia꞉sa꞉ga꞉, a꞉ma꞉la꞉ tililia꞉ga꞉, Ya꞉lusalem dibolo aya toloma꞉no꞉ a꞉la꞉asulo꞉. A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ So꞉l eyo꞉ bobalo꞉ so꞉mia꞉sen kalu eyo꞉ o꞉lika꞉ a꞉la꞉liki mo꞉fo꞉s nowo꞉ sa꞉sa꞉la꞉sa꞉ga꞉, emo꞉ dimiab amio꞉, eyo꞉ dia꞉ha꞉na꞉sa꞉ga꞉ Damaskasdo꞉ tolo꞉ wida꞉n misa꞉ kalu dosdomo꞉ walama꞉no꞉ a꞉la꞉liki, dabu ba꞉ba꞉ni ane.
Mo꞉fo꞉s a꞉no꞉ dia꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Damaskas amisa꞉no꞉ ko꞉na꞉ma fa꞉la꞉doma꞉no꞉ dowab amio꞉, wigibole a꞉naka ho꞉ nowo꞉ wabeleg o꞉ngo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ Hebene halona a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ so꞉so꞉lilia꞉ga꞉ tindaki, So꞉l e a꞉ma꞉ hegelia꞉ga꞉ difa꞉.
A꞉la꞉gabiki So꞉l e a꞉na hena sulufo꞉ tina꞉sa꞉ga꞉, to nowo꞉ emo꞉ sa꞉labiki dabu. “So꞉l, So꞉l, Giyo꞉ Ne waga mogagila꞉ya?”
A꞉la꞉sa꞉labiki, So꞉l eyo꞉, “Alan, Ge o꞉ba?” a꞉la꞉sio꞉. “Ne Ya꞉su ko꞉lo꞉ gilo꞉ mogagila꞉yo꞉ Ne.
Ge dasilia꞉ga꞉, amisa꞉n usa tihamana. A꞉namio꞉, kalu imilig noma꞉yo꞉ gilo꞉ dimidama꞉no꞉wo꞉ walasa꞉ma꞉ib” a꞉la꞉sio꞉.
Kalu So꞉l o꞉lia꞉lo꞉ ane a꞉no꞉, to sa꞉lab a꞉no꞉ dabu ko꞉sega, kalu misio꞉ mo꞉ba꞉dabiki, iyo꞉ modaki, towo꞉ mo꞉sa꞉laki kagafo꞉len.
A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ So꞉l e dasila꞉sa꞉ga꞉, siya꞉yo꞉ sigido꞉ ko꞉sega kelego꞉wo꞉ mada mo꞉ba꞉ba꞉no꞉ dowabiki, iliyo꞉ e dagiya gasilia꞉ga꞉, Damaskas amisa꞉n a꞉na tililia꞉gane.
E ho꞉len otaleno꞉ siyo꞉ mo꞉ba꞉ba꞉no꞉ dowabiki, e ma꞉n o꞉lia꞉ ho꞉n o꞉lia꞉yo꞉ mo꞉mo꞉no꞉.
Damaskas amisa꞉n a꞉namio꞉, tilidabu kalu nowo꞉, Ananaias e a꞉na sen. E ho꞉le ba꞉dakiyo꞉, Alana꞉yo꞉ “Ananaias!” a꞉la꞉hoidabiki dabu. Eyo꞉ a꞉ma꞉la꞉bo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Alan, ne weko꞉.”
Alana꞉yo꞉ emo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Ge Tog Digalo꞉ a꞉na ha꞉na꞉ga꞉, Yuda꞉sa꞉ aya fa꞉la꞉dowakiyo꞉, Tasus amisa꞉n kalu nowo꞉, ene wiyo꞉ So꞉l ko꞉lo꞉, e ba꞉ba꞉nikiyo꞉, emo꞉wo꞉ dabu ba꞉da꞉ni hamana. Mo꞉wo꞉ E a a꞉na dulugu sa꞉la꞉liki sab ko꞉lo꞉ eyo꞉lo꞉ ofolakiyo꞉, kalu imilig nowo꞉, ene wiyo꞉ Ananaias, e elo꞉wa ya꞉ga꞉, e dagiyo꞉ wa꞉la go꞉lalikiyo꞉, ene siyo꞉ o꞉li o꞉bo꞉ba꞉ki a꞉la꞉likiyo꞉ ofowo꞉ ba꞉ba꞉ ko꞉lo꞉lab ko꞉lo꞉, ge elo꞉wa hamana.”
<range>
Ananaias eyo꞉ a꞉ma꞉la꞉bo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Alan, ne kalu koma꞉lo꞉ gi tilidabu kaluka꞉isale Ya꞉lusalemdo꞉ sab o꞉mo꞉lo꞉ mogago꞉ dimida꞉seno꞉ modo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ dabu.
A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ e bobalo꞉ so꞉mia꞉sen misa꞉ kaluwa꞉ to halaido꞉ dia꞉sa꞉ga꞉, o꞉go꞉ amisa꞉n wena ya꞉ga꞉, tilidabu kaluka꞉isale a꞉no꞉ ta꞉lia꞉sa꞉ga꞉, dibolo aya to꞉loma꞉ni mio꞉.”
Ko꞉sega Alana꞉yo꞉ emo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Ha꞉la꞉ kaluwo꞉ a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ ene misa꞉ kaluwo꞉, a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ Isolael kalu o꞉lia꞉yo꞉ tambo No꞉no꞉n wiyo꞉ walama꞉ki, kalu we No꞉no꞉n da꞉fe alifa꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ ge elo꞉wa hamana.
E Ni wiyo꞉ wida꞉likilo꞉, hida꞉yo꞉ ko꞉li ko꞉lilo꞉wo꞉ ba꞉da꞉i ha꞉na꞉no꞉wo꞉, No꞉no꞉no꞉ walama꞉no꞉” a꞉la꞉sio꞉.
A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ Ananaias e aya ha꞉na꞉sa꞉ga꞉ tina꞉ga꞉yo꞉, e dagiyo꞉ Solo꞉ go꞉lakiyo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Nao So꞉l, Ne Alana꞉ gelo꞉wa iliga꞉tabi mio꞉. Ge toga ya꞉len amilo꞉, Ya꞉su gelo꞉ amilo꞉ handalowo꞉ a꞉ma꞉ iliga꞉tabi mio꞉. Ge wa꞉ka o꞉li ba꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Godeya꞉ Mamayo꞉ ge amio꞉ wa꞉lifoma꞉ki, ne gelo꞉wa iliga꞉fo꞉.”
A꞉la꞉sa꞉labiki, wigibo a꞉naka si amilo꞉ kelego꞉ noma꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ o꞉ngo꞉ a꞉no꞉ sululabiki, e o꞉li a꞉ba꞉ba꞉. A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ e dasilia꞉ga꞉ ho꞉na to꞉lolo꞉.
E ma꞉no꞉ na꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, halaido꞉wo꞉ o꞉li a꞉dowo꞉. Ho꞉len nolo꞉ So꞉l e tilidabu kalu nol o꞉lia꞉ Damaskas amisa꞉n a꞉na sen.
E Yu kaluwa꞉lo꞉ tolo꞉ wida꞉sen aya bo꞉bo꞉ge walama꞉ni ha꞉na꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, “Ya꞉su E Godeya꞉ Inso꞉le” a꞉la꞉liki wido꞉.
Kaluka꞉isale iyo꞉ to man elo꞉ widab a꞉no꞉ da꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, iligaki a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Ya꞉lusalem usamilo꞉ kaluka꞉isale Ya꞉su amilo꞉ tilidabu ilo꞉ mogagila꞉leno꞉ kalu weyele? A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ e amisa꞉n wenamilo꞉ mio꞉ we, iyo꞉ ta꞉lia꞉sa꞉ga꞉, bobalo꞉ so꞉mia꞉sen kalulo꞉wa tiliya꞉ha꞉na꞉ni a꞉gabele?” a꞉la꞉sio꞉.
Ko꞉sega So꞉l elo꞉ to widab a꞉no꞉ mada halaido꞉ fa꞉la꞉dowaki, Ya꞉su E Godeya꞉lo꞉ Da꞉feyo꞉ Kaluwo꞉ Eka꞉ a꞉la꞉liki hendele fanda sa꞉labiki, Yu kalu Damaskasdo꞉ sen a꞉ma꞉yo꞉, a꞉ma꞉la꞉do꞉ a꞉la꞉sa꞉ma꞉no꞉wo꞉ aundo꞉ma dowo꞉.
A꞉ma꞉ fa꞉s amio꞉, ho꞉len modo꞉wo꞉ ta꞉ta꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, Yu kaluwo꞉ kegea꞉sa꞉ga꞉, So꞉l e sana soma꞉no꞉ nenela꞉sa꞉ga꞉ saefa꞉.
Ko꞉sega So꞉l eyo꞉ ililo꞉ saefa꞉ a꞉no꞉ dabu. Ho꞉len o꞉lia꞉ nulu o꞉lia꞉ amio꞉, iliyo꞉ amisa꞉n amilo꞉ tog ha꞉na꞉sen a꞉namio꞉ e ta꞉lia꞉sa꞉ga꞉ sana soma꞉no꞉ a꞉la꞉liki yasila꞉len.
Ko꞉sega nulu no amio꞉, Sola꞉ ene kudu sian kalu iliyo꞉ e asuwa꞉taki, asa disa꞉la꞉sa꞉ga꞉, amisa꞉na꞉lo꞉ ilif tolo꞉ amilo꞉ ho꞉ gulu nowa meya꞉ sunda꞉sa꞉ga꞉, ha꞉sa to꞉lolo꞉.
E amisa꞉n a꞉namilo꞉ seno꞉ sili alita꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Ya꞉lusalem a꞉na fa꞉la꞉dowa꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, tilidabu kalu a꞉namilo꞉ sen a꞉no꞉lia꞉ gasama꞉no꞉ asulo꞉ ko꞉sega, e Ya꞉su amio꞉ hendele tilidabu a꞉la꞉bo꞉, iyo꞉ mo꞉fanda asulo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉, iliyo꞉ e tagilaki mo꞉gasili.
Ko꞉sega Banabas eyo꞉ So꞉l e asuwa꞉takiyo꞉, e iliga꞉felo꞉ kalulo꞉wa tilia꞉gane. Banabas eyo꞉ imo꞉ dinafa fanda sa꞉lakiyo꞉, So꞉l e Damaskas tog a꞉na ha꞉na꞉lena, elo꞉ Alan ba꞉ba꞉ a꞉no꞉lia꞉, Alana꞉lo꞉ emo꞉lo꞉ towo꞉ sio꞉ a꞉no꞉lia꞉ So꞉l e amisa꞉na ha꞉na꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Ya꞉suwa꞉ wi sa꞉ma꞉no꞉wo꞉ e mo꞉tagilaki, amisa꞉na wida꞉len a꞉la꞉liki, Banabas eyo꞉ imo꞉wo꞉ fanda wido꞉.
A꞉la꞉kudu miabiki, So꞉l e i o꞉lia꞉ gasaliaki, Ya꞉lusalem us a꞉namio꞉ nanogo꞉ egele dimidaki, So꞉l e Ya꞉suwa꞉ wiyo꞉ halaido꞉ wido꞉.
So꞉l e Yu kalu, Gilig tolo꞉ sa꞉lan i o꞉lia꞉yo꞉ towa꞉yo꞉ kego꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ iliyo꞉ e sana soma꞉no꞉ dowo꞉.
Ao i, tilidabu nolba꞉yo꞉ a꞉no꞉ da꞉da꞉ga꞉, iliyo꞉ e Sa꞉sa꞉lia amisa꞉na tililia꞉ ha꞉na꞉ga꞉, Tasus amisa꞉n a꞉na hamana꞉ki ho꞉n ko꞉suwa iliga꞉fo꞉.
A꞉la꞉go꞉ko꞉lo꞉ ho꞉len a꞉namio꞉ tilidabu kaluka꞉isale, Yudia hen o꞉lia꞉ Galili heno꞉lo꞉, Samalia꞉ heno꞉lo꞉ us a꞉namio꞉ ha꞉fo꞉ dowaki sagalo꞉ sen. Iliyo꞉ Godeya꞉ mano꞉ dinafa kuduha꞉nabikiyo꞉, Godeya꞉ Mamaya꞉yo꞉ ili asulo꞉wo꞉ halale alitaki, kalu modo꞉wo꞉ wa꞉ka a꞉kudu mio꞉.
Bida eyo꞉ amisa꞉n ko꞉li ko꞉lilo꞉ sia꞉la꞉ga꞉, tilidabu kaluka꞉isale, Laida amisa꞉n amilo꞉ seno꞉ e ba꞉ba꞉ni ane.
E a꞉na fa꞉la꞉dowo꞉ amio꞉, kalu nowo꞉ Ainias a꞉na galili. Ainias e giligi siliki, e donayo꞉ ola꞉fo꞉ a꞉no꞉ wo꞉ba sen.
Bida e fa꞉la꞉dowakiyo꞉, Ainias emo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Ainias, Ya꞉su Kelisowa꞉yo꞉ ge falele alitab ko꞉lo꞉ ge dasila꞉sa꞉ga꞉, geondo꞉ kamboloma.” A꞉la꞉sa꞉labiki, wigibo a꞉naka Ainias e dasi.
Laida amisa꞉n a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ Salon fua꞉lo꞉ hen a꞉namilo꞉ sen kaluka꞉isale iyo꞉, Ainias e ko꞉lo꞉ falele alitab a꞉no꞉ ba꞉da꞉ga꞉, iyo꞉ asulo꞉ nodola꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Alano꞉ kudu ane.
Yoba amisa꞉n amio꞉, tilidabu ga nowo꞉ siliki, ene wiyo꞉ Tabita, ko꞉sega Gilik towa꞉ sa꞉lakiyo꞉, Dokas a꞉la꞉sa꞉lan. E man nafa dimida꞉liki, wa꞉feyo꞉ kaluka꞉isale kelego꞉lo꞉ma a꞉no꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ asuwa꞉ta꞉sen.
Ho꞉len a꞉namio꞉, e walaf ba꞉la꞉sa꞉ga꞉ sowo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ ene do꞉mo꞉wo꞉ ho꞉no꞉ mulu alita꞉sa꞉ga꞉, galale wa꞉l amilo꞉wa dia꞉folen.
Lidia amisa꞉n o꞉lia꞉ Yoba amisa꞉n o꞉lia꞉ ko꞉na꞉ma ko꞉lo꞉, tilidabu kaluka꞉isale iliyo꞉ Bida e Lidia a꞉na sab a꞉la꞉da꞉da꞉ga꞉, iliyo꞉ kalu a꞉la꞉yo꞉ elo꞉wa iliga꞉ta꞉ga꞉, emo꞉wo꞉ ha꞉nolo sa꞉laki a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Ge o꞉go꞉ mada nilo꞉wa mena!”
A꞉la꞉sa꞉labiki, Bida e a꞉la꞉ o꞉lia꞉ ha꞉na꞉ga꞉ fa꞉la꞉dowabikiyo꞉, iliyo꞉ e tililia꞉ga꞉, galale wa꞉l amio꞉ tiane. Ga sa꞉ba꞉lo꞉ nolo꞉ elo꞉wa hege kagafo꞉liki, ya꞉foda꞉likiyo꞉, Tabita e o꞉silikilo꞉ helebeso꞉g sa꞉ga꞉la꞉sen elo꞉ dimido꞉ a꞉no꞉ Bida emo꞉ wido꞉.
Bida eyo꞉ kaluka꞉isaleyo꞉ tambo ha꞉la꞉ya iliga꞉ta꞉sa꞉ga꞉, e gulalu siliki Godemo꞉ dulugu sio꞉. E ga sowo꞉lo꞉ doba꞉da꞉ nodolakiyo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Tabita, ge dasima!” A꞉la꞉sa꞉labiki, ga a꞉no꞉ siyo꞉ fasila꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Bida e sikudu ba꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, e dasi asi.
Bida eyo꞉ ga a꞉no꞉ dagiya gasilia꞉ga꞉, dasi alifa꞉. A꞉la꞉dimida꞉sa꞉ga꞉, eyo꞉ tilidabu kaluka꞉isale o꞉lia꞉ ga sa꞉ba꞉lo꞉ o꞉lia꞉yo꞉ hoida꞉sa꞉ga꞉, ga sowo꞉ a꞉no꞉ a꞉ma꞉la꞉ dasi sab a꞉la꞉liki imo꞉wo꞉ wido꞉.
Elo꞉ dimido꞉ a꞉no꞉, Yoba amisa꞉n amio꞉ sa꞉la꞉i ha꞉nabikiyo꞉, tambo dabu ko꞉lo꞉ iyo꞉ Alan amio꞉ modo꞉ tilidabu.
Bida e ho꞉len nolo꞉ Yoba amisa꞉n a꞉namio꞉, no꞉ do꞉go꞉fdo꞉ dinafaya꞉sen kalu, Saimon e aya sen.
Sesalia amisa꞉n a꞉namio꞉, kalu nowo꞉ ene wiyo꞉ Konilius a꞉na sen. Eyo꞉ Loma꞉ ami kalu “Itali” a꞉la꞉sa꞉lan us a꞉namio꞉ nanogo꞉ dimidaki, e da꞉la꞉di fudo꞉ otalen bo꞉fo꞉lowan kalu nowo꞉ e.
Konilius o꞉lia꞉ ene eso꞉lo꞉ o꞉lia꞉ma꞉yo꞉ Godeya꞉ mando꞉ kudu ha꞉na꞉likiyo꞉, iyo꞉ ho꞉leno꞉ tambo Godemo꞉ dulugu sa꞉la꞉len a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ Yu kalu molelo꞉ma wa꞉feyo꞉ o꞉mo꞉wo꞉ dimia꞉len.
Ho꞉len no amio꞉, ofa꞉si ga꞉lo asola dowabiki, e ho꞉le ba꞉dakiyo꞉, Godeya꞉ ma꞉mula꞉ kaluwo꞉ elo꞉wa ya꞉sa꞉ga꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Konilius!”
A꞉la꞉sa꞉labiki, Konilius e ba꞉da꞉kiyo꞉, tagilaki a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Kalu alan, o꞉ba?” A꞉la꞉dabuba꞉dabiki, ma꞉mula꞉ kaluwa꞉yo꞉ emo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Gilo꞉ dulugu sa꞉la꞉seno꞉ a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ boba kelego꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ wa꞉feyo꞉ kalumo꞉lo꞉ dimia꞉sen a꞉no꞉lo꞉, o꞉go꞉ Godemo꞉lo꞉ boba dimi o꞉ngo꞉ fa꞉la꞉dowo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ Godeya꞉yo꞉ a꞉no꞉ ba꞉da꞉ga꞉ sagalab.
A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ Saimon Bida e mena꞉ki, o꞉go꞉ ge kalu nolo꞉ Yoba amisa꞉na iliga꞉foma. Bida e no꞉ do꞉go꞉fdo dinafaya꞉sen kalu, Saimon o꞉lia꞉ so꞉lu ho꞉n aniba sab ko꞉lo꞉, e gelo꞉wa mena꞉ki, kalu nolo꞉ iliga꞉foma.”
<range>
Ma꞉mula꞉ kaluwa꞉yo꞉ a꞉la꞉sa꞉la꞉sa꞉ga꞉ ha꞉na꞉ga꞉ dotabiki, Konilius eyo꞉ ene nanogdo꞉ dian kalu a꞉la꞉ a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ ene da꞉la꞉di nowo꞉ elo꞉wa mena꞉ki ho꞉ido꞉.
Konilius elo꞉ dabu a꞉no꞉ imo꞉wo꞉ tambo malolo꞉ mia꞉sa꞉ga꞉, i a꞉no꞉ Yoba amisa꞉na iliga꞉fo꞉.
Ho꞉len no amio꞉ iyo꞉ ha꞉na꞉la꞉ga꞉yo꞉, amisa꞉no꞉ ko꞉na꞉ma fa꞉la꞉doma꞉niki disi dowabikiyo꞉, Bida e Godemo꞉ sa꞉ma꞉ni, a fa꞉sa wa꞉la fa꞉la꞉ ane.
E a꞉na siliki, maiyo꞉ alan dowabiki, ma꞉no꞉wo꞉ sofa꞉ki sa꞉la꞉sa꞉ga꞉, iyo꞉ ma꞉no꞉ soda꞉lab amio꞉, e ho꞉le ba꞉ba꞉.
Eyo꞉ ho꞉le ba꞉dakiyo꞉, Hebeneyo꞉ kolaita꞉sa꞉ga꞉, kelego꞉ nowo꞉ helebeso꞉g alan o꞉ngo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ migif fa꞉la꞉da꞉in amio꞉ ta꞉lidota꞉ga꞉, ololo to꞉lo꞉lo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ tindabi ba꞉ba꞉.
Helebeso꞉g us amio꞉ no꞉ ko꞉li ko꞉lilo꞉ a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ sowa꞉ a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ o꞉ba꞉ ko꞉li ko꞉lilo꞉, Godeya꞉lo꞉ na꞉so꞉boka꞉ a꞉la꞉likilo꞉ saefa꞉ a꞉no꞉lo꞉ a꞉na delena ba꞉ba꞉.
A꞉no꞉ ba꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, to nowo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Bida, ge dasima! No꞉ we yasala꞉sa꞉ga꞉ maiya!”
A꞉la꞉sa꞉labiki, Bida eyo꞉ a꞉ma꞉la꞉bo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Alan, ne a꞉la꞉bo꞉ mada mo꞉dimidama꞉no꞉! Yu kaluwa꞉ ele difa꞉ usamilo꞉ ‘Na꞉so꞉bo’ a꞉la꞉do꞉ saefo꞉ a꞉no꞉ ne mada mo꞉nan.”
A꞉la꞉sa꞉labikiyo꞉, towo꞉ emo꞉wo꞉ wa꞉ka a꞉sio꞉, “Godeya꞉lo꞉ ‘gemo꞉lo꞉ we nafa ko꞉lo꞉ o꞉li na꞉bika꞉’ a꞉la꞉do꞉ sio꞉ a꞉no꞉, giyo꞉ ma꞉no꞉ a꞉no꞉ Godeya꞉ siwa꞉l amio꞉ mogago꞉ a꞉la꞉likiyo꞉ sa꞉la꞉so꞉bo” a꞉la꞉sio꞉.
A꞉la꞉dimida꞉lowo꞉wo꞉ otalen fa꞉la꞉dota꞉ga꞉, wigibo a꞉na꞉ka kelego꞉ a꞉no꞉ a꞉ma꞉la꞉ Hebene dia꞉gane.
Bida eyo꞉ ho꞉le ba꞉ba꞉ a꞉ma꞉ ha꞉go꞉ kedelena, Koniliusa꞉lo꞉ iliga꞉fo꞉ kalu i a꞉no꞉ amisa꞉na fa꞉la꞉dowa꞉ta꞉ga꞉, Saimona꞉ ayo꞉ keda꞉i ya꞉ga꞉, a elo꞉ a꞉na fa꞉la꞉dowo꞉.
Iyo꞉ a꞉na fa꞉la꞉dowakiyo꞉, “Saimon Bidayo꞉ wiyo꞉ saba?” a꞉la꞉ ho꞉le dabu.
Bida eyo꞉ ho꞉le ba꞉ba꞉ a꞉ma꞉ ha꞉go꞉ o꞉kedelen amio꞉, Godeya꞉ Mamaya꞉yo꞉ emo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Saimon, kalu otalena꞉yo꞉ ge kedab ko꞉lo꞉ ge dasila꞉sa꞉ga꞉, ha꞉g holona timana. I a꞉no꞉ No꞉no꞉n gelo꞉wa iliga꞉fo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ ge i o꞉lia꞉ ha꞉nakiyo꞉ kele asulakiyo꞉ ha꞉na꞉so꞉bo.”
<range>
A꞉la꞉sa꞉labiki da꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, Bida e ha꞉ga tina꞉sa꞉ga꞉, imo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Gililo꞉ keda꞉i mio꞉wo꞉ ne ko꞉lo꞉ giyo꞉ nelo꞉ amilo꞉ mio꞉we mo꞉wo꞉ o꞉ba?”
A꞉la꞉dabu ba꞉dabiki, iliyo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Loma꞉ da꞉la꞉di bo꞉fo꞉lowan kalu Konilius, nio꞉ e iliga꞉tabiki, gelo꞉wa mio꞉. Konilius, e man digalo꞉ kuduha꞉nakiyo꞉, Godeya꞉ mando꞉ kudu ha꞉na꞉sen ko꞉lo꞉ Yu kaluka꞉isale tambo e ko꞉lo꞉ wabuda꞉sen. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ Godeya꞉ ma꞉mula꞉ kaluwo꞉ elo꞉wa ya꞉sa꞉ga꞉ sa꞉lakiyo꞉, ‘Bida elo꞉ to sa꞉lab a꞉no꞉ gelo꞉ da꞉ba꞉niki, e mena꞉ki ho꞉lema’ a꞉la꞉sio꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ mio꞉.”
A꞉la꞉sa꞉labiki, Bida eyo꞉ iyo꞉ a꞉na alima꞉ki, a usa tilia꞉gane. Iyo꞉ alita꞉ga꞉yo꞉, kea꞉fo amio꞉ Bida o꞉lia꞉ Yoba tilidabu ao i nol o꞉lia꞉ Koniliusa꞉lo꞉ iliga꞉fo꞉ kalu a꞉no꞉lia꞉ iyo꞉ a꞉ma꞉la꞉ ha꞉na꞉ni ane.
Ho꞉len imiligo꞉ alita꞉ga꞉yo꞉, Sesalia amisa꞉na fa꞉la꞉dowo꞉. Konilius eyo꞉ i a꞉no꞉ mia꞉ib a꞉la꞉bo꞉ asula꞉sa꞉ga꞉, eyo꞉ ene so꞉lo꞉ o꞉lia꞉ ene milileyo꞉ elo꞉wa kegenefo꞉liki yasilo꞉.
A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ Bida e a usa tinabikiyo꞉, Konilius eyo꞉ Bidayo꞉ ebea꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, e wabudaki gulalu asi.
Ko꞉sega Bida eyo꞉ e gasiliakiyo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Dasima, nelo꞉ kalu ge o꞉ngo꞉” a꞉la꞉sio꞉.
Bida eyo꞉ e o꞉lia꞉ nenela꞉liki, a usa tina꞉ga꞉, kaluka꞉isale kegeo꞉wo꞉ modo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ sena ba꞉ba꞉.
Bida eyo꞉ kalu kegeo꞉ o꞉mo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Yuwa꞉ ele amio꞉, Yu kaluwa꞉yo꞉ ha꞉la꞉ kalu o꞉lia꞉yo꞉ ualo꞉ gasaya꞉so꞉bo a꞉la꞉saefa꞉. Ele a꞉no꞉ gio꞉ asulo꞉ ko꞉sega niyo꞉ kalu nowo꞉ ‘Godeya꞉ siwa꞉l amio꞉ e mogago꞉’ a꞉la꞉bo꞉ mo꞉sama꞉ki asulakiyo꞉, Godeya꞉yo꞉ nemo꞉ wido꞉.
A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ giyo꞉ ne mena꞉ki ho꞉idabikiyo꞉, ne mo꞉mo꞉beaki mio꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ gilo꞉ kalu nelo꞉ amio꞉ iliga꞉fo꞉ a꞉no꞉ o꞉bo꞉ sa꞉ma꞉nigo꞉wo꞉?”
A꞉la꞉sa꞉labiki, Konilius eyo꞉ a꞉ma꞉la꞉bo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “A꞉ma꞉ inali amio꞉, ne ofa꞉siyo꞉ ga꞉lo asola dowabikiyo꞉, ne aya siliki, Godemo꞉ dulugu sa꞉la꞉li sen amio꞉, wigibole a꞉naka kalu nowo꞉, helebeso꞉g ho꞉lo꞉, siyo꞉ funa꞉ a꞉la꞉ma꞉no꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ a꞉no꞉ nelo꞉wa fa꞉la꞉dowakiyo꞉, nemo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, ‘Konilius, gilo꞉ Godemo꞉lo꞉ dulugu sio꞉ a꞉no꞉ Godeyo꞉ dabu. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ gilo꞉ wa꞉feyo꞉ kalumo꞉lo꞉ boba dimisen a꞉no꞉ E asulaki go꞉.
<range>
A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ ge kalu nolo꞉ Yoba amisa꞉na iliga꞉ta꞉ga꞉, Saimon Bidayo꞉ nelowa mena꞉ki, sa꞉ma꞉ hamana. Bida e kalu noma꞉ aya sab. Kalu a꞉ma꞉ wi a꞉no꞉lo꞉ Saimon ko꞉lo꞉ e so꞉lu ho꞉n aniba siliki, no꞉ do꞉go꞉fdo dinafaya꞉liki ta꞉sen’ a꞉la꞉sio꞉.
A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ ge nelo꞉ wena mena꞉ki, niyo꞉ kalu we gelo꞉ amio꞉ bo꞉i iliga꞉fo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ ge mada o꞉li mio꞉. A꞉la꞉go꞉ko꞉lo꞉ nio꞉ o꞉ma Godeya꞉ siwa꞉l amio꞉ tambo kegenelia꞉ga꞉lo꞉ sen we, Godeya꞉lo꞉ gemo꞉lo꞉ sama꞉kilo꞉ sio꞉ a꞉no꞉, nilo꞉ da꞉ba꞉niki so꞉l.”
A꞉la꞉sa꞉labiki, Bida eyo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Niyo꞉ o꞉go꞉ fanda asulakiyo꞉, Godeya꞉yo꞉ henfelo꞉ kaluka꞉isale ko꞉li ko꞉lilo꞉ sab o꞉mo꞉wo꞉, mano꞉ imilig dimida꞉sen.
Kaluka꞉isale abeyo꞉, man digalo꞉le dimidaki, E ha꞉ga dowalega, Godeya꞉yo꞉ i o꞉mo꞉wo꞉ sagale alita꞉sen. Kaluka꞉isale henfelo꞉ amilo꞉ ko꞉li ko꞉lilo꞉wa a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉lo꞉ mio꞉ a꞉no꞉, Godeya꞉ tambo i o꞉mo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉ dimida꞉sen.
Godeya꞉ sagalo꞉ to ko꞉lo꞉ Isolael kaluka꞉isalemo꞉ saga꞉fo꞉ a꞉no꞉, Ya꞉su Alan, tambolo꞉ bo꞉fo꞉lowan, man a꞉no꞉ e dia꞉mio꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ kaluka꞉isaleyo꞉ to a꞉no꞉ da꞉dakiyo꞉, Gode o꞉lia꞉ o꞉li sagalaki, ege doma꞉ib.
Yon eyo꞉ ho꞉na to꞉lo꞉lan wida꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, Ga꞉lili hen us a꞉namio꞉ mo꞉mo꞉daki, Yesuwa꞉lo꞉ Yudia hen amilo꞉ dimido꞉ a꞉no꞉ gio꞉ asulo꞉
Niyo꞉ a꞉no꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ sio꞉. Ya꞉su, Nasa꞉la꞉d kalu e, Godeya꞉yo꞉ da꞉fea꞉sa꞉ga꞉, halaido꞉ o꞉lia꞉ Ene Mama o꞉lia꞉yo꞉ dimi ko꞉lo꞉ Ya꞉su e, Gode o꞉lia꞉ ilikiyo꞉, man nafa dimida꞉liki sia꞉len. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ eyo꞉ kaluka꞉isaleyo꞉ Seteneya꞉ bo꞉fo꞉likilo꞉ dikidia꞉sen a꞉no꞉ sili alifelo꞉.
Elo꞉ Isolael hen o꞉lia꞉ Ya꞉lusalem amisa꞉n amilo꞉ dimido꞉ a꞉no꞉ nio꞉ ba꞉ba꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ asulo꞉. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ tif amio꞉ iliyo꞉ e i malana alula꞉sa꞉ga꞉ sana sowo꞉ ko꞉sega, ho꞉len otalen ta꞉ta꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Godeya꞉yo꞉ e a꞉ma꞉la꞉ a꞉dasi alita꞉ga꞉, kalu nolbo꞉wo꞉ bo꞉ba꞉ki ta꞉fo꞉.
<range>
Ya꞉su e ko꞉lo꞉ dasili a꞉no꞉, kalu tambowa꞉yo꞉ mo꞉ba꞉ba꞉, ko꞉sega Godeya꞉lo꞉ tamin amilo꞉ da꞉feyo꞉ kalu nolba꞉ ba꞉ba. Kalu a꞉no꞉, ni ko꞉lo꞉ Ya꞉suwo꞉ dasila꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, negele silikiyo꞉ ma꞉n o꞉lia꞉ ho꞉n o꞉lia꞉yo꞉ na꞉len.
A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ nio꞉ kaluka꞉isalemo꞉wo꞉ Godeya꞉ to nafa a꞉no꞉ walama꞉kiyo꞉, Eyo꞉ nimo꞉wo꞉ sio꞉. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ E kaluka꞉isalelo꞉ mela꞉no꞉lo꞉ o꞉lab o꞉lia꞉ dane ane o꞉lia꞉lo꞉ alobanama꞉no꞉wo꞉, Godeya꞉yo꞉ E ko꞉lo꞉ da꞉feyo꞉ a꞉la꞉likiyo꞉, nimo꞉wo꞉ wida꞉melea꞉ki walalifa꞉.
Tamin amio꞉ dinali sa꞉lan kalu tambowa꞉yo꞉ Ya꞉su ko꞉lo꞉ sa꞉la꞉kiyo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, ‘Kaluka꞉isale abeyo꞉ eya tilida꞉dalega, Ya꞉su Keliso a꞉ma꞉ wiyalikiyo꞉, Godeya꞉yo꞉ mogago꞉ ililo꞉wo꞉ ga꞉lila꞉ma꞉ib.’”
Bida e to a꞉no꞉ko꞉ o꞉sa꞉la꞉lena, Godeya꞉ Mamayo꞉ kaluka꞉isale tolo꞉ da꞉da꞉lab ilo꞉wa tinda꞉ga꞉ dowo꞉.
Godeya꞉ Mamayo꞉ Yu kaluma i amio꞉lo꞉ dowa꞉sa꞉ga꞉, iyo꞉ to ko꞉li ko꞉lilo꞉ sa꞉laki, Godeya꞉ wiyo꞉ duludabiki, Yoba a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉lo꞉, Yu tilidabu kalu, Bida o꞉lia꞉lo꞉ mio꞉ a꞉no꞉, iliyo꞉ da꞉da꞉ga꞉ iligo꞉.
<range>
A꞉la꞉gabiki, Bidaya꞉yo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Kaluka꞉isale i we Godeya꞉ Mamayo꞉ nililo꞉ di o꞉ngo꞉ di ko꞉lo꞉, kalu nolba꞉yo꞉ i we ho꞉na to꞉loma꞉no꞉wo꞉ mo꞉ka꞉ma꞉ib.”
A꞉la꞉go꞉ko꞉lo꞉ Bida eyo꞉ iyo꞉ Ya꞉su Keliso wiya iliki ho꞉na to꞉loma a꞉la꞉sa꞉labiki, ho꞉na to꞉lolo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ iliyo꞉ Bida e ho꞉len nolo꞉ i o꞉lia꞉ o꞉doma꞉ki dabuba꞉ba꞉.
Iliga꞉felo꞉ kalu o꞉lia꞉ tilidabu kalu Yudia henamilo꞉ sen nol o꞉lia꞉yo꞉, Yu kaluma nolo꞉ Godeya꞉ to tilidabuka꞉ a꞉la꞉sa꞉labi dabu.
A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ Bida e Ya꞉lusalem ha꞉na꞉ga꞉ fa꞉la꞉dowabikiyo꞉, tilidabu kalu do꞉go꞉fo꞉ hege gedeo꞉ kalu iliyo꞉ Bidamo꞉wo꞉ gadi sa꞉laki a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Ge do꞉go꞉fo꞉ mo꞉gedeo꞉ kaluwa꞉ aya siliki, ma꞉no꞉ gegele na꞉len.”
<range>
A꞉la꞉sa꞉labiki, Bida eyo꞉ dimido꞉ fa꞉la꞉dowo꞉ o꞉leaumbo꞉ kalu imo꞉wo꞉ tambo fanda sa꞉laki a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Ne Yoba amisa꞉na siliki, dulugu sa꞉la꞉len amio꞉, ne ho꞉le ba꞉dakiyo꞉, Hebene kolaita꞉sa꞉ga꞉, kelego꞉ nowo꞉ helebeso꞉g alano꞉ o꞉ngo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ migif fa꞉la꞉da꞉in ami ta꞉lidota꞉ga꞉, ololo to꞉lola꞉i tindabi ba꞉ba꞉.
<range>
Helebeso꞉g us amio꞉ no꞉ ko꞉li ko꞉lilo꞉ a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ sowa꞉yo꞉ a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ o꞉ba꞉ ko꞉li ko꞉lilo꞉, Godeya꞉lo꞉ na꞉so꞉boka꞉ a꞉la꞉likilo꞉ saefa꞉ a꞉no꞉lo꞉ a꞉na delena ba꞉ba꞉.
A꞉no꞉ ba꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, to nowo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, ‘Bida, ge dasima! No꞉ we yasala꞉sa꞉ga꞉ maiya!’
A꞉la꞉sa꞉labiki, niyo꞉ a꞉ma꞉la꞉bo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, ‘Alan, ne a꞉la꞉bo꞉ mada mo꞉dimidama꞉no꞉! Yu kaluwa꞉ ele difa꞉ usamilo꞉ “Na꞉so꞉boka꞉” a꞉la꞉do꞉ saefo꞉ a꞉no꞉ ne mada mo꞉nan.’
A꞉la꞉sa꞉labikiyo꞉, towo꞉ nemo꞉wo꞉ wa꞉ka a꞉sio꞉, ‘Godeya꞉lo꞉ gemo꞉lo꞉, “we nafa ko꞉lo꞉ o꞉li na꞉bika꞉” a꞉la꞉do꞉ sio꞉ a꞉no꞉, giyo꞉ ma꞉no꞉ a꞉no꞉ Gode siwa꞉l amio꞉ mogago꞉ a꞉la꞉likiyo꞉ sa꞉la꞉so꞉bo’ a꞉la꞉sio꞉.
A꞉la꞉dimida꞉leno꞉ otalen fa꞉la꞉dota꞉ga꞉ wigibo a꞉naka kelego꞉ a꞉no꞉ a꞉ma꞉la꞉ Hebene ane.
Wigibo a꞉naka, kalu otalen, Konilius elo꞉ Sesalia a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉lo꞉ iliga꞉fo꞉ a꞉no꞉ a nilo꞉ sen a꞉na fa꞉la꞉dowo꞉.
A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ Godeya꞉ Mamaya꞉yo꞉ nemo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, ‘Ge i o꞉lia꞉ ha꞉nakiyo꞉, kele asula꞉likiyo꞉ ha꞉na꞉so꞉bo’ a꞉la꞉sio꞉. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ kalu do꞉go꞉fela꞉fo꞉ we ne o꞉lia꞉ ha꞉na꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Koniliusa꞉ a usa ane.
Konilius elo꞉ amilo꞉ fa꞉la꞉dowo꞉ a꞉no꞉ nemo꞉ malolo꞉ me. Ma꞉mula꞉ kaluwa꞉ Koniliusa꞉ aya fa꞉la꞉dota꞉ga꞉ ilikiyo꞉, emo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, ‘Saimon Bida a꞉no꞉ wena mena꞉ki, o꞉go꞉ ge kalu nolo꞉ Yoba amisa꞉na iliga꞉foma.
Eyo꞉ to nafayo꞉ gimo꞉wo꞉ sa꞉ma꞉ mia꞉b ko꞉lo꞉ gi o꞉lia꞉ gi ayamilo꞉ so꞉lo꞉ sab a꞉no꞉lo꞉ a꞉ma꞉la꞉ gasiliakilo꞉ mesa꞉no꞉ a꞉no꞉ walama꞉ib.’
Ma꞉mula꞉ kaluwa꞉yo꞉ to a꞉no꞉ sio꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ ne a꞉na ha꞉na꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, niyo꞉ towo꞉ halaido꞉ mo꞉mo꞉da wida꞉sen amio꞉, Godeya꞉ Mamayo꞉ tamina nilo꞉ amilo꞉ mio꞉ aumbo꞉, ilo꞉ amio꞉lo꞉ a꞉la꞉ mio꞉.
A꞉la꞉gabikiyo꞉, niyo꞉ Ya꞉suwa꞉lo꞉ nimo꞉lo꞉ tamina sio꞉ a꞉no꞉ a꞉asulakiyo꞉, eyo꞉ a꞉na sa꞉lakiyo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, ‘Yona꞉yo꞉ ho꞉n deya to꞉lola꞉len ko꞉sega o꞉go꞉ giliyo꞉ Godeya꞉ Ene Mamaleya꞉ to꞉loma꞉ib.’
Tamin amio꞉ nio꞉ Ya꞉su Kelisowa tilidadabikilo꞉ Godeya꞉lo꞉ boba nimo꞉lo꞉ dimi a꞉no꞉ o꞉go꞉ imo꞉wo꞉lo꞉ dimi ko꞉lo꞉ Godeya꞉lo꞉ dimidab a꞉no꞉ niyo꞉ waga ka꞉ma꞉no꞉wo꞉?” Bida a꞉la꞉sio꞉.
Yu amilo꞉ tilidabu kaluka꞉isaleyo꞉ to a꞉no꞉ da꞉dakiyo꞉, iyo꞉ wa꞉kabiyo꞉ mo꞉kele asulaka, Godeya꞉ wiyo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ dulugu sa꞉lakiyo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “O꞉go꞉ Yu kaluka꞉isalema i a꞉no꞉lo꞉ asugo꞉ nodola꞉sa꞉ga꞉, mela꞉no꞉wo꞉ dima꞉ki, Godeya꞉yo꞉ fogo꞉ hendele dimelo꞉b” a꞉la꞉sio꞉.
Sitifendo꞉ sa꞉ndab ho꞉len a꞉namio꞉, hida꞉yo꞉ alan fa꞉la꞉dowo꞉ a꞉ma꞉ ilikiyo꞉, tilidabu kaluka꞉isaleyo꞉ dalalelia꞉ga꞉, nolo꞉ Fonisia hen a꞉na, nolo꞉ Saibulus hen a꞉na, a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ nolo꞉ Antio꞉g amisa꞉n a꞉na ane. Iyo꞉ ha꞉na꞉siakiyo꞉, Godeya꞉ to nafayo꞉ Yu kaluka꞉isalemo꞉ ka wida꞉i ane.
Ko꞉sega Saibulus o꞉lia꞉ Salini amilo꞉ tilidabu kalu nolo꞉ Antio꞉g amisa꞉na ha꞉na꞉siakiyo꞉, Ya꞉su Alana꞉ to nafa a꞉no꞉, Yu kaluka꞉isalema imo꞉wo꞉lo꞉ wido꞉.
A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ Alana꞉ halaido꞉wo꞉ i amio꞉ asulo꞉wa dofo꞉liki wido꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ kaluka꞉isaleyo꞉ modo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ tilida꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Ya꞉su Alan e kudu ane.
Amisa꞉n a꞉namilo꞉ fa꞉la꞉dowo꞉ a꞉no꞉ Ya꞉lusalem tilidabu kaluka꞉isaleyo꞉ dabu ko꞉lo꞉ iliyo꞉ Banabaso꞉ Antio꞉g a꞉na iliga꞉fo꞉.
E a꞉na fa꞉la꞉dowaki ba꞉ba꞉yo꞉, Godeya꞉yo꞉ kaluka꞉isaleyo꞉ asufa꞉lo꞉biki ba꞉da꞉ga꞉, e sagalakiyo꞉, iyo꞉ Alan o꞉lia꞉ tambo ege dowaki, asugo꞉ himuwa oga꞉dita꞉ga꞉ doma꞉ki, e halale alifa꞉.
Banabas e kalu nafa, a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ tilidabu elo꞉wo꞉ halaido꞉ a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ Godeya꞉ Mamayo꞉ eyamio꞉ wa꞉lifo꞉liki wido꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ kaluka꞉isale modo꞉wo꞉ asugo꞉ nodola꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Ya꞉su Alan e ko꞉lo꞉ kudu ane.
A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ Banabas e So꞉l kelema꞉ni ane. E Tasus amisa꞉n a꞉na ha꞉na꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Solo꞉ galili ko꞉lo꞉ Antio꞉g amisa꞉na a꞉ma꞉la꞉ tililia꞉ mio꞉. A꞉la꞉yo꞉ dona imiligo꞉ tilidabu kaluka꞉isale o꞉lia꞉ siliki, kaluka꞉isale modo꞉mo꞉ wida꞉len. A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ kaluka꞉isale a꞉namilo꞉ sen a꞉ma꞉yo꞉ Ya꞉sulo꞉ kudu ha꞉nab kaluka꞉isale a꞉no꞉ “Keliso kaluka꞉isaleka꞉” a꞉la꞉liki Antio꞉g a꞉na mo꞉mo꞉da wikilo꞉.
<range>
Ho꞉len a꞉ma꞉ imilib amio꞉, Godeya꞉ dinali sa꞉lan kalu nolo꞉ Ya꞉lusalem a꞉na a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ Antio꞉g a꞉na ane.
Kalu i a꞉no꞉, nowo꞉ wiyo꞉ Agabus ko꞉lo꞉ e Godeya꞉ Mamaya꞉ halaido꞉wo꞉ eya iliki, ho꞉le ba꞉dabikiyo꞉, e kalu kegeo꞉ siwa꞉la kagayaki a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Henfelo꞉ wenamio꞉ maiyo꞉wo꞉ alan fa꞉la꞉doma꞉ib” a꞉la꞉sio꞉. (Kolodius e Lom hen bo꞉fo꞉lab ho꞉len a꞉namio꞉, dinali sio꞉ a꞉no꞉ hendele fa꞉la꞉dowakiyo꞉, maiyo꞉wo꞉ alan dowo꞉.)
A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ tilidabu kaluka꞉isale iliyo꞉ towo꞉ saitakiyo꞉, moleyo꞉ enedo꞉ asulab aumb kegea꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, Yudia hen amilo꞉ ao i sab nolo꞉ asuwa꞉fa꞉niki kegeo꞉.
Kegea꞉la꞉ga꞉, Banabas dia꞉ So꞉l dia꞉mo꞉ dimia꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Ya꞉lusalem misa꞉ kalulo꞉wa dia꞉hamana꞉ki, iliga꞉fo꞉.
O꞉g ho꞉len a꞉namio꞉, Misa꞉ kalu Helo꞉d eyo꞉ tilidabu kaluka꞉isale nolo꞉ mogagima꞉no꞉ a꞉la꞉likiyo꞉, to sa꞉ifa꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ iyo꞉ ta꞉lia꞉sa꞉ga꞉ dibolo aya disa꞉.
A꞉la꞉dimida꞉likiyo꞉, eyo꞉ Yona꞉ ao, Yemeso꞉ a꞉na helebesiya꞉ sana sowo꞉.
Ma꞉n moso dowo꞉fa꞉lo꞉ na꞉sen ho꞉len a꞉no꞉ fa꞉la꞉dowabikiyo꞉, Helo꞉d elo꞉ dimido꞉ a꞉no꞉ Yu kalu iyo꞉ da꞉da꞉ki sagaolo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉, Helo꞉d sagalab a꞉no꞉ eyo꞉ ba꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, Bida elo꞉ a꞉na ta꞉li.
Bida e ta꞉lia꞉sa꞉ga꞉, dibolo aya to꞉lo alita꞉ga꞉yo꞉, e bo꞉fo꞉melea꞉ki, da꞉la꞉di kalu do꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ do꞉go꞉fela꞉fo꞉ da꞉fea꞉sa꞉ga꞉, kalu fa꞉la꞉da꞉in fa꞉la꞉da꞉in yasilima꞉ ya꞉melea꞉ki, aloba꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉ ta꞉fo꞉. Tinio꞉ Asulo꞉ Ma꞉no꞉lo꞉ ma꞉no꞉ ho꞉len a꞉no꞉ edabikiyo꞉, Helo꞉da꞉yo꞉ Bida e a꞉na sili alitaki, kaluka꞉isale siwa꞉la mo꞉walilima꞉no꞉ asulo꞉.
A꞉la꞉go꞉ko꞉lo꞉ Bida e dibolo aya ta꞉li sabiki, tilidabu kaluka꞉isale iyo꞉ aya silikiyo꞉, Bidayo꞉ mada asuwa꞉foma꞉ki, Godemo꞉ halaido꞉ dulugu sa꞉la꞉li sen.
Bidayo꞉ mo꞉walilima꞉no꞉ ho꞉leno꞉ o꞉fa꞉la꞉doma꞉nigabikiyo꞉, nulu a꞉namio꞉ e dibolo aya ali. E sa꞉ni a꞉la꞉ya꞉ galolo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ da꞉la꞉di kalu a꞉la꞉ma꞉ alaba delen a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ nolo꞉ toga yasisen.
Wigibole a꞉naka, Alana꞉ ene ma꞉mul kaluwo꞉ Bidalo꞉wa handalowo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉, dibolo a us a꞉no꞉ ho꞉lena꞉ ho꞉lelia꞉ difa꞉. Ma꞉mul kaluwa꞉yo꞉ Bidaya꞉ o꞉fo꞉fa besega꞉takiyo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Ge bo꞉bo꞉ge dasima.” A꞉la꞉sa꞉labikiyo꞉, sa꞉ni ko꞉lo꞉ Bidaya꞉ dagi amilo꞉ galolo꞉ a꞉no꞉ ene asulo꞉ka a꞉duali.
A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ ma꞉mula꞉ kaluwa꞉yo꞉ emo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Ge go꞉no꞉n yafuwo꞉ ba꞉la꞉sa꞉ga꞉, butiyo꞉ sa꞉ga꞉lema.” A꞉la꞉sa꞉labiki Bidayo꞉ a꞉la꞉dimida꞉sa꞉ga꞉, ma꞉mula꞉ kaluwa꞉yo꞉ wa꞉ka a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Hido꞉ so꞉go꞉ sa꞉ga꞉la꞉sa꞉ga꞉, ne kudu mena” a꞉la꞉sio꞉.
Bida e ma꞉mula꞉ kalu ha꞉nab aumb kudu ha꞉naki, dibolo ayo꞉ ta꞉ta꞉ga꞉ handalowo꞉. Ko꞉sega eyo꞉ ma꞉mula꞉ kaluwa꞉lo꞉ dimido꞉ a꞉no꞉ hendele gab a꞉la꞉bo꞉, e mo꞉dinafa asulakiyo꞉, ofogabele a꞉la꞉asulo꞉.
A꞉la꞉yo꞉ ha꞉nakiyo꞉, da꞉la꞉diya꞉lo꞉ bo꞉fo꞉len agelo꞉ tinio꞉, a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ andebo꞉lo꞉ tininita꞉ga꞉, tog go꞉fo꞉ kiya꞉lo꞉ amisa꞉n amilo꞉ ha꞉na꞉sen ko꞉lo꞉ ifa꞉ a꞉na fa꞉la꞉dowabikiyo꞉, tog a꞉no꞉ ene asulo꞉ kolaitabiki, a꞉la꞉yo꞉ tog a꞉naka handalota꞉ga꞉, ida꞉ni ka ha꞉na꞉ga꞉, to so꞉go꞉fa fa꞉la꞉dowakiyo꞉, ma꞉mul kaluwo꞉ a꞉na kelege dowo꞉.
Ma꞉mul kalu e kelege dowabikiyo꞉, Bida eyamilo꞉ dimido꞉ a꞉no꞉ asulakiyo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Dimido꞉ we mada hendelo꞉b a꞉la꞉ asulo꞉l. Helo꞉da꞉ ene halaido꞉ Yu kaluwa꞉yo꞉lo꞉ nemo꞉lo꞉ dimidama꞉no꞉ a꞉no꞉lo꞉ kata꞉foma꞉ki, Alana꞉ ene ma꞉mula꞉ kaluwo꞉ nelo꞉wa iliga꞉fo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ eyo꞉ ne sili alifa꞉.”
Bidayo꞉ a꞉no꞉ asula꞉sa꞉ga꞉, kaluka꞉isalelo꞉ kegean a a꞉na ane. Iyo꞉ Yon Maga꞉ ene ano Maliaya꞉ aya kegenefo꞉liki, Godemo꞉ dulugu sa꞉la꞉lab ko꞉lo꞉ Bida e a꞉na ane.
Bidayo꞉ ha꞉na꞉ga꞉, ha꞉la꞉ amilo꞉ tog ifa꞉ a꞉no꞉ godogodolabiki, nanog dian ga, Loda, e da꞉da꞉ga꞉, tog a꞉no꞉ e kolama꞉ni ane.
Loda eyo꞉ Bidaya꞉ daganko꞉ da꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, e sagalo꞉wo꞉ alan dowaki, tog kolama꞉no꞉wo꞉ babalela꞉sa꞉ga꞉, e a꞉ma꞉la꞉ aya ha꞉na꞉sa꞉ga꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Bida e ha꞉la꞉ka o꞉lab.”
A꞉la꞉sa꞉labikiyo꞉, iliyo꞉ emo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Ge no꞉nolai sa꞉lab!” Ko꞉sega eyo꞉ to a꞉no꞉ hendele wa꞉ka halale a꞉sa꞉labikiyo꞉, iliyo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Ko, Bidaya꞉ ene ma꞉mula꞉ kalu ko꞉lo꞉ mio꞉wele?” a꞉la꞉sio꞉.
Iyo꞉ a꞉la꞉ nenelelabikiyo꞉, Bida eyo꞉ tog ifa꞉ a꞉no꞉ godogodo a꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉labiki, iliyo꞉ togo꞉ a꞉na koda꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Bida e ko꞉lo꞉ ba꞉dakiyo꞉ iligi sagalo꞉.
Bida eyo꞉ iyo꞉ ha꞉sa mesea꞉ki, dagiya꞉ da꞉fea꞉sa꞉ga꞉ hela꞉tabiki, Alana꞉lo꞉ e ko꞉lo꞉ dibolo aya a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉lo꞉ sili alifa꞉ a꞉no꞉ imo꞉wo꞉ malolo꞉ me. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉yo꞉ imo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “To we Yemes o꞉lia꞉ tilidabu kalu nol o꞉lia꞉mo꞉wo꞉ malolo꞉ mia꞉bi.” A꞉la꞉sa꞉la꞉sa꞉ga꞉, e hen nowa ane.
A꞉la꞉dimido꞉ ko꞉lo꞉, kea꞉fowo꞉ da꞉la꞉di kalu iliyo꞉ Bida e waga kelege dowo꞉wele a꞉la꞉liki, iyo꞉ kele asulaki, mada babale dowo꞉.
Helo꞉da꞉ ene nanog dian kaluwo꞉ Bidayo꞉ kelema꞉ni hamana꞉ki sio꞉ ko꞉sega, iliyo꞉ mo꞉galili ko꞉lo꞉, Helo꞉d eyo꞉ da꞉la꞉di kalu Bidalo꞉ bo꞉fo꞉len o꞉mo꞉wo꞉ wa꞉ka dabu ba꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉, iyo꞉ yasala꞉ma꞉no꞉ saefa꞉. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ Helo꞉d e Yudia hena ta꞉ta꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Sesalia amisa꞉na mesa꞉ni ane.
Helo꞉d eyo꞉ Taya kaluka꞉isale o꞉lia꞉ Saido꞉n kaluka꞉isale o꞉lia꞉mo꞉wo꞉ gadio꞉ alan dowa꞉sen. Ko꞉sega ili ma꞉no꞉wo꞉ Helo꞉da꞉ hena a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ dia꞉sen ko꞉lo꞉ Helo꞉d o꞉lia꞉ giso꞉ mo꞉dia꞉li mesa꞉no꞉ a꞉la꞉asulaki, iyo꞉ kegea꞉sa꞉ga꞉ Helo꞉d o꞉lia꞉ nenelema꞉no꞉ a꞉la꞉liki togo꞉ kedo꞉. A꞉la꞉go꞉ko꞉lo꞉ Balastus e Helo꞉da꞉ ene nanog dian kalu digalo꞉le nowo꞉ e ko꞉lo꞉ e i o꞉lia꞉ ko꞉le nenela꞉la꞉ga꞉, e o꞉lia꞉yo꞉ asugo꞉ imilise dowabiki, iyo꞉ asuwa꞉fa꞉no꞉ a꞉la꞉li saefa꞉.
Tolo꞉ nenelema꞉no꞉lo꞉ saefa꞉ ho꞉len a꞉namio꞉, Helo꞉d e misa꞉ kaluwa꞉ so꞉go꞉ ka꞉la꞉sa꞉ga꞉, i fofodo꞉ nafa a꞉na asifo꞉liki, kalu kegeo꞉ o꞉mo꞉wo꞉ towo꞉ halaido꞉ sio꞉.
To sa꞉lab a꞉no꞉ da꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, e sagalema꞉kiyo꞉, iliyo꞉ halale sa꞉la꞉likiyo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “To elo꞉ sa꞉lab ko꞉, kaluwa꞉ mego꞉fa꞉ sa꞉labaka꞉yo꞉, to elo꞉ a꞉ma꞉yo꞉ godeya꞉lo꞉ sa꞉lan aumgab.”
A꞉la꞉sa꞉labiki, Helo꞉d e Godeya꞉ wiyo꞉ mo꞉dulugu sa꞉labiki, wigibole a꞉naka Godeya꞉ ma꞉mula꞉ kaluwa꞉yo꞉ e walaf mogago꞉ dima꞉ki golo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ e fesa꞉ na꞉i ha꞉na꞉la꞉ga꞉ sowo꞉.
Ko꞉sega ho꞉len a꞉namio꞉ Godeya꞉ towo꞉ halaido꞉ fa꞉la꞉dowaki, kaluka꞉isaleyo꞉ asulo꞉wo꞉ modo꞉ nodola꞉i ane.
Banabas o꞉lia꞉ So꞉l o꞉lia꞉yo꞉ Ya꞉lusalemdo꞉ nanog dia꞉leno꞉ ililita꞉ga꞉yo꞉, Antio꞉go꞉ a꞉ma꞉la꞉ ha꞉nakiyo꞉, Yon Mag o꞉lia꞉ tililia꞉gane.
Antio꞉g sa꞉s a꞉namio꞉, dinali sa꞉lan kalu nol o꞉lia꞉ a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ widan kalu nol o꞉lia꞉yo꞉ a꞉na elen. Kalu i a꞉no꞉ nowo꞉ wiyo꞉ Banabas, nowo꞉ Simeon ene wiyo꞉ nowo꞉ Nigel, nowo꞉ Lusius e Salini kalu, nowo꞉ So꞉l, nowo꞉ Manain e so꞉wa silikiyo꞉, gamani misa꞉ Helo꞉d o꞉lia꞉ anayo꞉.
Iyo꞉ ma꞉no꞉lo꞉ mo꞉nakiyo꞉, Godemo꞉ dulugu sa꞉la꞉len amio꞉, Godeya꞉ Mamaya꞉yo꞉ imo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Banabas dia꞉ So꞉l dia꞉ we, ni nanog dima꞉ki da꞉feyo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ giliyo꞉lo꞉ a꞉la꞉yo꞉ tililia꞉ga꞉ da꞉fema.”
Mamaya꞉ a꞉la꞉saefa꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ iliyo꞉ ma꞉no꞉wo꞉ mo꞉naki, Godemo꞉ dulugu sa꞉la꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, ili dagiyo꞉ a꞉la꞉ma꞉ wa꞉la dia꞉ta꞉sa꞉ga꞉, a꞉la꞉yo꞉ a꞉na iliga꞉fo꞉.
A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ Banabas dia꞉ So꞉l dia꞉ a꞉no꞉, Godeya꞉ Mamaya꞉ iliga꞉tabiki, a꞉la꞉yo꞉ Selusia amisa꞉n a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉yo꞉ ho꞉n ko꞉suwa disa꞉la꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Saibulus ho꞉na꞉lo꞉ hegefa꞉ hen a꞉na ane.
Yon Mago꞉ a꞉la꞉yo꞉ asuwa꞉foma꞉ki, egele ha꞉na꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Salamis amisa꞉na fa꞉la꞉dowakiyo꞉, Godeya꞉ mano꞉ Yu kaluwa꞉lo꞉ tolo꞉ wida꞉sen a a꞉na wida꞉li sia꞉len.
Iyo꞉ hen ho꞉na꞉lo꞉ hegefa꞉ us a꞉na sia꞉la꞉ga꞉, Bafos amisa꞉n a꞉na fa꞉la꞉dowo꞉ amio꞉, Yu amilo꞉ madalilo꞉ dinali sa꞉lan kalu nowo꞉ Ba-Ya꞉su e a꞉na galili.
