E madalilo꞉ fo꞉falo꞉ dimida꞉seno꞉ e ko꞉lo꞉ Gilig to amio꞉, kalu a꞉no꞉ Elimas a꞉la꞉wikilo꞉, mo꞉wo꞉ Gilig to amilo꞉ Elimas a꞉la꞉do꞉ sa꞉lab a꞉ma꞉ ha꞉go꞉, fo꞉falo꞉ dimidan kalu. Hen a꞉namilo꞉ gamani misa꞉ kalu, Segius Bauluso꞉, e asulo꞉ di kalu ko꞉lo꞉ e Godeya꞉ towo꞉ da꞉ba꞉no꞉ asulabiki, Banabas o꞉lia꞉ So꞉l o꞉lia꞉yo꞉ elo꞉wa walama꞉ mena꞉ki saga꞉fo꞉. Ko꞉sega fo꞉falo꞉ dimida꞉sen kalu a꞉ma꞉yo꞉, e mili ko꞉lo꞉, Banabas dia꞉ So꞉l dia꞉mo꞉wo꞉ gis dowaki, misa꞉ kaluwo꞉ asugo꞉ mo꞉nodoma꞉ki, man walama꞉no꞉wo꞉, e ko꞉lo꞉.
<range>
<range>
A꞉la꞉go꞉ko꞉lo꞉ So꞉l, e wiyo꞉ nowo꞉ Fol, Godeya꞉ Mamayo꞉ e amio꞉ wa꞉lifo꞉liki, Elimas eko꞉ sikudu bo꞉fo꞉liki towo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉,
“Ge mada Seteneya꞉ inso꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ man digalo꞉ o꞉lia꞉lo꞉ gisdo꞉ dowa꞉seno꞉ ge. Ge madalilo꞉ dikili sa꞉lan man ko꞉li ko꞉lilo꞉ a꞉no꞉ asulo꞉wa wa꞉lifo꞉liki, Godeya꞉ to nafa digalo꞉ sa꞉lab a꞉no꞉ ge da꞉la꞉li sa꞉la꞉sen.
A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ Gode halaido꞉wa꞉yo꞉ ge sa꞉daliki, gi siyo꞉ kon dowaki, ofo꞉ gelo꞉ mo꞉ba꞉ba꞉ ka a꞉la꞉ga꞉, ho꞉len nolo꞉ o꞉doma꞉ib” a꞉la꞉sio꞉. Wigibole a꞉naka, Elimasa꞉ siyo꞉ funa꞉laki sololiabiki, eyo꞉ kalu nolo꞉ e gasilia꞉ hamana꞉ki, keda꞉i ane.
A꞉la꞉gabiki, misa꞉ kalu a꞉ma꞉yo꞉ dimido꞉ fa꞉la꞉dowab a꞉no꞉ ba꞉da꞉ga꞉, e Godeyo꞉ tilidabu. Mo꞉wo꞉ Alana꞉ to man ko꞉lo꞉ widab a꞉namio꞉ e mada alan iligo꞉.
Fol o꞉lia꞉ kalu a꞉la꞉ e o꞉lia꞉lo꞉ mio꞉ a꞉no꞉, Bafos amisa꞉no꞉ ta꞉ta꞉ga꞉, ho꞉n ko꞉suwa disa꞉la꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Bafilia hena ha꞉na꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Bega amisa꞉na fa꞉la꞉dowo꞉. Amisa꞉n a꞉na dota꞉ga꞉yo꞉, Yon Mago꞉ a꞉la꞉yo꞉ ta꞉ta꞉ga꞉, a꞉ma꞉la꞉ Ya꞉lusalem ane.
Kalu a꞉la꞉yo꞉ Bega ta꞉ta꞉ga꞉ aneyo꞉, Bisidia hen amio꞉ Antio꞉g amisa꞉n a꞉na fa꞉la꞉dowa꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Ha꞉fo꞉lo꞉ Dowan ho꞉leno꞉ dowabiki, Yu kaluwa꞉lo꞉ tolo꞉ wida꞉sen aya tina꞉ga꞉ sen.
Kalu noma꞉yo꞉ Mosesa꞉ ele sa꞉sa꞉lo꞉ o꞉lia꞉ dinali sa꞉lana꞉ to sa꞉sa꞉lo꞉ a꞉no꞉lia꞉yo꞉ agela꞉ mea꞉la꞉ga꞉yo꞉, alo꞉ bo꞉fo꞉lowan kalu i a꞉ma꞉yo꞉ a꞉la꞉mo꞉wo꞉ to sagetaki, “Nai, gego꞉ to mano꞉ kaluka꞉isaleya꞉ asulo꞉ halale alitakilo꞉ sa꞉ma꞉no꞉wo꞉ da꞉labolalega, gego꞉ sa꞉ma꞉ni mena” a꞉la꞉liki saga꞉fo꞉.
Fol e dasilia꞉sa꞉ga꞉ kagayakiyo꞉, iyo꞉ ha꞉sa mesea꞉ki, dagiya꞉ da꞉fea꞉sa꞉ga꞉ hela꞉tabikiyo꞉, imo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Isolael kalu o꞉lia꞉ Yu kaluma Godelo꞉ wabuda꞉len a꞉no꞉lia꞉yo꞉ gio꞉ to we dabuma!
Isolaela꞉ Godeya꞉yo꞉ nili ma꞉mu iyo꞉ da꞉feyo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ iyo꞉ Isib a꞉na sen amio꞉ modo꞉ fa꞉la꞉doma꞉kiyo꞉ dinafa bo꞉fo꞉la꞉ga꞉yo꞉, ene halaido꞉wa꞉ Isibdo꞉ seno꞉ kata꞉ta꞉ga꞉ tililia꞉mio꞉.
A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ donayo꞉ do꞉la꞉fo꞉ fa꞉la꞉da꞉in us a꞉namio꞉, iyo꞉ kalalili hen a꞉na sia꞉len amio꞉, man mogago꞉ ililo꞉wo꞉ Godeya꞉ dia꞉likiyo꞉ ka bo꞉fo꞉len.
A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ Kenan hen a꞉na ha꞉na꞉ga꞉ fa꞉la꞉dowakiyo꞉, Godeya꞉yo꞉ hendo꞉ biso꞉ so꞉lo꞉ doma꞉la꞉fo꞉ sen a꞉no꞉ yasa danela꞉sa꞉ga꞉, hen a꞉no꞉ kaluka꞉isale enedo꞉le o꞉mo꞉ dima꞉ki dimi.
A꞉la꞉do꞉ dimida꞉leno꞉, donayo꞉ 450 a꞉la꞉fo꞉ a꞉no꞉ gulula꞉. “A꞉ma꞉ fa꞉s amio꞉, Godeya꞉yo꞉ dinafa bo꞉fo꞉mela꞉no꞉ kalu nolo꞉ imo꞉ dimia꞉li a꞉la꞉likilo꞉ mio꞉wo꞉, dinali sa꞉lan kalu Samua꞉l elo꞉ fa꞉la꞉dowo꞉wa edo꞉.
Ho꞉len a꞉namio꞉, iliyo꞉ misa꞉ kalu ilo꞉ bo꞉fo꞉mela꞉no꞉wo꞉ nowo꞉ doma꞉ki asulaki, Godemo꞉ ha꞉iyabiki, Godeya꞉yo꞉ Bensamina꞉ e ma꞉mui us a꞉namio꞉ nowo꞉ Kisa꞉ inso꞉wo꞉ So꞉lo꞉ a꞉na da꞉feyo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ elo꞉ bo꞉fo꞉leno꞉ donayo꞉ do꞉la꞉fo꞉ fa꞉la꞉da꞉in dowo꞉.
Godeya꞉yo꞉ So꞉l e dugula꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Debidi e Isolael misa꞉ kalu ta꞉fo꞉. Godeya꞉yo꞉ Debidi dia꞉no꞉ sa꞉lakiyo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, ‘Ya꞉siya꞉ so꞉wa Debidi we, ne ba꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉ da꞉feyo꞉. No꞉no꞉ ha꞉fo꞉lo꞉ disa꞉yo꞉ e dowab ko꞉lo꞉, nilo꞉ emo꞉lo꞉ dimidama꞉kilo꞉ asulab a꞉no꞉ e tambowo꞉ dimidama꞉ib’ a꞉la꞉sio꞉.
“A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ kalu wema꞉ e ma꞉mu iya a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉yo꞉ Isolaeldo꞉ a꞉ma꞉la꞉ gasilia꞉no꞉wo꞉, Godeya꞉lo꞉ dinali sio꞉ aumbo꞉, Ya꞉suwo꞉ a꞉na fa꞉la꞉dowo꞉.
Ya꞉suwo꞉ o꞉semo꞉fa꞉la꞉dowo꞉ amio꞉, Yon eyo꞉ Isolael kaluka꞉isaleyo꞉ asugo꞉ nodola꞉sa꞉ga꞉, ho꞉na to꞉loma꞉nikiyo꞉, iyo꞉ tambomo꞉wo꞉ man a꞉na wida꞉len.
Yona꞉lo꞉ nanog dia꞉leno꞉ elema꞉nikiyo꞉, eyo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, ‘Giliyo꞉ ne o꞉b a꞉la꞉asulaya? Ne gililo꞉ yasila꞉len o꞉ma. E ni fa꞉sa mia꞉ib. Niyo꞉ e budi sa꞉ga꞉lo꞉ amilo꞉ me ko꞉lo꞉ melealifa꞉ a꞉no꞉ ne fagela꞉ma꞉no꞉wo꞉ mo꞉lido꞉’ a꞉la꞉sio꞉.
“Nao i, A꞉bla꞉hama꞉ ema꞉mu i o꞉lia꞉ Yu kaluma Godelo꞉ wabuda꞉len o꞉lia꞉yo꞉, gio꞉ tambo dabuma. Nilo꞉ a꞉ma꞉la꞉lo꞉ gasili to nafa a꞉no꞉ Godeya꞉yo꞉ nimo꞉wo꞉ sama꞉ki, nilo꞉wa iliga꞉fo꞉.
Ya꞉luselam kaluka꞉isale o꞉lia꞉ ene misa꞉ kalu o꞉lia꞉yo꞉ Ya꞉su e a꞉ma꞉la꞉do꞉ gasilia꞉no꞉ kalulo꞉b a꞉la꞉bo꞉ mo꞉fanda asulo꞉. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ iliyo꞉ Ha꞉fo꞉lo꞉ Dowan ho꞉len tambo a꞉namio꞉, dinali sa꞉lan kaluwa꞉lo꞉ to sa꞉sa꞉lo꞉ a꞉no꞉ agela꞉likiyo꞉, to a꞉ma꞉ ha꞉go꞉lo꞉ mo꞉dinafa asulo꞉. Ko꞉sega Yu iliyo꞉ Ya꞉su e sana sowo꞉ a꞉namio꞉, dinali sa꞉lan kaluwa꞉lo꞉ to sa꞉sa꞉lo꞉ a꞉no꞉ a꞉na ilili alifa꞉.
Iliyo꞉ Ya꞉suwa꞉lo꞉ mogago꞉ dimido꞉ kudu sa꞉lakilo꞉ sa꞉ma꞉no꞉wo꞉ nowo꞉ mo꞉ba꞉ba꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ iliyo꞉ Bailat eyo꞉ e sana soma꞉ki, susio꞉.
Iliyo꞉ Godeya꞉ to sa꞉sa꞉lo꞉ aumbo꞉ dimida sa꞉ndala꞉sa꞉ga꞉, iliyo꞉ i malana amilo꞉ dehedo꞉ a꞉no꞉ tagalia꞉sa꞉ga꞉, u no꞉no꞉lo꞉wa dia꞉gane.
E sowo꞉ ko꞉sega, Godeya꞉yo꞉ e a꞉ma꞉la꞉ dasi alifa꞉.
A꞉la꞉dimidabikiyo꞉, kaluka꞉isale e o꞉lia꞉lo꞉ tamin amilo꞉ Ga꞉lili a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉lo꞉ Ya꞉lusalem amilo꞉ sia꞉lowan a꞉ma꞉yo꞉, Ya꞉suwo꞉ ho꞉len nolo꞉ galilia꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉ ba꞉da꞉len. A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ kaluka꞉isale i a꞉ma꞉yo꞉ inin siya꞉ ba꞉ba꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ o꞉go꞉ iliyo꞉ Isolael kaluka꞉isalemo꞉wo꞉ wida꞉lab.
“Godeya꞉yo꞉ nili ma꞉mu imo꞉lo꞉ tamin amilo꞉ dinali sio꞉ a꞉no꞉, o꞉go꞉ inin ma꞉mu i nimo꞉wo꞉ ililialitakiyo꞉, Ya꞉suwo꞉ dasi alifa꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ na꞉no꞉ man nafa we gimo꞉wo꞉ wido꞉l. Gisalo꞉ bugo꞉, heb andeb a꞉namio꞉ a꞉la꞉sa꞉sa꞉lo꞉, “‘Ge na꞉ so꞉wa ko꞉lo꞉, ni o꞉go꞉ gi go꞉l dowab’ a꞉la꞉sa꞉sa꞉lo꞉.
<range>
Ya꞉suwo꞉ sowa꞉sa꞉ga꞉ a꞉labiki, Godeya꞉yo꞉ e a꞉ma꞉la꞉ dasi alifa꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ tif amio꞉ e do꞉mo꞉wo꞉ mada mo꞉hesema꞉ib. A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ Godeya꞉yo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, ‘Niyo꞉ Debidimo꞉lo꞉ dinali sio꞉ a꞉no꞉ gimo꞉ dimiakiyo꞉, gio꞉ nafa halaido꞉ mesea꞉ki sa꞉ma꞉nigo꞉l.’
A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ Gisalo꞉ sa꞉sa꞉lo꞉ no amio꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, ‘Giyo꞉ go꞉no꞉n da꞉feyo꞉ kalu a꞉no꞉ o꞉ido꞉ amio꞉ mo꞉hesema꞉ki ta꞉fa꞉no꞉’ a꞉la꞉sio꞉.
“Debidi e Godeya꞉lo꞉ to saefa꞉ a꞉no꞉ kudu ha꞉na꞉la꞉ga꞉ sowabiki, e ma꞉mu ilo꞉ dane anelo꞉ o꞉ido꞉ aniba o꞉ido꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ elo꞉ a꞉na hese ane.
Ko꞉sega sowo꞉ kalu ko꞉lo꞉ Godeya꞉lo꞉ o꞉ido꞉ amilo꞉ dasi alifa꞉ a꞉no꞉ ene do꞉mo꞉wo꞉ mo꞉hese ane.
“A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ ni nao i, na꞉no꞉ to we gimo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉ wido꞉l. Ya꞉su we nili mogago꞉ dila꞉ma꞉niki mio꞉ a꞉la꞉ asuluma.
Ya꞉su wema꞉yo꞉ kaluka꞉isale abeyo꞉ eya tilida꞉dab a꞉no꞉, ili mogago꞉wo꞉ dila꞉sa꞉ga꞉, digalo꞉ kaluka꞉isale wikilaki ga꞉li ta꞉fa꞉ib. Mosesa꞉ ele saefa꞉ a꞉ma꞉yo꞉ a꞉la꞉bo꞉ mada mo꞉dimidan ko꞉sega kalu wema꞉yo꞉ dimido꞉.
Gio꞉ dinali sa꞉lan kaluwa꞉lo꞉ bugo꞉ amilo꞉ tamina hagugo꞉ sa꞉sa꞉lo꞉ we, gi amio꞉ fa꞉la꞉dowabena꞉ki, dinafa dowa꞉bi.
Dinali sa꞉lan kaluwa꞉yo꞉ Godeya꞉ towo꞉ dia꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉ a꞉la꞉sa꞉sa꞉lo꞉, “‘Dabuma! Gio꞉ Ni man sa꞉labo꞉ mogagi dio꞉ge sa꞉labdo꞉ a꞉no꞉ gio꞉ molo asula꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉ soma꞉ib. Mo꞉wo꞉ o꞉g ho꞉len gilo꞉ sab wenamio꞉, niyo꞉ nanog ko꞉li dimida꞉ma꞉no꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ kalu nolba꞉yo꞉ gemo꞉wo꞉ malolo꞉ mealega, giyo꞉ to a꞉no꞉ mo꞉ tilida꞉babe.’” Fol eyo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉.
Fol dia꞉ Banabas dia꞉yo꞉ towo꞉ sa꞉la꞉sa꞉ga꞉ ha꞉na꞉nigab amio꞉, kalu kegeo꞉ a꞉ma꞉yo꞉, a꞉la꞉yo꞉ Ha꞉fo꞉lo꞉ Dowan ho꞉len no amio꞉ tamin amilo꞉ man wido꞉ a꞉no꞉ wa꞉ka walama꞉ki, dabu ba꞉ba꞉.
Fol dia꞉ Banabas dia꞉yo꞉ tolo꞉ wida꞉sen aya ta꞉ta꞉ga꞉ ha꞉nakiyo꞉, Yu kaluka꞉isale o꞉lia꞉ Yu kaluma Godelo꞉ wabuda꞉len a꞉no꞉lia꞉ egele tola꞉i ha꞉nakiyo꞉, imo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Godeya꞉yo꞉ asuwa꞉fa꞉ib ko꞉lo꞉ gio꞉ E ko꞉lo꞉ dinafa kudu ha꞉na꞉bi” a꞉la꞉sio꞉.
Ha꞉fo꞉lo꞉ Dowan ho꞉len nowo꞉ fa꞉la꞉dowabikiyo꞉, amisa꞉n kaluka꞉isale nolo꞉ tambo Alana꞉ to man a꞉no꞉ da꞉ba꞉no꞉ a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ kegeo꞉
A꞉la꞉gabikiyo꞉, Yu kaluwa꞉yo꞉ kegeo꞉ a꞉no꞉ ba꞉da꞉ga꞉, a꞉la꞉mo꞉wo꞉ kulufa꞉yaki, Fol elo꞉ to widab a꞉no꞉ madali dikili sa꞉lab a꞉la꞉likiyo꞉, a꞉la꞉mo꞉wo꞉ dio꞉ge sio꞉.
Ko꞉sega Fol dia꞉ Banabas dia꞉yo꞉ a꞉ma꞉la꞉bo꞉ halale a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Na꞉no꞉ Yu kalu gimo꞉wo꞉ Godeya꞉ to mano꞉ gi ko꞉le wido꞉ a꞉la꞉bo꞉ Godeya꞉ sio꞉, ko꞉sega gio꞉ to a꞉no꞉ gola ba꞉dakiyo꞉, mela꞉no꞉ mela꞉no꞉ a꞉no꞉ giliyo꞉ dio꞉l a꞉la꞉bo꞉ mo꞉egab a꞉la꞉sulo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ na꞉no꞉ o꞉go꞉ Yu kaluka꞉isalema o꞉lo꞉wa ha꞉na꞉sa꞉ga꞉ walama꞉no꞉.
Mo꞉wo꞉ we, Alana꞉yo꞉ nenbo꞉wo꞉ saitakiyo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, ‘Niyo꞉ gego꞉ Yu kaluka꞉isalema usa ilikiyo꞉, ho꞉len o꞉ngo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ dimio꞉l. Niyo꞉ henfelo꞉ kaluka꞉isaleyo꞉ tambo a꞉ma꞉la꞉ gasilima꞉kiyo꞉, gi henfelo꞉ amio꞉ towo꞉ dia꞉ha꞉na꞉ga꞉ sa꞉la꞉mela꞉ib.’”
Yu kaluka꞉isalema iliyo꞉ to a꞉no꞉ da꞉da꞉la꞉ga꞉ sagalakiyo꞉, a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Godeya꞉ to we mada nafale” a꞉la꞉sa꞉la꞉liki, kaluka꞉isale tambo mela꞉no꞉lo꞉ dima꞉kilo꞉ da꞉feyo꞉ a꞉ma꞉yo꞉, Alano꞉ tilida꞉du.
A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ Alana꞉ to man wido꞉ a꞉no꞉ amisa꞉na a꞉namilo꞉ kandayo꞉ a꞉no꞉ tambo da꞉da꞉i ha꞉na꞉la꞉ga꞉ ililila꞉.
Ko꞉sega Yu kalu iliyo꞉ misa꞉ ka꞉isale Yuwa꞉ mando꞉ kudu ha꞉na꞉sen i o꞉lia꞉ amisa꞉n ko꞉go꞉do꞉ kalu o꞉lia꞉yo꞉ a꞉la꞉mo꞉wo꞉ gadima꞉ki, digene me. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ a꞉la꞉mo꞉wo꞉ hida꞉yo꞉ alan dima꞉ki, dikida꞉litabikiyo꞉, a꞉la꞉yo꞉ hen a꞉namilo꞉ eleno꞉ o꞉luso꞉no꞉.
A꞉la꞉dimidabiki, Fol dia꞉ Banabas dia꞉ma꞉yo꞉ a꞉la꞉ma꞉ gido꞉fo꞉ amilo꞉ hena꞉mu a꞉no꞉ fifi alita꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, a꞉la꞉yo꞉ Aikonium amisa꞉na ane.
A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ Antio꞉gdo꞉ tilidabu kaluka꞉isale a꞉no꞉ Godeya꞉ Mamayo꞉ i amio꞉ wa꞉lita꞉ga꞉, iyo꞉ ha꞉fo꞉ disa꞉laki sagalo꞉.
Fol dia꞉ Banabas dia꞉yo꞉ Aikonium amisa꞉n a꞉namio꞉ Yu kaluwa꞉lo꞉ tolo꞉ wida꞉sen aya tina꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Godeya꞉ to man nafayo꞉, a꞉la꞉ma꞉lo꞉ Antio꞉gdo꞉ wida꞉len o꞉leaum, halale widabiki, Yu kaluka꞉isale o꞉lia꞉ Yu kaluka꞉isalema o꞉lia꞉yo꞉ asugo꞉ modo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ nodolo꞉.
Ko꞉sega Yu kalu mo꞉tilidabu nol sen a꞉ma꞉yo꞉ Yu kaluka꞉isalema iyo꞉ tilidabu kaluka꞉isalemo꞉wo꞉ gadima꞉ki towo꞉ dimi.
A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ Fol dia꞉ Banabas dia꞉yo꞉ amisa꞉n a꞉namio꞉ ho꞉leno꞉ modo꞉ siliki, Alana꞉ wiya iliki, to mano꞉ halale wida꞉len. A꞉la꞉ma꞉lo꞉ Godeya꞉lo꞉ kanulu alifa꞉ tolo꞉ widab a꞉no꞉ nolba꞉yo꞉ hendelelo꞉b a꞉la꞉bo꞉ba꞉kiyo꞉, Alana꞉yo꞉ a꞉la꞉mo꞉wo꞉ halaido꞉wo꞉ dimiabiki, a꞉la꞉ma꞉yo꞉ molo ha꞉na꞉no꞉wo꞉ ko꞉li ko꞉lilo꞉ dimido꞉.
Amisa꞉n kaluka꞉isale a꞉namilo꞉ seno꞉ usa aloba꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉, nolo꞉ Yu kalu o꞉lia꞉ dowaki, nolo꞉ iliga꞉felan kalu a꞉la꞉ a꞉no꞉lia꞉ dowo꞉.
A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ Yu kalu nol o꞉lia꞉ Yu kaluma nol o꞉lia꞉ a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ ini misa꞉ kalu o꞉lia꞉yo꞉ kegenefo꞉liki nenelo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉, iliyo꞉ Fol dia꞉ Banabas dia꞉yo꞉ hida꞉yo꞉ ko꞉li ko꞉lilo꞉ dimia꞉no꞉ a꞉laki, uwa꞉ agoda꞉sa꞉ga꞉ sana soma꞉no꞉ saefa꞉.
Ko꞉sega ililo꞉ dimidama꞉nigab a꞉no꞉ a꞉la꞉ma꞉yo꞉ da꞉da꞉ga꞉, a꞉la꞉yo꞉ Likonia hen a꞉na nai ane. A꞉na sia꞉likiyo꞉, a꞉la꞉yo꞉ to nafayo꞉ Lista amisa꞉n o꞉lia꞉ Debe amisa꞉n a꞉na wida꞉li ha꞉nakiyo꞉, amisa꞉n anibamilo꞉ kandayo꞉ a꞉no꞉lo꞉ wida꞉li sia꞉len.
<range>
Lista amisa꞉n a꞉namio꞉, kalu imilig nowo꞉, anowa꞉ e sa꞉la꞉liakiyo꞉ gib a꞉la꞉yo꞉ mogago꞉ o꞉ngo꞉ ka sa꞉la꞉li ko꞉lo꞉ kalu a꞉no꞉ eneno꞉ mada mo꞉sia꞉lowan.
Kalu a꞉no꞉ Fol elo꞉ Godeya꞉ to man widab a꞉no꞉ dinafa da꞉dabiki, Fol eyo꞉ e sikudu ba꞉da꞉ga꞉, kalu e amio꞉ tilidabuwo꞉ alabo꞉lo꞉b a꞉la꞉asula꞉sa꞉ga꞉, kalu o꞉mo꞉wo꞉ ogolo ho꞉le sa꞉laki, “Ge dasi kagama!” A꞉la꞉sa꞉labiki kalu giliga꞉sen a꞉no꞉ tiyabala꞉sa꞉ga꞉, sia꞉len.
<range>
Kalu kegeo꞉ a꞉ma꞉yo꞉ Fol elo꞉ dimidab a꞉no꞉ ba꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Likonia to egele nenelaki sagalaki ho꞉le sio꞉, “Gode a꞉la꞉ nowo꞉, kalu do꞉mo꞉le fa꞉la꞉dota꞉ga꞉, nilo꞉ us wena mio꞉ ko꞉lo꞉lab!” a꞉la꞉sio꞉.
A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ iliyo꞉ Banabaso꞉ “Sus” wikilo꞉ a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ Fol e towo꞉ wala sa꞉lab ko꞉lo꞉ e “Ha꞉mis” wikilo꞉.
Sus gulugulula꞉sen a a꞉no꞉, amisa꞉n a꞉no꞉ ilif tolo꞉ ha꞉la꞉ya elen ko꞉lo꞉ Sus godemo꞉lo꞉ bobalo꞉ so꞉mia꞉sen kalu a꞉ma꞉yo꞉, kao de o꞉lia꞉ mamo o꞉lia꞉yo꞉ dia꞉ya꞉ga꞉, amisa꞉n toga difa꞉. Mo꞉wo꞉ iliyo꞉ Fol dia꞉ Banabas dia꞉ma꞉ wi wabudaki, somia꞉no꞉ asulaki go꞉.
Ko꞉sega Fol dia꞉ Banabas dia꞉yo꞉ ililo꞉ dimidama꞉nigab a꞉no꞉ da꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉, iliyo꞉ ka ta꞉foma꞉kiyo꞉, a꞉la꞉ma꞉yo꞉ so꞉g ko꞉lo꞉ a꞉no꞉ bidila꞉sa꞉ga꞉, kalu kegeo꞉lab us a꞉na nai ha꞉na꞉ga꞉, a꞉na halale sio꞉,
“Kaluka꞉isale gililo꞉ dimidab we, waga asulabiki dimidaya? Na꞉no꞉lo꞉ henfelo꞉ kalule, ge o꞉ngo꞉ mio꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ gililo꞉ madali godemo꞉lo꞉ duluda꞉lab a꞉no꞉ kata꞉ta꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Gode mela꞉no꞉lo꞉ a꞉lab a꞉no꞉, Hebeneyo꞉lo꞉, henfelo꞉wo꞉lo꞉, so꞉lu ho꞉no꞉ o꞉lia꞉ kelego꞉ a꞉namio꞉lo꞉ da꞉labdo꞉ dimido꞉ a꞉no꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ duluguma꞉ki, walama꞉ni mio꞉.
Taminde amio꞉, Godeya꞉yo꞉ kaluka꞉isaleyo꞉ ini man mogago꞉ dimida꞉melea꞉ki ta꞉fo꞉.
Ko꞉sega kaluka꞉isaleyo꞉ e hendele alabo꞉lo꞉b a꞉la꞉bo꞉ asuluma꞉kiyo꞉, eyo꞉ man nafale dimida꞉len. Eyo꞉ ho꞉no꞉ timina꞉ki dimia꞉sen a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ egelo꞉ amio꞉ fowo꞉ ho꞉len enedo꞉leya helema꞉ki dimia꞉sen. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ giliyo꞉ dia꞉sa꞉ga꞉ nab amio꞉, gio꞉ sagalo꞉wo꞉ alan doma꞉ki ta꞉fo꞉len.” Fol eyo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉.
To a꞉no꞉ imo꞉wo꞉ sio꞉ ko꞉sega kaluka꞉isale iliyo꞉ boba somia꞉no꞉ a꞉no꞉ mo꞉ta꞉fa꞉no꞉, dimidama꞉no꞉le asulabiki, imo꞉wo꞉ mo꞉dimidama꞉ki, a꞉la꞉ma꞉yo꞉ towo꞉ halaido꞉ sa꞉la꞉i ha꞉nabi, iliyo꞉ mo꞉dimido꞉.
Tif amio꞉, Yu kalu Aikoniumdo꞉ seno꞉ a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ Antio꞉gdo꞉ seno꞉ ya꞉sia꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Lista a꞉na fa꞉la꞉dota꞉ga꞉yo꞉, kaluka꞉isale kegeo꞉ a꞉no꞉ digene alitabiki, iyo꞉ Fol emo꞉wo꞉ gadia꞉sa꞉ga꞉, uwa꞉ agodo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ e sowab a꞉la꞉asulaki, do꞉mo꞉wo꞉ susululia꞉ga꞉, amisa꞉n ha꞉la꞉ya sandifo꞉.
Ko꞉sega tilidabu kaluka꞉isale iyo꞉ ya꞉sa꞉ga꞉, e banagalilia꞉tabiki, Fol e a꞉ma꞉la꞉ dasilia꞉ga꞉, amisa꞉n usa a꞉ma꞉la꞉ ane. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ o꞉g a꞉no꞉ a꞉naka alita꞉ga꞉, a꞉la꞉yo꞉ amisa꞉n a꞉no꞉ ta꞉ta꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Debe amisa꞉na ha꞉na꞉ni ane.
A꞉la꞉yo꞉ ha꞉na꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Godeya꞉ to mano꞉ Debe a꞉na wido꞉ amio꞉, kaluka꞉isaleyo꞉ asugo꞉ modo꞉ nodolo꞉. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ a꞉la꞉yo꞉ a꞉ma꞉la꞉ Lista ane. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ Aikonium ane. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉yo꞉ Bisidia hena ha꞉na꞉likiyo꞉, Antio꞉g a꞉na fa꞉la꞉dowo꞉.
A꞉la꞉yo꞉ a꞉na ha꞉na꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, tilidabu kaluka꞉isale a꞉no꞉ man hendele usa tiha꞉na꞉sa꞉ga꞉, tilidabu halaido꞉wo꞉ dima꞉ki, widaki a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Nio꞉ hida꞉yo꞉ ko꞉li ko꞉lilo꞉ ko꞉le ba꞉da꞉i ha꞉na꞉la꞉ga꞉, Godeya꞉ enedo꞉ bo꞉fo꞉likilo꞉ ha꞉g amilo꞉ doma꞉no꞉wo꞉ niliyo꞉ a꞉na dia꞉no꞉” a꞉la꞉wida꞉i ane.
Amisa꞉n a꞉la꞉lo꞉ ane a꞉namio꞉, Fol dia꞉ Banabas dia꞉yo꞉ tilidabu kaluka꞉isalelo꞉ bo꞉fo꞉mela꞉no꞉wo꞉ misa꞉ kalu a꞉na da꞉fe alifa꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ Alana꞉do꞉ tilidabu kaluka꞉isale a꞉no꞉ Alana꞉yo꞉ bo꞉fo꞉melea꞉ki, ma꞉no꞉ mo꞉naki, Godemo꞉ dulugu salifa꞉.
A꞉la꞉yo꞉ Bisidia hen a꞉namio꞉ sia꞉la꞉ga꞉yo꞉, Bafilia hena fa꞉la꞉dota꞉ga꞉ ha꞉nakiyo꞉, Bega amisa꞉n a꞉na to mano꞉ wido꞉. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ a꞉la꞉yo꞉ hen a꞉na ta꞉ta꞉ga꞉yo꞉, Atalia amisa꞉na ha꞉na꞉ga꞉ fa꞉la꞉dowo꞉.
<range>
Atalia a꞉na a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉yo꞉, a꞉la꞉yo꞉ ho꞉n ko꞉suwa disa꞉la꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Antio꞉g amisa꞉na ane. Amisa꞉n a꞉no꞉ tamin amilo꞉ tilidabu kaluwa꞉lo꞉ a꞉la꞉yo꞉ mano꞉ widalikilo꞉ Godeya꞉ asuwa꞉foma꞉ki dulugu sio꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ o꞉go꞉ nanogo꞉ a꞉no꞉ edaki, hen a꞉na fa꞉la꞉dowo꞉.
A꞉la꞉yo꞉ a꞉na fa꞉la꞉dowakiyo꞉, tilidabu kaluka꞉isaleyo꞉ tambo kegea꞉sa꞉ga꞉, a꞉la꞉ma꞉ dagiya꞉lo꞉ Godeya꞉ nanog dimido꞉ a꞉no꞉ imo꞉wo꞉ malolo꞉ me. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ Godeya꞉yo꞉ Yu kaluka꞉isalemalo꞉ asugo꞉ nodola꞉sa꞉ga꞉ tilidabuma꞉ki, togo꞉ waga kodo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉liki imo꞉wo꞉ malolo꞉ me.
A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ a꞉la꞉yo꞉ tilidabu kaluka꞉isale nol i a꞉no꞉lia꞉ ho꞉leno꞉ modo꞉ ka o꞉len.
Fol dia꞉ Banabas dia꞉yo꞉ Antio꞉g a꞉na sen amio꞉, Yudia kalu nolo꞉ ya꞉sa꞉ga꞉, tilidabu kaluka꞉isale o꞉mo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉walasio꞉, “Mosesa꞉ ele saefa꞉ a꞉no꞉ mo꞉kuduha꞉naki, do꞉go꞉fo꞉ mo꞉hege gedealega, Godeya꞉yo꞉ giyo꞉ a꞉ma꞉la꞉bo꞉ mo꞉gasilia꞉ib,” a꞉la꞉liki wido꞉.
Fol dia꞉ Banabas dia꞉yo꞉ to a꞉no꞉ dabu amio꞉, mo꞉sagalabiki, egelebo꞉ towa꞉yo꞉ kega꞉la꞉ga꞉, halaido꞉ nenelo꞉. A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ sa꞉s amilo꞉ tilidabu kaluka꞉isale iyo꞉ Fol dia꞉ Banabas dia꞉yo꞉ a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ tilidabu kalu nolo꞉lo꞉ Ya꞉lusalem ha꞉na꞉ga꞉, iliga꞉felo꞉ kalu o꞉lia꞉ sa꞉sdo꞉ bo꞉fo꞉lowan kalu nol o꞉lia꞉yo꞉, hida꞉yo꞉ a꞉no꞉ dinafama꞉ hamana꞉ki, a꞉na da꞉feyo꞉.
Tilidabu kaluka꞉isale a꞉ma꞉yo꞉ iyo꞉ Ya꞉lusalem a꞉na iliga꞉tabiki ha꞉nakiyo꞉, iyo꞉ Fonisia hen o꞉lia꞉ Samalia hen o꞉lia꞉ a꞉na tinia꞉li ha꞉naki, iliyo꞉ tilidabu kaluka꞉isale nol o꞉mo꞉wo꞉ Yu kaluka꞉isalema iyo꞉ asugo꞉ ho꞉gi nodola꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Ya꞉su amilo꞉ tilidabu a꞉no꞉ imo꞉wo꞉ wida꞉li ane ko꞉lo꞉ to a꞉no꞉ da꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉ sagalo꞉ alan dowo꞉.
Iyo꞉ ha꞉na꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Ya꞉lusalem fa꞉la꞉dowabikiyo꞉, iliga꞉felo꞉ kalu o꞉lia꞉ sa꞉sdo꞉ bo꞉fo꞉lowan kalu o꞉lia꞉ sa꞉s amilo꞉ tilidabu kaluka꞉isale o꞉lia꞉ma꞉yo꞉ imo꞉wo꞉ sagaliliabiki, Godeya꞉lo꞉ a꞉la꞉ amilo꞉ a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉lo꞉ dimido꞉ a꞉no꞉ tambo Ya꞉lusalemdo꞉ senbo꞉wo꞉ malolo꞉ me.
To a꞉no꞉ da꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Fa꞉lisi amilo꞉ Ya꞉su tilidabu kalu nolo꞉ dasila꞉sa꞉ga꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Yu kaluka꞉isalema tilida꞉dab a꞉ma꞉yo꞉ Mosesa꞉ ele saefa꞉ a꞉no꞉ kudu ha꞉na꞉sa꞉ga꞉, iyo꞉ do꞉go꞉fo꞉ hege gedea꞉bi.”
A꞉la꞉sa꞉labiki, iliga꞉felo꞉ kalu o꞉lia꞉ sa꞉sdo꞉ bo꞉fo꞉lowan kalu o꞉lia꞉yo꞉ kegea꞉sa꞉ga꞉, dabu ba꞉ba꞉ a꞉no꞉ nenela꞉li sen.
Iyo꞉ nenela꞉len amio꞉, Bida e us a꞉na dasilia꞉ga꞉yo꞉ towo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Ni nao i, tamin amio꞉ Yu kaluka꞉isalema a꞉no꞉ Godeya꞉ to man nafa ko꞉lo꞉ nilo꞉ widab a꞉no꞉ da꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉ tilidabuma꞉kiyo꞉, Godeya꞉yo꞉ ni us wenamio꞉ keda꞉sa꞉ga꞉ ne a꞉na da꞉fe alifa꞉, a꞉la꞉bo꞉ gio꞉ asulo꞉.
Godeya꞉yo꞉ nili kufa꞉ uso꞉ tambo tigini ba꞉ba꞉ ko꞉lo꞉, Yu kaluka꞉isalema iyo꞉lo꞉ o꞉li tilida꞉dab a꞉la꞉bo꞉ nimo꞉wo꞉ widakiyo꞉, Mama Malilo꞉ nimo꞉lo꞉ dimi o꞉leaumbo꞉, imo꞉wo꞉lo꞉ dimi.
Godeya꞉yo꞉ ni o꞉lia꞉ i o꞉lia꞉yo꞉ imilo꞉ ba꞉dabiki, iyo꞉ Ya꞉suwa tilida꞉dab amio꞉, ililo꞉ mogago꞉wo꞉ hala꞉sa꞉ga꞉, malilo꞉ ta꞉fo꞉.
Tamin amio꞉ hida꞉yo꞉ ni o꞉lia꞉ nini ma꞉mu i o꞉lia꞉ma꞉yo꞉ dia꞉ga꞉lo꞉ ha꞉na꞉no꞉ mo꞉lilo꞉ dowo꞉ a꞉no꞉, o꞉go꞉ giliyo꞉ Yu kaluka꞉isalema ho꞉gi tilidabu a꞉ma꞉yo꞉ dia꞉ hamana꞉ki, kelena wa꞉lamilo꞉ dia꞉fa꞉nigab a꞉no꞉, mo꞉wo꞉ ha꞉? Godeya꞉lo꞉ wedima꞉ib a꞉no꞉ ge alobana ba꞉dakigaya?
Giliyo꞉ a꞉la꞉bo꞉ ga꞉so꞉bo! Nio꞉ Ya꞉su Alana tilida꞉dabikiyo꞉, Eyo꞉ nio꞉ kanulaki, a꞉ma꞉la꞉ gasili aumbo꞉, Yu kaluka꞉isalema iyo꞉lo꞉ a꞉ma꞉la꞉ gasilia꞉ga꞉ ta꞉fo꞉.” Bida eyo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉.
Kaluka꞉isale kegeo꞉ a꞉no꞉ tambo hela꞉ta꞉ga꞉, da꞉da꞉li sabikiyo꞉, Fol dia꞉ Banabas dia꞉yo꞉, Yu kaluka꞉isalema usamio꞉ Godeya꞉lo꞉ molo ha꞉na꞉no꞉ a꞉la꞉mo꞉lo꞉ dimidama꞉kilo꞉ dimi a꞉no꞉ a꞉la꞉ma꞉yo꞉ dimido꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ imo꞉ malolo꞉ me.
A꞉la꞉ma꞉yo꞉ malola꞉la꞉ga꞉ eletabikiyo꞉, Yemes eyo꞉ a꞉ma꞉la꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Nao i, to nilo꞉ sa꞉ma꞉nigo꞉l we, gio꞉ dabuma.
Godeya꞉lo꞉ tamin amilo꞉ Yu kaluka꞉isalema imo꞉wo꞉ kanulakiyo꞉, nolo꞉ ene so꞉lo꞉le doma꞉ki da꞉feyo꞉ a꞉no꞉, Saimon Bidaya꞉yo꞉ towo꞉ tamin amilo꞉ widabo꞉ o꞉m.
Bidaya꞉ to sio꞉ a꞉no꞉lia꞉, Godeya꞉lo꞉ dinali sa꞉lan kaluwa꞉lo꞉ tamin amilo꞉ sa꞉sa꞉lo꞉ to a꞉no꞉lia꞉ imilo꞉ dowab ko꞉lo꞉ Godeya꞉ to amio꞉ a꞉la꞉sa꞉sa꞉lo꞉ da꞉lab,
“‘no꞉ dinafayaki, a ho꞉gi nafaleyo꞉ wa꞉ka a꞉dialifa꞉no꞉. Alan Niyo꞉ tamin amilo꞉ dinali sio꞉ aumbo꞉, o꞉go꞉ dimido꞉l.’”
<range>
<range>
A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ Yemes eyo꞉ wa꞉kabiyo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Ni asulo꞉ amio꞉, Yu kaluka꞉isalemalo꞉ Godemo꞉lo꞉ nodolo꞉ i o꞉mo꞉wo꞉, niliyo꞉ hida꞉yo꞉wo꞉ mo꞉dia꞉fa꞉niki.
A꞉la꞉do꞉ mo꞉dimidakiyo꞉, niliyo꞉ imo꞉wo꞉ to sa꞉sa꞉lakiyo꞉, ma꞉no꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ madali godemo꞉lo꞉ bobalo꞉ dimi a꞉no꞉ na꞉so꞉bo. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ wo꞉wo꞉ dia꞉so꞉bo. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ no꞉ ho꞉bo꞉ a꞉no꞉lia꞉, no꞉wo꞉ dagasa silisa꞉nda꞉sa꞉ga꞉, ho꞉bo꞉wo꞉ mo꞉ane a꞉no꞉lia꞉yo꞉, na꞉so꞉bo. A꞉la꞉likiyo꞉ imo꞉wo꞉ asuluma꞉kiyo꞉, mo꞉fo꞉s amio꞉ sa꞉sa꞉liga꞉fa꞉niki.
Mo꞉wo꞉ Mosesa꞉ ele saefa꞉ a꞉no꞉, ma꞉muima꞉ ma꞉lu a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ da꞉da꞉i mio꞉wo꞉, amisa꞉no꞉ tambo wida꞉la꞉ga꞉ ililitakiyo꞉, Yu kaluwa꞉lo꞉ tolo꞉ wida꞉sen a a꞉namio꞉lo꞉, Ha꞉fo꞉ Dowan ho꞉leno꞉ tambo wida꞉i mio꞉.” Yemesa꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉.
To a꞉no꞉ nenela꞉sa꞉ga꞉ saitakiyo꞉, iliga꞉felo꞉ kaluwo꞉lo꞉, sa꞉sdo꞉ bo꞉fo꞉lowan kaluwo꞉lo꞉, sa꞉s kaluka꞉isale tambo kegeo꞉ iliyo꞉, Fol dia꞉ Banabas dia꞉lo꞉ Antio꞉gdo꞉ ha꞉na꞉no꞉wo꞉, kalu nolo꞉ da꞉feyo꞉. Kalu nowo꞉ Yuda꞉s Basabas, nowo꞉ Sailas ko꞉lo꞉ kalu a꞉la꞉ we, tilidabu kaluka꞉isalelo꞉ bo꞉fo꞉lowan ko꞉lo꞉ elen.
Antio꞉g ha꞉nakiyo꞉, ililo꞉ mo꞉fo꞉s sa꞉sa꞉lo꞉ dia꞉ganeyo꞉ we. Ni iliga꞉felo꞉ kalu o꞉lia꞉ sa꞉sdo꞉ bo꞉fo꞉lowan kalu o꞉lia꞉ gi gao niliyo꞉ mada o꞉m a꞉lo꞉ to sa꞉laki, Yu kaluka꞉isalema ko꞉lo꞉ tilidabu, Antio꞉g amisa꞉ndo꞉ sabo꞉, Silia hen amilo꞉ sabo꞉, a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ Silisia hen amilo꞉ sab gimo꞉wo꞉ sagalaki, mo꞉fo꞉so꞉ a꞉na iliga꞉to꞉l.
Kalu nolo꞉ nilo꞉ wena a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ gilo꞉wa ya꞉ga꞉ wido꞉ ko꞉lo꞉, to wido꞉ a꞉ma꞉yo꞉ gio꞉ kele asulo꞉wo꞉ dima꞉kiyo꞉, no꞉nolo꞉ alifa꞉ka꞉, niyo꞉ a꞉la꞉dabu. Kalu a꞉no꞉ nili da꞉fea꞉sa꞉ga꞉ iliga꞉foma.
A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ nio꞉ kegea꞉sa꞉ga꞉, towo꞉ imilig dia꞉ta꞉ga꞉, ni o꞉lia꞉lo꞉ ha꞉fo꞉lo꞉ disa꞉ kaluwo꞉ Fol dia꞉ Banabas dia꞉yo꞉ da꞉feyo꞉. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ kalu nolo꞉ a꞉la꞉ gasa mena꞉ki da꞉fea꞉sa꞉ga꞉, gilo꞉wa iliga꞉to꞉l.
A꞉la꞉ma꞉ ene mela꞉no꞉ walema꞉no꞉wo꞉ mo꞉keleasulaki, Ya꞉su Keliso Alana꞉ nanog dimida꞉len ko꞉lo꞉ gilo꞉wa iliga꞉to꞉l.
A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ niliyo꞉ kalu a꞉la꞉ nowo꞉, Yuda꞉s dia꞉ Sailas dia꞉yo꞉, to nililo꞉ sa꞉sa꞉lo꞉l a꞉no꞉ko꞉ a꞉la꞉ma꞉yo꞉lo꞉ sama꞉ki iliga꞉to꞉l.
A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ Godeya꞉ Mamayo꞉ ni o꞉lia꞉ iliki, to we a꞉na saefa꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ hida꞉yo꞉ nolo꞉ gimo꞉ dima꞉kiyo꞉ mo꞉sa꞉ma꞉no꞉, ko꞉sega ele imilig gimo꞉wo꞉ sa꞉ma꞉nigo꞉lo꞉ we.
Ma꞉no꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ madali godemo꞉lo꞉ dimiab a꞉no꞉ na꞉so꞉bo. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ no꞉ ho꞉bo꞉ a꞉no꞉lia꞉, no꞉wo꞉ dagasa silisa꞉nda꞉sa꞉ga꞉, ho꞉bo꞉wo꞉ mo꞉ane a꞉no꞉lia꞉yo꞉, na꞉so꞉bo. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ wo꞉wo꞉ dia꞉so꞉bo. Man a꞉no꞉ kuduha꞉nalega, gio꞉ kobale mesa꞉ib. To nililo꞉ gimo꞉lo꞉ so꞉lo꞉lo꞉ o꞉m.
Mo꞉fo꞉s sa꞉sa꞉lo꞉ a꞉no꞉ dia꞉sa꞉ga꞉, kalu iyo꞉ Ya꞉lusalem a꞉no꞉ ta꞉ta꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Antio꞉g a꞉na ha꞉na꞉ga꞉ fa꞉la꞉dowakiyo꞉, sa꞉s kaluka꞉isaleyo꞉ kegea꞉sa꞉ga꞉, mo꞉fo꞉s sa꞉sa꞉lo꞉ a꞉no꞉ agelema꞉ki, dimi.
Mo꞉fo꞉s sa꞉sa꞉lo꞉ a꞉no꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ agelaki, da꞉bu amio꞉, tilidabu ililo꞉ halale alitakilo꞉ to sio꞉ a꞉no꞉ da꞉dakiyo꞉, sagalo꞉wo꞉ alan dowo꞉.
A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ Yuda꞉s dia꞉ Sailas dia꞉yo꞉, Godeya꞉ ene dinali sa꞉lan kalu dowo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ a꞉la꞉ma꞉yo꞉ tilidabu ililo꞉wo꞉ halale dowa꞉i hamana꞉ki, tilidabu kaluka꞉isalemo꞉wo꞉ wala sa꞉la꞉len.
A꞉la꞉yo꞉ ho꞉len nolo꞉ to mano꞉ wida꞉liki, Antio꞉g a꞉naka o꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, a꞉la꞉lo꞉ iliga꞉fo꞉ kalulo꞉wa a꞉ma꞉la꞉ hamana꞉kiyo꞉, iliyo꞉ a꞉la꞉mo꞉wo꞉ sagale alita꞉sa꞉ga꞉, a꞉ma꞉la꞉ Ya꞉lusalem iliga꞉fo꞉.
<range>
Ko꞉sega Fol dia꞉ Banabas dia꞉yo꞉ a꞉naka o꞉siliki, a꞉la꞉ o꞉lia꞉ kalu nol o꞉lia꞉ma꞉yo꞉ Alana꞉ to mano꞉ wida꞉len.
Ho꞉len nolo꞉ ta꞉ta꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, Fol eyo꞉ Banabasbo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Na꞉no꞉ a꞉ma꞉la꞉ amisa꞉n ko꞉li ko꞉lilo꞉ Alana꞉ to mando꞉ wida꞉i anelo꞉ a꞉namio꞉ ha꞉na꞉ga꞉, iyo꞉ waga dimida꞉li sabele a꞉la꞉liki ba꞉da꞉i ha꞉na꞉nigo꞉l” a꞉la꞉sio꞉.
A꞉la꞉sa꞉labiki, Banabas eyo꞉ Yon Mago꞉ tililia꞉ga꞉ ha꞉na꞉no꞉ asulo꞉ ko꞉sega, Fol eyo꞉ Mag e tililiha꞉na꞉no꞉ a꞉la꞉bo꞉ mo꞉asulo꞉, mo꞉wo꞉ tamin amio꞉ ililo꞉ wida꞉i ane amio꞉, Mag e Bafilia hen a꞉namio꞉ a꞉la꞉yo꞉ ta꞉ta꞉ga꞉, nanogo꞉ elo꞉ dia꞉i ha꞉na꞉len a꞉no꞉ kata꞉fo꞉.
<range>
To a꞉namio꞉ a꞉la꞉yo꞉ alan kega꞉sa꞉ga꞉, alobo꞉no꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ Banabas eyo꞉ Yon Mago꞉ e tililia꞉ga꞉, ho꞉n ko꞉su disa꞉la꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Saibulus a꞉na ane.
Ko꞉sega Fol eyo꞉ Sailaso꞉ tililia꞉ga꞉, ha꞉nabikiyo꞉, tilidabu kaluka꞉isaleya꞉yo꞉ a꞉la꞉mo꞉wo꞉ Godeya꞉yo꞉ asuwa꞉foma꞉kiyo꞉ dulugu sa꞉la꞉sa꞉ga꞉, a꞉la꞉yo꞉ ane.
A꞉la꞉yo꞉ Silia hen a꞉na a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ Silisia hena ha꞉nakiyo꞉, sa꞉s kaluka꞉isaleya꞉ tilidabuwo꞉ halaido꞉ doma꞉ki, wida꞉li ane.
A꞉la꞉yo꞉ ha꞉na꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Debe fa꞉la꞉dota꞉ga꞉, Lista fa꞉la꞉dowakiyo꞉, tilidabu so꞉wa nowo꞉ a꞉na galili. Ene wiyo꞉ Timoti a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ ene anowo꞉ Yu ka꞉isale Ya꞉su amilo꞉ tilidabuwo꞉ e, ko꞉sega ene iyayo꞉ Gilig kalu.
Keliso kaluka꞉isale, Lista a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ Aikonium amisa꞉n amilo꞉ sen a꞉ma꞉yo꞉ man elo꞉wo꞉ nafa ba꞉ba꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ e digalo꞉ so꞉wa a꞉la꞉sa꞉la꞉sen.
Fol eyo꞉ Timotiyo꞉ e tililia꞉ sia꞉mela꞉no꞉ asulo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ ene do꞉go꞉fo꞉ hege gede alifa꞉. Mo꞉wo꞉ Yu kaluka꞉isale amisa꞉n a꞉namilo꞉ sen a꞉ma꞉yo꞉ Timotiya꞉ iyayo꞉ Gilig kalu a꞉la꞉asulo꞉.
Iyo꞉ amisa꞉n ko꞉li ko꞉lilo꞉wa wida꞉li siakiyo꞉, iliga꞉felo꞉ kalu ililo꞉ Ya꞉lusalem a꞉na nenela꞉la꞉ga꞉lo꞉ saefa꞉ a꞉no꞉ tilidabu kaluka꞉isaleya꞉yo꞉ kudu hamana꞉ki, wida꞉li ane.
A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ sa꞉s a꞉namio꞉, kaluka꞉isaleya꞉ tilidabuwo꞉ halaido꞉ fa꞉la꞉dowo꞉ a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉, kaluka꞉isale nolo꞉lo꞉ asugo꞉ nodolaki, modo꞉ fa꞉la꞉dowo꞉.
Godeya꞉ Mamaya꞉yo꞉ Fol o꞉lia꞉ e o꞉lia꞉lo꞉ sia꞉sen kalu iyo꞉ Esia hen amio꞉ mano꞉ walama꞉no꞉wo꞉ ka꞉laki go꞉. A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ iyo꞉ ha꞉na꞉siakiyo꞉, Filigia hen o꞉lia꞉ Galesia hen us a꞉namio꞉ tigini ane.
Iyo꞉ Misia hen eleya fa꞉la꞉dowakiyo꞉, Bitinia hen amio꞉ ha꞉na꞉no꞉ asulo꞉ ko꞉sega Ya꞉suwa꞉ Mamaya꞉yo꞉ a꞉namilo꞉ ha꞉na꞉no꞉wo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉.
A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ iyo꞉ Misia hen a꞉no꞉ da꞉la꞉li ha꞉na꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Toloas amisa꞉na tiane.
A꞉na silikiyo꞉, nulu amio꞉ Fol eyo꞉ ho꞉le ba꞉dakiyo꞉, Masedonia kalu nowo꞉ ene hena kagafo꞉liki, Fol e mena꞉ki a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Ge Masedonia ya꞉sa꞉ga꞉, nio꞉ asuwa꞉fa꞉ni mena” a꞉la꞉liki susiabiki ba꞉ba꞉.
Fol elo꞉ ho꞉le ba꞉dab a꞉no꞉ nimo꞉wo꞉ sa꞉labikiyo꞉, Godeya꞉ mano꞉ nio꞉ a꞉na walama꞉ki sa꞉lab a꞉la꞉ asulakiyo꞉, nio꞉ Masedonia ha꞉na꞉niki, wigibo a꞉naka dimadali.
Nio꞉ dimidalia꞉sa꞉ga꞉, ho꞉n ko꞉suwo꞉ Toloas a꞉na disa꞉la꞉sa꞉ga꞉, ho꞉na꞉lo꞉ hegefa꞉ hen Samotilas a꞉na fofa꞉sa꞉ dia꞉sa꞉ga꞉ onolo ha꞉nakiyo꞉, ho꞉len imilig nowo꞉ ta꞉ta꞉ga꞉, Neabolis a꞉na fa꞉la꞉dowo꞉.
Nio꞉ a꞉na fa꞉la꞉dota꞉ga꞉, hena ha꞉na꞉la꞉ga꞉, Filibai a꞉na fa꞉la꞉dowo꞉. Filibai a꞉no꞉ Masedonia hen amilo꞉ amisa꞉n alano꞉ e. Tamin amio꞉ Lom kaluwa꞉ amisa꞉n a꞉no꞉ bo꞉fo꞉len. Nio꞉ ho꞉len nowo꞉ a꞉na sen.
Ha꞉fo꞉lo꞉ Dowan ho꞉leno꞉ fa꞉la꞉dowabiki, nio꞉ Yu kaluwa꞉lo꞉ dulugu sa꞉la꞉sen hen a꞉no꞉ keda꞉i ha꞉nakiyo꞉, amisa꞉no꞉ ta꞉ta꞉ga꞉, ho꞉na꞉ aniba ka꞉isale nolo꞉ a꞉namilo꞉ kegenefo꞉len a꞉no꞉lia꞉ siliki, towo꞉ imo꞉wo꞉ wido꞉.
To nililo꞉ widabdo꞉ da꞉da꞉len ka꞉isale nowo꞉ wiyo꞉ Lidia. Ka꞉isale we Taiataila amisa꞉n ga ko꞉lo꞉ helebeso꞉g ho꞉mo꞉solo꞉ nafalelo꞉ kililia꞉seno꞉ o꞉m ko꞉lo꞉ e Godeya꞉ wilo꞉ wabulu sa꞉la꞉seno꞉ e. Alana꞉yo꞉ ga a꞉ma꞉ asugo꞉ kolaitabikiyo꞉, Fol elo꞉ to widab a꞉no꞉ tilidabu.
A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ ga a꞉no꞉ a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ kaluka꞉isale ene a a꞉namilo꞉ sen a꞉no꞉lia꞉yo꞉, tambo ho꞉na to꞉lolo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ Lidia eyo꞉ nio꞉ e aya mena꞉ki susiakiyo꞉, “Gio꞉ ne hendele Alan amio꞉ tilida꞉dab a꞉la꞉asulalega, ni aya mesa꞉ mena,” a꞉la꞉sa꞉labikiyo꞉, nio꞉ e o꞉lia꞉ ane.
Ho꞉len no amio꞉, nio꞉ tolo꞉ dulugu sa꞉la꞉sen hena ha꞉na꞉no꞉ ha꞉na꞉len amio꞉, madalilo꞉ nanog dian ga nowo꞉ toga gido꞉. Ga e amio꞉ mama mogago꞉wo꞉ dofo꞉liki, tif amilo꞉ dimidama꞉nigabo꞉ e ho꞉le ba꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉, dinali sa꞉la꞉sen. A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉, ga o꞉lo꞉ biso꞉wa꞉yo꞉ moleyo꞉ modo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ dia꞉sen.
Ga we Foldo꞉ ni kudu ya꞉ga꞉ yakiyo꞉, towo꞉ halale sa꞉laki, “Kalu i we, Gode Iwalulo꞉ a꞉laba꞉ Ene nanog dian kalu wema꞉yo꞉, gilo꞉ a꞉ma꞉la꞉do꞉ gasilia꞉b man a꞉no꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ wida꞉i yab” a꞉la꞉sio꞉.
Ga a꞉ma꞉yo꞉ ho꞉len modo꞉ amio꞉ a꞉la꞉sa꞉la꞉li ya꞉len ko꞉lo꞉, Fol e mo꞉bea꞉sa꞉ga꞉, nodolakiyo꞉ mama mogago꞉mo꞉wo꞉ towo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Niyo꞉ Ya꞉su Kelisowa꞉ wi halaido꞉ a꞉na ilikiyo꞉, ge ga we ta꞉fo꞉ hamana!” A꞉la꞉sa꞉labikiyo꞉, wigibo a꞉naka mama mogago꞉ e amilo꞉ elen a꞉no꞉ ta꞉fo꞉gane.
Madali nanogdo꞉ dian ga o꞉lo꞉ biso꞉ a꞉ma꞉yo꞉ wa꞉kabiyo꞉ iliyo꞉ moleyo꞉ mo꞉dia꞉nigo꞉bo꞉lo꞉b a꞉la꞉asulaki, iliyo꞉ Fol dia꞉ Sailas dia꞉yo꞉ ta꞉lia꞉sa꞉ga꞉, amisa꞉n kalulo꞉ kegea꞉sen a꞉na susululia꞉ga꞉, Loma꞉ mo꞉walilabdo꞉ da꞉dan kalulo꞉wa ta꞉takiyo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Kalu a꞉la꞉ we Yu kalu ko꞉lo꞉ nili amisa꞉n wenamio꞉ mogago꞉ dimida꞉lab.
<range>
Lom kaluka꞉isale nililo꞉ man mo꞉dimidama꞉no꞉ a꞉la꞉likilo꞉ saefa꞉ a꞉no꞉, kalu a꞉la꞉ wema꞉yo꞉ man a꞉no꞉ kudu hamana꞉ki wida꞉lab.”
A꞉la꞉sa꞉labiki, kaluka꞉isale kegeo꞉ i a꞉ma꞉yo꞉ elo꞉ sa꞉lab a꞉no꞉ hendele a꞉la꞉asulakiyo꞉, iyo꞉ a꞉no꞉lo꞉ egele dowaki, a꞉la꞉mo꞉wo꞉ gadio꞉ dowo꞉. Loma꞉ mo꞉walilabdo꞉ da꞉dan kaluwa꞉yo꞉ a꞉la꞉ma꞉ so꞉go꞉ kalu nolba꞉ bidila꞉sa꞉ga꞉, bi buluwa꞉ sanama a꞉la꞉sio꞉.
Iliyo꞉ a꞉la꞉yo꞉ moma꞉ni sa꞉nda꞉sa꞉ga꞉, dibolo aya to꞉lolo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉, dibolo alo꞉ bo꞉fo꞉lowan kalumo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉yo꞉ dinafa bo꞉fo꞉melea꞉ki salifa꞉.
Bo꞉fo꞉lowan kaluwa꞉yo꞉ to a꞉no꞉ da꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉, a꞉la꞉yo꞉ dibolo a usamilo꞉ halaido꞉ galaleya to꞉lo alita꞉ga꞉, a꞉la꞉ma꞉ gibo꞉ i ko꞉no꞉ a꞉la꞉ya꞉ diga꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉ uludu alifa꞉.
Nulu us amio꞉, Fol dia꞉ Sailas dia꞉yo꞉ Godemo꞉ dulugu sa꞉la꞉liki, gisalo꞉wo꞉ mola꞉labiki, dibolo kalu nolo꞉ da꞉da꞉li sen.
Wigibo a꞉naka hiniyo꞉ alan silaki, dibolo ayo꞉ ida꞉lakiyo꞉, togo꞉ tambo kolai a꞉taki, dibolo kalu seniya꞉lo꞉ dila꞉ a꞉no꞉ ene asulo꞉ a꞉dufufudo꞉.
Bo꞉fo꞉lowan kaluwo꞉ si kagayaki ba꞉ba꞉ amio꞉, dibolo ayo꞉ togo꞉ kolalifelo꞉wa ba꞉da꞉ga꞉, eyo꞉ dibolo kalu tambo dalaido꞉wele a꞉la꞉asulakiyo꞉ e helebesiyo꞉ dia꞉sa꞉ga꞉, enena꞉ma꞉la꞉ sana soma꞉nigabiki, Fol eyo꞉ towo꞉ halale sa꞉lakiyo꞉, “Nio꞉ tambo o꞉so꞉l ko꞉lo꞉, ge go꞉no꞉n a꞉ma꞉la꞉yo꞉ mogagila꞉so꞉bo!”
<range>
Dibolo alo꞉ bo꞉fo꞉lowan kaluwa꞉yo꞉ deyo꞉ dolia꞉ mena꞉ki ho꞉ida꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, e bo꞉i ha꞉na꞉sa꞉ga꞉ Fol dia꞉ Sailas dia꞉lo꞉wa bibisoda꞉liki tulu ali.
Eyo꞉ a꞉la꞉yo꞉ ha꞉la꞉ya tilili handalowakiyo꞉, a꞉la꞉mo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉ dabuba꞉ba꞉, “Godeya꞉yo꞉ ne gasilima꞉kiyo꞉, waga dimidama꞉no꞉wele?”
A꞉la꞉ma꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Ge o꞉lia꞉ gi ayamilo꞉ sa꞉sen a꞉no꞉lia꞉yo꞉ Ya꞉su Alana tilida꞉dalikiyo꞉, Godeya꞉yo꞉ gio꞉ a꞉ma꞉la꞉ gasilima꞉ib” a꞉la꞉sio꞉.
A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ Fol dia꞉ Sailas dia꞉ma꞉yo꞉ Ya꞉su Alana꞉ mano꞉ e o꞉lia꞉, e ayamilo꞉ sa꞉sen tambo o꞉lia꞉mo꞉wo꞉ wido꞉.
Nulu us a꞉naka, bo꞉fo꞉lowan kalu eyo꞉ a꞉la꞉yo꞉ tililia꞉sa꞉ga꞉, a꞉la꞉ma꞉ do꞉mo꞉ amilo꞉ gegede alifelo꞉ a꞉no꞉ ho꞉na꞉ to꞉go꞉de alifelabiki, o꞉g a꞉naka e o꞉lia꞉ e ayamilo꞉ sa꞉sen o꞉lia꞉yo꞉ ho꞉na to꞉lofelo꞉.
A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉yo꞉ dibolo alo꞉ bo꞉fo꞉lowan kaluwa꞉yo꞉ a꞉la꞉yo꞉ e aya tililia꞉ ha꞉na꞉sa꞉ga꞉, ma꞉no꞉wo꞉ maya꞉ki so꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉ dime. E o꞉lia꞉ e ayamilo꞉ sa꞉sen tambo o꞉lia꞉yo꞉ Godeyo꞉ tilidabu ko꞉lo꞉ iyo꞉ sagalo꞉wo꞉ mada alan dowo꞉.
Kea꞉fo ho꞉le bidabiki, Loma꞉ mo꞉walilabdo꞉ da꞉dan kalu iliyo꞉ dibololo꞉ bo꞉fo꞉len o꞉mo꞉wo꞉ to saga꞉takiyo꞉, “Kalu a꞉la꞉ko꞉ sili alifoma” a꞉la꞉liki, da꞉la꞉di kalumo꞉ saga꞉fo꞉.
A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ dibolo alo꞉ bo꞉fo꞉lowan kaluwa꞉yo꞉ Fo꞉lbo꞉wo꞉ towo꞉ saga꞉takiyo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Ga꞉go꞉ sili alita꞉bika꞉ a꞉la꞉li saga꞉fo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ ga꞉go꞉ sagala꞉liki hamana.”
Ko꞉sega Fola꞉yo꞉ a꞉ma꞉la꞉bo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Na꞉no꞉ Lom kalu ko꞉sega iliyo꞉ mo꞉mo꞉walilaki, na꞉no꞉ kaluka꞉isale siwa꞉la yame tanda꞉ya꞉sa꞉ga꞉, dibolowa to꞉lolo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ o꞉go꞉ na꞉no꞉ iliyo꞉ wo꞉no꞉le sili alifa꞉no꞉ asulab ko꞉sega na꞉no꞉ a꞉la꞉bo꞉ mo꞉dimidama꞉no꞉. Inino꞉ ya꞉sa꞉ga꞉, na꞉no꞉ ha꞉sa tililia꞉ga꞉ ha꞉la꞉ ta꞉talega, na꞉no꞉ a꞉na ha꞉na꞉no꞉.”
Da꞉la꞉di kaluwa꞉yo꞉ ha꞉na꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Fol elo꞉ to sa꞉lab a꞉no꞉ Loma꞉ mo꞉walilabdo꞉ da꞉dan kalu imo꞉wo꞉ sa꞉labikiyo꞉, a꞉la꞉yo꞉ Lom kaluka꞉ a꞉la꞉do꞉ sio꞉ a꞉no꞉ iyo꞉ da꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉, tagi dowo꞉.
Iyo꞉ dibolo aya ha꞉na꞉sa꞉ga꞉, hala dimido꞉ a꞉no꞉ foga꞉le sa꞉la꞉sa꞉ga꞉, a꞉la꞉yo꞉ ha꞉la꞉ya tililia꞉ ha꞉na꞉ga꞉, ili amisa꞉no꞉ ta꞉ta꞉ga꞉ hamana꞉ki, towo꞉ halaido꞉ sio꞉.
A꞉la꞉go꞉ko꞉lo꞉, a꞉la꞉yo꞉ ha꞉na꞉nikiyo꞉, Lidia ene aya ha꞉na꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, Keliso kaluka꞉isale nolo꞉ a꞉na galilia꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, ili asulo꞉wo꞉ halale alitakiyo꞉, towo꞉ salita꞉ga꞉, a꞉la꞉yo꞉ a꞉na ane.
Fol dia꞉ Sailas dia꞉yo꞉ ha꞉nakiyo꞉, Amfibolis amisa꞉n o꞉lia꞉ Abolonia amisa꞉n a꞉no꞉lo꞉ tinia꞉li ha꞉na꞉ga꞉, Tesalonaika amisa꞉n a꞉na fa꞉la꞉dowo꞉. Amisa꞉n a꞉namio꞉, Yu kaluwa꞉lo꞉ tolo꞉ wida꞉sen ayo꞉ elen ko꞉lo꞉, Fol elo꞉ dimidan o꞉leaumbo꞉, e a꞉na ha꞉na꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Godeya꞉ towo꞉ wida꞉len. So꞉go꞉ agelo꞉ otalen a꞉namilo꞉, Ha꞉fo꞉lo꞉ Dowa꞉sen ho꞉len a꞉no꞉ tambo eyo꞉ Yu kaluwa꞉lo꞉ tolo꞉ wida꞉sen ayamio꞉ ha꞉na꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Godeya꞉ to tamin amilo꞉ sa꞉sa꞉lo꞉ a꞉no꞉ e a꞉fanda wido꞉.
<range>
Tamin amilo꞉ dinali sa꞉lan ililo꞉ sa꞉sa꞉lo꞉ a꞉namio꞉ Godeya꞉lo꞉ Da꞉feyo꞉ Kalu e mada nagalo꞉ dia꞉la꞉ga꞉ soma꞉ib ko꞉sega e a꞉ma꞉la꞉ dasima꞉ib a꞉la꞉sa꞉sa꞉lo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ wido꞉. A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ kalu nilo꞉ mando꞉ wido꞉l Ya꞉su we, Godeya꞉lo꞉ Da꞉feyo꞉ Kaluwo꞉ e. Fol eyo꞉ a꞉la꞉wido꞉.
Fol elo꞉ to sa꞉lab a꞉no꞉ da꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Yu kalu nolo꞉ a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ Gilik kalu Godemo꞉lo꞉ wabuda꞉sen modo꞉le, a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ amisa꞉n misa꞉ ka꞉isale modo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ iyo꞉ asulo꞉ nodola꞉sa꞉ga꞉, a꞉la꞉ o꞉lia꞉ a꞉dowo꞉.
Ko꞉sega Yu misa꞉ kalu iliyo꞉ Fol dia꞉ Sailas dia꞉mo꞉wo꞉ alan mobeaki gadia꞉sa꞉ga꞉, iyo꞉ amisa꞉ndo꞉ kegea꞉sen henamilo꞉ kalu bo꞉bo꞉gedo gadia꞉sen a꞉no꞉ kegea꞉sa꞉ga꞉ gadima꞉kiyo꞉, towo꞉ digini sio꞉. Iliyo꞉ to a꞉no꞉ iligi dabu ko꞉lo꞉, Fol dia꞉ Sailas dia꞉yo꞉ ta꞉lia꞉niki, Yesan aya ane.
Ko꞉sega kalu a꞉la꞉ a꞉no꞉ mo꞉ba꞉dabikiyo꞉, iliyo꞉ Yesan o꞉lia꞉ tilidabu kalu nol a꞉namilo꞉ elen a꞉no꞉ susulu sa꞉la꞉la꞉sa꞉ga꞉, gumiti kalu imo꞉ mo꞉walilima꞉ki tililia꞉ yakiyo꞉, a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Fol dia꞉ Sailas dia꞉yo꞉ amisa꞉n tambo amio꞉ mogago꞉wo꞉ dimida꞉li sia꞉len ko꞉lo꞉, o꞉go꞉ a꞉la꞉yo꞉ amisa꞉n wena fa꞉la꞉dowabi, Yesan e aya tililia꞉gane ko꞉lo꞉ sab. I a꞉no꞉ tambo Ya꞉su e misa꞉ kalu a꞉la꞉liki sa꞉lakiyo꞉, Loma꞉ misa꞉ alan Sisaya꞉ ene ele difa꞉yo꞉ iyo꞉ tambo o꞉go꞉so꞉.”
<range>
Amisa꞉n kaluka꞉isale o꞉lia꞉ gumiti kalu i o꞉lia꞉ma꞉yo꞉ to a꞉no꞉ iligi da꞉da꞉ga꞉, iyo꞉ tambo kulufa꞉yo꞉wo꞉ alan dowaki, towo꞉ halale tandeo꞉.
A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ gumiti kalu iliyo꞉, Yesan o꞉lia꞉ tilidabu kalu nol o꞉lia꞉mo꞉wo꞉ iyo꞉ sili alifoma꞉ki moleyo꞉ silima a꞉la꞉sa꞉labiki, iliyo꞉ moleyo꞉ dia꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉ sili alifa꞉.
O꞉g nulu a꞉namio꞉, tilidabu kalu iyo꞉ Fol dia꞉ Sailas dia꞉yo꞉ Belia a꞉na iliga꞉tabiki, a꞉la꞉yo꞉ ha꞉na꞉sa꞉ga꞉ Belia amisa꞉na fa꞉la꞉dowa꞉ta꞉ga꞉yo꞉, Yu kaluwa꞉lo꞉ tolo꞉ wida꞉sen a a꞉na ane.
Belia kaluka꞉isale iyo꞉, Tesalonaika kaluka꞉isale i o꞉le o꞉ngo꞉ma ko꞉lo꞉ Belia kaluka꞉isaleya꞉ kufa꞉ uso꞉ kolaifa꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ iyo꞉ Fola꞉ to sa꞉lab a꞉no꞉ sagalo꞉ da꞉dabiki, iliyo꞉ Fol e towo꞉ hendele sa꞉labele a꞉la꞉li, Godeya꞉ towo꞉ ho꞉leno꞉ tambo agelaliki, dinafa alobana asulo꞉.
A꞉la꞉go꞉ko꞉lo꞉ Yu kaluka꞉isale asugo꞉ modo꞉ nodolo꞉ a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ Gilig kalu o꞉lia꞉ Gilig ka꞉isale amilo꞉ amisa꞉n misa꞉ dowo꞉ a꞉no꞉lo꞉ modo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ tilidabu.
Ko꞉sega Yu kalu Tesalonaikalo꞉ sen a꞉ma꞉yo꞉, Fol eyo꞉ Godeya꞉ towo꞉ Belia a꞉na widab a꞉la꞉ asulaki, iyo꞉ a꞉na ya꞉sa꞉ga꞉, amisa꞉n kaluka꞉isaleyo꞉ Fol dia꞉mo꞉wo꞉ kulufema꞉ki towo꞉ ko꞉li ko꞉lilo꞉ digini me.
Wigibo a꞉namio꞉, tilidabu kaluka꞉isale iliyo꞉ Folo꞉ so꞉lu ho꞉n aniba iliga꞉fo꞉, ko꞉sega Sailas dia꞉ Timoti dia꞉yo꞉ mo꞉hanaki, ka sen.
Kalu nol Fol elo꞉ tililia꞉ga꞉lo꞉ Atens a꞉namilo꞉ ane a꞉no꞉, a꞉ma꞉la꞉ yabi, eyo꞉ Sailas dia꞉ Timoti dia꞉yo꞉ elo꞉ amio꞉ mada bo꞉bo꞉ge mena꞉ki saga꞉fo꞉.
Fol e a꞉la꞉yo꞉ yasila꞉liki, Atens a꞉na silikiyo꞉, e amisa꞉n usamilo꞉ madali gode dimido꞉ a꞉no꞉ modo꞉ ba꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉, kele asulakiyo꞉ hida꞉yo꞉ alan dowo꞉.
A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ e Yu kaluwa꞉lo꞉ tolo꞉ wida꞉sen aya ha꞉na꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Yu kalu o꞉lia꞉ Gilig kalu, Godemo꞉ gulugululasen o꞉lia꞉mo꞉wo꞉ dinafa wido꞉. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ ho꞉leno꞉ tambo e kelego꞉lo꞉ kililia꞉sen hen a꞉namio꞉lo꞉ ha꞉na꞉sa꞉ga꞉, kaluka꞉isale kegea꞉lab o꞉mo꞉wo꞉lo꞉ dinafa wida꞉len.
Fol eyo꞉ Ya꞉su ko꞉lo꞉ sowa꞉sa꞉ga꞉lo꞉ a꞉ma꞉lo꞉ dasi a꞉no꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ wida꞉len amio꞉, widan kalu nolo꞉ Ebikuli man a꞉no꞉ kuduha꞉na꞉sen a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ nolo꞉ Sitoig man o꞉lo꞉ kuduha꞉na꞉sen ko꞉lo꞉ kalu iyo꞉ ya꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Fol o꞉lia꞉yo꞉ towo꞉ kego꞉. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ nolba꞉yo꞉ a꞉la꞉dabuba꞉ba꞉, “Kalu we o꞉ngo꞉malo꞉ o꞉ngo꞉ to sa꞉lab ko꞉lo꞉, to o꞉bo꞉ngo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ sa꞉laba?” A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ kalu nolba꞉yo꞉, “E ho꞉gi godeya꞉ mano꞉ nowo꞉ a꞉dia꞉yaki widab” a꞉la꞉sio꞉.
Iliyo꞉ Fol e tililia꞉ ha꞉na꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Aleobagus hen a꞉namio꞉, kaunsil kalulo꞉ kegeab us a꞉na tililia꞉ tina꞉ga꞉, emo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉dabu ba꞉ba꞉, “Gilo꞉ man ho꞉gi wido꞉ a꞉no꞉ nimo꞉wo꞉ walama꞉nigaya?
Giyo꞉ mano꞉ ko꞉li wido꞉ amio꞉, nio꞉ ho꞉gi dabu ko꞉lo꞉ a꞉ma꞉ ha꞉go꞉ giyo꞉ fanda sama” a꞉la꞉sio꞉.
Atens kaluka꞉isale o꞉lia꞉ mageso꞉ mio꞉ kalu a꞉namilo꞉ sen o꞉lia꞉yo꞉ madali siliki, to ho꞉gi dia꞉mio꞉ sa꞉lab a꞉no꞉ da꞉da꞉liki nenela꞉len.
A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ Fol e kaunsil ili tolo꞉ nenela꞉lab usa dasilia꞉ga꞉ kagayaki a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Atens kalu giyo꞉, ni ba꞉ba꞉ amio꞉, gulugululan gililo꞉wo꞉ ko꞉li ko꞉lilo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉lab.
Ne amisa꞉n us wena sia꞉likiyo꞉, gili madali gode ko꞉li ko꞉lilo꞉ gililo꞉ gulugululan a꞉no꞉ dinafa ba꞉ba꞉. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ u imilig dibido꞉ wa꞉l amilo꞉ wi sa꞉sa꞉lo꞉wo꞉ we ‘Gode Wilo꞉ Babalab a꞉ma꞉no꞉’ a꞉la꞉ sa꞉sa꞉lo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ ba꞉ba꞉. A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ giyo꞉ Gode mo꞉asulo꞉fo꞉likilo꞉, gulugulula꞉sen a꞉no꞉ o꞉go꞉ gimo꞉wo꞉ fanda sa꞉ma꞉nigo꞉l.
“Gode wema꞉yo꞉ henfelo꞉wo꞉ dimida꞉sa꞉ga꞉, mela꞉no꞉lo꞉ a꞉labo꞉ tambowo꞉ E dimida꞉sa꞉ga꞉ ta꞉fo꞉. Gode we henfelo꞉wo꞉lo꞉, akino꞉lo꞉, eneno꞉ biso꞉ a꞉la꞉liki bo꞉fo꞉lab ko꞉lo꞉ e gulugululan a, kaluwa꞉ dagiya꞉ dimido꞉ a꞉namio꞉ mo꞉ta꞉sen.
Godeya꞉yo꞉ mela꞉no꞉ meho꞉wo꞉ o꞉lia꞉ kelego꞉ henfelo꞉ amilo꞉ a꞉lab we tambo kaluka꞉isalemo꞉ dimi ko꞉lo꞉ Gode e halaido꞉wo꞉ o꞉li ko꞉lo꞉lab. A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ kaluka꞉isaleya꞉ Gode e a꞉asuwa꞉fa꞉no꞉wo꞉ mo꞉lido꞉. Tamin amio꞉ Godeya꞉ kalu imilig nowo꞉ dimido꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ o꞉go꞉ henfelo꞉ amilo꞉ kaluka꞉isale ko꞉li ko꞉lilo꞉ sab we a꞉na fa꞉la꞉dowo꞉. Kaluka꞉isale a꞉no꞉ semo꞉fa꞉la꞉dowo꞉ amio꞉, Godeya꞉yo꞉ hen ililo꞉wo꞉ ele alifela꞉sa꞉ga꞉, ho꞉len a꞉na doma꞉ib a꞉la꞉bo꞉ dinali da꞉fe salifelo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉lab.
<range>
Henfelo꞉ kaluka꞉sale tambowa꞉yo꞉ Gode e kelelia꞉ga꞉yo꞉, fa꞉la꞉doma꞉ki, kaluwo꞉ a꞉na dimido꞉. A꞉la꞉fo꞉ ko꞉sega, Gode e ni o꞉lia꞉yo꞉ ko꞉na꞉lo꞉ mo꞉a꞉lab.
Godeya꞉yo꞉ nimo꞉wo꞉ halaido꞉wo꞉ dimia꞉labiki, nio꞉ a꞉na iliki, nanogo꞉ a꞉na dimida꞉lo꞉l. Giasi kalu nolba꞉yo꞉ a꞉la꞉sa꞉sa꞉lo꞉, ‘Nio꞉ Ene so꞉wa ko꞉lo꞉lab.’
“A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ nio꞉ Godeya꞉ ene so꞉wa ko꞉lo꞉ God e u madali gode, dagiya꞉lo꞉ dimido꞉ o꞉mele a꞉la꞉bo꞉ asula꞉so꞉bo. E kaluwa꞉ asulo꞉wa꞉lo꞉ dimido꞉ golo꞉ o꞉ silbayo꞉ o꞉ngo꞉ma.
Tamin amio꞉ kaluka꞉isaleyo꞉ babalo꞉ dofo꞉liki dimidabiki, Godeya꞉yo꞉ ka ta꞉fo꞉len ko꞉sega, o꞉go꞉ kaluka꞉isale henefelo꞉ we tambolo꞉ a꞉lab a꞉no꞉ asulo꞉wo꞉ nodoma꞉ki, towo꞉ halaido꞉ sio꞉.
Mo꞉wo꞉ Godeya꞉yo꞉ henfelo꞉ kaluka꞉isalelo꞉ mo꞉walilima꞉no꞉wo꞉ ho꞉len imilig nowo꞉ da꞉fe alifa꞉ ko꞉lo꞉lab. A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ kalu elo꞉ da꞉feyo꞉ a꞉ma꞉yo꞉ mo꞉walilakiyo꞉, digalo꞉ man a꞉na iliki mo꞉walilima꞉ib.”
Iyo꞉ kalu sowo꞉ a꞉ma꞉la꞉ dasi a꞉la꞉do꞉ sa꞉lab a꞉no꞉ da꞉dakiyo꞉, nolba꞉yo꞉ Folo꞉ dio꞉ge sio꞉ ko꞉sega nolba꞉yo꞉ “To a꞉no꞉ nio꞉ a꞉da꞉ba꞉no꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ wa꞉ka sama” a꞉la꞉sio꞉.
A꞉la꞉ dimida꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Fol e Aleobagus kanisolo꞉ kegea꞉sen hen a꞉no꞉ a꞉na ta꞉fo꞉gane.
Fol elo꞉ to wido꞉ a꞉no꞉ kalu nolo꞉ tilidabu ko꞉lo꞉ Ya꞉su kudu ane. Tilidabu kalu nowo꞉ Dionisius, Aleobagus kaunsil kalu nowo꞉ e. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ nowo꞉ ga Damalis, a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ kaluka꞉isale nolo꞉lo꞉ tilidabu.
Tif amio꞉, Fol e Atens amisa꞉no꞉ ta꞉ta꞉ga꞉, Kolin amisa꞉na ane.
A꞉namio꞉ kalu imilig nowo꞉ a꞉na galili, ene wiyo꞉ Akwila. Ene hen elo꞉ sa꞉la꞉liyo꞉, Pontus, ko꞉sega e o꞉lia꞉ ene inga Bisila o꞉lia꞉yo꞉ o꞉go꞉ Itali hen a꞉na ta꞉fo꞉ mio꞉ mo꞉wo꞉, Lom misa꞉ kalu, Kalodius e sa꞉lakiyo꞉, “Yu kalu mio꞉, gio꞉ hen Lom we ta꞉ta꞉sa꞉ga꞉ hamana” a꞉la꞉sio꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ a꞉la꞉yo꞉ a꞉na ya꞉sa꞉ga꞉ sen.
A꞉la꞉yo꞉ helebeso꞉g alo꞉ diano꞉ a꞉la꞉ma꞉ dubia꞉sen a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ Fol elo꞉ nanogo꞉ o꞉leo꞉ngo꞉ dian kalu ko꞉lo꞉ e a꞉la꞉ o꞉lia꞉ siliki, nanog a꞉no꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ dia꞉len.
Ha꞉fo꞉lo꞉ Dowan ho꞉leno꞉ tambo amio꞉, Fol eyo꞉ Yu kaluwa꞉lo꞉ tolo꞉ wida꞉sen aya ha꞉na꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Yu kalu o꞉lia꞉ Gilig kalu o꞉lia꞉yo꞉ asugo꞉ nodoma꞉kiyo꞉, towo꞉ wido꞉.
Sailas dia꞉ Timoti dia꞉yo꞉ Masedonia hena a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ Fol elo꞉wa fa꞉la꞉dowabikiyo꞉, e nanog nowo꞉ mo꞉diaki, ho꞉leno꞉ tambo Yu kaluka꞉isalemo꞉wo꞉ man wida꞉likiyo꞉, Godeya꞉lo꞉ Da꞉feyo꞉ kaluwo꞉, Ya꞉su Keliso eka꞉ a꞉la꞉liki wida꞉len.
Ko꞉sega Yu kalu iyo꞉ to elo꞉ wido꞉ a꞉no꞉ gola ba꞉daki, e dio꞉ge sa꞉labikiyo꞉, Fol eyo꞉ so꞉g sa꞉ga꞉lo꞉ enedo꞉ a꞉no꞉ duda꞉sa꞉ga꞉ hena꞉mu ko꞉lo꞉ babedo꞉ a꞉no꞉ fifilaki a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Gio꞉ falasilalega, ginido꞉ hala dimido꞉ a꞉na auma꞉ib. Ne amio꞉ halayo꞉ aundo꞉ma ko꞉lo꞉ ne ga꞉li doma꞉no꞉. O꞉g wena a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉yo꞉, ne Yu kaluka꞉isalema imo꞉wo꞉ towo꞉ walama꞉ ha꞉na꞉nigo꞉l.”
A꞉la꞉sa꞉la꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, Fol e tolo꞉ wida꞉sen ayo꞉ ta꞉ta꞉sa꞉ga꞉, a anib amilo꞉ Titius Yastus ene aya ti ane. Kalu a꞉no꞉ Godeya꞉ wiyo꞉ dulugu sa꞉la꞉sen ko꞉lo꞉ Folo꞉ e o꞉lia꞉ sen.
Tolo꞉ wida꞉sen a o꞉lo꞉ biso꞉ kalu, Kilisbus, e o꞉lia꞉ ene so꞉lo꞉ o꞉lia꞉yo꞉ Alano꞉ tilidabu ko꞉lo꞉ Kolin kaluka꞉isale modo꞉ to elo꞉wo꞉ da꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, iyo꞉lo꞉ Alano꞉ tilidadabiki, iyo꞉ ho꞉no꞉ to꞉lolo꞉.
Nulu no amio꞉, Fol e ho꞉le badakiyo꞉, Alana꞉yo꞉ emo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Ge mano꞉ walama꞉no꞉wo꞉, tagilakiyo꞉ eda꞉so꞉bo. Walafo꞉ ko꞉ dofo꞉lubi.
Mo꞉wo꞉ ne ho꞉leno꞉ tambo ge o꞉lia꞉ dofo꞉mela꞉no꞉. Amisa꞉n kaluka꞉isale modo꞉ sab we nino꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ gisa꞉yo꞉ ge mo꞉mogagima꞉ib” Alana꞉yo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉
A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ Fol e donayo꞉ imilig a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ ele do꞉go꞉fela꞉fo꞉wo꞉ Kolin amisa꞉n a꞉naka siliki, Godeya꞉ mano꞉ imo꞉wo꞉ a꞉na wida꞉len.
Galio e Akaya hen a꞉namio꞉ gamani kalu dowakiyo꞉, Yu kalu nolo꞉ kegeakiyo꞉, Fol e ta꞉lia꞉sa꞉ga꞉, mo꞉walilima꞉ni ane.
Iliyo꞉ mo꞉walilakiyo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Kalu wema꞉yo꞉ kaluka꞉isalemo꞉ widakiyo꞉, Godeya꞉lo꞉ ele saefa꞉yo꞉ mo꞉kuduha꞉naki, nio꞉ hala guluguluma꞉kiyo꞉ e wido꞉ ko꞉lo꞉, gemo꞉ mo꞉walilima꞉ki tililia꞉ mio꞉.”
Fol eyo꞉ towo꞉ a꞉ma꞉la꞉bo꞉ sa꞉ma꞉nigabikiyo꞉, Galio꞉ eyo꞉ Yu kalu imo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Yu kalu giliyo꞉, kalu wema꞉yo꞉ gamani ele difa꞉ amio꞉ hala nowo꞉ o꞉go꞉so꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ mo꞉walilima꞉ni mio꞉ kibo꞉bowo꞉, niyo꞉ o꞉li do꞉bo꞉lo.
Ko꞉sega hida꞉yo꞉ we, gini towo꞉ a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ wiyo꞉ ko꞉li ko꞉lilo꞉ a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ gini ele saefa꞉ a꞉no꞉lo꞉ gio꞉ a꞉na towa꞉ kego꞉ ko꞉lo꞉, to we gegele ka digalila꞉bi. Niyo꞉ hida꞉yo꞉ we mo꞉mo꞉walilima꞉no꞉.”
To a꞉no꞉ sa꞉la꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Galio eyo꞉ iyo꞉ hamana꞉ki, o꞉luga꞉felo꞉
Iliyo꞉ ha꞉la꞉ya ha꞉nakiyo꞉, kaluka꞉isale kegeo꞉ a꞉ma꞉yo꞉ wida꞉sen alo꞉ bo꞉fo꞉lowan kalu, Sostenes emo꞉wo꞉ gadiaki, e ta꞉lia꞉sa꞉ga꞉, mo꞉walilia꞉sen hena so꞉no꞉. Ko꞉sega Galio eyo꞉ ililo꞉ dimidab a꞉no꞉ mo꞉kele asulo꞉.
Kolin amisa꞉n amio꞉, Fol e ho꞉len nolo꞉ tilidabu kaluka꞉isale o꞉lia꞉ a꞉na sa꞉ga꞉, Keliso kaluka꞉isale a꞉namilo꞉ senbo꞉wo꞉ ta꞉biyo꞉ a꞉la꞉sa꞉la꞉ga꞉, Fol eyo꞉, Bisilia o꞉lia꞉ Akwila o꞉lia꞉yo꞉ ho꞉n ko꞉suwa disa꞉la꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Silia꞉ hen a꞉namida꞉ ane. E semo꞉ ane, Senkilia amisa꞉n a꞉naka silikiyo꞉, Fol eyo꞉ Godemo꞉ dinali saefo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ Yu man kudu ha꞉naki, e misa꞉ fo꞉no꞉ gedeo꞉.
Iyo꞉ ha꞉na꞉sa꞉ga꞉ Efesa꞉s amisa꞉n a꞉na fa꞉la꞉dowakiyo꞉, Fol e Bisilia o꞉lia꞉ Akwila o꞉lia꞉yo꞉ a꞉na꞉ka ta꞉ta꞉ga꞉, e Yu kaluwa꞉lo꞉ tolo꞉ wida꞉sen aya ha꞉na꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Yu kalu o꞉lia꞉ towo꞉ nenelo꞉.
Iliyo꞉ Fol e ho꞉len modo꞉ nolo꞉ i o꞉lia꞉yo꞉ o꞉doma a꞉la꞉dabu ba꞉dabikiyo꞉, Fol eyo꞉ ne wilo꞉ mo꞉doma꞉no꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉.
Ko꞉sega e ha꞉na꞉nikiyo꞉, eyo꞉ a꞉la꞉ dinali saitakiyo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Godeya꞉yo꞉ ne a꞉ma꞉la꞉ mena꞉ki da꞉fealega, ne a꞉mia꞉no꞉.” A꞉la꞉sa꞉la꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, e ho꞉n ko꞉suwa disa꞉la꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Efesa꞉so꞉ a꞉na ta꞉ta꞉ga꞉, ane.
Fol e ho꞉n ko꞉suwa ha꞉na꞉ga꞉, Sesalia fa꞉la꞉dowakiyo꞉, e Ya꞉lusalem fa꞉la꞉na꞉sa꞉ga꞉, tilidabu kaluka꞉isalemo꞉wo꞉ sagalo꞉ towo꞉ sa꞉la꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, e Antio꞉g amisa꞉n amio꞉ a꞉ma꞉la꞉ ane.
Ho꞉len nolo꞉ Antio꞉g a꞉na sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, e Galesia o꞉lia꞉ Filigia hen a꞉namio꞉, amisa꞉n nowa, amisa꞉n nowa a꞉la꞉sia꞉likiyo꞉, tilidabu kaluka꞉isaleya꞉ asulo꞉wo꞉ halalema꞉ki, wida꞉li sia꞉len.
Fol e sia꞉labikiyo꞉, Yu kalu nowo꞉, Abolos e Alegsandia kalu ko꞉lo꞉ e Efesa꞉s amisa꞉na mesa꞉ni mio꞉. E Godeya꞉ to sa꞉sa꞉lo꞉wo꞉ fanda asululiaki, to digalo꞉lelo꞉ sa꞉la꞉seno꞉ e.
A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ Alana꞉ Man a꞉no꞉ e asulo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ eyo꞉ iligi mada wida꞉sen. E man nolo꞉ semo꞉asulaki, Yona꞉lo꞉ ho꞉na to꞉lolan man a꞉nako꞉ asulo꞉ ko꞉sega elo꞉ Ya꞉suwa꞉lo꞉ dimido꞉ man ko꞉lo꞉ wido꞉ a꞉no꞉ digalo꞉ wido꞉.
Abolos eyo꞉ Yu kaluwa꞉lo꞉ tolo꞉ wida꞉sen aya ha꞉na꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Godeya꞉ mano꞉ mo꞉tagigi sio꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ Bisilia o꞉lia꞉ Akwila o꞉lia꞉ma꞉yo꞉ to widab a꞉no꞉ da꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, a꞉la꞉ma꞉yo꞉ Aboloso꞉ aya tililia꞉ ha꞉na꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Godeya꞉ man nolo꞉ emo꞉wo꞉ dinafa a꞉fanda wido꞉.
A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ Abolos e Akaya hen a꞉na ha꞉na꞉no꞉ dowabikiyo꞉, Efesa꞉s tilidabu kaluka꞉isale iyo꞉ e hamana꞉kiyo꞉ asulo꞉ imilise dowaki, Akayalo꞉ tilidabu kaluka꞉isale a꞉ma꞉yo꞉ e dinafa tililima꞉kiyo꞉, iliyo꞉ mo꞉fo꞉s nowo꞉ sa꞉sa꞉liga꞉fo꞉. Abolos eyo꞉ Akaya fa꞉la꞉dowa꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, Godeya꞉lo꞉ kanulalitabikilo꞉ tilidabu kaluka꞉isale a꞉no꞉, Abolos eyo꞉ mada asufa꞉.
Mo꞉wo꞉ e amisa꞉na꞉ siwa꞉l amio꞉, Yu kalu o꞉lia꞉ towa꞉yo꞉ kego꞉. Eyo꞉ Godeya꞉ to sa꞉sa꞉lo꞉ a꞉no꞉ widakiyo꞉, Ya꞉su e, Godeya꞉lo꞉ Da꞉feyo꞉ Kaluwo꞉ e a꞉la꞉liki dinafa fanda wido꞉.
Abolos e Kolin a꞉na elen amio꞉, Fol e wa꞉l toga ya꞉la꞉ga꞉, Efesa꞉s a꞉na fa꞉la꞉dowakiyo꞉, tilidabu kaluka꞉isale nolo꞉ a꞉na galilia꞉sa꞉ga꞉, imo꞉ dabu ba꞉ba꞉, “Gio꞉ ho꞉gi tilidabu amio꞉, Godeya꞉ Mamayo꞉ a꞉namio꞉ diyo꞉?” To a꞉no꞉ da꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉, iliyo꞉ a꞉ma꞉la꞉bo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “A, Godeya꞉ Mamayo꞉ a꞉lab a꞉la꞉bo꞉, nio꞉ mo꞉dabu.”
<range>
A꞉la꞉sa꞉labikiyo꞉, Fol eyo꞉ a꞉la꞉dabuba꞉ba꞉, “Gio꞉ ho꞉n amio꞉ wangabi to꞉lolo꞉wo꞉?” Iliyo꞉ a꞉ma꞉la꞉bo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Nio꞉ Yona꞉lo꞉ to꞉lolan man a꞉no꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ di.”
A꞉la꞉sa꞉labi, Fol eyo꞉ imo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Yona꞉lo꞉ to꞉lolo꞉ a꞉no꞉ kaluka꞉isaleyo꞉ asugo꞉ nodola꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Godeyo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ kudu hamana꞉ki, a꞉na tolo꞉lo꞉. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ Yon eyo꞉ kalu ni fa꞉s amilo꞉ mia꞉nigab a꞉no꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ tilida꞉da꞉bi a꞉la꞉liki wido꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ kalu elo꞉ sio꞉ a꞉no꞉, Ya꞉su o꞉m.”
To a꞉no꞉ da꞉da꞉ga꞉ dowabiki, iyo꞉ Ya꞉su Kelisowa꞉ wiya iliki, ho꞉na to꞉lolo꞉.
Fol e dagiyo꞉ ili wa꞉la dia꞉tabiki, Mama Nafayo꞉ i amio꞉ a꞉na dowakiyo꞉, iyo꞉ towo꞉ ko꞉li ko꞉lilo꞉ tolaki, Godeya꞉ mano꞉ a꞉na wido꞉.
Kalu a꞉namio꞉, kugula꞉fo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ sen.
Fol e Yu kaluwa꞉lo꞉ tolo꞉ wida꞉sen aya ha꞉na꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, Godeya꞉ ene kaluka꞉isale ko꞉lo꞉ bo꞉fo꞉lab man a꞉na widaki, kaluka꞉isaleyo꞉ to elo꞉ a꞉no꞉ tilidabuma꞉kiyo꞉, e ele otalen a꞉namio꞉ halale wida꞉len.
Ko꞉sega kalu nolo꞉ asulo꞉ ililo꞉wo꞉ halaidaki goladowakiyo꞉, iliyo꞉ Alana꞉ man a꞉namio꞉ mogago꞉ towo꞉ kalaba sio꞉. A꞉la꞉gabiki, Fol eyo꞉ i a꞉na ta꞉ta꞉ga꞉yo꞉, tilidabu kaluka꞉isale o꞉lia꞉yo꞉ egele ha꞉na꞉sa꞉ga꞉, ho꞉leno꞉ tambo amio꞉ Tilanus sugul aya siliki, nenela꞉len.
Donayo꞉ a꞉la꞉ us a꞉namio꞉, to a꞉no꞉ko꞉ nenela꞉li sen ko꞉lo꞉, Yu kalu o꞉lia꞉ Gilig kalu o꞉lia꞉yo꞉ Asia hen a꞉namilo꞉ sen a꞉no꞉ Alana꞉ to a꞉no꞉ tambo dabu.
A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ Godeya꞉yo꞉ Fol eya a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉yo꞉ molo ha꞉na꞉no꞉ ko꞉li ko꞉lilo꞉ dimido꞉.
A꞉la꞉go꞉ko꞉lo꞉, ha꞉fa꞉fdo꞉ halan helebeso꞉g o꞉lia꞉ nanog diakilo꞉ ka꞉lan helebeso꞉g a꞉no꞉lia꞉ Fol amilo꞉ golab a꞉no꞉, dia꞉ha꞉na꞉sa꞉ga꞉, walaf kaluka꞉isalemo꞉wo꞉ dimiab amio꞉, iyo꞉ falele alifelo꞉ a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ nolo꞉ mama mogago꞉ dowo꞉ a꞉no꞉ sili alifo꞉gane.
Yu kalu nolo꞉ mama mogago꞉wo꞉ o꞉lu ga꞉fela꞉li sia꞉sen ko꞉lo꞉ o꞉g a꞉namio꞉ iyo꞉ Ya꞉su Kelisowa꞉ wiya da꞉fe ba꞉dakiyo꞉, mama mogago꞉ nolo꞉ o꞉luga꞉felaki a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Fol elo꞉ Ya꞉su wi ko꞉lo꞉ wido꞉ a꞉na ilikiyo꞉, mama mogago꞉ ge hamana” a꞉la꞉sio꞉.
Bobalo꞉ so꞉mia꞉sen kalu nowo꞉ wiyo꞉ Sikeba, ene so꞉wa doma꞉la꞉fo꞉ a꞉ma꞉yo꞉ a꞉la꞉dimidabikiyo꞉, mama mogago꞉ nolba꞉yo꞉ imo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Ne Ya꞉su asulo꞉. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ Fol elo꞉ dimido꞉wo꞉ dabu. Ko꞉sega kalu ge o꞉ba?”
<range>
A꞉la꞉sa꞉labiki, kalu mama mogago꞉lo꞉ dowo꞉ a꞉ma꞉yo꞉ i o꞉lia꞉ alan bubaki, kalu doma꞉la꞉fo꞉ i a꞉no꞉ yame tanda꞉sa꞉ga꞉, helebeso꞉g tambo bidila꞉ ko꞉lo꞉, iyo꞉ ho꞉bo꞉lo꞉ a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ dalaido꞉.
Yu kalu o꞉lia꞉ Gilig kalu o꞉lia꞉ Efesa꞉sdo꞉ sen a꞉no꞉ tambo, dimido꞉ a꞉no꞉ da꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, iyo꞉ tagilakiyo꞉, Ya꞉su Alan a꞉ma꞉ wiyo꞉ wabudaki, dulugu sio꞉.
A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ tilidabu kaluka꞉isale modo꞉ a꞉no꞉ kalaba ya꞉sa꞉ga꞉, mogago꞉ dimida꞉len ilido꞉wo꞉ tambo foga꞉le sio꞉.
Kalu nolo꞉ fofalo꞉ dimida꞉sen i a꞉ma꞉yo꞉ ene fofalo꞉ dimida꞉sen mo꞉fo꞉s ko꞉lo꞉ kambolola꞉ a꞉no꞉ dia꞉sa꞉ga꞉, tambo siwa꞉la gido꞉. Mo꞉fo꞉s de amilo꞉ gido꞉ a꞉no꞉ di mole agelo꞉wo꞉ 50,000 silba o꞉ngo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ gido꞉.
A꞉la꞉do꞉ dimido꞉ a꞉namio꞉, Alana꞉ to we kalab amio꞉ halaido꞉ fa꞉la꞉dowakiyo꞉, kaluka꞉isaleyo꞉ tambo da꞉da꞉li ha꞉na꞉ga꞉ ilido꞉.
A꞉ma꞉ fa꞉s amio꞉, Fol e Masedonia a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ Akaya hen a꞉no꞉ tinia꞉liki, Ya꞉lusalem ha꞉na꞉no꞉ asulo꞉. “Ne a꞉na ha꞉na꞉ga꞉yo꞉, Lom a꞉namio꞉lo꞉ ha꞉na꞉no꞉ asulo꞉l” a꞉la꞉sio꞉.
A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ Fol elo꞉ asuwa꞉ta꞉sen kalu a꞉la꞉, Timoti o꞉lia꞉ Elastus a꞉no꞉ Masedonia iliga꞉takiyo꞉, e Asia hen a꞉naka o꞉elen.
Ho꞉len a꞉namio꞉ Alana꞉ man o꞉lo꞉ kudu ha꞉na꞉lab a꞉no꞉lia꞉yo꞉ kego꞉wo꞉ mada alan fa꞉la꞉dowo꞉.
Kalu nowo꞉ ene wiyo꞉ Demitias, eyo꞉ silbayo꞉ dia꞉sa꞉ga꞉, madali gode, Atemis a꞉no꞉ misido꞉ momada꞉sa꞉ga꞉, amisa꞉n kalumo꞉ kililia꞉sen. Kalu egeledo꞉ nanogdo꞉ dimidab i a꞉no꞉lo꞉ mole alan dia꞉sen.
Demitias eyo꞉ nanogdo꞉ dia꞉sen kalu a꞉no꞉ tambo kegea꞉sa꞉ga꞉, imo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Nanog nilido꞉ dimida꞉sen wema꞉yo꞉, moleyo꞉ nafa dia꞉sen a꞉no꞉ gio꞉ asulab.
Ko꞉sega kalu we, Fol e nili amisa꞉n o꞉lia꞉ Esia heno꞉lo꞉ wida꞉li sia꞉likiyo꞉ ililima꞉nigab ko꞉lo꞉, nili dagiya꞉lo꞉ dimido꞉ gode a꞉no꞉, gode hendelema a꞉la꞉wido꞉ ko꞉lo꞉, kaluka꞉isaleya꞉ asulo꞉wo꞉ e no꞉nolo꞉ alita ta꞉fo꞉. A꞉la꞉do꞉ go꞉ a꞉no꞉ gio꞉ tamina ba꞉ba꞉ a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ dabu.
A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ o꞉go꞉ nili mole anama꞉kilo꞉ nanogdo꞉ dia꞉sen wema꞉, wi nafayo꞉ mogagila꞉ma꞉ib. Imili weno꞉ ko꞉mba. Ko꞉sega nili gode Atemis, Asia heno꞉ tambo o꞉lia꞉ henfelo꞉ tambo amio꞉ wabuda꞉sen a꞉no꞉, ene wi alan a꞉no꞉ wilo꞉ma doma꞉ib. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ ene gulugululan a a꞉no꞉ o꞉ngo꞉mal a꞉la꞉asuluma꞉ib” Demetius eyo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉.
Kaluka꞉isaleyo꞉ to a꞉no꞉ da꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉, kulufa꞉yakiyo꞉, towo꞉ halaido꞉ sa꞉lakiyo꞉, “Efesa꞉s kaluka꞉isaleya꞉ gode alandeyo꞉ Atemis eka꞉.”
A꞉la꞉ ho꞉le sa꞉la꞉liki ha꞉nakiyo꞉, amisa꞉n kaluka꞉isaleyo꞉ tambo kulufa꞉yo꞉ kegeakiyo꞉, kalu a꞉la꞉ Gaius dia꞉ Alistakus dia꞉ a꞉no꞉, Fol o꞉lia꞉ Masedonia a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉lo꞉ mio꞉ a꞉no꞉ ta꞉lia꞉sa꞉ga꞉, kegea꞉sen a us a꞉na anilia꞉ga꞉ tiane.
Fol e kaluka꞉isalelo꞉ kegeab a꞉namio꞉ towo꞉ sa꞉ma꞉ ha꞉na꞉no꞉ asulo꞉ ko꞉sega, tilidabu kalu iliyo꞉ e mo꞉hamana꞉ki ta꞉li.
A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ Esia hen amilo꞉ gamani misa꞉ kalu nolba꞉yo꞉, Fol e mili ko꞉lo꞉, iyo꞉ e mo꞉hamana꞉kiyo꞉, towo꞉ hagugu saga꞉fo꞉.
Kaluka꞉isale kegeo꞉ a꞉ma꞉yo꞉, noma꞉yo꞉ to ko꞉li halale sa꞉la꞉b amio꞉, noma꞉yo꞉lo꞉ to ko꞉li ka sa꞉la꞉li a꞉lakiyo꞉, tambo no꞉nolo꞉ dowo꞉. A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ iyo꞉ mo꞉wo꞉ wena iliki kegeo꞉ a꞉la꞉bo꞉, kalu modo꞉wo꞉ mo꞉asulo꞉.
A꞉la꞉gabikiyo꞉, Yu kaluwa꞉yo꞉ Alisanda, e susululia꞉ga꞉ tamina ta꞉takiyo꞉, to elo꞉ sa꞉ma꞉no꞉wo꞉ emo꞉wo꞉ a꞉na wala sio꞉. Alisanda eyo꞉ towo꞉ dinafa fanda sa꞉ma꞉no꞉ a꞉la꞉liki, kaluka꞉isale towo꞉ hela꞉fo꞉ma꞉kiyo꞉, dagiyo꞉ da꞉feyo꞉.
Ko꞉sega kalu kegeo꞉ i a꞉ma꞉yo꞉, e Yu kalulo꞉b a꞉la꞉bo꞉ ele ba꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, ofa꞉si a꞉la꞉ a꞉namio꞉, towo꞉ halale sa꞉la꞉likiyo꞉, “Efesa꞉s kaluka꞉isaleya꞉ gode alandeyo꞉ Atemis eka꞉” a꞉la꞉sa꞉la꞉liki, mo꞉bulufo꞉.
A꞉la꞉ga꞉i ha꞉na꞉la꞉ga꞉yo꞉, kiaba꞉ ene nanogdo꞉ diakilo꞉ mo꞉fo꞉sdo꞉ sa꞉sa꞉lan kalu a꞉ma꞉yo꞉, kalu kegeo꞉ tolo꞉ sa꞉la꞉len a꞉no꞉ hela꞉foma a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉yo꞉, imo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Efesa꞉s kalu gio꞉ dabuma. Nili gode alan Atemisa꞉ misido꞉ u momado꞉ a꞉no꞉, akina a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉lo꞉ sulufo꞉ tia꞉ a꞉no꞉lia꞉, ene gulugululan a a꞉no꞉lia꞉yo꞉ Efesa꞉s nili bo꞉fo꞉lo꞉l ko꞉lo꞉ henfelo꞉ kaluka꞉isaleyo꞉ tambowa꞉yo꞉ nili bo꞉fo꞉lab a꞉la꞉ asulufo꞉lab.
To so꞉lo꞉l we hendele a꞉lab ko꞉lo꞉, kalu imilig noma꞉yo꞉ o꞉ngo꞉ma a꞉la꞉bo꞉ mo꞉sa꞉ma꞉ib. A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ giliyo꞉ ha꞉sa dowaki, hala nowo꞉ dimida꞉so꞉bo.
Kalu a꞉la꞉ wema꞉yo꞉ gulugululan ayamilo꞉ kelego꞉ nowo꞉ mo꞉afale di a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉, nili gode mo꞉dio꞉ge sio꞉. Ko꞉sega giliyo꞉ a꞉la꞉ we madali tililia꞉ mio꞉.
Kalu noma꞉yo꞉ Demitius e o꞉lia꞉lo꞉ nanogdo꞉ dian o꞉lia꞉mo꞉wo꞉ hala nowo꞉ dimido꞉lalega, mo꞉walilima꞉no꞉wo꞉ digalo꞉ da꞉lab a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ gamani misa꞉ kalu iyo꞉ sab ko꞉lo꞉, a꞉na tililia꞉ga꞉, ililo꞉ hala dimido꞉ a꞉no꞉ fanda sa꞉ma꞉ni ha꞉na꞉bi.
Giliyo꞉ hala dimido꞉ sa꞉ma꞉no꞉ nolo꞉ dowalega, nili ele difa꞉ a꞉no꞉ kuduha꞉nakiyo꞉, kegea꞉sa꞉ga꞉ ua digalema꞉niki.
Nilido꞉ o꞉gdo꞉ dimido꞉ wema꞉yo꞉ mo꞉lo꞉ma ka dimido꞉ ko꞉lo꞉, nio꞉ o꞉li ka mo꞉walilimabe ko꞉lo꞉ ne tagilab. Gamani kaluwa꞉yo꞉ dabu ba꞉dalega, nio꞉ tolo꞉ mo꞉sa꞉ma꞉no꞉ doma꞉ib.” A꞉la꞉ sa꞉la꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, kaluka꞉isaleyo꞉ hamana꞉ki, towo꞉ sio꞉.
Kaluka꞉isaleya꞉lo꞉ gadiakilo꞉ halaido꞉ to sa꞉la꞉leno꞉ edabikiyo꞉, Fol eyo꞉ tilidabu kaluwo꞉ ho꞉le kegea꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, iyo꞉ halale mesea꞉ki towo꞉ sa꞉la꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, “gio꞉ ta꞉biyo꞉” a꞉la꞉sa꞉la꞉sa꞉ga꞉, e Masedonia hena ha꞉na꞉ni ane.
A꞉na fa꞉la꞉dowa꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, amisa꞉n ko꞉lilo꞉ a꞉na tinia꞉li ha꞉nakiyo꞉, kaluka꞉isaleyo꞉ halale alitaki, mano꞉ wida꞉li ha꞉na꞉la꞉ga꞉, Gilig hena fa꞉la꞉dowo꞉.
E ele otaleno꞉ a꞉naka o꞉sa꞉ga꞉, ho꞉n ko꞉suwa a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ Silia hen ha꞉na꞉no꞉ asulabiki, Yu kaluwa꞉yo꞉ e a꞉namilo꞉ sa꞉mba꞉no꞉ saitab a꞉no꞉ eneno꞉ da꞉da꞉ga꞉, e a꞉ma꞉la꞉ Masedonia hen doba꞉da꞉ ha꞉na꞉ni ane.
Kalu e o꞉lia꞉ aneyo꞉ nowo꞉ Sobada, e Belia amisa꞉n kalu Bilusa꞉ inso꞉, nowo꞉ a꞉la꞉ Alistakus o꞉lia꞉ Sekudus a꞉no꞉ Tesalonaika kalu. Nowo꞉ Gaius, Debe kalu, a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ nowo꞉ Timoti, nowo꞉ a꞉la꞉ Tikikus o꞉lia꞉ Tolofimus a꞉no꞉ Asia kalu.
Toloas amisa꞉n a꞉namio꞉, kalu i a꞉no꞉ tamina ha꞉na꞉sa꞉ga꞉, nio꞉ a꞉na galima꞉ni yasilab.
Sagala꞉sa꞉ga꞉lo꞉ Ma꞉n Mosolo꞉ na꞉sen a꞉no꞉ ho꞉leno꞉ ilita꞉ga꞉, nio꞉ ho꞉n ko꞉suwa disa꞉la꞉sa꞉ga꞉, ho꞉leno꞉ bila꞉fo꞉wo꞉ alita꞉ga꞉yo꞉, iyo꞉ Toloas a꞉na galilia꞉ga꞉, ho꞉len dom a꞉la꞉fo꞉wo꞉ a꞉na sen.
Doma꞉yo꞉ nio꞉ Yesu Asulo꞉ Ma꞉no꞉ naki kegeo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉, Fol e o꞉agela꞉yo꞉ ha꞉na꞉no꞉ ko꞉lo꞉, towo꞉ wida꞉li ha꞉na꞉la꞉ga꞉, nulu uso꞉ a꞉namio꞉ o꞉wida꞉len.
Nio꞉ a iwalulo꞉ a꞉na kegeakiyo꞉, nafayo꞉ modo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ da꞉ifoliki, a꞉na wida꞉la꞉len.
Fol e nuluwo꞉ mano꞉ wida꞉li ha꞉na꞉labiki, kalu so꞉wa nowo꞉, ene wiyo꞉ Yutikus, e a asol fofodo꞉ a꞉namio꞉ ho꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ gulu a꞉ma꞉ wa꞉l ami siliki da꞉da꞉len ko꞉lo꞉, e mida꞉iya꞉la꞉ga꞉, ofowo꞉ ha꞉nakiyo꞉, sulufo꞉ tinda꞉ga꞉, hena beseyo꞉. Iliyo꞉ e gasilia꞉ni tiane ko꞉sega e o꞉ma sowo꞉lo꞉bi ba꞉ba꞉.
A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ Fol e tina꞉ga꞉, so꞉wa a꞉no꞉ a꞉ma꞉ wa꞉la fafola꞉foliki, imo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉ “Gio꞉ tagilaki iliga꞉so꞉bo! So꞉wa we o꞉sab.”
A꞉la꞉bo꞉ sa꞉la꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, Fol e a꞉ma꞉la꞉ fa꞉la꞉na꞉sa꞉ga꞉, ma꞉n dowa꞉fa꞉yo꞉ go꞉go꞉bea꞉sa꞉ga꞉ ua mo꞉no꞉. Ma꞉no꞉ na꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, Fol eyo꞉ to man ko꞉ wida꞉liki aneyo꞉, ho꞉le bidabikiyo꞉, e ta꞉fo꞉gane.
Iyo꞉ a꞉ma꞉la꞉ aya ha꞉nakiyo꞉, so꞉wa a꞉no꞉ mo꞉sowo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ sagala꞉li tililia꞉gane.
Fol e hena ha꞉na꞉no꞉ asulo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ eyo꞉ nio꞉ ho꞉n ko꞉suwa hamana꞉ki dimidali ko꞉lo꞉ nio꞉ ho꞉n ko꞉suwa disa꞉la꞉sa꞉ga꞉, e Asos amisa꞉na galima꞉ni, nio꞉ tamina ane.
Asos a꞉namio꞉, Fol e galilia꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, nio꞉ tambo ho꞉n ko꞉suwa disa꞉la꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Mitilene a꞉na ane.
Ho꞉len no amio꞉, Kios hen aniba ha꞉na꞉la꞉ga꞉ alita꞉ga꞉yo꞉, Samos hen a꞉na fa꞉la꞉dowo꞉. Ho꞉len a꞉ma꞉ fa꞉s amio꞉, nio꞉ ha꞉na꞉la꞉ga꞉, Miletus a꞉na fa꞉la꞉dowo꞉.
Fol eyo꞉ Bentekos ho꞉len a꞉namio꞉ Ya꞉lusalemo꞉ e doma꞉no꞉ a꞉lakiyo꞉, e bo꞉bo꞉ge ha꞉naki, Efesa꞉s amisa꞉n Esia hen a꞉namio꞉, ho꞉leno꞉ modo꞉wo꞉ mo꞉doma꞉no꞉ asulaki, e tigini ane.
Miletus a꞉na silikiyo꞉, Fol eyo꞉ Efesa꞉s sa꞉sdo꞉ bo꞉fo꞉lowan kalu a꞉no꞉ e a꞉na galima꞉ mena꞉ki, towo꞉ saga꞉fo꞉.
Iyo꞉ ya꞉sa꞉ga꞉ elo꞉wa fa꞉la꞉dowabiyo꞉, eyo꞉ imo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Ne tamina Esia hen wena ya꞉sa꞉ga꞉, ho꞉leno꞉ tambo gi o꞉lia꞉ silikilo꞉ dimida꞉len a꞉no꞉ gio꞉ asulufo꞉lab.
Yu kalu iliyo꞉ ne mogagila꞉ma꞉no꞉ saefa꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ ne hida꞉yo꞉ ko꞉li ko꞉lilo꞉ di. Ne Godeya꞉ ene nanog dia꞉li ha꞉na꞉len amio꞉, no꞉no꞉n a꞉ma꞉la꞉ ha꞉ga dota꞉ga꞉, ne si ho꞉no꞉ gula꞉liki, Alana꞉ ene nanog dia꞉leno꞉, gio꞉ asulab.
Niyo꞉ Godeya꞉ mano꞉ kalu kegeo꞉ siwa꞉l amio꞉ kalaba wida꞉sen, a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ gili ayamio꞉lo꞉ walama꞉ni ya꞉sen. Gilo꞉ asuwa꞉fa꞉no꞉ man a꞉no꞉ niyo꞉ mo꞉go꞉lu alitakiyo꞉, gimo꞉wo꞉ tambo fanda wida꞉sen, a꞉no꞉ gio꞉ asulab.
Niyo꞉ Yu kalu o꞉lia꞉ Gilig kalu o꞉lia꞉mo꞉wo꞉ hagugu alitakiyo꞉, ‘gio꞉ asugo꞉ Godemo꞉ nodola꞉sa꞉ga꞉, nili Alan Ya꞉suwa tilidabuma’ a꞉la꞉likiyo꞉ wido꞉.
“O꞉go꞉ ne Godeya꞉ Mamaya꞉lo꞉ sa꞉lab aumb kuduha꞉naki, Ya꞉lusalem ha꞉na꞉nigo꞉l ko꞉lo꞉, a꞉namio꞉ nelo꞉ amio꞉ o꞉bo꞉ngo꞉ fa꞉la꞉doma꞉nigabele babalab.
Ko꞉sega imilig nowo꞉ ne asulufo꞉lo꞉l. Amisa꞉n tambo nelo꞉ sia꞉len amio꞉, Godeya꞉ Mamaya꞉yo꞉ nemo꞉wo꞉ sa꞉la꞉li ha꞉nakiyo꞉, ne hida꞉yo꞉ halaido꞉wo꞉ diaki, dibolowa to꞉loma꞉ib a꞉la꞉liki sa꞉la꞉lab.
A꞉la꞉fo꞉ ko꞉sega, Godeya꞉ kanulo꞉ man to nafa a꞉no꞉ Ya꞉su Alana꞉yo꞉ nemo꞉ walama꞉ki dimi, ko꞉lo꞉ niyo꞉ nanog we dimida꞉i ha꞉na꞉la꞉ga꞉ ililila kibo꞉bowo꞉, ni mela꞉no꞉ we, o꞉li walema꞉no꞉ ko꞉lo꞉lab.
“Ne gi usa sia꞉likilo꞉ Godeya꞉ ene kaluka꞉isale ko꞉lo꞉ bo꞉fo꞉lab man a꞉no꞉ widabilo꞉ da꞉da꞉len kalu gio꞉, ni misio꞉ wa꞉kabiyo꞉ mada mo꞉ba꞉ba꞉ib, a꞉la꞉ asulo꞉l.
Kelego꞉ tambo Godeya꞉lo꞉ gimo꞉lo꞉ asulab a꞉no꞉, ne mo꞉gigili kagayaki, tambo wida꞉len. A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ gio꞉ soma꞉no꞉lo꞉ doba꞉da꞉ dowalega, halayo꞉ nemaka꞉, a꞉la꞉liki fanda so꞉lo꞉l.
<range>
Ginina꞉ma꞉la꞉yo꞉ dinafa bo꞉fo꞉likiyo꞉, sa꞉s kaluka꞉isaleyo꞉ Godeya꞉ ene inso꞉ Ya꞉suwa꞉ ho꞉bo꞉wa꞉lo꞉ kilili a꞉no꞉lo꞉, dinafa bo꞉fo꞉lubi. Kaluka꞉isale a꞉no꞉, Godeya꞉ sibi o꞉ngo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉, Godeya꞉ Mamaya꞉yo꞉ gimo꞉ bo꞉fo꞉melea꞉ki, gio꞉ a꞉na da꞉feyo꞉.
Ne ha꞉na꞉ga꞉ dotalikiyo꞉, kalu nolo꞉ ni fa꞉sa ya꞉siakiyo꞉, saila gasa o꞉ngo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ ya꞉ga꞉, sibiyo꞉ o꞉lu sa꞉ndaki, yasala꞉ma꞉ib, niyo꞉ a꞉la꞉asulab.
A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ gini sa꞉s usamilo꞉ elen nol a꞉ma꞉yo꞉, tilidabu kaluka꞉isaleyo꞉ e kudu mena꞉ki, susulu sa꞉la꞉lakiyo꞉, mano꞉ dikili walama꞉ib.
A꞉la꞉dimidama꞉ib ko꞉lo꞉ gio꞉ dinafa bo꞉fo꞉lubi. Dona otalen us a꞉namio꞉, niyo꞉ gimo꞉wo꞉ hagugu sa꞉la꞉likiyo꞉, ho꞉lenowo꞉lo꞉ nuluwo꞉lo꞉ giyo꞉ nofolakiyo꞉, wida꞉len a꞉no꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ asulufo꞉lubi.
“A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ o꞉go꞉ niyo꞉ gio꞉ Godeya꞉ dagiya difa꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ Godeya꞉lo꞉ kanulo꞉ to man a꞉ma꞉yo꞉ giliyo꞉ asulufo꞉ko꞉ a꞉lalikiyo꞉, to man a꞉ma꞉yo꞉ gio꞉ halale alitakiyo꞉, Godeya꞉lo꞉ malilo꞉ ta꞉felo꞉ kalu nolbo꞉lo꞉ boba kelego꞉ dimi o꞉li aumbo꞉ gimo꞉wo꞉lo꞉ o꞉li o꞉ngo꞉ ka dimia꞉ib.
Ne kalu noma꞉lo꞉ momado꞉ so꞉g o꞉lia꞉ mole da꞉lab a꞉no꞉ ba꞉da꞉ga꞉yo꞉ mo꞉mesela꞉sen.
Niyo꞉ no꞉no꞉n asuwa꞉takiyo꞉, na꞉ dagi wema꞉ nanogo꞉ dimida꞉sa꞉ga꞉, ne o꞉lia꞉lo꞉ dowab a꞉no꞉lo꞉ a꞉ma꞉ asuwa꞉ta꞉sen, a꞉no꞉ gio꞉ asulo꞉.
Giliyo꞉ wa꞉feyo꞉ kalu asuwa꞉foma꞉kiyo꞉, nanog halaido꞉ nilo꞉ dimida꞉sen a꞉no꞉ gio꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ widakigo꞉l. Ya꞉su Alana꞉yo꞉ towo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, ‘Dimiabdo꞉ ge mada sagalo꞉wo꞉ alan doma꞉ib ko꞉sega diabdo꞉ ge sagalo꞉wo꞉ ha꞉lu doma꞉ib.’ To we giliyo꞉ asulufo꞉lubi.”
Fol eyo꞉ to a꞉no꞉ sa꞉la꞉sa꞉ga꞉ edakiyo꞉, iyo꞉ tambo gulalu siliki, Fol e Godemo꞉ dulugu sio꞉.
Iyo꞉ tambo ya꞉foda꞉liki, fafulakiyo꞉ Folo꞉ mimilo꞉.
Fol eyo꞉ iyo꞉ wa꞉kabiyo꞉ mo꞉ba꞉ba꞉ib a꞉la꞉do꞉ sio꞉ a꞉no꞉ iyo꞉ asulakiyo꞉, nofolo꞉ alan dowo꞉. A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ iliyo꞉ e ho꞉n ko꞉suwa disa꞉ma꞉ki, tililia꞉gane.
Nio꞉ Efesa꞉s sa꞉sdo꞉ bo꞉fo꞉lowan kalumo꞉wo꞉ ta꞉biyo꞉ a꞉la꞉bo꞉ sa꞉la꞉sa꞉ga꞉, ho꞉n ko꞉suwa disa꞉la꞉sa꞉ga꞉, ho꞉na꞉lo꞉ hegefa꞉ hen, Ko꞉s a꞉na tigini ane. Ho꞉len a꞉ma꞉ fas amio꞉ nio꞉ ha꞉na꞉sa꞉ga꞉ Lodes a꞉na fa꞉la꞉dowo꞉. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ ho꞉len a꞉ma꞉ fa꞉s amio꞉ nio꞉ Batala a꞉na fa꞉la꞉dowa꞉ta꞉ga꞉yo꞉, ho꞉n ko꞉su nowo꞉, Fonisia hena ha꞉nabiki, nio꞉lo꞉ a꞉na disa꞉la꞉sa꞉ga꞉ ane.
<range>
Nio꞉ ha꞉nakiyo꞉, ho꞉na꞉lo꞉ hegefa꞉ hen Saibulus a꞉no꞉ dagi fo꞉fo꞉ndolo ba꞉da꞉ ta꞉ta꞉i aneyo꞉, Silia hen a꞉na ha꞉naki, Taya amisa꞉na fa꞉la꞉dowakiyo꞉, kelego꞉wo꞉ a꞉na segeselabiki, nio꞉lo꞉ a꞉na sili alifa꞉.
Taya amisa꞉n a꞉namio꞉ tilidabu kaluka꞉isale nolo꞉ a꞉na galilia꞉sa꞉ga꞉, ho꞉len dom a꞉la꞉fo꞉wo꞉ i o꞉lia꞉ silikiyo꞉, Godeya꞉ Mamaya꞉yo꞉ tilidabu kaluka꞉isale o꞉mo꞉wo꞉ asulo꞉wo꞉ dimiabiki, iliyo꞉ Fol e Ya꞉lusalem ha꞉nabena꞉ki, hagugu sio꞉.
Nio꞉ ho꞉len a꞉namilo꞉ mesa꞉no꞉wo꞉ aumbo꞉ edakiyo꞉, amisa꞉n a꞉no꞉ ta꞉ta꞉ga꞉ kaluka꞉isaleyo꞉ so꞉wagalin o꞉lia꞉ negele tambo ho꞉n seya tia꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ a꞉na gulalufo꞉liki, Godemo꞉ dulugu sio꞉.
Dulugu sa꞉la꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉ imo꞉wo꞉ ta꞉biyo꞉ a꞉la꞉bo꞉ sa꞉la꞉sa꞉ga꞉, iyo꞉ amisa꞉na a꞉ma꞉la꞉ ha꞉nabiki, nio꞉ ho꞉n ko꞉suwa disa꞉.
Nio꞉ Taya a꞉na ta꞉ta꞉ga꞉ ha꞉nakiyo꞉, Tolemes amisa꞉na fa꞉la꞉dowa꞉ta꞉ga꞉yo꞉, tilidabu kaluka꞉isale nolo꞉ a꞉na galilia꞉sa꞉ga꞉, ho꞉len imilig nowo꞉ a꞉na ali.
Kea꞉fowo꞉ nio꞉ Tolemes a꞉no꞉ ta꞉ta꞉ga꞉ ha꞉nakiyo꞉, Sesalia a꞉na fa꞉la꞉dowa꞉sa꞉ga꞉, amisa꞉n kalu nowo꞉ Filib ene aya ali. Filib e to nafalo꞉ walama꞉no꞉ kalu nowo꞉ e. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ iliga꞉felo꞉ kalu iyo꞉ asuwa꞉foma꞉ki, tamin amilo꞉ kalu doma꞉la꞉fo꞉ da꞉feyo꞉wo꞉ nowo꞉ e.
Filiba꞉ ida꞉la꞉la꞉ bola꞉so꞉ fa꞉la꞉da꞉in a꞉ma꞉yo꞉ Godeya꞉ towo꞉ widaki, dinali sa꞉la꞉sen.
Nio꞉ ho꞉len nolo꞉ i o꞉lia꞉ a꞉na o꞉dowo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ dinali sa꞉lan kalu nowo꞉, Agabus e Yudia hen a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ a꞉na tia꞉.
E nilo꞉wa fa꞉la꞉dowakiyo꞉, Fola꞉ yafuwo꞉ dia꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Agabus ene gido꞉fo꞉ o꞉lia꞉ dagi o꞉lia꞉yo꞉ yafuwa꞉ mela꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Nilo꞉ dimido꞉l we aumbo꞉, Ya꞉lusalem amilo꞉ yafulo꞉ biso꞉ Yu kalu sab a꞉ma꞉yo꞉ mela꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Yu kaluma imo꞉wo꞉ dimia꞉ib a꞉la꞉bo꞉ Mamaya꞉yo꞉ dinali sio꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ gimo꞉ wido꞉l.”
To a꞉no꞉ da꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉, ni o꞉lia꞉ amisa꞉n kalu a꞉na sen o꞉lia꞉ma꞉yo꞉, Fol e Ya꞉lusalem halonamio꞉ mo꞉hamana꞉kiyo꞉, towa꞉yo꞉ ha꞉nolo sio꞉.
Ko꞉sega Fol eyo꞉ a꞉ma꞉la꞉ sa꞉la꞉kiyo꞉, “Gi ko꞉lo꞉ ya꞉fodait koma꞉yo꞉, ne nofolo꞉wo꞉ alan dowaki, halaido꞉lo꞉ mo꞉doma꞉kilo꞉ dimidait ko꞉ mo꞉wo꞉ ha꞉? Ya꞉lusalemo꞉ ne dibolo amio꞉ mela꞉sa꞉ga꞉ tololalega o꞉li ko꞉m. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ ne Ya꞉su Alana꞉ wi wabulu sa꞉la꞉len a꞉na iliyo꞉ ne sana sowalega, ne o꞉li soma꞉no꞉” Fol eyo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉.
Niliyo꞉ asulo꞉ elo꞉ we mo꞉ ka꞉ma꞉no꞉lo꞉biki, wa꞉kabiyo꞉ mo꞉ha꞉nolo sa꞉ma꞉no꞉ a꞉la꞉likiyo꞉, niliyo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Alana꞉lo꞉ dimidama꞉no꞉ a꞉no꞉ ka fa꞉la꞉doma꞉ki, ta꞉fa꞉no꞉.”
A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ ho꞉len no amio꞉ nio꞉ dimidalia꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Ya꞉lusalem halona ha꞉na꞉no꞉ ane.
Sesalialo꞉ tilidabu kalu nolo꞉ negele ha꞉na꞉sio꞉. Nio꞉ Nasona꞉ aya mesea꞉ki, iliyo꞉ a꞉na tililia꞉gane. Nason e Saibulus kalu ko꞉lo꞉ tamin amilo꞉ tilidabu kalu dowo꞉wo꞉ e.
Nio꞉ Ya꞉lusalem a꞉na fa꞉la꞉dowabiki, tilidabu kaluka꞉isaleyo꞉ ni ba꞉da꞉ga꞉yo꞉ mada sagalo꞉wo꞉ alan dowo꞉.
Ho꞉len a꞉ma꞉ fa꞉s amio꞉, nio꞉ Yemeso꞉ ba꞉ba꞉niki, Foldo꞉ nio꞉ tambo a꞉na ane amio꞉, sa꞉sdo꞉ bo꞉fo꞉lowan kaluwo꞉ tambo a꞉na sena ba꞉ba꞉.
A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ Fol eyo꞉ mada o꞉m a꞉la꞉bo꞉ sa꞉la꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉ Yu kaluka꞉isalemalo꞉wa ha꞉na꞉ga꞉lo꞉, Godeya꞉ nanog dimido꞉ a꞉no꞉, imo꞉wo꞉ malolo꞉ me.
Fol elo꞉ malolab a꞉no꞉ da꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, iliyo꞉ Godeya꞉ wiyo꞉ a꞉na dulugu sio꞉ ko꞉lo꞉, iliyo꞉ Folbo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Nao, o꞉go꞉ Yu kaluka꞉isale tauseno꞉ modo꞉wo꞉ tilidabu ko꞉lo꞉ iyo꞉ Mosesa꞉ ele saefa꞉ a꞉no꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ halale kudu ha꞉na꞉lab a꞉no꞉ ge o꞉go꞉ asula꞉bi.
Giyo꞉ Yu kaluka꞉isaleyo꞉ ha꞉la꞉ o꞉lia꞉lo꞉ sab o꞉mo꞉ wida꞉li siakiyo꞉, Mosesa꞉ ele saefa꞉ a꞉no꞉ Yu kaluwa꞉yo꞉ dila꞉ma꞉ki, a꞉la꞉ widabikiyo꞉, tilidabu kalu wilo꞉ sen a꞉ma꞉ dabu. Gi sa꞉lakiyo꞉, inin so꞉wagalino꞉ do꞉go꞉fo꞉ hege gedea꞉so꞉bo꞉ a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ Yuwa꞉ mano꞉lo꞉ kudu ha꞉na꞉so꞉boka꞉ a꞉la꞉do꞉ gilo꞉ wido꞉ a꞉no꞉ iyo꞉ asulufo꞉lab.
A꞉la꞉go꞉ko꞉lo꞉ niliyo꞉ waga dimidama꞉no꞉wele? Ge wena ya꞉ga꞉ sab a꞉la꞉bo꞉ iliyo꞉ da꞉ba꞉ib ko꞉lo꞉, nililo꞉ gemo꞉lo꞉ sa꞉ma꞉nigo꞉l a꞉no꞉ kudu ha꞉na꞉bi. Kalu fa꞉la꞉da꞉in nolo꞉ Godemo꞉lo꞉ dinali saefa꞉ a꞉no꞉ ne o꞉lia꞉ so꞉l.
<range>
O꞉go꞉ kalu i we, Godeya꞉ siwa꞉l amio꞉ malilo꞉ doma꞉no꞉ man kudu ha꞉na꞉ni ha꞉nab ko꞉lo꞉ gelo꞉ i we o꞉lia꞉ ha꞉na꞉ga꞉ ilido꞉ dimidab o꞉leaum, giyo꞉lo꞉ a꞉la꞉dimidama꞉ni hamana. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ man ililo꞉ dimidan ho꞉len a꞉namilo꞉ boba dimian a꞉no꞉ gi kililia꞉bi. A꞉la꞉dimidalikiyo꞉, iyo꞉ misa꞉ fo꞉no꞉ o꞉li hanula꞉ma꞉ib. Giyo꞉ a꞉la꞉dimidalikiyo꞉, Yu kaluka꞉isaleyo꞉ dimido꞉ a꞉no꞉ ba꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, gi Mosesa꞉ ele saefa꞉ a꞉no꞉ hendele kudu ha꞉nabo꞉lo꞉b a꞉la꞉asuluma꞉ib ko꞉lo꞉ kaluka꞉isalelo꞉ to da꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉lo꞉ sio꞉ a꞉no꞉ madali sio꞉lo꞉b a꞉la꞉asuluma꞉ki, ge i o꞉lia꞉ hamana.
“A꞉la꞉fo꞉ ko꞉sega, Yu kaluka꞉isalema ko꞉lo꞉ tilidabu o꞉mo꞉wo꞉ niliyo꞉ mo꞉fo꞉so꞉ tamina sa꞉sa꞉ligetakiyo꞉, imo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, ‘Gio꞉ madali godemo꞉lo꞉ fofa tolo꞉ dimido꞉ ma꞉no꞉ a꞉no꞉ mogago꞉ dowo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ na꞉so꞉bo. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ no꞉ ho꞉bo꞉ a꞉no꞉lia꞉, no꞉wo꞉ dagasa sili sa꞉nda꞉sa꞉ga꞉, ho꞉bo꞉wo꞉ mo꞉ane a꞉no꞉lia꞉yo꞉, na꞉so꞉bo. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ wo꞉wo꞉ dia꞉ta꞉so꞉bo.’ Nio꞉ a꞉la꞉sa꞉sa꞉lo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉, iyo꞉ man a꞉na kudu hamana꞉kiyo꞉, mo꞉fo꞉so꞉ tamina sa꞉sa꞉liga꞉fo꞉.”
Iyo꞉ a꞉la꞉sa꞉la꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, kea꞉fo amio꞉ Fol eyo꞉ kalu fa꞉la꞉da꞉in i a꞉no꞉ tililia꞉sa꞉ga꞉, iyo꞉ tambo Godeya꞉ siwa꞉l amio꞉ malilo꞉ doma꞉no꞉ man a꞉no꞉ kudu ha꞉na꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, Fol eyo꞉ Godeya꞉ malilo꞉ aya ha꞉na꞉sa꞉ga꞉, bobalo꞉ so꞉mia꞉sen kalumo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Soagelo꞉ imilig nowo꞉ tandaleta꞉ga꞉yo꞉, kalu fa꞉la꞉da꞉in we malilo꞉ doma꞉no꞉wo꞉ elema꞉ib ko꞉lo꞉ iyo꞉ kelego꞉wo꞉ boba somena꞉ki, a꞉ma꞉la꞉ wena ma꞉ib” a꞉la꞉sio꞉.
Soagelo꞉ a꞉no꞉ ko꞉na꞉ma kedefa꞉no꞉ dowabikiyo꞉, Yu kalu Esia hena a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉lo꞉ mio꞉ a꞉ma꞉yo꞉, Fol e Godeya꞉ malilo꞉ aya sena ba꞉da꞉ga꞉yo꞉, iyo꞉ kaluka꞉isaleyo꞉ kegea꞉sa꞉ga꞉, ili asulo꞉wo꞉ da꞉gali felo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉, kalu kegeo꞉ a꞉ma꞉yo꞉ Fol e ta꞉li.
Iyo꞉ halale sa꞉la꞉likiyo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Isolael kalu gio꞉ nio꞉ asuwa꞉foma. Kalu we, heno꞉ tambo wida꞉li sia꞉likiyo꞉, kaluka꞉isalemo꞉wo꞉ Mosesa꞉ ele difa꞉ a꞉no꞉ mo꞉kuduhama꞉naki sio꞉. Eyo꞉ Godeya꞉ Malilo꞉ a we dio꞉ge sa꞉la꞉len. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ o꞉go꞉ eyo꞉ Yu kaluma nolo꞉ Godeya꞉ Malilo꞉ hen we Godeya꞉ siwa꞉l amio꞉ mogagakiyo꞉, tililia꞉mio꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ a꞉lab” a꞉la꞉sio꞉.
(Ililo꞉ sio꞉ a꞉no꞉ mo꞉wo꞉ we. Tamin amio꞉, iyo꞉ Tolofimus, Efesa꞉s kalu e, Fol o꞉lia꞉ Ya꞉lusalem amio꞉ sia꞉labiki ba꞉ba꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ iliyo꞉ Fol e kalu a꞉no꞉ Malilo꞉ a usa tililia꞉mio꞉ a꞉la꞉asulakiyo꞉, towo꞉ halaido꞉ a꞉na sio꞉.)
Amisa꞉n kaluka꞉isaleyo꞉ to a꞉no꞉ da꞉da꞉ga꞉yo꞉, iyo꞉ tambo iligakiyo꞉, ko꞉li ko꞉lile dalalelia꞉ga꞉ kegeakiyo꞉, Fol e a꞉na ta꞉lia꞉sa꞉ga꞉, ha꞉la꞉ya susulia꞉ga꞉ ta꞉taki, Malilo꞉ a a꞉ma꞉ togo꞉ uludo꞉.
Iyo꞉ Folo꞉ samba꞉no꞉ sa꞉ndabikiyo꞉, Lom da꞉la꞉diya꞉ misa꞉ kalu e, ililo꞉ gadiakiyo꞉ yame tandeab a꞉no꞉ da꞉da꞉ga꞉, eyo꞉ da꞉la꞉dilo꞉ bo꞉fo꞉lowan kalu i o꞉lia꞉ da꞉la꞉dileyo꞉lo꞉ tililia꞉ga꞉, nai ya꞉la꞉ga꞉, kalu kegeo꞉lo꞉ halale tandea꞉lab a꞉na fa꞉la꞉dowo꞉. Kaluka꞉isale iliyo꞉ da꞉la꞉di misa꞉ kalu o꞉lia꞉ ene da꞉la꞉dile kalu i a꞉no꞉ fa꞉la꞉dowabiki ba꞉da꞉ga꞉yo꞉, Fol sa꞉nda꞉leno꞉ a꞉na ta꞉fo꞉.
<range>
Da꞉la꞉diya꞉ misa꞉ kaluwo꞉ a꞉na fa꞉la꞉dowakiyo꞉, Fol e ta꞉lia꞉sa꞉ga꞉, sa꞉ni a꞉la꞉ya꞉ melealifoma꞉ki sa꞉la꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, Fol we o꞉b kaluwele, eyo꞉ o꞉b dimido꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉liki dabu ba꞉ba꞉.
Ko꞉sega kaluka꞉isale kegeo꞉ nolba꞉yo꞉ to imiliko꞉ mo꞉sa꞉laki, nolba꞉yo꞉ to ko꞉li ko꞉lilo꞉ sio꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ misa꞉ kalu e, to hendeleyo꞉ mo꞉dinafa da꞉ba꞉no꞉ dowabikiyo꞉, eyo꞉ Folo꞉ da꞉la꞉di kalulo꞉ sa꞉sen aya tililia꞉ hamana꞉ki sio꞉.
Iyo꞉ Folo꞉ aya tililia꞉ga꞉, wo꞉ldo꞉ kodo꞉wa fa꞉la꞉dowabikiyo꞉, kaluka꞉isale kegeo꞉ i a꞉no꞉ gadio꞉wo꞉ mada alan dowo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ da꞉la꞉di kaluwa꞉yo꞉ Folo꞉ fo꞉fo꞉lelia꞉ga꞉ a usa tiane.
Kalu kudu mio꞉ a꞉ma꞉yo꞉ ho꞉le sa꞉lakiyo꞉, “Folko꞉ sanalema!” a꞉la꞉sio꞉.
Iliyo꞉ Folo꞉ a usamio꞉ o꞉tina꞉niki, isagena kagayabiki, Fol eyo꞉ misa꞉ kalumo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉dabuba꞉ba꞉, “Niyo꞉ gemo꞉wo꞉ to nowo꞉ sa꞉ma꞉no꞉wo꞉ o꞉liyo꞉?” Fol eyo꞉ Gilig to a꞉la꞉liki dabu ba꞉dabiki, misa꞉ kalu eyo꞉ a꞉ma꞉la꞉ sa꞉laki, “Ge Gilig towo꞉ asulo꞉lo꞉ka꞉?
Ge Isib kalu ko꞉lo꞉ kalulo꞉ yasala꞉sen kalu 4,000 a꞉la꞉fo꞉wo꞉ gilo꞉ kalalili hena a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ kegeakilo꞉ gamani kalu o꞉lia꞉ gisdo꞉ dia꞉leno꞉, hendele geyele?”
A꞉la꞉dabu ba꞉dabiki, Fol eyo꞉ a꞉ma꞉la꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “A, ne Yu kalu, Silisia hen amio꞉ Tasus amisa꞉n alan a꞉no꞉ kaluwo꞉ ne ko꞉lo꞉ giyo꞉ ne kaluka꞉isale kegeo꞉ wemo꞉wo꞉ towo꞉ sama꞉kiyo꞉, fogo꞉ dimia꞉no꞉wo꞉ o꞉liyo꞉?”
Emo꞉wo꞉ fogo꞉ dimiabikiyo꞉, Fol e wo꞉la꞉ mia kagafo꞉liki, kaluka꞉isale kegeo꞉ a꞉no꞉ hela꞉foma꞉ki, dagiya꞉ da꞉feyo꞉. Kaluka꞉isale iyo꞉ hela꞉tabiki, Fol eyo꞉ kaluka꞉isalemo꞉wo꞉ inin Alam to sa꞉la꞉likiyo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉.
“Ko꞉go꞉do꞉ kalu o꞉lia꞉ nao i, gio꞉ dabuma. Niyo꞉ halalo꞉ mo꞉dimido꞉ a꞉la꞉liki, gimo꞉ fanda sa꞉ma꞉nigo꞉l.”
Iyo꞉ Fol elo꞉ ini Alam tolo꞉ sa꞉lab a꞉no꞉ da꞉dakiyo꞉, iyo꞉ mada hela꞉ta꞉ga꞉ dabu.
Da꞉dabiki, Fol eyo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Ne Yu kalu, Silisia hen amio꞉ Tasus amisa꞉n a꞉na sa꞉la꞉li ko꞉sega, ne amisa꞉n wena siliki anayo꞉. Ne Gamaliel e ha꞉ga꞉ ilikiyo꞉, nili ma꞉muwa꞉ mano꞉ nemo꞉ kefele wido꞉ ko꞉lo꞉, o꞉gdo꞉ gili Godemo꞉lo꞉ kudu ha꞉nab o꞉leaumbo꞉, niyo꞉lo꞉ Godeya꞉ man o꞉leo꞉ngo꞉ dinafa kudu ha꞉na꞉sen.
Niyo꞉ Alana꞉ Mando꞉ kuduha꞉nab a꞉no꞉ ka ta꞉foma꞉ki, niyo꞉ mogagakiyo꞉, tilidabu kalu o꞉lia꞉ ka꞉isale o꞉lia꞉yo꞉ ta꞉lia꞉sa꞉ga꞉, dibolo aya to꞉lo alifela꞉sa꞉ga꞉, nolo꞉ sana sowa꞉sen.
Niyo꞉ a꞉la꞉dimida꞉senka꞉ a꞉la꞉likiyo꞉, Bobalo꞉ so꞉mia꞉sen misa꞉ kaluwo꞉ a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ kaunsil kalu o꞉lia꞉ma꞉yo꞉ hendeleka꞉ a꞉la꞉likiyo꞉ gimo꞉wo꞉ o꞉li malolo꞉ma꞉ib. Iliyo꞉ mo꞉fo꞉so꞉ sa꞉sa꞉la꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Yu kalu Damaskasdo꞉ sab i o꞉mo꞉ dimina꞉ki, nemo꞉ dimiab amio꞉, niyo꞉ tilidabu kaluka꞉isale a꞉namilo꞉ sab a꞉no꞉ Ya꞉lusalem a꞉ma꞉la꞉ tililia꞉sa꞉ga꞉, mo꞉walilima꞉ki, a꞉na ane.
Ofo꞉ disi dowabikiyo꞉, ne Damaskas ko꞉na꞉ma fa꞉la꞉doma꞉no꞉ dota꞉sen amio꞉, wigibole a꞉naka ho꞉ nowo꞉ wabeleg o꞉ngo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ Hebene halona a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ so꞉so꞉lilia꞉ga꞉ tindakiyo꞉, ne ho꞉ a꞉ma꞉ hegelia꞉ga꞉ difa꞉.
A꞉la꞉gabiki ne hena sulufo꞉ tina꞉sa꞉ga꞉, to nowo꞉ nemo꞉ sa꞉labiki dabu. ‘So꞉l, So꞉l, giyo꞉ Ne waga mogagelaya?’
A꞉la꞉sa꞉labiki, niyo꞉, ‘Alan, ge o꞉ba?’ a꞉la꞉sio꞉. ‘Ne Ya꞉su, Nasa꞉la꞉d kalu. Gilo꞉ mogagila꞉leyo꞉ Ne’ a꞉la꞉sio꞉.
Kalu negeledo꞉ ane a꞉ma꞉yo꞉ ho꞉len tia꞉ a꞉no꞉ ba꞉ba꞉ ko꞉sega kalu to nemo꞉lo꞉ sa꞉lab a꞉no꞉ iyo꞉ mo꞉fanda dabu.
A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ niyo꞉ emo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉dabu ba꞉ba꞉, ‘Giyo꞉ ne o꞉b dimidama꞉ki asulaya?’ Niyo꞉ a꞉la꞉dabubo꞉do꞉liki, Alana꞉yo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, ‘Ge dasilia꞉ga꞉, Damaskas amisa꞉n usa ti hamana. A꞉namio꞉, nanog ko꞉lo꞉ gilo꞉ dimidama꞉no꞉wo꞉ noma꞉yo꞉ dinafa wala sa꞉ma꞉ib’ a꞉la꞉sio꞉.
Ne ho꞉ a꞉no꞉ ba꞉ba꞉ amio꞉ siyo꞉ bumale bido꞉ ko꞉lo꞉, mo꞉ba꞉da꞉li ha꞉na꞉no꞉ dowabiki, kalu negeledo꞉ ane a꞉ma꞉yo꞉ nemo꞉ gasilia꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Damaskas ane.
Ne a꞉na sen amio꞉, Damaskas kalu nowo꞉ Ananaias eyo꞉ ne ba꞉ba꞉ni mio꞉. Kalu we Mosesa꞉ ele saefa꞉ a꞉no꞉ kudu ha꞉na꞉len ko꞉lo꞉ Yu kaluka꞉isale amisa꞉ndo꞉ sab a꞉ma꞉yo꞉ e wabulu sa꞉la꞉sen.
Kalu e nelo꞉wa ya꞉ga꞉ kagayakiyo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, ‘Nao So꞉l, ge siyo꞉ a꞉dinafa bo꞉ba꞉ki so꞉lo꞉l’ Wigibole a꞉naka, ni siyo꞉ falele alitabiyo꞉, niyo꞉ e ba꞉ba꞉.
A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ Ananaias eyo꞉ nemo꞉wo꞉ wa꞉ka a꞉la꞉sio꞉, ‘Nili ma꞉muwa꞉ Gode eyo꞉, ge da꞉feakiyo꞉, elo꞉ dimidama꞉no꞉ asulo꞉ aumbo꞉ asuluma꞉ki go꞉ a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ Godeya꞉ ene Digalo꞉ Kalu bo꞉ba꞉ki, a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ ene to sa꞉labo꞉ dabuma꞉ki, ge a꞉na da꞉feyo꞉.
Ene towo꞉ widakiyo꞉, gilo꞉ ba꞉ba꞉ o꞉lia꞉ dabu o꞉lia꞉yo꞉ kaluka꞉isale tambomo꞉wo꞉ gi fanda walama꞉ib.
A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ ge wenamio꞉ o꞉b yasila꞉leya? Ge dasilia꞉ga꞉, ho꞉no꞉ to꞉lola꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, Alan emo꞉ dulugu sa꞉lalikiyo꞉, mogago꞉ gilo꞉wo꞉ hama꞉ib.’ Ananaias eyo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉.
A꞉la꞉go꞉ko꞉lo꞉ ne Ya꞉lusalem a꞉ma꞉la꞉ ya꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Godeya꞉ Malilo꞉ ayamio꞉ dulugu sa꞉la꞉lena, ne ho꞉le ba꞉dakiyo꞉, Alana꞉yo꞉ towo꞉ nemo꞉ sa꞉la꞉lena ba꞉ba꞉. ‘Ge dasima! Giyo꞉ to nilo꞉wo꞉ Ya꞉lusalem wenamio꞉ wida꞉lalega, amisa꞉n kaluka꞉isale iyo꞉ mada mo꞉tigi da꞉ba꞉ib ko꞉lo꞉ ge bo꞉bo꞉ge ta꞉fo꞉ hamana.’
<range>
Niyo꞉ a꞉ma꞉la꞉bo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, ‘Kalu Alan, ne Yu tolo꞉ wida꞉sen a nola tena꞉likiyo꞉, ge amilo꞉ tilidabu kaluka꞉isaleyo꞉ yasala꞉sa꞉ga꞉ dibolo aya to꞉lola꞉sen a꞉no꞉, kaluwo꞉ tambowo꞉ asulufo꞉lab.
A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ Alan, ge wilo꞉ wida꞉sen Sitifen, elo꞉ sana sowo꞉ a꞉namio꞉, niyo꞉lo꞉ e o꞉li sa꞉ndab a꞉la꞉ asulakiyo꞉, Sitifendo꞉ sa꞉ndab kalu a꞉ma꞉ so꞉g ho꞉go꞉fela꞉yo꞉, ni ta꞉lisen.’
A꞉la꞉sa꞉la꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, Alana꞉yo꞉ nemo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, ‘Ge ka hamana. Niyo꞉ ge Yu kalumalo꞉ amio꞉ ko꞉na꞉ iliga꞉fa꞉no꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ ge Ya꞉lusalemo꞉ ta꞉fo꞉ hamana.’ Alana꞉yo꞉ nemo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉.”
Fol eyo꞉ malolabikiyo꞉, kalu kegeo꞉ o꞉li da꞉da꞉len, ko꞉sega Fol eyo꞉ to a꞉no꞉ sa꞉labikiyo꞉, iyo꞉ gadia꞉sa꞉ga꞉, a꞉ma꞉la꞉yo꞉ towo꞉ halale sa꞉lakiyo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Kalu we henfelo꞉ wilo꞉ mesa꞉no꞉ mo꞉ego꞉ ko꞉lo꞉, e sanalema.”
Iliyo꞉ halale tandeakiyo꞉, so꞉g wa꞉l amilo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉wo꞉ hagolia꞉ sandifelaki, sa꞉yo꞉ sagulia꞉ga꞉ sandifelo꞉ A꞉no꞉ ba꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉ ililo꞉ dimidab a꞉no꞉ Fol eyo꞉ mo꞉wo꞉ fanda sama꞉ki, da꞉la꞉diya꞉ misa꞉ kaluwa꞉yo꞉ ene da꞉la꞉dile kalumo꞉ sa꞉lakiyo꞉, Folo꞉ ilo꞉ sa꞉sen a usa tililia꞉ tina꞉ga꞉, yame tandea꞉sa꞉ga꞉, dabu ba꞉da꞉bi a꞉la꞉sio꞉.
<range>
Iliyo꞉ Folo꞉ meya꞉ sa꞉mba꞉no꞉ a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ melabikiyo꞉, eyo꞉ da꞉la꞉dilo꞉ bo꞉fo꞉lowan kalu anib a꞉namilo꞉ kagafo꞉len o꞉mo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉dabuba꞉ba꞉, “Gio꞉ Lom kalule a꞉no꞉ mo꞉ mo꞉walilo꞉ka, madali sa꞉mba꞉no꞉ a꞉la꞉likiyo꞉, gili ele difa꞉ a꞉ma꞉yo꞉ waga saefa꞉ da꞉laba?”
Da꞉la꞉di bo꞉fo꞉lowan kaluwo꞉ to a꞉no꞉ da꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, da꞉la꞉diya꞉ misa꞉ kalulo꞉wa ha꞉na꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Fol elo꞉ to sio꞉ a꞉no꞉ emo꞉wo꞉ sa꞉laki a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Kalu we Lom kalule dowo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ nio꞉ waga dimidama꞉no꞉wele?”
A꞉la꞉sa꞉labikiyo꞉, misa꞉ kalu a꞉no꞉ ha꞉na꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Folbo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉dabu ba꞉dakiyo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Ge hendele Lom kalule dowo꞉lalega, nemo꞉ sama.” “A꞉, ne Lom kalule ko꞉lo꞉lo꞉l” a꞉la꞉sio꞉.
A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ da꞉la꞉di misa꞉ kaluwa꞉yo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Ne Lom kalule doma꞉nikiyo꞉, moleyo꞉ mada modo꞉wa꞉ kilili.” A꞉la꞉sa꞉labikiyo꞉, Fol eyo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Ko꞉sega ne Lom kaluleya꞉ sa꞉la꞉li ko꞉lo꞉ ne Lom kalule ko꞉lo꞉lab.”
To a꞉no꞉ da꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, da꞉la꞉di kalu iyo꞉ emo꞉lo꞉ dabu ba꞉ba꞉no꞉ a꞉la꞉likilo꞉ elen a꞉no꞉ tagilaki, a꞉ma꞉la꞉ gigili kagayo꞉. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ da꞉la꞉di misa꞉ kaluwa꞉yo꞉, Fol e Lom kalule ko꞉lo꞉ sa꞉niya꞉lo꞉ elo꞉ melo꞉ a꞉no꞉ asulakiyo꞉, e tagi dowo꞉.
Da꞉la꞉di misa꞉ kalu e, Yu kaluka꞉isale kegeo꞉ a꞉ma꞉yo꞉ Folbo꞉lo꞉ towo꞉ diga꞉li sio꞉ a꞉no꞉ mo꞉wo꞉ o꞉ba a꞉la꞉liki kedo꞉. A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ ho꞉len no amio꞉ eyo꞉ Fol e fage alita꞉sa꞉ga꞉, bobalo꞉ so꞉mia꞉sen misa꞉ kalu iyo꞉lo꞉, Yuwa꞉ kanisol kaluwo꞉lo꞉ tambo kegenema꞉ki saga꞉felo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ iyo꞉ kegeakiyo꞉, Folo꞉ tililia꞉ga꞉, usa ta꞉fo꞉.
Fol eyo꞉ Kanisol kalu a꞉no꞉ko꞉ si kudu ba꞉da꞉ga꞉yo꞉, a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Ni nao, ne Godeya꞉ nanog dimida꞉ilo꞉ mio꞉ a꞉namio꞉ mela꞉no꞉ nilo꞉ we, Godeya꞉ siwa꞉l amio꞉ no꞉no꞉no꞉ digalo꞉le dimida꞉i mio꞉ a꞉la꞉asulo꞉l.”
A꞉la꞉sa꞉labiki, Bobalo꞉ so꞉mia꞉sen misa꞉ kalu, Ananaias eyo꞉ Fol e anib amilo꞉ kagafo꞉lab o꞉mo꞉wo꞉ Fola꞉ mego꞉fa bolema a꞉la꞉liki sio꞉. A꞉la꞉sa꞉labiki Fol eyo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Ge a o꞉fo꞉f amilo꞉ ho꞉lo꞉ nafa mulu o꞉leo꞉ngo꞉ dowo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ Godeya꞉yo꞉ gelo꞉ bolelema꞉ib. Gio꞉ Mosesa꞉ ele difa꞉ a꞉na ilikiyo꞉ ne mo꞉walilima꞉niki sab ko꞉sega, giyo꞉ ne bolema a꞉la꞉do꞉ sa꞉lab a꞉ma꞉yo꞉ ele saefa꞉ a꞉no꞉ o꞉go꞉sab.”
<range>
Fol eyo꞉ a꞉la꞉sa꞉labiki, e anib amio꞉lo꞉ kalu kagafo꞉len a꞉ma꞉yo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Ge Godeya꞉ Bobalo꞉ so꞉mia꞉sen misa꞉ kalu ko꞉mo꞉wo꞉ giyo꞉ mogagi mada sa꞉laka꞉!”
A꞉la꞉sa꞉labiki, Fol eyo꞉ a꞉ma꞉la꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Nao i ha꞉iyo꞉. E Bobalo꞉ so꞉mia꞉sen misa꞉ kalulo꞉b a꞉la꞉bo꞉ ne mo꞉fanda asulo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ ne a꞉la꞉bo꞉ asulo꞉ kibo꞉bowo꞉, niyo꞉ to a꞉no꞉ mo꞉so꞉mo꞉lo꞉. Mo꞉wo꞉ Godeya꞉ to sa꞉sa꞉lo꞉ amio꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, ‘Gili misa꞉ kalu bo꞉fo꞉lab mo꞉wo꞉ mogago꞉ towo꞉ sa꞉la꞉so꞉bo.’”
Fol e kanisol kalu kegeo꞉ amio꞉, kalu nolo꞉ Fa꞉lisi a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ kalu nolo꞉ Sadusi kalu ko꞉lo꞉ elena ba꞉da꞉ga꞉yo꞉, eyo꞉ imo꞉wo꞉ towo꞉ halale a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Ni nao i, ne Fa꞉lisi kalu a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ dowo꞉lo꞉ Fa꞉lisi kalu. Niyo꞉ Godeya꞉lo꞉ sowo꞉ kalu ko꞉lo꞉ a꞉ma꞉la꞉do꞉ a꞉dasi alifa꞉ib a꞉no꞉ hendele dimidama꞉ib a꞉la꞉liki tilidabu ko꞉lo꞉ ne o꞉go꞉ a꞉na mo꞉walilab.”
Fol eyo꞉ to a꞉no꞉ sa꞉labikiyo꞉, Fa꞉lisi kalu o꞉lia꞉ Sadusi kalu o꞉lia꞉ towo꞉ egele kegakiyo꞉, kanisol iyo꞉ asulo꞉ a꞉la꞉ dowo꞉.
Mo꞉wo꞉ Sadusi iliyo꞉ sowo꞉wo꞉ a꞉ma꞉la꞉yo꞉ mo꞉dasima꞉ib a꞉la꞉tiliasulaki, ma꞉mula꞉ kalu o꞉lia꞉ mama o꞉lia꞉yo꞉ aundo꞉mo꞉ a꞉lab a꞉la꞉ tiliasulo꞉. Ko꞉sega Fa꞉lisi kalu iliyo꞉ a꞉no꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ tambo tili asulab.
A꞉no꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ tiliasulakiyo꞉, towo꞉ halaido꞉ halale tandea꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, elelo꞉ asulo꞉ kalu nolo꞉, Fa꞉lisi ko꞉lo꞉ iyo꞉ dasila꞉sa꞉ga꞉ towo꞉ halaido꞉ kegaki a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Kalu wenamio꞉ hala dimido꞉ nowo꞉ aundo꞉ma ba꞉ba꞉. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ mamayele, ma꞉mula꞉ kaluwele, emo꞉wo꞉ sio꞉wele nio꞉ mo꞉dinafa asulo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ niliyo꞉ e mo꞉walila꞉so꞉bo” a꞉la꞉sio꞉.
To kegakiyo꞉ bubo꞉ a꞉no꞉ mada alan fa꞉la꞉dowabikiyo꞉, da꞉la꞉di misa꞉ kalu e iyo꞉ Folo꞉ ta꞉li siliki susulutandakiyo꞉ gedema꞉ib a꞉la꞉asulaki, ene da꞉la꞉di kaluwo꞉ ho꞉ida꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Folo꞉ gasilia꞉ga꞉, ilo꞉ sa꞉sen aya tililia꞉ hamana꞉ki sio꞉.
O꞉g nulu a꞉namio꞉, Alan e ya꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Fola꞉ aniba kagayaki, emo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Gilo꞉ asulo꞉wo꞉ halaido꞉ dowa꞉bi. Giyo꞉ Ya꞉lusalem kaluka꞉isalemo꞉wo꞉ ne wi ko꞉lo꞉ wido꞉ o꞉li aumbo꞉, Lom a꞉namio꞉lo꞉ a꞉la꞉ka wida꞉bi” a꞉la꞉sio꞉.
Kea꞉fowo꞉, Yu kalu iyo꞉ nenela꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, Folo꞉ sana soma꞉no꞉ a꞉la꞉saefa꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ Folo꞉ semo꞉sana sowo꞉ amio꞉, iliyo꞉ ma꞉no꞉ o꞉lia꞉ ho꞉n o꞉lia꞉yo꞉ mada semo꞉naki elefo꞉ difa꞉ ko꞉lo꞉, Folo꞉ sana sowa꞉sa꞉ga꞉ ami ma꞉no꞉wo꞉ a꞉na ma꞉no꞉ a꞉la꞉ tili saefa꞉.
Tolo꞉ saefa꞉ kalu agelo꞉wo꞉ do꞉la꞉fo꞉ fa꞉la꞉da꞉in a꞉no꞉ tinio꞉ a꞉ma꞉ saefa꞉.
Iyo꞉ ha꞉na꞉sa꞉ga꞉, bobalo꞉ so꞉mia꞉sen kalu i o꞉lia꞉ Yu ko꞉go꞉do꞉ kalu o꞉lia꞉mo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Nio꞉ Folo꞉ semo꞉sanaifa꞉ amio꞉, ho꞉n o꞉lia꞉ ma꞉n o꞉lia꞉yo꞉ elefo꞉ dia꞉to꞉l ko꞉lo꞉ semo꞉ma꞉no꞉ a꞉la꞉liki tili salia꞉ difa꞉.
A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ gi o꞉lia꞉ kanisol kalu gio꞉ ha꞉na꞉sa꞉ga꞉, da꞉la꞉di misa꞉ kalumo꞉wo꞉ dikili sa꞉lakiyo꞉, Folbo꞉lo꞉ mo꞉walilo꞉ a꞉no꞉ wa꞉ka a꞉fanda da꞉ba꞉no꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ tililia꞉ mena꞉ki, gio꞉ sa꞉ma꞉ni hamana. Da꞉la꞉di iliyo꞉ Fol e tililia꞉ yalikiyo꞉, gilo꞉ amio꞉ o꞉fa꞉la꞉doma꞉ni yaliki, niliyo꞉ e usa sa꞉mba꞉no꞉. Nio꞉ a꞉la꞉dimidama꞉no꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ gio꞉ to a꞉no꞉ sa꞉ma꞉ni hamana.”
To nenelakiyo꞉ saitab a꞉no꞉, Fola꞉ e babo a꞉ma꞉ da꞉da꞉la꞉ga꞉yo꞉, e da꞉la꞉dilo꞉ sa꞉sen aya ha꞉na꞉ga꞉, Folbo꞉wo꞉ to a꞉no꞉ malolo꞉ me.
Fol e to a꞉no꞉ da꞉da꞉ga꞉yo꞉, da꞉la꞉dilo꞉ bo꞉fo꞉lowan kalu nowo꞉ ho꞉lelia꞉sa꞉ga꞉, emo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “So꞉wa wema꞉yo꞉ da꞉la꞉diya꞉ misa꞉ kalumo꞉wo꞉ to nowo꞉ sama꞉ mio꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ e a꞉na tililia꞉ hamana” a꞉la꞉sio꞉.
A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ da꞉la꞉di bo꞉fo꞉lowan kaluwa꞉yo꞉ so꞉wa a꞉no꞉ tililia꞉ga꞉, ene misa꞉ kalumo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “So꞉wa wema꞉yo꞉ to nolo꞉ gemo꞉ sa꞉ma꞉ni mio꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ dibolo kalu Fol eyo꞉ gelo꞉wa tililia꞉ hamana a꞉la꞉liki, nemo꞉ dabu ba꞉dabiki, a꞉na tililia꞉ mio꞉.”
Da꞉la꞉diya꞉ misa꞉ a꞉ma꞉yo꞉ so꞉wa a꞉no꞉ dagiya gasiliya꞉ga꞉, o꞉fo꞉f doba꞉ba꞉ ta꞉ta꞉ga꞉ ha꞉nakiyo꞉, “Ge nemo꞉wo꞉ o꞉b sa꞉ma꞉ni mio꞉wo꞉?” a꞉la꞉dabu ba꞉ba꞉.
So꞉wa a꞉ma꞉yo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Yu kalu iliyo꞉ nenela꞉sa꞉ga꞉ towo꞉ saefa꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ aliyo꞉ kanisolo꞉ amio꞉ Folo꞉ ge tililia꞉ ya꞉bi a꞉la꞉bo꞉ Yu kaluwa꞉yo꞉ gemo꞉wo꞉ dabu ba꞉ba꞉ib. Iyo꞉ Folbo꞉lo꞉ mo꞉walilo꞉ a꞉no꞉ wa꞉ka a꞉fanda da꞉ba꞉no꞉ a꞉la꞉likiyo꞉ ge dikili sa꞉ma꞉ib.
Ko꞉sega ililo꞉ dabuba꞉dab aumbo꞉ dimida꞉so꞉bo. Mo꞉wo꞉ kaluwo꞉ do꞉la꞉fo꞉ fa꞉la꞉da꞉in a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ tininila꞉ a꞉no꞉ usa yasila꞉ga꞉, Folo꞉ a꞉na banaifo꞉la꞉ga꞉ sa꞉mba꞉ib. Iliyo꞉ Folo꞉ mo꞉sanaitakiyo꞉, ho꞉n o꞉lia꞉ ma꞉n o꞉lia꞉yo꞉ elefo꞉ difa꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ semo꞉ma꞉ib a꞉la꞉liki tili saefa꞉ ko꞉lo꞉lab. Iyo꞉ dimidalia꞉sa꞉ga꞉, gilo꞉ a꞉ma꞉la꞉ to sa꞉labo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ yasilab.”
To a꞉no꞉ da꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, da꞉la꞉diya꞉ misa꞉ kaluwa꞉yo꞉ so꞉wa o꞉mo꞉wo꞉ hagugu sa꞉lakiyo꞉, “Giyo꞉ to we nemo꞉wo꞉ sio꞉ka꞉ a꞉la꞉likiyo꞉, kalu nolbo꞉wo꞉ sa꞉la꞉so꞉bo” A꞉la꞉sa꞉la꞉sa꞉ga꞉ so꞉wa a꞉no꞉ a꞉ma꞉la꞉ iliga꞉fo꞉.
Da꞉la꞉diya꞉ misa꞉ kalu eyo꞉, da꞉la꞉dilo꞉ bo꞉fo꞉lowan kalu a꞉la꞉ nowo꞉ ho꞉ida꞉sa꞉ga꞉, a꞉la꞉mo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Ga꞉go꞉ da꞉la꞉di kalu 200 a꞉la꞉fo꞉, a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ hos wa꞉la silikilo꞉ da꞉la꞉di kaluwo꞉ 70 a꞉la꞉fo꞉ a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ da꞉ inso꞉lo꞉ sandima꞉no꞉wo꞉ 200 a꞉la꞉fo꞉ a꞉no꞉ tambo dimidalia꞉sa꞉ga꞉, nulu ofa꞉siyo꞉ agato꞉wa dowalikiyo꞉, Sesalia amisa꞉na ha꞉na꞉bi.
A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ Fol e dinafa hamana꞉kiyo꞉, hos nolo꞉ emo꞉ dimia꞉sa꞉ga꞉, a꞉na asita꞉ga꞉, gamani misa꞉ kalu, Fela꞉ksdo꞉ amio꞉ fa꞉la꞉doma꞉ ha꞉na꞉bi.”
To a꞉no꞉ sa꞉la꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, eyo꞉ mo꞉fo꞉so꞉ iliga꞉takiyo꞉ a꞉la꞉sa꞉sa꞉lo꞉.
Ne Kolodius Lisias, niyo꞉ mo꞉fo꞉so꞉ we gamani misa꞉ alan kalu Fela꞉ks gemo꞉ sa꞉sa꞉liga꞉to꞉l. Niyo꞉ sagalo꞉ towo꞉ gemo꞉wo꞉ so꞉lo꞉l.
Yu kalu iliyo꞉ kalu we ta꞉lia꞉sa꞉ga꞉ sana soma꞉nigabikiyo꞉, niyo꞉ e Lom kalulo꞉b asula꞉sa꞉ga꞉, niyo꞉ o꞉lia꞉ ni da꞉la꞉di o꞉lia꞉ma꞉ ha꞉na꞉sa꞉ga꞉, e asuwa꞉taki gasili.
Niyo꞉ Yu kalu ililo꞉ diga꞉li sio꞉ a꞉no꞉ mo꞉wo꞉ fanda ba꞉ba꞉no꞉ a꞉la꞉liki, e Yuwa꞉ kanisolo ilo꞉ amio꞉ tililia꞉gane.
E mo꞉walili ba꞉ba꞉ amio꞉, iliyo꞉ Yuwa꞉ ini ele a꞉no꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ alobana kedo꞉ ko꞉sega, kalu we ni ba꞉ba꞉ amio꞉, e dibolo a to꞉loma꞉no꞉ hala dimido꞉ a꞉no꞉ mo꞉ba꞉ba꞉. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ e sana soma꞉no꞉ hala dimido꞉wo꞉ mo꞉ba꞉ba꞉.
Yu kalu ililo꞉ kalu we ko꞉lo꞉ sana soma꞉no꞉ a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉lo꞉ dimidaitab a꞉no꞉ ne da꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉, niyo꞉ Fol e gelo꞉wa bo꞉bo꞉ge iliga꞉to꞉l. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ e o꞉lia꞉lo꞉ kego꞉ kalu iyo꞉lo꞉ gelo꞉wa ya꞉sa꞉ga꞉, gi siwa꞉la mo꞉walilaki sama꞉kiyo꞉, gelo꞉wa hamana a꞉la꞉sio꞉. Eyo꞉ mo꞉fo꞉so꞉ a꞉na sa꞉sa꞉lo꞉.
Da꞉la꞉di kalu iyo꞉, ini misa꞉ kaluwa꞉lo꞉ sio꞉ aumb kudu ha꞉naki, nuluwo꞉ Folo꞉ tililia꞉ ha꞉na꞉sa꞉ga꞉ Antibatilis amisa꞉n a꞉na fa꞉la꞉dowo꞉.
Kea꞉fowo꞉ hos wa꞉la silikilo꞉ da꞉la꞉di kalu iyo꞉ Folo꞉ a꞉ma꞉ka tililia꞉ga꞉ ha꞉nabikiyo꞉, da꞉la꞉di kalu nolo꞉ a꞉ma꞉la꞉ ilo꞉ sa꞉sen aya ane.
Da꞉la꞉di kalu Foldo꞉ tililia꞉gane a꞉no꞉ Sesalia fa꞉la꞉dowakiyo꞉, iliyo꞉ gamani misa꞉ kalumo꞉wo꞉ mo꞉fo꞉so꞉ dimiakiyo꞉, Fol elo꞉ tililia꞉ga꞉ elo꞉wa ta꞉fo꞉.
Gamani misa꞉ kaluwa꞉yo꞉ mo꞉fo꞉s sa꞉sa꞉lo꞉ a꞉no꞉ agela꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Fol emo꞉wo꞉, “Gi heno꞉ o꞉ba?” a꞉la꞉dabu ba꞉ba꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ misa꞉ kaluwa꞉yo꞉ Folo꞉ Silisia kalulo꞉b a꞉la꞉asulakiyo꞉, emo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Gemo꞉lo꞉ diga꞉li sio꞉ kalu a꞉no꞉ wena fa꞉la꞉dowalikiyo꞉, ge nio꞉ a꞉na mo꞉walili da꞉ba꞉no꞉.” A꞉la꞉sa꞉la꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, Fol e Helo꞉da꞉ a alan a꞉namilo꞉ dibolo a a꞉na disalifoliki, bo꞉fo꞉melea꞉ki ta꞉fo꞉.
<range>
Ho꞉len bila꞉fo꞉wo꞉ ta꞉ta꞉ga꞉yo꞉, Bobalo꞉ so꞉mia꞉sen misa꞉ kalu, Ananaiaso꞉ a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ Yu ko꞉go꞉do꞉ kalu nolo꞉ a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ mo꞉walilabdo꞉ asuwa꞉ta꞉sen kalu Tetuluso꞉, iyo꞉ Sesalia ha꞉na꞉sa꞉ga꞉, gamani misa꞉ kalu si wa꞉l amio꞉ Fol elo꞉ hala dimido꞉ diga꞉li sio꞉ a꞉no꞉ fanda sio꞉.
Folo꞉ a usa mena꞉ki ho꞉lelia꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, Tetulus eyo꞉ Folbo꞉lo꞉ diga꞉li sio꞉ a꞉na falasilema꞉kiyo꞉, Fela꞉ksbo꞉wo꞉ malolo꞉ miakiyo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Fela꞉ks kalu alan, hen nililo꞉ we gilo꞉ bo꞉fo꞉len amio꞉, nio꞉ sagala꞉liki ha꞉sa sa꞉i mio꞉ a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ gilo꞉ asulo꞉ alan nafa koma꞉yo꞉ nio꞉ asuwa꞉ta꞉sen.
Gilo꞉ tambo dimido꞉ a꞉no꞉ asulakiyo꞉, amisa꞉no꞉ tambowa꞉yo꞉ mada sagalaki, nio꞉ mada o꞉m a꞉la꞉sa꞉la꞉sen.
Gio꞉ mo꞉beabena꞉ki, sambowo꞉ mo꞉sa꞉ma꞉no꞉ ko꞉sega giyo꞉ nimo꞉wo꞉ nofolakiyo꞉, nilo꞉ to ha꞉lu sa꞉ma꞉nigo꞉l a꞉no꞉ ge mada dabuma꞉ki, sa꞉ma꞉nigo꞉l.
Kalu we kulufa꞉yakilo꞉ hideya꞉lo꞉ mo꞉mo꞉da꞉seno꞉ e a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ Yu kaluka꞉isaleyo꞉ heno꞉ tambo sen amio꞉ e gadima꞉kiyo꞉ eyo꞉ digene mia꞉sen. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ eyo꞉ gamani gilo꞉ we mogagima꞉ki, e misa꞉ doma꞉no꞉ a꞉laki, iliyo꞉ Nasalet gamani a꞉la꞉wikilo꞉. Eyo꞉ a꞉la꞉dimidabiyo꞉, nio꞉ ba꞉ba꞉.
A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ eyo꞉ Malilo꞉ Ayo꞉ mogagima꞉nigabiki, nio꞉ e a꞉na ta꞉li. Fela꞉ks, Kalu alan giyo꞉ enebo꞉wo꞉ mo꞉walilaka dabu ba꞉dakiyo꞉, nililo꞉ so꞉lo꞉l we, gio꞉ hendelelo꞉b a꞉la꞉asuluma꞉ib.” Tetulus eyo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉.
<range>
<range>
Yu kalu kegeo꞉ sen a꞉ma꞉yo꞉ Tetulus elo꞉ hendele sa꞉lab a꞉la꞉liki, iliyo꞉lo꞉ sio꞉.
A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ gamani misa꞉ kalu Fela꞉ks eyo꞉ Fol e towo꞉ sama꞉kiyo꞉ fogo꞉ dimiabiki, Fol eyo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Ge donayo꞉ modo꞉wo꞉ wena silikiyo꞉, Yu kaluka꞉isale nio꞉, giyo꞉ bo꞉fo꞉likiyo꞉ mo꞉walila꞉sen ko꞉lo꞉, niyo꞉ halalo꞉ mo꞉dimido꞉ a꞉la꞉likiyo꞉, o꞉go꞉ ne towo꞉ saga꞉la꞉li fanda sa꞉ma꞉nigo꞉l.
Ho꞉len kugula꞉fo꞉ us a꞉namio꞉, ne Ya꞉lusalem ha꞉na꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Godemo꞉ wabulu sa꞉ma꞉ni ane ko꞉lo꞉ giyo꞉ nilo꞉ sa꞉labo꞉ hendelelo꞉b a꞉la꞉likilo꞉, kalu nolbo꞉lo꞉ dabu kelema꞉no꞉wo꞉ halaido꞉ma.
Ne Godeya꞉ Malilo꞉ A amio꞉ kalu nol o꞉lia꞉yo꞉ towa꞉lo꞉ kego꞉wo꞉, Yu kalu wema꞉yo꞉ mada mo꞉ba꞉ba꞉. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ ne Yu kaluwa꞉lo꞉ tolo꞉ wida꞉sen ayamio꞉lo꞉, amisa꞉na sia꞉likiyo꞉lo꞉, kaluka꞉isaleyo꞉ ni digene alitabikiyo꞉, iyo꞉ mada mo꞉ba꞉ba꞉.
A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ ililo꞉ nemo꞉lo꞉ diga꞉lilakilo꞉ mo꞉walilab we, nilo꞉ dimido꞉wo꞉ we hendele a꞉la꞉bo꞉, iliyo꞉ mo꞉fanda walama꞉ib.
Ko꞉sega nelo꞉ golo꞉wo꞉ imilig nowo꞉ gemo꞉wo꞉ fanda sa꞉ma꞉nigo꞉l. Kalu i wema꞉yo꞉ Alana꞉ Mando꞉ kudu ha꞉nab a꞉no꞉ hala kudu ha꞉nab a꞉la꞉sio꞉. A꞉la꞉fo꞉ ko꞉sega, niyo꞉ nili ma꞉muwa꞉ Gode a꞉no꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ wabudakiyo꞉, Alana꞉ man a꞉no꞉ kuduha꞉na꞉sen. Mosesa꞉ ele sa꞉sa꞉lo꞉ o꞉lia꞉ dinali sa꞉lan kaluwa꞉lo꞉ to sa꞉sa꞉lifa꞉ a꞉no꞉ tambo ne tilidabu. Yuwa꞉ man a꞉no꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ kudu ane.
A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ digalo꞉ kalu sowo꞉wo꞉lo꞉, mogago꞉lo꞉ dimidan kalu sowo꞉wo꞉lo꞉ Godeya꞉lo꞉ a꞉ma꞉la꞉ a꞉dasi alifa꞉ib a꞉no꞉ ne hendele tilida꞉daki, yasilo꞉l. Tilida꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉lo꞉ nilo꞉ yasilo꞉l aumb, kalu i wema꞉lo꞉ yasilab.
A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ niyo꞉ mo꞉keleasuluma꞉kiyo꞉, Gode o꞉lia꞉ kaluka꞉isale o꞉lia꞉ma꞉ siwa꞉l amio꞉, ho꞉leno꞉ tambo niyo꞉ digalo꞉ man dimida꞉sen.
Dona nolo꞉ ta꞉ta꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, ne a꞉ma꞉la꞉ Ya꞉lusalem ya꞉ga꞉, niasi kaluka꞉isale usamilo꞉ wa꞉feyo꞉ kalu o꞉mo꞉wo꞉ moleyo꞉ boba dimiaki, Godemo꞉wo꞉ boba so꞉mia꞉ni mio꞉.
