Niyo꞉ Godeya꞉ siwa꞉la malilo꞉ dowan man a꞉no꞉ kudu ane ko꞉lo꞉, Godeya꞉ Malilo꞉ a us a꞉na ne ti ane amio꞉, kalu i wema꞉yo꞉ ne a꞉na ba꞉ba꞉. Ko꞉sega kaluka꞉isaleyo꞉ nelo꞉amio꞉ mo꞉kegeo꞉ a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ kaluka꞉isale egelebo꞉ gadima꞉kilo꞉ digini mian man a꞉no꞉ aundo꞉ma elen.
Ho꞉len a꞉namio꞉, Yu kalu nolo꞉ Asia hen a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ mio꞉ a꞉no꞉ a꞉na sen ko꞉lo꞉ i a꞉ma꞉yo꞉ nemo꞉wo꞉ diga꞉li sa꞉lakilo꞉ mo꞉walilima꞉no꞉wo꞉ dowo꞉lalega, kalu i a꞉no꞉ gi siwa꞉la kagafo꞉liki ne a꞉na mo꞉walilima꞉no꞉ o꞉li.
Kalu i a꞉no꞉ wilo꞉malalega, kalu o꞉go꞉do꞉ sab wema꞉yo꞉, kanisol inido꞉wo꞉ Ya꞉lusalem kegeakilo꞉ ne mo꞉walilo꞉ a꞉namio꞉, nilo꞉ hala dimido꞉ ba꞉ba꞉ a꞉no꞉ gemo꞉wo꞉ sama꞉ki, giyo꞉ imo꞉wo꞉ dabu bo꞉ba.
Ililo꞉ to ne o꞉lia꞉lo꞉ golo sa꞉ma꞉ibo꞉ imilig we. Iliyo꞉ nelo꞉ mo꞉walilo꞉ amio꞉, ne halale sa꞉laki, ‘Godeya꞉lo꞉ sowo꞉ kalu ko꞉lo꞉ a꞉ma꞉la꞉do꞉ a꞉dasi alifa꞉ib a꞉no꞉ hendele dimidama꞉ib a꞉la꞉liki niyo꞉ tilidabu ko꞉lo꞉ ne o꞉go꞉ a꞉na mo꞉walilab.’” Fol eyo꞉ to a꞉na edo꞉.
Fela꞉ks eyo꞉ Alana꞉ Man kudu ha꞉nan a꞉no꞉ e asulo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ mo꞉walilima꞉no꞉ a꞉na ele alita꞉ga꞉, imo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Da꞉la꞉diya꞉ misa꞉ kalu, Lisias, e yalikiyo꞉, gililo꞉ mo꞉walilab we, niyo꞉ a꞉na alobana sa꞉ma꞉no꞉.”
A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ Fela꞉ks eyo꞉ da꞉la꞉di bo꞉fo꞉lowanbo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Giyo꞉ Fol e dibolo aya disa꞉la꞉bi. Ko꞉sega, ene mili kaluwa꞉yo꞉ eka asuwa꞉foma꞉ki, togo꞉ ka꞉la꞉so꞉bo” a꞉la꞉sio꞉.
Ho꞉len nolo꞉ ta꞉ta꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, Fela꞉ksa꞉ inga Dulusia, e Yu ka꞉isale ko꞉lo꞉ a꞉la꞉yo꞉ Folo꞉ disalifo꞉labdo꞉ a꞉na ha꞉na꞉ga꞉yo꞉, Folo꞉ ho꞉lelia꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Fol elo꞉ Ya꞉su Keliso tilidabu a꞉no꞉ malolabiki, a꞉la꞉yo꞉ da꞉da꞉len.
Fol eyo꞉ digalo꞉ doma꞉no꞉ man o꞉lia꞉ kalu enen a꞉ma꞉la꞉lo꞉ asulo꞉ tilidoma꞉no꞉ man o꞉lia꞉ Godeya꞉ tif amilo꞉ nio꞉ mo꞉walilima꞉no꞉ man a꞉no꞉ widabikiyo꞉, Fela꞉ks e tagila꞉sa꞉ga꞉, a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “A꞉naka elema! Ne tif amio꞉ ho꞉leno꞉ dowalega, ge ho꞉ida꞉sa꞉ga꞉, a꞉na toma꞉no꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ ge hamana.”
A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ Fela꞉ks eyo꞉ Fola꞉yo꞉ emo꞉wo꞉ moleyo꞉ dimina꞉ki a꞉la꞉asulo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ ho꞉len nol amio꞉ e Folo꞉ ho꞉ida꞉sa꞉ga꞉, towo꞉ nenela꞉sen.
Dona a꞉la꞉yo꞉ ta꞉ta꞉ga꞉yo꞉, Bosias Festus e gamani misa꞉ kalu ho꞉gi dowabikiyo꞉, Fela꞉ks eyo꞉ Yu kaluka꞉isale sagalema꞉kiyo꞉, Folo꞉ dibolo aya ka o꞉mesea꞉ki ta꞉taki, Fela꞉ks e misa꞉ kalu eleno꞉ a꞉na ta꞉fo꞉.
Festus e gamani misa꞉ ho꞉giyo꞉ dowakiyo꞉, ho꞉len otaleno꞉ Sesalia sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, e Ya꞉lusalem halonamio꞉ a꞉na ane.
Festus e a꞉na fa꞉la꞉dowabikiyo꞉, bobalo꞉ so꞉mia꞉sen misa꞉ kalu i o꞉lia꞉ Yu ko꞉go꞉do꞉ kalu i o꞉lia꞉yo꞉ elo꞉wa fa꞉la꞉dowakiyo꞉, Fol elo꞉ hala dimido꞉ a꞉no꞉ emo꞉wo꞉ malolo꞉ me.
Festus eyo꞉ iyo꞉ asuwa꞉foma꞉ki, iliyo꞉ emo꞉wo꞉ dabu ba꞉dakiyo꞉, Fol e a꞉ma꞉la꞉ Ya꞉lusalem iliga꞉foma꞉ki, ha꞉na꞉lo sio꞉. Mo꞉wo꞉ Fol e Ya꞉lusalemo꞉ yalikiyo꞉, iliyo꞉ e toga banaifo꞉la꞉ga꞉ a꞉na sana soma꞉no꞉ dimidaifo꞉liki, dabu ba꞉ba꞉.
Iliyo꞉ a꞉la꞉dabu ba꞉dabiki, Festus eyo꞉ a꞉ma꞉la꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Fol e Sesalia dibolo aya sab a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ ne a꞉namio꞉ ko꞉na꞉ma ha꞉na꞉no꞉.
A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ Fol e hendele halabo꞉ dimido꞉lalega, misa꞉ kalu gililo꞉wo꞉ nolo꞉ ne o꞉lia꞉ ha꞉na꞉sa꞉ga꞉, a꞉na mo꞉walilima꞉no꞉” a꞉la꞉sio꞉.
Festus e ho꞉len ola꞉fo꞉ o꞉ do꞉la꞉fo꞉ i o꞉lia꞉ o꞉la꞉ga꞉yo꞉, e Sesalia a꞉na ti ane ko꞉lo꞉, ho꞉len a꞉ma꞉ fa꞉s amio꞉, e mo꞉walilima꞉no꞉ aya ha꞉na꞉ga꞉ silikiyo꞉, Fol e mena꞉ki, ho꞉ido꞉.
Fol e a꞉na tindabikiyo꞉, Yu kalu Ya꞉lusalem a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉lo꞉ mio꞉ i a꞉ma꞉yo꞉, Fol e banagalia꞉foliki, elo꞉ mogago꞉ dimido꞉ a꞉no꞉ Festus e dabuma꞉ki sa꞉la꞉len ko꞉sega, hendele sa꞉lab a꞉la꞉bo꞉ mo꞉fanda asulo꞉.
Iliyo꞉ emo꞉wo꞉ diga꞉li sa꞉la꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, Fol eyo꞉ enena꞉ma꞉la꞉ asuwa꞉takiyo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Niyo꞉ Yuwa꞉ mano꞉ mada mo꞉o꞉go꞉so꞉ a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉, Godeya꞉ Malilo꞉ a a꞉no꞉ mo꞉mogagila꞉ a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ gamani misa꞉ kalu Sisamo꞉wo꞉ mogago꞉lo꞉ mo꞉dimido꞉.”
Fol eyo꞉ a꞉la꞉sa꞉la꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Festus eyo꞉ Yu kaluwo꞉ sagale alitakiyo꞉, Folbo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉dabu ba꞉ba꞉, “Ge Ya꞉lusalem ha꞉na꞉sa꞉ga꞉, ililo꞉ gemo꞉lo꞉ diga꞉lilab we, ni siwa꞉la mo꞉walilima꞉no꞉wo꞉ o꞉liyele?”
A꞉la꞉dabu ba꞉dabiki, Fol eyo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “A, ne Sisa elo꞉ mo꞉walilan a wena mo꞉walilab ko꞉lo꞉ ne wenaka mo꞉walilima꞉no꞉. Niyo꞉ Yu kaluka꞉isalemo꞉wo꞉ halabo꞉ mada mo꞉dimido꞉ a꞉la꞉bo꞉ giyo꞉ asulo꞉.
Niyo꞉ hala nowo꞉ dimido꞉ ami sana soma꞉no꞉ kibo꞉bowo꞉, ne mo꞉nai ho꞉no꞉bo꞉lo. Ko꞉sega ililo꞉ nemo꞉lo꞉ su agelabko꞉ hendelema ko꞉lo꞉ giyo꞉ ili dagi amio꞉ dia꞉tab a꞉no꞉ digalo꞉ma. Ne mada Sisa ene mo꞉walilima꞉ki asulab.”
Festus eyo꞉ to a꞉no꞉ ene kanisol o꞉lia꞉ nenela꞉sa꞉ga꞉, eyo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Ge Sisamo꞉wo꞉ mo꞉walilima꞉ki dabuba꞉daleba꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ ge Sisalo꞉wa ha꞉na꞉ib.”
Ho꞉len nolo꞉ ta꞉ta꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, misa꞉ kalu Agiliba o꞉lia꞉ ado Benaisi o꞉lia꞉yo꞉ Festuso꞉ ba꞉ba꞉ni ya꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Sesalia a꞉na fa꞉la꞉dowo꞉.
A꞉la꞉yo꞉ ho꞉len modo꞉wo꞉ a꞉na silikiyo꞉, Festus eyo꞉ Fol elo꞉ mo꞉walilo꞉ a꞉no꞉ misa꞉ kalu o꞉lia꞉ nenelaki a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Fela꞉ks elo꞉ dibolo kalu nowo꞉ wenaka to꞉lo alita꞉ga꞉ ta꞉fo꞉gane ko꞉lo꞉lab.
Ne Ya꞉lusalemdo꞉ ane amio꞉, bobalo꞉ so꞉mia꞉sen misa꞉ kalu i o꞉lia꞉ Yu ko꞉go꞉do꞉ kalu o꞉lia꞉ i a꞉ma꞉ nemo꞉ aloba꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉ wa꞉dema꞉ki, salifa꞉.
Ko꞉sega niyo꞉ imo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, ‘Lom nili man amio꞉, kalu noma꞉yo꞉ kalu nolbo꞉wo꞉ towo꞉ diga꞉li sa꞉la꞉sa꞉ga꞉, mo꞉ mo꞉walilo꞉ amio꞉, “e dimido꞉” a꞉la꞉bo꞉ mo꞉sa꞉la꞉sen. Tamin amio꞉ emo꞉lo꞉ diga꞉li sa꞉lab kalu o꞉lia꞉ kagafo꞉likiyo꞉, eyo꞉ towo꞉ dinafa fanda sa꞉lab ami, niliyo꞉ mo꞉walilia꞉sa꞉ga꞉, a꞉na fanda ga꞉fa꞉ib.’
Niyo꞉ imo꞉wo꞉ to a꞉no꞉ wido꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ ne a꞉ma꞉la꞉ yakiyo꞉, i o꞉lia꞉ mio꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ ho꞉len a꞉ma꞉ fa꞉s amio꞉ niyo꞉ iyo꞉ mo꞉ka꞉laki, ne mo꞉walila꞉sen aya ha꞉na꞉ga꞉ silikiyo꞉, kalu a꞉no꞉ mena꞉ki ho꞉ido꞉.
Yu kaluwa꞉yo꞉ dasila꞉sa꞉ga꞉ Fol elo꞉ hala dimido꞉ sa꞉lab amio꞉, nilo꞉ asulo꞉ a꞉no꞉ iliyo꞉ a꞉la꞉bo꞉ mo꞉sio꞉.
Iliyo꞉ ini gulugululan man a꞉no꞉lia꞉ sowo꞉ kalu nowo꞉ ene wiyo꞉ Ya꞉su a꞉no꞉lia꞉ sa꞉laki kego꞉. Kalu a꞉no꞉ dasila꞉sa꞉ga꞉, mela꞉no꞉ a꞉lab a꞉la꞉liki Fol e sio꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ egelebo꞉ towa꞉yo꞉ kego꞉.
To ililo꞉ sa꞉lab a꞉no꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ nilo꞉ alobana walama꞉no꞉ babale dowabiki, niyo꞉ kalu e Ya꞉lusalem ha꞉na꞉sa꞉ga꞉ a꞉na mo꞉walilima꞉ hamana꞉ki, dabu ba꞉ba꞉.
Ko꞉sega e a꞉la꞉bo꞉ mo꞉dimidama꞉no꞉ a꞉laki, e Sisa ene mo꞉walilima꞉ki, dibolo aka yasi mesa꞉no꞉ asulo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ niyo꞉ e Sisalo꞉ amio꞉ iliga꞉fa꞉no꞉ togo꞉ semo꞉ ba꞉dabiki, e dibolo ka ta꞉fo꞉lo꞉l.”
Festus eyo꞉ a꞉la꞉sa꞉labiki, Agiliba eyo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Kalu a꞉ma꞉ enedo꞉ to sa꞉labo꞉, no꞉no꞉n mada da꞉ba꞉no꞉ asulab.” A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ Festus a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Ge ali da꞉ba꞉ib.”
Ho꞉len a꞉ma꞉ fas amio꞉ Agiliba o꞉lia꞉ Benaisi o꞉lia꞉yo꞉ ya꞉ga꞉ yakiyo꞉, kaluka꞉isaleyo꞉ a꞉la꞉ma꞉ wiyo꞉ wabulu sio꞉ ko꞉lo꞉, kegea꞉sen aya tinakiyo꞉, da꞉la꞉di misa꞉ kalu i o꞉lia꞉ ko꞉go꞉do꞉ kalu o꞉lia꞉yo꞉ egele ti ane. Festus eyo꞉ Folo꞉ tililia꞉ mena꞉ki sio꞉ ko꞉lo꞉, Folo꞉ tililia꞉ fa꞉la꞉dowabiki,
Festus eyo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Misa꞉ kalu Agiliba, ge a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ kaluka꞉isale wenamilo꞉ kegeo꞉ gio꞉ kalu we bo꞉ba. Ne Ya꞉lusalemdo꞉ ane amio꞉, Yu kaluka꞉isale ililo꞉ gadio꞉wo꞉ nemo꞉ sa꞉ma꞉ mio꞉ a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ Sesalia a꞉namio꞉lo꞉ nelo꞉wa ya꞉sa꞉ga꞉, kalu we sanalema꞉no꞉ a꞉la꞉likiyo꞉ halale sio꞉.
Niyo꞉ mo꞉walilo꞉ amio꞉, elo꞉ sanalema꞉no꞉ man hala dimido꞉ nowo꞉ mo꞉ba꞉ba꞉ ko꞉sega, eneno꞉ e Sisamo꞉ mo꞉walilima꞉ki a꞉la꞉dabu ba꞉dabiki, niyo꞉ e Lom a꞉na iliga꞉fa꞉no꞉ saefa꞉.
Niyo꞉ e iligetakilo꞉ hala elo꞉ dimido꞉ a꞉no꞉ sa꞉sa꞉lelia꞉ga꞉, Lom alan misa꞉ kalumo꞉lo꞉ iliga꞉fa꞉no꞉wo꞉ mo꞉bo꞉do꞉l ko꞉lo꞉ o꞉gdo꞉ kalu kegeo꞉ gio꞉ tambo a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ misa꞉ kalu Agiliba gilo꞉ tambo dabuma꞉kiyo꞉, kalu we gilo꞉wa tililia꞉mio꞉. To elo꞉ sa꞉lab a꞉no꞉ nio꞉ da꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉ nenelakiyo꞉, mo꞉fo꞉s amilo꞉ nilo꞉ sa꞉sa꞉lima꞉no꞉wo꞉ a꞉na doma꞉ib.
Mo꞉wo꞉ niyo꞉ dibolo kalu nowo꞉ elo꞉ hala dimido꞉wo꞉ mo꞉fo꞉s amio꞉ mo꞉sa꞉sa꞉la꞉sa꞉ga꞉ iligetalega, man a꞉no꞉ hala dimidama꞉no꞉lo꞉b a꞉la꞉asulo꞉l.” Festus eyo꞉ imo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉.
Agiliba eyo꞉ Folbo꞉wo꞉ towo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Gilo꞉ sa꞉ma꞉no꞉ asulo꞉ aumbo꞉ sama.” A꞉la꞉sa꞉labiyo꞉, Fol eyo꞉ dagiyo꞉ duluda꞉sa꞉ga꞉, emo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Misa꞉ kalu Agiliba, niasi Yu kalu ililo꞉ nemo꞉lo꞉ diga꞉li sa꞉lab a꞉no꞉ o꞉go꞉ ne gi milifa kagafo꞉liki, fanda sama꞉kiyo꞉ fogo꞉ dimiabko꞉, ne sagalo꞉.
<range>
Mo꞉wo꞉ giyo꞉ Yu nili mano꞉ dinafa asulo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ nili tilidabu ko꞉lilo꞉ amilo꞉ aloba꞉dakiyo꞉ kego꞉ a꞉no꞉lo꞉ ge asulo꞉. A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ nilo꞉ gemo꞉lo꞉ fanda sa꞉ma꞉nigo꞉l we, dinafa da꞉da꞉bi.
“Ne so꞉wa silikiyo꞉, niasi kalu o꞉lia꞉ sa꞉ga꞉ analiakiyo꞉, ne Ya꞉lusalem a꞉na sen ko꞉lo꞉ nilo꞉ man dimida꞉i mio꞉ a꞉no꞉ Yu kalu iyo꞉ tambo fanda asulufo꞉lab.
Fa꞉lisi kaluwa꞉ ele ko꞉li ko꞉lilo꞉ difa꞉ a꞉no꞉ gulugululan nolba꞉lo꞉ ele difa꞉ a꞉no꞉ tinio꞉ ko꞉lo꞉lab. Fa꞉lisiya꞉ ele difa꞉ a꞉no꞉ nelo꞉ kudu ha꞉na꞉sen ko꞉lo꞉ dona modo꞉ us a꞉namio꞉ iliyo꞉ ne dinafa asulo꞉. Iliyo꞉ ne dinafa fanda sa꞉ma꞉no꞉ dowo꞉ ko꞉sega a꞉la꞉do꞉ mo꞉gab. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ Fa꞉lisi kalu nio꞉, Yu nililo꞉ gulugululan man ko꞉li ko꞉lilo꞉ widan us amio꞉, ele kudu ha꞉na꞉sen a꞉no꞉, nolo꞉ nili tinio꞉ ko꞉lo꞉lab.
Ko꞉sega Godeya꞉lo꞉ nili ma꞉mu imo꞉wo꞉ to dinali sio꞉ a꞉no꞉ hendele ilili alifa꞉ib a꞉la꞉likiyo꞉, ne hendele tilida꞉daki, yasila꞉len ko꞉lo꞉, o꞉go꞉ ne a꞉na mo꞉walila꞉lab.
A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ Yuwa꞉ so꞉lo꞉ kugula꞉fo꞉ a꞉ma꞉yo꞉ Godeya꞉lo꞉ dinali sio꞉ a꞉no꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ ilili alifoma꞉kiyo꞉, iliyo꞉ ho꞉lenowo꞉lo꞉, nuluwo꞉lo꞉ Godeyo꞉ wabuda꞉liki yasila꞉sen. Misa꞉ kalu Agiliba, nelo꞉ dinali sio꞉ imilig a꞉no꞉ko꞉ tilida꞉dabiki, iliyo꞉ a꞉na mo꞉walilaki, diga꞉li sa꞉lab.
Godeya꞉yo꞉ sowo꞉ kaluwo꞉ a꞉ma꞉la꞉ a꞉dasi alita꞉sen a꞉la꞉do꞉ Yu kalu gio꞉ mo꞉tilida꞉daidko꞉ mo꞉wo꞉ ha꞉?
“Tamin amio꞉, Ya꞉su Nasa꞉la꞉do꞉ a꞉ma꞉ wi ko꞉lo꞉ wa꞉la꞉ sa꞉nama꞉kiyo꞉, niyo꞉ man ko꞉li ko꞉lilo꞉wo꞉ halaido꞉ dimidama꞉no꞉ a꞉la꞉tiliasulo꞉.
Bobalo꞉ so꞉mia꞉sen misa꞉ kalu iyo꞉ asulo꞉ imilise dowabiki, niyo꞉ ini wiya ilikiyo꞉, ne Ya꞉lusalem mo꞉mo꞉dakiyo꞉, Ya꞉su amilo꞉ tilidabu kalu modo꞉wo꞉ dibolo aya to꞉lolo꞉. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ kalu i a꞉no꞉ sana soma꞉nikiyo꞉, niyo꞉lo꞉ ‘sanama’ a꞉la꞉sa꞉la꞉sen.
Niyo꞉ Yu kaluwa꞉ tolo꞉ wida꞉sen a nowa nowa a꞉la꞉ sia꞉likiyo꞉, Keliso kaluka꞉isaleyo꞉ yame tandeaki, hida꞉yo꞉ ko꞉li ko꞉lilo꞉ imo꞉ dimia꞉sen. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ ini tilidabu a꞉no꞉ ta꞉foma꞉kiyo꞉, dibo꞉do꞉. Ne imo꞉wo꞉ mada alan gadiakiyo꞉, iyo꞉ nagalo꞉wo꞉ dima꞉ki, Yu kaluma amisa꞉n amio꞉ hen ko꞉li ko꞉lilo꞉ a꞉na keda꞉li sia꞉len.
“Ho꞉len imilise no amio꞉, nanog a꞉no꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ dimidama꞉kiyo꞉, bobalo꞉ so꞉mia꞉sen misa꞉ kalu iliyo꞉ halaido꞉ nemo꞉ dimiabiki, Damaskas amisa꞉na ha꞉na꞉ni ane.
Misa꞉ kalu, Agiliba ge da꞉da꞉ melea. Ne tog a꞉na ha꞉na꞉len amio꞉ disi dowabikiyo꞉, ho꞉wo꞉ mada alan, ofa꞉siyo꞉ o꞉ngo꞉ma ko꞉lo꞉ Hebene halona a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ so꞉solelia꞉ga꞉ tindakiyo꞉, ne o꞉lia꞉lo꞉ ane kalu a꞉no꞉lo꞉ tambo ho꞉lelia꞉ga꞉ dia꞉tabiki ba꞉ba꞉.
Nio꞉ hena sulufo꞉ ti ha꞉na꞉sa꞉ga꞉, fufulufo꞉liki dabu amio꞉, nemo꞉wo꞉ Alam to sa꞉lakiyo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, ‘So꞉l, So꞉l giyo꞉ nemo꞉wo꞉ nagalo꞉ waga dimiaya? Gilo꞉ dimidako꞉, mo꞉lo꞉ma ka dimidab ko꞉lo꞉ i meyo꞉wa꞉lo꞉ go꞉no꞉n a꞉ma꞉la꞉lo꞉ olo꞉wo꞉ a꞉ngab.’
“A꞉la꞉sa꞉labiki, niyo꞉ ‘Alan, ge o꞉ba?’ a꞉la꞉sio꞉. “‘Ne Ya꞉su. Gilo꞉ mogaga꞉leko꞉ Ne.
Ge dasila꞉sa꞉ga꞉ kagama. Niyo꞉ ge no꞉no꞉n nanog dian kalu fa꞉la꞉doma꞉ki da꞉feyo꞉. Gilo꞉ ba꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉lo꞉ asululiab a꞉no꞉lia꞉, nilo꞉ tifa gemo꞉lo꞉ a꞉walama꞉no꞉ a꞉no꞉lo꞉, kalu nolbo꞉lo꞉ walama꞉no꞉ a꞉no꞉, ge ko꞉lo꞉ da꞉fema꞉no꞉ a꞉la꞉liki, ne gelo꞉wa fa꞉la꞉doma꞉ mio꞉.
Giasi kalu o꞉lia꞉ Yu kaluma o꞉lia꞉ma꞉yo꞉ ge mogagima꞉no꞉ dowalikiyo꞉, niyo꞉ ge gasilia꞉no꞉. Yu kaluka꞉isalema ili siyo꞉ fagela꞉sa꞉ga꞉, iyo꞉ sululeyo꞉ ta꞉ta꞉ga꞉, ho꞉len doba꞉da꞉ nodolaki, Seteneya꞉ halaido꞉ amilo꞉ elen a꞉no꞉ ta꞉ta꞉ga꞉, Godelo꞉wa hamana꞉kiyo꞉, Niyo꞉ ge Yu kaluka꞉isalema ilo꞉wa iliga꞉fa꞉no꞉. Iyo꞉ a꞉la꞉dimidalikiyo꞉, mogago꞉ ililo꞉wo꞉ hala꞉sa꞉ga꞉ ga꞉lila꞉ma꞉no꞉ a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉, kaluka꞉isale ne tamina tilida꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉lo꞉, wi ililo꞉ dia꞉sa꞉ga꞉lo꞉ sab o꞉leo꞉ngo꞉ dimiaki, i o꞉lia꞉ gasalifa꞉no꞉’ Alana꞉yo꞉ nemo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉.
<range>
“A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ misa꞉ kalu Agiliba, na꞉lo꞉ ho꞉le ba꞉ba꞉ a꞉no꞉ mada kudu ane.
Ne kaluka꞉isalemo꞉wo꞉ widakiyo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, ‘Gililo꞉ mogago꞉ dimida꞉seno꞉ ta꞉ta꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Godelo꞉ doba꞉da꞉ nodola꞉bi. A꞉ma꞉ fa꞉s amio꞉, asulo꞉wo꞉ hendele nodolo꞉ a꞉la꞉liki widakiyo꞉, man nafayo꞉ dimida꞉lubi.’ Tamin amio꞉ niyo꞉ Damaskas amisa꞉n kaluka꞉isalemo꞉ wido꞉. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ Ya꞉lusalem o꞉lia꞉ Yudia hen tambo꞉ amio꞉ ha꞉na꞉ga꞉ ilikiyo꞉ wida꞉len. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉yo꞉, ne Yu kaluka꞉isalema imo꞉wo꞉lo꞉ wida꞉li ane.
Niyo꞉ a꞉la꞉wido꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ ne Godeya꞉ Malilo꞉ aya silikiyo꞉, Yu kalu iyo꞉ ne ta꞉lia꞉sa꞉ga꞉, sana soma꞉no꞉ asulab.
Ko꞉sega ne ho꞉len a꞉na a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ mio꞉ amio꞉, Godeya꞉yo꞉ ne asuwa꞉ta꞉i ya꞉ga꞉, o꞉go꞉ ne wena kagafo꞉liki, wilo꞉ kalu o꞉lia꞉ wilo꞉ma kalu o꞉lia꞉mo꞉wo꞉ to hendeleyo꞉ malolo꞉ mio꞉l. To nolo꞉ mo꞉malolo꞉ miakiyo꞉, Moses o꞉lia꞉ dinali sa꞉lan kalu o꞉lia꞉ma꞉lo꞉ kelego꞉ fa꞉la꞉doma꞉ib a꞉la꞉do꞉ sio꞉ a꞉no꞉ko꞉ wido꞉l.
To a꞉no꞉ we, Godeya꞉lo꞉ Da꞉feyo꞉ Kalu e nagalo꞉ alan dia꞉ ha꞉na꞉ga꞉ sota꞉ga꞉yo꞉, sowo꞉lo꞉ mo꞉dasilan a꞉no꞉ tamin amio꞉ e ko꞉lo꞉ a꞉dasima꞉ib. A꞉la꞉dimida꞉sa꞉ga꞉, eyo꞉ ene kaluka꞉isale o꞉lia꞉ Yu kaluka꞉isalema o꞉lia꞉mo꞉wo꞉ Godeya꞉ ho꞉len a꞉no꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ walama꞉ib. Dinali sa꞉lan kaluwa꞉yo꞉ a꞉la꞉bo꞉ fa꞉la꞉doma꞉ib a꞉la꞉likilo꞉ dinali saefa꞉ a꞉no꞉ niyo꞉ wido꞉l.”
Fol eyo꞉ to a꞉no꞉ o꞉sa꞉la꞉lenka, Festus eyo꞉ halalelaki a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Ge no꞉nololowo꞉ kalu. Ge asulo꞉wo꞉ modo꞉ diabiki, asulo꞉ gilo꞉ko꞉ no꞉nolab.”
A꞉la꞉sa꞉labiki, Fol eyo꞉ a꞉ma꞉la꞉bo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Misa꞉ kalu Festus, ge wilo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ ne mada no꞉nolo꞉ma. Nilo꞉ to so꞉lo꞉l wenamio꞉, mo꞉wo꞉ da꞉labiki hendele so꞉lo꞉l.
To nilo꞉ so꞉lo꞉l we, wo꞉no꞉lebo꞉ mo꞉dimido꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ Misa꞉ kalu Agiliba e dabu, ne a꞉la꞉ asulo꞉l. E asulo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉labiki, niyo꞉ kalab amio꞉ emo꞉wo꞉ a꞉na malolo꞉.
Misa꞉ kalu Agiliba ge, dinali sa꞉lan kaluwa꞉lo꞉ sio꞉ a꞉no꞉ ge tilida꞉daya? A꞉, niyo꞉ ge hendele tilida꞉dab a꞉la꞉asulo꞉l.”
A꞉la꞉sa꞉labiki, Agiliba eyo꞉ Folbo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉dabu ba꞉ba꞉, “Ho꞉len abolda꞉su wenaka, ne asulo꞉ nodola꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Kelisowa tilidabuma꞉ki sa꞉layele?”
A꞉la꞉sa꞉labiki, Fol eyo꞉ a꞉ma꞉la꞉bo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Ho꞉len o꞉g wenakabiyo꞉lo꞉ o꞉ ho꞉len sambo dowa꞉i ha꞉na꞉ga꞉lalikiyo꞉lo꞉, gelo꞉ a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ kaluka꞉isale nilo꞉ sa꞉labdo꞉ da꞉da꞉likilo꞉ sab we tambo, ne o꞉ngo꞉ doma꞉ki, Godemo꞉ dulugu so꞉lo꞉l. Ko꞉sega sa꞉ni wema꞉yo꞉ giyo꞉lo꞉ galolo꞉ma꞉kiyo꞉ mo꞉asulo꞉.”
Fol eyo꞉ a꞉la꞉sa꞉la꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, misa꞉ kalu Agiliba o꞉lia꞉ Festus o꞉lia꞉ Beniasi o꞉lia꞉lo꞉ sen kaluka꞉isaleyo꞉ a꞉na dasilia꞉ga꞉, ha꞉nakiyo꞉, egelebo꞉ nenelaki a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Kalu we halalo꞉ mo꞉dimido꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ e dibolo amio꞉ to꞉loma꞉no꞉wo꞉ o꞉ sanasoma꞉no꞉wo꞉ mo꞉lo꞉malo꞉b.”
<range>
A꞉la꞉go꞉ko꞉lo꞉ Agiliba eyo꞉ Festusbo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Kalu we eneno꞉ e Sisamo꞉ mo꞉walilima꞉ki a꞉la꞉bo꞉ mo꞉sio꞉ kibo꞉bowo꞉, e ga꞉li sili alifo꞉lo” a꞉la꞉sio꞉.
Iliyo꞉ nio꞉ ho꞉n ko꞉suwa disa꞉la꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Itali hen a꞉na ha꞉na꞉no꞉ a꞉la꞉saefa꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ Folo꞉ a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ dibolo kalu nolo꞉ tililia꞉sa꞉ga꞉, da꞉la꞉di fudo꞉ otalen bo꞉fo꞉lowan kalu nowo꞉, Yulius ko꞉lo꞉ emo꞉ tililia꞉ hamana꞉ki ta꞉fo꞉. Yulius eyo꞉ Loma꞉ misa꞉ kalu alan ene ami us a꞉na nanogo꞉ dimida꞉sen. Ho꞉n ko꞉su nowo꞉, Adamitium a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉lo꞉ mio꞉ a꞉no꞉ Esia hen a꞉namida꞉ amisa꞉n ko꞉li ko꞉lilo꞉wa fa꞉la꞉dowa꞉li a꞉la꞉liki ha꞉na꞉nigabiki, nio꞉ a꞉na disa꞉la꞉sa꞉ga꞉ ane. Masedonia hena, Tesalonaika amisa꞉n kalu nowo꞉, Alistakus e ni o꞉lia꞉ disa꞉la꞉sa꞉ga꞉ ane.
<range>
A꞉ma꞉ kea꞉fowo꞉, nio꞉ Saido꞉n a꞉na fa꞉la꞉dowakiyo꞉, Yulius eyo꞉ Folo꞉ nofola꞉sa꞉ga꞉ asuwa꞉takiyo꞉, Fol e ene mili kaluwa꞉yo꞉ asuwa꞉foma꞉ki a꞉lakiyo꞉, Fol e ga꞉li sia꞉mela꞉ki ta꞉fo꞉.
Nio꞉ a꞉ma꞉la꞉ disa꞉la꞉sa꞉ga꞉ ha꞉nakiyo꞉, fufayo꞉ nilo꞉ doba꞉ yabiki, nio꞉ Saibulu hen ho꞉na꞉lo꞉ hegefa꞉ anib fufalo꞉ mo꞉ba꞉ma꞉no꞉ a꞉namida꞉ ane.
Saibulus hena ta꞉ta꞉ga꞉yo꞉ nio꞉ so꞉lu ho꞉n alan a꞉no꞉ onolo ta꞉notakiyo꞉, Silisia o꞉lia꞉ Bamfilia hen a꞉no꞉ tininita꞉ga꞉ aneyo꞉, Lisia hen amio꞉, Maila amisa꞉na fa꞉la꞉dowo꞉.
A꞉na fa꞉la꞉dota꞉ga꞉yo꞉, Yulius eyo꞉ ho꞉n ko꞉su nowo꞉ Alegsandia a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ ya꞉ga꞉, Italilo꞉ ha꞉na꞉ibo꞉ ba꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉, nio꞉ ho꞉n ko꞉su no a꞉na disa꞉ma꞉no꞉ sio꞉ ko꞉lo꞉, nio꞉ ua disa꞉la꞉sa꞉ga꞉ ane.
Ho꞉len nolo꞉ nio꞉ ho꞉n ko꞉su a꞉no꞉ ha꞉sa ha꞉na꞉ga꞉ ha꞉nakiyo꞉, Nidus amisa꞉n anib a꞉na fa꞉la꞉dowo꞉ ko꞉sega, fufayo꞉ nilo꞉ ha꞉na꞉no꞉lo꞉ doba꞉da꞉ yab ko꞉lo꞉, tigini ha꞉na꞉no꞉wo꞉ mo꞉dowabi, nio꞉ nodota꞉ga꞉ Kilit hen a꞉namida꞉ ha꞉na꞉no꞉ ha꞉nakiyo꞉, hen ko꞉lo꞉ bofiya꞉, Salmone a꞉na ta꞉ta꞉ga꞉yo꞉ Kilit ho꞉na꞉lo꞉ hegefa꞉ anib fufalo꞉ mo꞉ba꞉ma꞉no꞉ doba꞉da꞉ ane.
Nio꞉ Kilit hen a꞉nib a꞉na halaido꞉ ba꞉da꞉i ha꞉na꞉la꞉ga꞉, ho꞉n ko꞉sulo꞉ kagaya꞉sen hege ane hen nafa, Lasea amisa꞉n anib a꞉na fa꞉la꞉dowakiyo꞉ kagayo꞉.
Nio꞉ ho꞉len modo꞉wo꞉ a꞉na wala꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Yu ilililo꞉ ma꞉n o꞉lo꞉ mo꞉ma꞉no꞉ ho꞉len a꞉no꞉ o꞉ma tinio꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ fufalo꞉ yan ho꞉leno꞉ fa꞉la꞉dowo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉, nio꞉ ho꞉n ko꞉suwo꞉ ha꞉na꞉no꞉wo꞉ halaido꞉ doma꞉nigab. Fol eyo꞉ tagilaki, imo꞉wo꞉ hagugu sio꞉,
“Kalu gio꞉ dabuma. Nio꞉ o꞉go꞉ ho꞉n ko꞉su we ka ha꞉nalega, nio꞉ mogagakiyo꞉, kelego꞉ o꞉lia꞉ ho꞉n ko꞉su o꞉lia꞉yo꞉ walaki, nio꞉ nolo꞉ soma꞉no꞉.”
Fol elo꞉ sio꞉ a꞉no꞉, Yulius eyo꞉ mo꞉tili da꞉daki, ho꞉n ko꞉sulo꞉ biso꞉ o꞉lia꞉ o꞉lo꞉ dia꞉ha꞉nan kalu o꞉lia꞉ma꞉lo꞉ to sa꞉labdeyo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ kudu ane.
Fufa alano꞉ yalikiyo꞉, nio꞉ ho꞉n ko꞉sulo꞉ kagaya꞉sen hege ane hen a꞉namilo꞉ mesa꞉no꞉wo꞉ halaido꞉ doma꞉ib ko꞉lo꞉, ho꞉n ko꞉su amilo꞉ sen kalu modo꞉wa꞉yo꞉ saitakiyo꞉, Kilit hen anib doba꞉da꞉ ha꞉na꞉ga꞉, Fina꞉ks amisa꞉n a꞉na ha꞉na꞉ga꞉ sena, fufa alano꞉ ho꞉len a꞉na yalikiyo꞉ nio꞉ a꞉na mesa꞉no꞉ a꞉la꞉liki saefa꞉. Mo꞉wo꞉ Fina꞉ks a꞉namio꞉, ho꞉n ko꞉sulo꞉ kagaya꞉sen hege ane hen nafa ko꞉lo꞉ nio꞉ dona fufa yabo꞉ a꞉na kagafo꞉liki, yasi mesa꞉no꞉wo꞉ nafa ko꞉lo꞉lab.
Fa꞉fa꞉so꞉ fo꞉fo꞉ndolo doba꞉da꞉ yabiki ba꞉ba꞉sa꞉ga꞉, ililo꞉ nenela꞉sa꞉ga꞉lo꞉ saefa꞉ a꞉no꞉ dimidama꞉no꞉ ho꞉leno꞉ fa꞉la꞉dowab a꞉la꞉asulakiyo꞉, iyo꞉ ko꞉suwo꞉ fasila꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Kilit hen aniba ha꞉na꞉ga꞉ ane.
A꞉na ha꞉na꞉sen amio꞉, mo꞉amalela꞉ a꞉naka fufa alano꞉, Kilit hendo꞉ doba꞉da꞉ a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ yakiyo꞉, ho꞉n ko꞉su a꞉no꞉ anilia꞉ga꞉ ha꞉naki, fufalo꞉ yab doba꞉da꞉lo꞉ nodoma꞉no꞉wo꞉ halaido꞉ dowabiki, nio꞉ ho꞉n ko꞉su a꞉no꞉ fufaya꞉ dia꞉hamana꞉ki ka ta꞉fo꞉. Fufa a꞉ma꞉ wiyo꞉, Yulakilo꞉ a꞉la꞉sa꞉lan.
<range>
Nio꞉ ha꞉na꞉sa꞉ga꞉, ho꞉na꞉lo꞉ hegefa꞉ hen ha꞉lu nowo꞉, Kauda a꞉na fa꞉la꞉dowakiyo꞉, fufaya꞉yo꞉ mo꞉bama꞉ki, anib a꞉na ha꞉na꞉ni ane. A꞉na ha꞉nakiyo꞉, ho꞉n ko꞉su ha꞉lu nolo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ susululia꞉ yab a꞉no꞉ mo꞉basale hamana꞉ki, ho꞉n ko꞉su alan a꞉ma꞉ wa꞉la dia꞉ta꞉ga꞉ melakiyo꞉, halaido꞉ dimido꞉.
Nio꞉ halaido꞉ ba꞉da꞉i ha꞉na꞉la꞉ga꞉, dia꞉takiyo꞉, ho꞉n ko꞉su alan a꞉no꞉ halalema꞉kiyo꞉, kegel nolo꞉ ho꞉n ko꞉su a꞉ma꞉ ha꞉ga to꞉lo felesa꞉ga꞉, nodolo꞉ o꞉lia꞉ sili sunu alifa꞉.
Fufa alan yakiyo꞉, ho꞉no꞉ ma꞉fio꞉wo꞉ alan a꞉ma꞉yo꞉ ho꞉n ko꞉suwa mada alan bese tandeo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ a꞉ma꞉ kea꞉fowo꞉, ho꞉n ko꞉su amilo꞉ kelego꞉ disa꞉ a꞉no꞉ ho꞉na mo꞉mo꞉da sandifelo꞉.
A꞉la꞉ga꞉i ha꞉na꞉la꞉ga꞉yo꞉, ho꞉len asola꞉ fa꞉la꞉dowabikiyo꞉, iliyo꞉ ho꞉n ko꞉sulo꞉ hamana꞉kilo꞉ nanogo꞉ dian kelego꞉ nol a꞉no꞉ ene dagiya꞉ dia꞉ga꞉ ho꞉na sandifelo꞉.
Ho꞉len modo꞉ sen a꞉namio꞉, of o꞉lia꞉ tamin o꞉lia꞉ mo꞉ba꞉daki, fufayo꞉ alan o꞉ya꞉lab a꞉ma꞉yo꞉, nili asulo꞉wo꞉ kelegelaki, nio꞉ soma꞉nigo꞉bo꞉lo꞉b a꞉la꞉asulo꞉.
Ho꞉leno꞉ modo꞉ sen a꞉namio꞉, kalu i a꞉no꞉ ma꞉no꞉lo꞉ mo꞉mo꞉no꞉ dowa꞉i mio꞉ a꞉no꞉ ba꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Fol eyo꞉ dasilia꞉ga꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Kalu gio꞉, gio꞉ Kilit hen a꞉na mo꞉ta꞉fo꞉ mia꞉no꞉ a꞉la꞉likiyo꞉, nilo꞉ gimo꞉lo꞉ hagugu to sio꞉ a꞉no꞉ kudu ane kibo꞉bowo꞉, hida꞉yo꞉ we gio꞉ mo꞉ba꞉daki, kelego꞉wo꞉ mo꞉walemo꞉lo.
Ko꞉sega o꞉go꞉ niyo꞉ gimo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉so꞉lo꞉l. Gio꞉ imilig nowo꞉ ho꞉na꞉yo꞉ mo꞉kanda soma꞉ib, ko꞉lo꞉ gio꞉ mo꞉tagilaki, halaido꞉ doma. Ho꞉n ko꞉su wenako꞉ mada mogagima꞉ib.
Ne Gode eno꞉ dowaki, emo꞉ wabulu sa꞉la꞉sen ko꞉lo꞉ ali nuluwo꞉ ene ma꞉mul kalu nowo꞉ nelo꞉wa ya꞉ga꞉ kagayakiyo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉,
‘Fol ge tagila꞉so꞉bo. Ge ha꞉na꞉ga꞉ Sisaya꞉ siwa꞉la kagafo꞉liki, mo꞉walilima꞉ib ko꞉lo꞉ Godeya꞉ ge ko꞉lo꞉ kanulakiyo꞉, ho꞉n ko꞉su amilo꞉ disa꞉ kalu a꞉no꞉lo꞉ Godeya꞉yo꞉ tambo gasilialiki, mo꞉soma꞉ib’ a꞉la꞉sio꞉.
A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ Godeya꞉yo꞉ nemo꞉lo꞉ sio꞉ o꞉leaum ka dimidama꞉nigab a꞉la꞉tiliasulo꞉l ko꞉lo꞉ gio꞉ halaido꞉ dowaki, tagila꞉so꞉bo.
A꞉la꞉bo꞉ fa꞉la꞉doma꞉ib ko꞉sega tamin amio꞉ fufaya꞉yo꞉ ho꞉n ko꞉suwo꞉ dia꞉ ha꞉na꞉ga꞉, ho꞉na꞉lo꞉ hegefa꞉ hen a꞉na basama꞉ki ha꞉na꞉no꞉.” Fol eyo꞉ imo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉.
Nio꞉ Medita꞉linean so꞉lu ho꞉n us a꞉naka sia꞉leno꞉, ho꞉len agelo꞉wo꞉ do꞉ a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ fa꞉la꞉da꞉in dowabikiyo꞉, nulu usamio꞉ ho꞉n ko꞉sulo꞉ dia꞉sian kalu iliyo꞉ ha꞉la꞉ya dowabolo꞉b a꞉la꞉asulo꞉.
A꞉la꞉asulakiyo꞉ iliyo꞉ me amio꞉ hida꞉yo꞉ suda꞉sa꞉ga꞉, ho꞉n ki da꞉fe ba꞉ba꞉ agelo꞉wo꞉ 40 mita a꞉la꞉fo꞉ fa꞉la꞉dowo꞉. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ o꞉fina꞉ga꞉ a꞉da꞉fe ba꞉ba꞉ amio꞉, 30 mita a꞉la꞉fo꞉ fa꞉la꞉dowo꞉.
Nio꞉ ho꞉n ko꞉su we ulo꞉ elena ha꞉na꞉ga꞉ basama꞉nigabele a꞉la꞉ kele asulakiyo꞉, iliyo꞉ go꞉fo꞉ ki hida꞉yo꞉ fa꞉la꞉da꞉in, me amilo꞉ sunualifelo꞉ a꞉no꞉ ho꞉n ko꞉suwo꞉ halale kagafomelea꞉ki, a꞉na fage to꞉lolo꞉. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ ho꞉le balima꞉li, inin godemo꞉ dulugu sa꞉la꞉len.
Ho꞉n ko꞉sulo꞉ dia꞉sian kalu iyo꞉ sili alifo꞉ ha꞉na꞉no꞉ asulakiyo꞉, iyo꞉ go꞉fo꞉ ki hida꞉yo꞉ nolo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ migifa fage to꞉lolabolo꞉b a꞉la꞉bo꞉ba꞉ki dikidakiyo꞉, iyo꞉ ko꞉su ha꞉lu wa꞉lamilo꞉ difa꞉ a꞉no꞉ fagela꞉sa꞉ga꞉, tolola꞉li tiane.
Ko꞉sega Fol eyo꞉ Yulius o꞉lia꞉ da꞉la꞉di kalu o꞉lia꞉mo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Ho꞉n ko꞉sulo꞉ dia꞉sian kalu i wema꞉yo꞉ ho꞉n ko꞉su we ta꞉ta꞉ga꞉ nai ha꞉nalega, gilo꞉ gasilia꞉no꞉ togo꞉ aundo꞉ma doma꞉ib.”
A꞉la꞉sa꞉labikiyo꞉, da꞉la꞉di kalu i a꞉ma꞉yo꞉ ho꞉n ko꞉su ha꞉lulo꞉ fage to꞉lolab me a꞉no꞉ gede alitabiki, ho꞉n ko꞉su a꞉no꞉ sulufo꞉ tina꞉ga꞉, ha꞉lelea꞉gane.
Ho꞉idabikiyo꞉ Fol eyo꞉ imo꞉wo꞉ ma꞉no꞉wo꞉ maya꞉kiyo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Gio꞉ ho꞉leno꞉ do꞉ a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ fa꞉la꞉da꞉in amio꞉, kele asulo꞉wo꞉ alan dowo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ ma꞉no꞉wo꞉ mo꞉dinafa mo꞉no꞉.
A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ gio꞉ ma꞉no꞉wo꞉ maya. Mo꞉nalega, halaido꞉ aundo꞉ma dowaki soma꞉ib. Ko꞉sega gio꞉ ma꞉no꞉ nalega, gio꞉ imilig nowo꞉ hida꞉yo꞉ imilig mo꞉dia꞉ib”
Fol eyo꞉ to a꞉no꞉ sa꞉la꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, eyo꞉ ma꞉n so꞉fa꞉ nolo꞉ dia꞉sa꞉ga꞉, ili milifa kagafo꞉liki, Godemo꞉ mada o꞉m a꞉la꞉sa꞉la꞉sa꞉ga꞉, a꞉na gululia꞉ga꞉ mo꞉no꞉.
A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ iyo꞉ tambo asulo꞉wo꞉ halaido꞉ a꞉dowakiyo꞉, ma꞉no꞉wo꞉ a꞉na mo꞉no꞉.
Iyo꞉ ho꞉n ko꞉su usamilo꞉ disa꞉ agelo꞉wo꞉ 276 a꞉la꞉fo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ sen.
Iyo꞉ tambo ma꞉no꞉wo꞉ na꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, ho꞉n ko꞉su hideyabena꞉ki, da꞉si wit wo꞉fa꞉ a꞉no꞉ so꞉lu ho꞉na sandifelo꞉.
Ho꞉le bidabikiyo꞉, iyo꞉ hen nowo꞉ ba꞉ba꞉ ko꞉sega heno꞉ we o꞉mo꞉lo꞉b a꞉la꞉bo꞉ mo꞉fanda asulo꞉. Iyo꞉ ho꞉n anib amilo꞉ dugu ane a꞉na sa꞉felo꞉wo꞉ ba꞉da꞉ga꞉, ho꞉n ko꞉su a꞉namio꞉ o꞉li kagama꞉no꞉lo꞉b a꞉la꞉asulaki, iyo꞉ a꞉namida꞉ ha꞉na꞉ga꞉, sa꞉ wa꞉la kagama꞉niki a꞉la꞉sio꞉.
A꞉la꞉go꞉ko꞉lo꞉ iliyo꞉ go꞉fo꞉ ki hida꞉yo꞉ fa꞉la꞉da꞉indo꞉ suwo꞉ me a꞉no꞉ gegedela꞉sa꞉ga꞉, ho꞉n a꞉naka ta꞉felo꞉. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ ho꞉n ko꞉sulo꞉ nodoma꞉no꞉lo꞉ melo꞉ me a꞉no꞉lo꞉ fagela꞉. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ ko꞉su hamana꞉kilo꞉ so꞉g deheda꞉sen a꞉no꞉ migiya amilo꞉ a꞉na fage dehele alita꞉sa꞉ga꞉, fufayo꞉ a꞉na balia꞉ ha꞉na꞉ga꞉, sa꞉ wa꞉la kagama꞉ni ane.
Ko꞉sega so꞉lu ho꞉n uska o꞉ha꞉nakiyo꞉, ho꞉n ko꞉su migi ha꞉g a꞉no꞉ sa꞉ya halale gelabiki, mo꞉ililo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉, tif doba꞉da꞉yo꞉ ho꞉n ma꞉fiyo꞉ alan gululia꞉ yaki, ho꞉n ko꞉su seba bolabikiyo꞉ basale ane.
A꞉la꞉gabikiyo꞉ dibolo kaluwo꞉ ho꞉no꞉ dasia꞉takiyo꞉ dalale ha꞉nabena꞉kiyo꞉, da꞉la꞉di kaluwa꞉yo꞉ iyo꞉ yasalema꞉no꞉ asulo꞉.
Ko꞉sega Yulius eyo꞉ Fol e mo꞉soma꞉ki asuwa꞉takiyo꞉, da꞉la꞉di kaluwa꞉lo꞉ yasalema꞉no꞉ asulo꞉ a꞉no꞉ ka꞉lakiyo꞉, kalu ho꞉ndo꞉ dasa꞉sen a꞉no꞉, iyo꞉ tambo ho꞉na ho꞉lufela꞉sa꞉ga꞉, dasa꞉i ha꞉na꞉la꞉ga꞉, sa꞉lo꞉wa fa꞉la꞉doma꞉ni hamana a꞉la꞉sio꞉.
A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ kalu ho꞉ndo꞉ mo꞉dasa꞉sen a꞉no꞉ tambo ho꞉n ko꞉su ko꞉lo꞉ basali ha꞉na꞉siab heb a꞉no꞉ ta꞉lidota꞉ga꞉ ha꞉liliya꞉ ha꞉na꞉la꞉ga꞉, sa꞉lowa hamana a꞉la꞉sio꞉. A꞉la꞉do꞉ dimido꞉ a꞉na ilikiyo꞉ iyo꞉ tambo ha꞉la꞉ya fa꞉la꞉dosdo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ imilig nowo꞉ ho꞉na꞉yo꞉ mo꞉kanda sowo꞉.
Nio꞉ tambo gendo꞉ mo꞉dowo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ ha꞉la꞉ya o꞉li dasilia꞉ga꞉, ha꞉la꞉ya fa꞉la꞉dowa꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, ho꞉na꞉lo꞉ hegefa꞉ hen Malta a꞉na fa꞉la꞉dowo꞉bo꞉lo꞉b a꞉la꞉asulo꞉.
O꞉g a꞉namio꞉ ho꞉no꞉ tindaki hido꞉ ko꞉lo꞉, kalu a꞉namilo꞉ sen a꞉ma꞉yo꞉, nimo꞉ mano꞉ mada nafale dimidakiyo꞉, iliyo꞉ deyo꞉ gili alitaki, nio꞉ dinafa tili dowo꞉.
Fol eyo꞉ de eleyo꞉ kegenelia꞉ga꞉, deya dia꞉tab amio꞉, sowa꞉ kisa꞉wa꞉lo꞉ usa delen ko꞉lo꞉, ofabiki handalowakiyo꞉, Fola꞉ dagiya ma꞉buluta꞉ga꞉ sunu helefo꞉len.
Amisa꞉n kaluka꞉isale a꞉ma꞉yo꞉ sowa꞉yo꞉ Fola꞉ dagiyo꞉ sunu helefolabiki ba꞉da꞉ga꞉yo꞉, egelebo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Kalu we hendele tamin amio꞉ kalu nowo꞉ e sana sowo꞉lo꞉b ko꞉lo꞉ a꞉ma꞉ wa꞉l diakiyo꞉, e so꞉lu ho꞉n amio꞉ soma꞉no꞉ ko꞉sega e ha꞉la꞉ya dasefa꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ mo꞉mesea꞉kiyo꞉, so꞉wa꞉ wema꞉yo꞉ soma꞉ki o꞉lab.”
Iliyo꞉ a꞉la꞉asulaki nenelo꞉ ko꞉sega, Fol eyo꞉ dagiyo꞉ fugala꞉labiki, sowa꞉ a꞉no꞉ deya tagafo꞉ tiya꞉ a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ e nagalo꞉ mo꞉di.
Iliyo꞉ Fol e dagiyo꞉ da꞉ima꞉ibele, o꞉ e wigibo a꞉naka soma꞉nigabele a꞉la꞉asula꞉liki yasila꞉li ane ko꞉sega, e amio꞉ hida꞉yo꞉ nowo꞉ mo꞉fa꞉la꞉dowabikiyo꞉, iliyo꞉ a꞉no꞉ ba꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉, asulo꞉wo꞉ a꞉nodolaki, kalu we godelo꞉b a꞉la꞉sio꞉.
Nilo꞉ fa꞉la꞉dowo꞉ hen a꞉no꞉ Malta misa꞉ kalu Bubilus ene hen ko꞉lo꞉ eyo꞉ nio꞉ asuwa꞉takiyo꞉, ene aya tililia꞉ga꞉, ho꞉len otaleno꞉ eyo꞉ nio꞉ dinafa bo꞉fo꞉len.
Bubilusa꞉ iyayo꞉ ofo꞉ walaf o꞉lia꞉ kuf nagalaki, ila꞉ ho꞉n o꞉lia꞉yo꞉ dowo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ uwob ka alifo꞉len. Fol e elo꞉wa ha꞉na꞉sa꞉ga꞉, dagiyo꞉ eya golofo꞉liki, Godemo꞉ dulugu sa꞉labikiyo꞉, e falelo꞉.
Elo꞉ dimido꞉ a꞉no꞉ ba꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, ho꞉na꞉lo꞉ hegefa꞉ hen a꞉namilo꞉ walaf kalu sen nol a꞉no꞉, Fol elo꞉wa mio꞉ ko꞉lo꞉, iyo꞉ falele alifelo꞉.
Iliyo꞉ nio꞉ sagale alitaki, man nafale ko꞉li ko꞉lilo꞉ nimo꞉ dimido꞉ ko꞉lo꞉, nio꞉ ho꞉n ko꞉suwa ha꞉na꞉nigabikiyo꞉, kelego꞉ nililo꞉ mo꞉dowo꞉ aumbo꞉, nimo꞉wo꞉ tambo dimi.
Nio꞉ ele otaleno꞉ a꞉na sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, ha꞉na꞉no꞉ ko꞉lo꞉, ho꞉n ko꞉su nowo꞉ Alegsandia a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉lo꞉ mio꞉ a꞉no꞉, fufalo꞉ mio꞉ ho꞉len a꞉namio꞉ Malta a꞉na kagafo꞉len. O꞉go꞉ a꞉namio꞉ fufayo꞉ edo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ ha꞉na꞉no꞉ a꞉la꞉asulo꞉. Ho꞉n ko꞉su a꞉ma꞉ migi amio꞉, madali gode ao a꞉la꞉ a꞉no꞉ misido꞉ momada꞉ alifa꞉. Madali gode a꞉no꞉ so꞉wa a꞉la꞉ alelo꞉ imilig amilo꞉ sa꞉la꞉li. Nio꞉ ho꞉n ko꞉su a꞉na disa꞉la꞉sa꞉ga꞉ ane.
Nio꞉ ha꞉na꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, Silakus amisa꞉n a꞉na fa꞉la꞉dota꞉ga꞉, ho꞉len otaleno꞉ a꞉na sen.
Silakus a꞉no꞉ ta꞉ta꞉ga꞉ aneyo꞉, Legium amisa꞉na fa꞉la꞉dowo꞉. Ho꞉len a꞉ma꞉ fa꞉s amio꞉, fa꞉fa꞉so꞉ fa꞉s doba꞉da꞉ yabikiyo꞉ nio꞉ ha꞉na꞉sa꞉ga꞉, ho꞉len a꞉ma꞉ fa꞉s amio꞉ Buteoli amisa꞉na fa꞉la꞉dowo꞉.
Amisa꞉n a꞉namio꞉, tilidabu kalu nolo꞉ a꞉na galilia꞉ga꞉, iliyo꞉ soagelo꞉ imilig nowo꞉ i o꞉lia꞉ a꞉naka mesea꞉ki sio꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ a꞉na sa꞉ga꞉, Lom a꞉na ane.
Nilo꞉ fa꞉la꞉doma꞉i yab a꞉la꞉bo꞉ Lom amilo꞉ tilidabu kaluka꞉isale nolo꞉ da꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, iyo꞉ nilo꞉ galima꞉ni mio꞉ ko꞉lo꞉, Abius Maget amisa꞉n ta꞉ta꞉sa꞉ga꞉ mio꞉wo꞉, mageso꞉ a nowo꞉ A Otalen a꞉la꞉wikilo꞉lo꞉ a꞉na galili. Fol eyo꞉ kalu a꞉no꞉ ba꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, e Godemo꞉ mada o꞉m a꞉la꞉sa꞉la꞉sa꞉ga꞉, e halaido꞉ di.
Nio꞉ Lom fa꞉la꞉dowo꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, Lom gamani kalu iyo꞉ Fol e dibolo a amio꞉ mo꞉to꞉lolaki, e ena꞉li a nowa mesea꞉ki ta꞉takiyo꞉, da꞉la꞉di kalu nolo꞉ a꞉na bo꞉fo꞉melea꞉ki ta꞉fo꞉.
Ho꞉len otaleno꞉ ta꞉ta꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, Fol eyo꞉ Yu ko꞉go꞉do꞉ kaluwo꞉ ho꞉le kegea꞉sa꞉ga꞉, towo꞉ imo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Ni nao i, niyo꞉ kaluka꞉isale nililo꞉mo꞉wo꞉ mogago꞉lo꞉ mo꞉dimida꞉b a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ nili ma꞉muwa꞉ mano꞉lo꞉ mo꞉mogagila꞉ ko꞉sega, ne Ya꞉lusalem amio꞉ mo꞉walilima꞉kiyo꞉ ta꞉lia꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Lom kalumo꞉wo꞉ a꞉na dimi.
Iyo꞉ nemo꞉lo꞉ diga꞉di sio꞉ a꞉no꞉ aloba꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, nelo꞉ sana soma꞉no꞉ mo꞉wo꞉ mo꞉ba꞉ba꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ ne sili alifa꞉no꞉ asulo꞉.
Ko꞉sega Yu misa꞉ kalu iliyo꞉ a꞉la꞉bo꞉ mo꞉dimidama꞉ki asulabiki, ne Sisa emo꞉ mo꞉walilima꞉ki a꞉la꞉liki dabu ba꞉ba꞉. A꞉la꞉dimido꞉ ko꞉sega, Yu kaluka꞉isale na꞉lo꞉mo꞉wo꞉ niyo꞉ gadiakilo꞉ imo꞉wo꞉ a꞉mo꞉walilima꞉no꞉wo꞉ nowo꞉ aundo꞉ma.
A꞉la꞉dimida꞉i mio꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ o꞉go꞉ niyo꞉ gio꞉ ba꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉ gimo꞉wo꞉ malolo꞉ mia꞉ni ho꞉ido꞉. Isolael kalu niliyo꞉ tilida꞉sa꞉ga꞉lo꞉ yasilo꞉ a꞉na ilikiyo꞉, ne sa꞉ni a꞉na uludu alifa꞉.”
Fol eyo꞉ a꞉la꞉sa꞉labiki, Yu ko꞉go꞉do꞉ kalu iyo꞉ a꞉ma꞉la꞉bo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Ge a꞉la꞉go꞉ka꞉ a꞉la꞉likiyo꞉ mo꞉fo꞉so꞉ nimo꞉wo꞉ Yudia a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉yo꞉ mo꞉sa꞉sa꞉ligefo꞉. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ nao i nolo꞉ ko꞉na꞉ a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ mio꞉ a꞉ma꞉yo꞉lo꞉ gilo꞉ mogago꞉ dimido꞉wo꞉ we a꞉la꞉bo꞉ nimo꞉wo꞉ mo꞉malolo꞉ me.
Heno꞉ tambo amio꞉ kaluka꞉isaleyo꞉ ho꞉gi gulugulan man fa꞉la꞉dowab a꞉no꞉ mogago꞉ dimida꞉lab a꞉la꞉sio꞉ dabu ko꞉lo꞉ asulo꞉ gilo꞉wo꞉ nilo꞉ da꞉ba꞉no꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ sa꞉la꞉bi.”
Iliyo꞉ Fola꞉yo꞉ towo꞉ sama꞉kiyo꞉ ho꞉len nowo꞉ da꞉fe alifa꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ ho꞉len a꞉na fa꞉la꞉dowabikiyo꞉, kaluka꞉isale modo꞉wo꞉ Fola꞉ aya kegeo꞉. Kea꞉folo꞉ a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ aneyo꞉ gelo꞉ a꞉namio꞉, Godeya꞉ ene kaluka꞉isale ko꞉lo꞉ bo꞉fo꞉lab man a꞉no꞉ widakiyo꞉, iyo꞉ Ya꞉suwo꞉ tilidabuma꞉ki, Mosesa꞉ ele saefa꞉ o꞉lia꞉ Dinali Sa꞉lan kaluwa꞉lo꞉ sa꞉sa꞉lo꞉ a꞉no꞉ agela꞉ miakiyo꞉, fanda wido꞉.
Fola꞉lo꞉ to sa꞉lab a꞉no꞉ kalu nolo꞉ tilidabu ko꞉sega nolo꞉ mo꞉tilidabu.
Iliyo꞉ asulo꞉ imilise mo꞉dowa꞉sa꞉ga꞉, nolo꞉ ha꞉na꞉nigabiki, Fol eyo꞉ elema꞉nikiyo꞉, towo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Godeya꞉ Mamaya꞉yo꞉ ge ma꞉mu imo꞉wo꞉ to hendeleyo꞉ dinali sa꞉lan kalu Aisaya eya a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ sa꞉lakiyo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉,
“‘Kaluka꞉isale ilo꞉wa ha꞉na꞉sa꞉ga꞉, imo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉sa꞉la꞉bi. Gio꞉ ni towo꞉ mada da꞉da꞉mela꞉ib ko꞉sega, hendeleyo꞉ mada mo꞉fanda asuluma꞉ib. Gio꞉ nilo꞉ dimidano꞉ ba꞉da꞉mela꞉ib ko꞉sega ha꞉go꞉ mada mo꞉dinafa asuluma꞉ib.
Mo꞉wo꞉ kaluka꞉isale i wema꞉ asulo꞉wo꞉ halaido꞉ dowaki, ka꞉la꞉no꞉ kagedeliaki, a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ siyo꞉ suguli ko꞉lo꞉ a꞉lab. A꞉la꞉bo꞉ mo꞉ngo꞉ kibabeyo꞉, ili siyo꞉ kolaitaliki o꞉li ba꞉babe, ka꞉la꞉no꞉ togo꞉ alitaliki da꞉babe, a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ asulo꞉wo꞉ kolaitaliki asulumabe. Iyo꞉ nelo꞉doba꞉da꞉ nodolalikiyo꞉, Niyo꞉ iyo꞉ falele alifo꞉.’ Aisayayo꞉ a꞉la꞉sa꞉sa꞉lo꞉.
“A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ gio꞉ dinafa asula꞉bi. Godeya꞉lo꞉ kalu gasilia꞉no꞉ to man nafa a꞉no꞉ Yu kaluka꞉isalema ilo꞉wa iliga꞉fo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ iyo꞉ hendele iligi da꞉ba꞉ib.” Fol eyo꞉ imo꞉wo꞉ wido꞉.
<range>
Dona a꞉la꞉ a꞉namio꞉ Fol e a elo꞉ sab a꞉no꞉ kililia꞉liki silikiyo꞉, kaluka꞉isaleyo꞉ elo꞉wa yab a꞉no꞉ e sagalo꞉ ba꞉da꞉sen.
A꞉la꞉gabiki, kalu noma꞉yo꞉ Folo꞉ mo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ eyo꞉ Godeya꞉ ene kaluka꞉isale ko꞉lo꞉ bo꞉fo꞉lab man o꞉lia꞉, Ya꞉su Keliso Alan a꞉ma꞉ mano꞉ halaido꞉ wido꞉.





























































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































Fol ne, Sailaso꞉, Timotiyo꞉ niliyo꞉ to we sa꞉sa꞉lakiyo꞉, Do Gode o꞉lia꞉ Alan Ya꞉su Keliso o꞉lia꞉ma꞉ kaluka꞉isale, Tesalonaika sa꞉s usamilo꞉ sab o꞉mo꞉ sa꞉sa꞉liga꞉to꞉l. Godeya꞉ ene kanulo꞉ o꞉lia꞉ ha꞉sa mesa꞉no꞉ man a꞉no꞉lia꞉yo꞉ gi o꞉lia꞉ dofo꞉melea꞉ki, Godemo꞉ dulugu so꞉lo꞉l.
Ho꞉leno꞉ tambo niliyo꞉ gio꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ Godemo꞉ dulugu sa꞉lakiyo꞉, mada o꞉m a꞉la꞉sa꞉la꞉sen.
Giliyo꞉ tili da꞉da꞉ga꞉ man nafale dimida꞉sen, a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ nol o꞉lia꞉yo꞉ ha꞉fo꞉ disa꞉laki, iyo꞉ asuwa꞉ta꞉sen, a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ Ya꞉su Kelisowo꞉ hendele a꞉ma꞉la꞉ mia꞉nigab a꞉la꞉bo꞉ giliyo꞉ tilida꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉, yasila꞉lab ko꞉lo꞉ halale kagaya꞉sen. Niliyo꞉ gililo꞉ dimido꞉ a꞉no꞉ asula꞉liki, Do Godemo꞉ mada o꞉m a꞉la꞉sa꞉la꞉sen.
Godeya꞉ to nafa a꞉no꞉ gilo꞉wa fa꞉la꞉dowabikiyo꞉, to mosole ko꞉lo꞉ fa꞉la꞉dowo꞉ma. To a꞉no꞉ niliyo꞉ hendele tilida꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉, halale widakiyo꞉, Godeya꞉ ene halaido꞉ o꞉lia꞉ Mama Malilo꞉ enedo꞉ o꞉lia꞉yo꞉ mio꞉. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ niliyo꞉ gi o꞉lia꞉ silikiyo꞉, gio꞉ asuwa꞉foma꞉kiyo꞉, nililo꞉ man nafale dimido꞉ a꞉no꞉ giliyo꞉ asulufo꞉lab. Alan Ya꞉su o꞉lia꞉ nililo꞉ man nafale dimido꞉ aumbo꞉ giliyo꞉ kudu ane. Giliyo꞉ hida꞉yo꞉wo꞉ alan di ko꞉sega Mama Malilo꞉ a꞉ma꞉ sagalo꞉wa ilikiyo꞉, Ene to nafa a꞉no꞉ sagala꞉liki dabu. A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ ni naoi, Godeya꞉lo꞉ asula꞉lab kaluka꞉isale gi a꞉na enedo꞉ da꞉fe alifelo꞉wo꞉ o꞉m niliyo꞉ a꞉la꞉asulo꞉. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ niliyo꞉ Godemo꞉wo꞉ mada o꞉m a꞉la꞉sa꞉la꞉sen.
<range>
<range>
Giliyo꞉ a꞉la꞉dimido꞉ ko꞉lo꞉, o꞉go꞉ tilidabu kaluka꞉isale Masedonia hen o꞉lia꞉ Akaya hen a꞉namilo꞉ sab tambo a꞉ma꞉yo꞉ gililo꞉ man nafale dimido꞉ a꞉no꞉ asula꞉liki, gio꞉ kudu ha꞉nab.
A꞉la꞉dimida꞉i ha꞉nab ko꞉lo꞉ Alana꞉ towo꞉ geya handalota꞉ga꞉, Masedonia hen o꞉lia꞉ Akaya hen o꞉lia꞉ya ane komba. Ko꞉sega gililo꞉ Gode amilo꞉ tilidabu to a꞉no꞉ heno꞉ nololo꞉ da꞉da꞉li ha꞉nab ko꞉lo꞉ niliyo꞉ gililo꞉ tilidabu a꞉no꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ a꞉sa꞉ma꞉no꞉wo꞉ mo꞉lido꞉.
Mo꞉wo꞉ gililo꞉ dimido꞉ a꞉no꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ ililo꞉ nemo꞉lo꞉ malolo꞉meyo꞉ we. Nio꞉ gelo꞉wa fa꞉la꞉dowo꞉ amio꞉ tililiale. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ giliyo꞉ madali godeyo꞉ ta꞉ta꞉ga꞉, Gode mela꞉no꞉lelo꞉ a꞉lab a꞉no꞉ tilida꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Ene nanogo꞉ dimidale.
A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ Godeya꞉ Inso꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ a꞉ma꞉la꞉ mia꞉no꞉ a꞉no꞉ giliyo꞉ yasila꞉labeka꞉ a꞉la꞉bo꞉, iliyo꞉ nemo꞉wo꞉ malolo꞉ me ko꞉lo꞉ so꞉lo꞉l. Godeya꞉ Inso꞉ Ya꞉su e sowa꞉sa꞉ga꞉ a꞉ma꞉la꞉ a꞉dasilia꞉ga꞉ Hebene sab. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ nio꞉ Godeya꞉lo꞉ gadia꞉sa꞉ga꞉ wa꞉ldo꞉ dimiab a꞉namio꞉ diabena꞉ki, Ya꞉suwa꞉yo꞉ nio꞉ a꞉ma꞉la꞉ gasila꞉sen.
Ni nao i, nio꞉ gelo꞉wa ya꞉sa꞉ga꞉ ilikilo꞉ nanog dimido꞉ a꞉no꞉ mo꞉wala꞉.
Nio꞉ Filibai siliki, gilo꞉wa o꞉mia꞉no꞉ amio꞉, kaluka꞉isaleya꞉lo꞉ nimo꞉lo꞉ dikidiakilo꞉ dio꞉ge sio꞉ a꞉no꞉ gio꞉ asulo꞉. Ko꞉sega nili Godeya꞉yo꞉ nio꞉ asufa꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ kalu nolba꞉yo꞉ nimo꞉wo꞉ gis alan dowabikiyo꞉, nio꞉ mo꞉tagilaki Godeya꞉ to nafa a꞉no꞉ gimo꞉wo꞉ ka wido꞉l.
Niliyo꞉ to widakiyo꞉, towo꞉ halayo꞉ mo꞉widaki, asulo꞉wo꞉ nowa dia꞉fo꞉likiyo꞉ mo꞉wido꞉l, a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ dikidakiyo꞉ mo꞉wido꞉l.
A꞉la꞉do꞉ mo꞉go꞉ ko꞉lo꞉, Godeya꞉ to nafayo꞉ sama꞉kiyo꞉, Eyo꞉ nio꞉ dibebea꞉sa꞉ga꞉ da꞉feyo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ nio꞉ elo꞉ asulo꞉ o꞉leaumbo꞉ hendele wida꞉sen. A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ niliyo꞉ kaluka꞉isaleyo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ sagale alitaki wido꞉ma. Gode nili asulo꞉lo꞉ dibibiakilo꞉ bo꞉fo꞉lab a꞉no꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ sagale alita꞉sen.
Niliyo꞉ kelego꞉ gililo꞉ da꞉lab a꞉no꞉ mo꞉meselaka susululakiyo꞉, gimo꞉wo꞉ mo꞉kai a꞉la꞉ sa꞉la꞉sen. Man nililo꞉ dimida꞉sen a꞉no꞉ giliyo꞉ asulab a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉, Gode elo꞉ mada asulufo꞉lab.
Giliyo꞉lo꞉ a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ kalu nolba꞉yo꞉lo꞉ nio꞉ wabulu sama꞉kiyo꞉ mo꞉kedo꞉. Kelisowa꞉lo꞉ iliga꞉felo꞉ kaluwo꞉ ni ko꞉lo꞉, giliyo꞉ nio꞉ tilido꞉ma꞉kiyo꞉ o꞉li sa꞉ma꞉no꞉ dowo꞉ ko꞉sega, a꞉la꞉do꞉ mo꞉gaki, gi o꞉lia꞉ sen amio꞉, nio꞉ ha꞉sa siliki, anowa꞉lo꞉ so꞉wa galin ko꞉lo꞉ bo꞉fo꞉lowan o꞉ngo꞉ dowa꞉sen.
<range>
Nio꞉ gimo꞉wo꞉ mada ha꞉fo꞉wo꞉ disa꞉ ko꞉lo꞉, Godeya꞉ to nafayo꞉ gimo꞉ sa꞉ma꞉no꞉wo꞉ sagalo꞉. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ niliyo꞉ gio꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ mada kanulakiyo꞉, nili mela꞉no꞉wo꞉ o꞉li walema꞉no꞉.
Ni nao i, nililo꞉ halaido꞉ nanog dimido꞉ a꞉no꞉ gio꞉ mada asulo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉lab. Niliyo꞉ Godeya꞉ to nafa gimo꞉lo꞉ wida꞉len amio꞉, ni tili doma꞉no꞉wo꞉ gio꞉ kele asulabena꞉kiyo꞉, niliyo꞉ ho꞉lenowo꞉lo꞉, nuluwo꞉lo꞉ nanogo꞉ dia꞉len.
Nio꞉ tilidabu kaluka꞉isale gi o꞉lia꞉ silikiyo꞉, nio꞉ malilo꞉ man o꞉lia꞉ digalo꞉ man o꞉lia꞉ dimidaki, kalu nolba꞉yo꞉ hala dimido꞉ a꞉la꞉bo꞉ mo꞉sama꞉ki dimida꞉sen. Gio꞉lo꞉ Godeya꞉lo꞉ man nilo꞉ dimido꞉ a꞉no꞉ ba꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉ asulo꞉.
Iyaya꞉lo꞉ ene so꞉wa asulakilo꞉ tilidowan aumbo꞉, niliyo꞉ gena꞉li gena꞉li a꞉la꞉ bo꞉fo꞉len, a꞉la꞉bo꞉ gio꞉ asulo꞉.
A꞉la꞉do꞉ dimida꞉len a꞉namio꞉, giliyo꞉ Godeya꞉lo꞉ asulab man aumb dimidama꞉kiyo꞉, niliyo꞉ gio꞉ halale alitaki, nofolo꞉ towo꞉ sa꞉la꞉liki, towo꞉ halaido꞉ wida꞉len. Mo꞉wo꞉ Godeya꞉ ene ho꞉ alan usa mesea꞉ki a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉, Elo꞉ bo꞉fo꞉lowan kaluka꞉isale o꞉lia꞉ usa doma꞉ki, Gode Eyo꞉ gio꞉ ho꞉ida꞉lab.
Niliyo꞉ Godeya꞉ to wida꞉len amio꞉, gio꞉ kaluwa꞉ tole sa꞉lab a꞉la꞉bo꞉ mo꞉da꞉daki, Godeya꞉ ene to hendele sa꞉labolo꞉b a꞉la꞉ da꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉ tilidabu ko꞉lo꞉, niliyo꞉ Godemo꞉wo꞉ mada o꞉m a꞉la꞉bo꞉ wa꞉ka a꞉la꞉ sa꞉la꞉len. A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ Godeya꞉ to a꞉no꞉, tilidabu kaluka꞉isale gi usa do꞉waki, nanogo꞉ dia꞉b.
Ni nao i, Keliso kaluka꞉isale, Yudia hen amilo꞉ sa꞉sen o꞉mo꞉wo꞉lo꞉ hida꞉yo꞉ fa꞉la꞉dowo꞉ aumbo꞉, gimo꞉wo꞉lo꞉ o꞉leo꞉ngo꞉ ka di. Yu kaluwa꞉lo꞉ hida꞉yo꞉ imo꞉lo꞉ dimi o꞉leaumbo꞉, giasi kaluwa꞉yo꞉ gimo꞉wo꞉lo꞉ hida꞉yo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉dimi.
Ya꞉su Alan o꞉lia꞉ Godeya꞉ dinali sa꞉lan kalu nolo꞉lo꞉ Yu kalu i a꞉ma꞉yo꞉ sanale. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ i a꞉ma꞉yo꞉ nio꞉lo꞉ o꞉lu ga꞉fela꞉sen. Niliyo꞉ Yu kaluka꞉isalemayo꞉ wida꞉la꞉ga꞉ dowab amio꞉, Godeya꞉yo꞉ iyo꞉ gasiliabena꞉kiyo꞉, Yu kalu i a꞉ma꞉yo꞉ nililo꞉ sa꞉ma꞉no꞉wo꞉ ka꞉ma꞉no꞉ a꞉la꞉li kedo꞉. Ililo꞉ a꞉la꞉do꞉ dimido꞉ a꞉ma꞉yo꞉ Godeyo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ mo꞉be alifa꞉, a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ kaluka꞉isale tambomo꞉wo꞉ giso꞉ alan dowa꞉sen. Inin mogago꞉ dimida꞉len a꞉namio꞉, dibida꞉i ya꞉la꞉ga꞉ wa꞉litab ko꞉lo꞉ Godeya꞉lo꞉ gadio꞉ wa꞉l a꞉no꞉ inibo꞉ o꞉go꞉ dimiab ko꞉m.
<range>
Ni nao i, tamin amio꞉ Yu kaluwa꞉lo꞉ hida꞉yo꞉ dimi a꞉namio꞉, na꞉no꞉ do꞉mo꞉wa꞉yo꞉ alobanaga꞉ta꞉ga꞉ ane ko꞉sega, asulo꞉wo꞉ imilise o꞉dofolikiyo꞉, gio꞉ wa꞉ka galima꞉no꞉ a꞉la꞉liki, niliyo꞉ togo꞉ mada keda꞉len.
Nio꞉ gelo꞉wa mia꞉no꞉ asulo꞉. No꞉no꞉n ne gelo꞉wa mia꞉no꞉ asulaki, togo꞉ keda꞉len ko꞉sega Setene eyo꞉ nio꞉ ka꞉la꞉lab.
Nili Alan Ya꞉su e yalikiyo꞉, nio꞉ e wo꞉lokana kagayakiyo꞉, nilo꞉ halale kagama꞉no꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ nilo꞉ sagale alifa꞉no꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ nilo꞉ nanogo꞉ dimida꞉sa꞉ga꞉ tinio꞉ a꞉la꞉likilo꞉ boba a꞉no꞉ o꞉ba? Kaluka꞉isale gi o꞉m.
Giliyo꞉ ni ko꞉lo꞉ wabuda sagale alitakiyo꞉, hendeleyo꞉ gi dowab.
Niliyo꞉ gio꞉ ba꞉ba꞉no꞉ alan asula꞉li ha꞉na꞉la꞉ga꞉yo꞉, na꞉no꞉ Atens amisa꞉n a꞉na siliki, Timotiyo꞉ gilo꞉wa iliga꞉fa꞉no꞉ a꞉la꞉liki nenela꞉sa꞉ga꞉ saefa꞉. Nili nao Timoti, Gode o꞉lia꞉ nanog diakilo꞉, Ya꞉su Kelisowa꞉ to nafalo꞉ wida꞉li sia꞉seno꞉ e. A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ tilidabu gililo꞉wo꞉ halale alitakiyo꞉, gio꞉ halaido꞉ ha꞉na꞉melea꞉kiyo꞉, Timotiyo꞉ gilo꞉wa iliga꞉fo꞉.
<range>
Hida꞉yo꞉ gililo꞉ diab koma꞉yo꞉, tilidabu gililo꞉wo꞉ babalelabena꞉ki, Timotiyo꞉ gelo꞉wa iliga꞉fo꞉. Hida꞉yo꞉ wengo꞉wo꞉ Gode eyo꞉ nimo꞉ dima꞉ki da꞉feyo꞉lo꞉b a꞉la꞉bo꞉ gio꞉ asulo꞉.
Hendele, nio꞉ gi o꞉lia꞉ sen amio꞉, hida꞉yo꞉wo꞉ nilo꞉ amio꞉ fa꞉la꞉doma꞉ib a꞉la꞉bo꞉ gimo꞉wo꞉ sa꞉la꞉len ko꞉lo꞉ ninindo꞉ sa꞉la꞉len aumbo꞉ fa꞉la꞉dowab a꞉no꞉ gio꞉ asulab.
A꞉no꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ asulakiyo꞉, niyo꞉ mo꞉yasilima꞉no꞉ dowo꞉lo꞉biki, Timotiyo꞉ gi tilidabuwo꞉ fanda bo꞉ba꞉kiyo꞉, gelo꞉wa iliga꞉fo꞉ko. Ni asulakiyo꞉, Setene e gilo꞉wa fa꞉la꞉dowa꞉sa꞉ga꞉, tilidabu gililo꞉wo꞉ da꞉feyo꞉lalega, nilido꞉ nanog di a꞉no꞉ o꞉ngo꞉ malo꞉ngo꞉ fa꞉la꞉doma꞉ibele, a꞉la꞉asulaki tagilo꞉.
A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ Timoti e gilo꞉ amilo꞉ seno꞉ ta꞉ta꞉ga꞉, o꞉go꞉ nilo꞉ wena fa꞉la꞉dowakiyo꞉, gilo꞉ tilidabu o꞉lia꞉ ha꞉fo꞉ disa꞉la꞉sen man a꞉no꞉lia꞉yo꞉ nimo꞉wo꞉ mada towo꞉ nafa ko꞉lo꞉ malolo꞉ miab. Giliyo꞉ nio꞉ asula꞉likiyo꞉, sagalo꞉wo꞉ alan dowa꞉sen ko꞉lo꞉, gio꞉ misio꞉ bo꞉bo꞉losa꞉ a꞉la꞉do꞉ nililo꞉ asula꞉sen aumbo꞉, giliyo꞉lo꞉ nio꞉ bo꞉bo꞉losa꞉ a꞉la꞉asula꞉senka꞉ a꞉la꞉liki, Timoti eyo꞉ nimo꞉wo꞉ malolo꞉ miabe.
Ni nao i, niliyo꞉ to a꞉no꞉ dabu ko꞉lo꞉ nio꞉ nagalo꞉ o꞉lia꞉ hida꞉yo꞉ alan o꞉lia꞉lo꞉ ba꞉dab us a꞉namio꞉, tilidabu gililo꞉wo꞉ halaido꞉ a꞉lab koma꞉yo꞉ nio꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ halale alitakigab.
Gio꞉ Kalu Alan o꞉lia꞉ oga꞉dita꞉ga꞉ halaido꞉ kagafo꞉lab ko꞉lo꞉, nio꞉ o꞉go꞉ mela꞉no꞉wo꞉ nafale ko꞉lo꞉ dio꞉l.
Giliyo꞉ nio꞉ mada alan sagale alifa꞉ ko꞉lo꞉, niliyo꞉ Godeya꞉lo꞉ wabulusa꞉lakiyo꞉ emo꞉wo꞉ mada o꞉m a꞉la꞉sa꞉la꞉sen a꞉no꞉ ko꞉mba.
Gio꞉ wa꞉kabiyo꞉ a꞉ba꞉ba꞉no꞉ a꞉lakiyo꞉, gili tilidabuwo꞉ a꞉halale alifoma꞉kiyo꞉, nuluwo꞉lo꞉ ho꞉lenowo꞉lo꞉ niliyo꞉ Godemo꞉wo꞉ towo꞉ sa꞉la꞉len.
A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ o꞉go꞉ gio꞉ ba꞉ba꞉ mia꞉no꞉ a꞉la꞉likiyo꞉, Do Gode o꞉lia꞉ nili Alan Ya꞉su o꞉lia꞉ma꞉yo꞉ togo꞉ dinafa walama꞉ki, niliyo꞉ dulugu so꞉lo꞉l.
Nililo꞉ gimo꞉lo꞉ ha꞉fo꞉ disa꞉la꞉sen man a꞉no꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ anayab o꞉leaumbo꞉, gegelebo꞉lo꞉ a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ nol o꞉lia꞉lo꞉ ha꞉fo꞉ disa꞉lan man a꞉no꞉lo꞉ wa꞉lita꞉ga꞉ alalia꞉ga꞉ hamana꞉ki, Godemo꞉ dulugu so꞉lo꞉l.
A꞉la꞉fo꞉lalikiyo꞉, Godeya꞉yo꞉ asulo꞉ gililo꞉wo꞉ halale alita꞉len ko꞉lo꞉, Ya꞉su Alan o꞉lia꞉ ene malilo꞉ kaluka꞉isale tambo o꞉lia꞉lo꞉ yab amio꞉, gio꞉ hala dimido꞉wo꞉ aundo꞉ma dowaki, malilo꞉ elena bo꞉ba꞉ki, dulugu so꞉lo꞉l.
Ni nao i, to nolo꞉ a꞉sa꞉ma꞉nigo꞉l. Godelo꞉ sagalema꞉no꞉ man a꞉no꞉ giliyo꞉ kudu hamana꞉ki, niliyo꞉ tamin amio꞉ gimo꞉wo꞉ wido꞉ ko꞉lo꞉, gio꞉ kudu ha꞉na꞉lab. Ko꞉sega o꞉go꞉ gio꞉ man a꞉no꞉ wa꞉ka halale a꞉kudu ha꞉na꞉ melea꞉ki, Ya꞉su Alana꞉ wi amio꞉ niliyo꞉ to a꞉no꞉ wa꞉ka halale so꞉lo꞉l.
Nilo꞉ Ya꞉su Alana꞉ wi amilo꞉ to ko꞉lo꞉ fanda wido꞉ a꞉no꞉ giliyo꞉ asulo꞉.
Godeya꞉lo꞉ asulab aumbo꞉ we. Gio꞉ Godeya꞉ eno꞉le dowaki, digalo꞉ dowa꞉bi. Gio꞉ uwo꞉wo꞉ dia꞉so꞉bo.
Gio꞉ malilo꞉ man o꞉lia꞉ digalo꞉ man a꞉no꞉lia꞉yo꞉ kudu ha꞉naki, ginin asulo꞉ a꞉no꞉ tilidowa꞉bi.
Ha꞉la꞉ kaluka꞉isaleyo꞉ Godeyo꞉ mo꞉asulaki, inin uwo꞉ dia꞉no꞉ asulab aundo꞉ kudu ha꞉na꞉sen a꞉la꞉bo꞉ gio꞉ dimida꞉so꞉bo.
A꞉la꞉gakiyo꞉, giliyo꞉ Keliso gao nowo꞉mbo꞉wo꞉ mogago꞉wo꞉ mo꞉dimidaki, a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ inin ingayo꞉ afa dia꞉so꞉bo. Kalu abeyo꞉ man mogago꞉lo꞉ dimidab a꞉no꞉ Godeya꞉yo꞉ e falasila꞉ma꞉ib a꞉la꞉bo꞉ niliyo꞉ tamina hagugu sio꞉.
Mo꞉wo꞉ Godeya꞉yo꞉ nio꞉ man mogago꞉ dimidama꞉ki ho꞉ido꞉ma. Eyo꞉ nio꞉ man digalo꞉ kudu ha꞉na꞉sa꞉ga꞉, malilo꞉le doma꞉ki ho꞉ido꞉.
A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ kalu abeyo꞉ to nilo꞉ wido꞉l welo꞉ gola ba꞉dab a꞉no꞉, kaluwa꞉ towo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ gola ba꞉daba. Malilo꞉ Mama gimo꞉lo꞉ dimia꞉sen Gode E ko꞉lo꞉ gola ba꞉dab.
Godeya꞉yo꞉ gegeledo꞉ ha꞉fo꞉ disa꞉ma꞉no꞉ man a꞉no꞉ gininbo꞉wo꞉ wido꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ nio꞉ to a꞉no꞉ wa꞉ka sa꞉sa꞉lema꞉no꞉wo꞉ aundo꞉ma.
Hendele, gio꞉ Masedonia hen amilo꞉ nao o꞉lia꞉ nado o꞉lia꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ Keliso sab a꞉no꞉ tambomo꞉wo꞉ ha꞉fo꞉wo꞉ disa꞉la꞉sen. Ko꞉sega ni nao i, gio꞉ man a꞉no꞉ wa꞉ka halale a꞉kudu ha꞉na꞉melea꞉kiyo꞉, niliyo꞉ gimo꞉wo꞉ halale so꞉lo꞉l.
Gio꞉ ha꞉sa mesa꞉no꞉ man a꞉no꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ kudu ha꞉na꞉bi. Gio꞉ kelego꞉ noma꞉lo꞉ dimidabo꞉ mo꞉sa꞉laki, kelego꞉ go꞉no꞉ndo꞉wo꞉ dinafa tilidowa꞉bi. Gio꞉ bo꞉sulakima, go꞉no꞉n dagiya꞉ nanogo꞉ dimida꞉bi. Nililo꞉ tamin amilo꞉ gimo꞉lo꞉ sio꞉ o꞉leaumbo꞉ wa꞉ka so꞉lo꞉l.
Gio꞉ a꞉la꞉dimidalikiyo꞉, ha꞉la꞉ kaluka꞉isaleya꞉yo꞉ gili man dimido꞉ a꞉no꞉ ba꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉, ge hendele digalo꞉ kalu a꞉la꞉asuluma꞉ib. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ gio꞉ nowo꞉mbo꞉ asuwa꞉foma꞉kiyo꞉ mo꞉asuluma꞉ib.
Nao gio꞉, kaluka꞉isale sowab amio꞉, ha꞉la꞉ kalu iliyo꞉ misio꞉ mo꞉ba꞉ba꞉no꞉lo꞉b a꞉lakiyo꞉ nofolo꞉wo꞉ alan dowa꞉sen ko꞉lo꞉, gio꞉ a꞉la꞉bo꞉ dimidabena꞉kiyo꞉, sowab kaluka꞉isale amilo꞉ fa꞉la꞉doma꞉ibo꞉, gimo꞉wo꞉ fanda sa꞉ma꞉nigo꞉l.
Nililo꞉ tilidabuwo꞉ we. Ya꞉suwo꞉ sowa꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, a꞉dasilia꞉gane ko꞉lo꞉, kaluka꞉isale abeyo꞉ Eya tilida꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉lo꞉ sowa꞉lab a꞉no꞉, Godeya꞉yo꞉ Ya꞉su o꞉lia꞉ tililia꞉ mia꞉ib.
Ya꞉su Alana꞉lo꞉ to wido꞉wo꞉ we, niliyo꞉ gimo꞉wo꞉ sa꞉ma꞉nigo꞉l. Alando꞉ yab ho꞉len a꞉namio꞉, kaluka꞉isale ni mela꞉no꞉lo꞉ o꞉sab we, sowo꞉ kaluka꞉isale i a꞉no꞉ tiginila꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, tamin amio꞉ ni ko꞉lebo꞉ mo꞉ha꞉na꞉ib.
Ya꞉su Alan e Hebene a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ yakiyo꞉, to halale sa꞉lab o꞉lia꞉, ma꞉mula꞉ misa꞉ kaluwa꞉lo꞉ to sa꞉lab o꞉lia꞉, Godeya꞉lo꞉ belolo꞉ foma꞉no꞉ olo bulu a꞉no꞉lia꞉, e tima꞉ib. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ kaluka꞉isale eya tilida꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉lo꞉ sowo꞉ i a꞉no꞉, tamina dasima꞉ib.
A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ Godeya꞉yo꞉ kaluka꞉isale mela꞉no꞉lo꞉ o꞉lab nio꞉ o꞉lia꞉, sowo꞉ dasilia꞉gane a꞉no꞉lia꞉yo꞉ halona dia꞉ga꞉, kola꞉ usa kegea꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, Alano꞉ akin amio꞉ ua galilia꞉ib. A꞉la꞉go꞉ko꞉lo꞉ nio꞉ Alan o꞉lia꞉yo꞉ mela꞉no꞉ mela꞉no꞉ mela꞉ib.
A꞉la꞉dimidama꞉ib ko꞉lo꞉, to wema꞉yo꞉ gegelebo꞉ asulo꞉wo꞉ halalema꞉kiyo꞉, sa꞉la꞉lubi.
Nao i, gio꞉ Ya꞉sulo꞉ mia꞉no꞉ ho꞉len o꞉lia꞉ ofa꞉si o꞉lia꞉yo꞉ a꞉na fa꞉la꞉doma꞉ibka꞉ a꞉la꞉bo꞉ gimo꞉wo꞉ mo꞉sa꞉sa꞉lima꞉no꞉.
Mo꞉wo꞉, Alan e yakiyo꞉, afalo꞉ dian kalu ko꞉lo꞉ nululo꞉ yan aumb mia꞉ib a꞉la꞉bo꞉, gio꞉ o꞉ma asulufo꞉lab.
Kaluka꞉isaleya꞉ sa꞉lakiyo꞉, “Nio꞉ hida꞉yo꞉wo꞉ aundo꞉ma, ga꞉li so꞉l,” a꞉la꞉sa꞉la꞉li sen amio꞉, ilo꞉ mogagila꞉ma꞉no꞉wo꞉ wigibole a꞉naka fa꞉la꞉dowaki iligila꞉ma꞉ib ko꞉lo꞉, ga alela꞉sen a꞉ma꞉lo꞉ nagalo꞉ fa꞉la꞉dowan aumbo꞉ fa꞉la꞉doma꞉ib ko꞉lo꞉ kaluka꞉isale a꞉no꞉ mada mo꞉yamisuluma꞉ib.
Ko꞉sega nao i, gio꞉ sololiya saba ko꞉lo꞉, ho꞉len a꞉no꞉ fa꞉la꞉dowalikiyo꞉, gio꞉ afalo꞉ dian kalu yab amilo꞉ iligan aumbo꞉ mo꞉iligima꞉ib.
Gio꞉ tambo ho꞉lena꞉ so꞉wa ko꞉lo꞉ ho꞉len usa a꞉lab. Nio꞉ sololi o꞉lia꞉ nulu dowab a꞉ma꞉ so꞉wama.
A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ kalu nolo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ alifo꞉lab o꞉leaumbo꞉, nio꞉ mo꞉dimidama꞉niki. Ko꞉sega nio꞉ sikaga siliki, ninina꞉ma꞉la꞉yo꞉ tilidoma꞉niki.
Mo꞉wo꞉ alilan o꞉lia꞉ aluna꞉ ho꞉no꞉ nakilo꞉ no꞉no꞉lan man a꞉no꞉lia꞉yo꞉, nulu a꞉na dimidan.
Ko꞉sega nio꞉ ho꞉lena꞉ so꞉wa ko꞉lo꞉ ninina꞉ma꞉la꞉yo꞉ tilidoma꞉niki. Kaluwa꞉lo꞉ bio꞉ ta꞉lian aumbo꞉, niliyo꞉ nol o꞉lia꞉yo꞉ ha꞉fo꞉ disa꞉laki, tilidabuwo꞉ dinafa ta꞉lia꞉niki. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ Godeya꞉lo꞉ nilo꞉ gasilia꞉no꞉ a꞉no꞉ hendele fa꞉la꞉doma꞉ib a꞉la꞉bo꞉ asula꞉liki yasilima꞉niki.
Godeya꞉yo꞉ nio꞉ Ene kulufa꞉yo꞉wa꞉lo꞉ falasila꞉ma꞉no꞉ a꞉no꞉ dima꞉ki da꞉feyo꞉ma. Ko꞉sega Godeya꞉yo꞉ nio꞉ gasiliakiyo꞉, Alan Ya꞉su Kelisowa a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ ene mela꞉no꞉wo꞉ nimo꞉ dima꞉ki da꞉fe alifa꞉.
Nio꞉ o꞉salikiyo꞉lo꞉, sowalikiyo꞉lo꞉ Ya꞉su o꞉lia꞉ mesea꞉kiyo꞉, Ya꞉su e ni asuwa꞉taki sowo꞉.
A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ gio꞉ o꞉gdo꞉ dimida꞉lab o꞉leaumbo꞉, gegelebo꞉ asuwa꞉takiyo꞉, asulo꞉wo꞉ halale alita꞉lubi.
Ni nao i, kaluka꞉isale gilo꞉ halaido꞉ asuwa꞉tab o꞉lia꞉, gili sa꞉s amilo꞉ bo꞉fo꞉lowan o꞉lia꞉, gi ko꞉lo꞉ hagugakilo꞉ digalo꞉ tolo꞉ sa꞉la꞉lab i a꞉no꞉, giliyo꞉ asulaki, a꞉ma꞉ ha꞉ga dowa꞉bi.
Iliyo꞉ nanog halaido꞉ dimidabo꞉lo꞉b a꞉la꞉bo꞉, giliyo꞉ dinafa asula꞉sa꞉ga꞉, imo꞉wo꞉ ha꞉fo꞉wo꞉ disa꞉lakiyo꞉, ili ha꞉ga mada dowa꞉bi. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ gio꞉ gegelebo꞉ ha꞉sa dowa꞉bi.
Ni nao i, gio꞉ kaluka꞉isale bo꞉sulakilo꞉ sab imo꞉wo꞉ hagugubo꞉ sa꞉la꞉bi. Kaluka꞉isale tagilakilo꞉ sab i a꞉no꞉ halale alitaki, towo꞉ sa꞉la꞉lubi. Kaluka꞉isale halaido꞉lo꞉ mo꞉sab a꞉no꞉ asuwa꞉ta꞉bi. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ kaluka꞉isale tambomo꞉wo꞉ ha꞉sa dowa꞉bi.
Kaluka꞉isale nolba꞉yo꞉ man mogago꞉lo꞉ dimidab o꞉mo꞉wo꞉ wa꞉deabena꞉ki, gio꞉ ka꞉la꞉lubi. Ho꞉leno꞉ tambo gegelebo꞉lo꞉, ha꞉la꞉ kalumo꞉wo꞉lo꞉, tambo ha꞉fo꞉wo꞉ disa꞉la꞉lubi.
Gio꞉ ho꞉leno꞉ tambo sagala꞉lubi. Godemo꞉wo꞉ dulugu sa꞉la꞉i ha꞉na꞉ mela꞉no꞉wo꞉ eda꞉so꞉bo.
<range>
Gilo꞉ amio꞉ kelego꞉ ko꞉li ko꞉lilo꞉wo꞉ fa꞉la꞉dowalikiyo꞉, Godemo꞉wo꞉ mada o꞉m a꞉la꞉sa꞉la꞉lubi. Gio꞉ Ya꞉su Kelisowa dowakiyo꞉, Godeya꞉yo꞉ gio꞉ man o꞉leo꞉ngo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ dimidama꞉ki asulab.
Mamaya꞉lo꞉ nanog dimidama꞉no꞉ a꞉no꞉ de o꞉ngo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ dalila꞉so꞉bo.
Kaluka꞉isale abeyo꞉ Godeya꞉ wiya a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ dinali sa꞉lalikiyo꞉, gio꞉ to a꞉no꞉ da꞉ba꞉no꞉wo꞉ mo꞉bea꞉so꞉bo.
To sa꞉lab a꞉no꞉ tambowo꞉ aloba꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉, nafa dowab a꞉no꞉ kudu ha꞉naki, man mogago꞉ a꞉no꞉ tambo tinia꞉i ha꞉na꞉lubi.
<range>
Ha꞉salo꞉ dowan Gode eyo꞉ gio꞉ malilo꞉le tambo ta꞉fo꞉ melea꞉ki, dulugu so꞉lo꞉l. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ Godeya꞉yo꞉ gili mela꞉no꞉ mama o꞉lia꞉ asulo꞉ o꞉lia꞉, do꞉mo꞉ o꞉lia꞉ma꞉yo꞉ man mogago꞉ mo꞉dimidama꞉ki ta꞉fo꞉ ha꞉na꞉la꞉ga꞉, Alan Ya꞉su Kelisolo꞉ yab amio꞉, hala dofo꞉leno꞉ mo꞉bo꞉ba꞉ki, dulugu so꞉lo꞉l.
Gode gilo꞉ da꞉fe alita꞉lab a꞉ma꞉yo꞉, Ene dinali sio꞉ a꞉no꞉ hendele dimida꞉sen ko꞉lo꞉ Eyo꞉ mada dimidama꞉ib.
Ni nao i, giliyo꞉ nio꞉ Godemo꞉ dulugu sa꞉la꞉biyo꞉.
Gao nol o꞉lia꞉ sagale alitakiyo꞉, ebean aumbo꞉ mimila꞉bi.
Alana꞉ wiya iliki, niyo꞉ to halaido꞉ we gimo꞉ so꞉lo꞉l ko꞉lo꞉ giliyo꞉ mo꞉fo꞉s sa꞉sa꞉lo꞉ we, Keliso kaluka꞉isale tambomo꞉wo꞉ agela꞉ mia꞉bi.
Nili Alan, Ya꞉su Kelisowa꞉ ene kanulan man a꞉no꞉ gi o꞉lia꞉ dowa꞉biyo꞉.
Fol ne, Sailaso꞉, Timotiyo꞉ niliyo꞉ to we sa꞉sa꞉lakiyo꞉, Do Gode o꞉lia꞉ Alan Ya꞉su Keliso o꞉lia꞉ma꞉ kaluka꞉isale Tesalonaika sa꞉s usamilo꞉ sab o꞉mo꞉ sa꞉sa꞉liga꞉to꞉l.
Godeya꞉ ene kanulo꞉ o꞉lia꞉ ha꞉sa mesa꞉no꞉ man a꞉no꞉lia꞉yo꞉ gi o꞉lia꞉ dofo꞉melea꞉ki, Godemo꞉ dulugu so꞉lo꞉l.
Ni nao i, gili tilidabuwo꞉ anayaki halaido꞉ fa꞉la꞉ndab a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ gegelebo꞉ ha꞉fo꞉ disa꞉lan man a꞉no꞉lo꞉ gi usamio꞉ alan dowa꞉i ha꞉nab ko꞉lo꞉ niliyo꞉ ho꞉leno꞉ tambo Godemo꞉ mada o꞉m a꞉la꞉sa꞉la꞉ mela꞉niki. A꞉la꞉do꞉ dimida꞉ mela꞉no꞉wo꞉ mada nafayo꞉ o꞉m.
Hida꞉yo꞉ o꞉lia꞉ nagalo꞉ o꞉lia꞉yo꞉ gilo꞉wa fa꞉la꞉dowa꞉lab amio꞉, gio꞉ halale kagayaki, tilidabuwo꞉ o꞉ta꞉li sen ko꞉lo꞉ nio꞉ sa꞉s nola ha꞉nakiyo꞉, gio꞉ a꞉la꞉ dimida꞉lab a꞉la꞉liki, gili wiyo꞉ wabulu sa꞉la꞉lab.
Giliyo꞉ a꞉la꞉dimido꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ Gode eyo꞉ kaluka꞉isale digalo꞉le aloba꞉da꞉sen a꞉la꞉bo꞉ fanda wida꞉lab. Gio꞉ Godeya꞉ enedo꞉ bo꞉fo꞉lab usa silikiyo꞉, hida꞉yo꞉ ko꞉li ko꞉lilo꞉wo꞉ dia꞉lab ko꞉lo꞉ gio꞉ a꞉na mesa꞉no꞉wo꞉ o꞉li ko꞉lo꞉lab a꞉la꞉liki wido꞉.
Gode eyo꞉ digalo꞉le mo꞉walila꞉sen ko꞉lo꞉, kalu abeyo꞉ gimo꞉lo꞉ hideyo꞉lo꞉ dimia꞉lab o꞉mo꞉wo꞉ Gode eyo꞉ kalu a꞉no꞉ wa꞉diaki hida꞉yo꞉ dimia꞉ib.
Hida꞉yo꞉lo꞉ dia꞉lab gi a꞉no꞉ a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ nio꞉lo꞉ Gode eyo꞉ ha꞉salo꞉ mesa꞉no꞉wo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ dimia꞉ib. Ya꞉su Alan e Hebene a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ handalowakiyo꞉, ene ma꞉mula꞉ kalu halaido꞉ o꞉lia꞉ de wa꞉sowa o꞉lia꞉lo꞉ yab a꞉namio꞉ ha꞉salo꞉ mesa꞉no꞉wo꞉ a꞉na dima꞉ib.
Kaluka꞉isale abeyo꞉ Godelo꞉ mo꞉asula꞉sen a꞉no꞉lia꞉ Ya꞉su Alana꞉ to nafalo꞉ mo꞉kudu ane a꞉no꞉lia꞉yo꞉, Eyo꞉ a꞉na wa꞉deaki falasila꞉ma꞉ib.
Imo꞉lo꞉ falasila꞉ma꞉no꞉wo꞉ we. Iyo꞉ Ya꞉su Alan o꞉lia꞉ ene halaido꞉ alan a꞉no꞉lia꞉ma꞉ anibamio꞉ mo꞉mesea꞉ki, kona꞉le ta꞉fa꞉ib. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ Gode eyo꞉ iyo꞉ mogagilaki falasilakiyo꞉ ha꞉na꞉mela꞉no꞉ mela꞉ib.
Ya꞉su Alan elo꞉ yab ho꞉len a꞉namio꞉, tilidabu kaluka꞉isale enedo꞉ da꞉feyo꞉ i a꞉ma꞉yo꞉ Ya꞉su Alano꞉ wabudakiyo꞉, molo asuluma꞉ib. Nililo꞉ gimo꞉lo꞉ wido꞉ a꞉no꞉ giliyo꞉ tilidabu ko꞉lo꞉ gio꞉lo꞉ i o꞉lia꞉ ua gasama꞉ib.
Nili Gode o꞉lia꞉ Ya꞉su Keliso Alan o꞉lia꞉ma꞉yo꞉ nio꞉ kanulo꞉ alifa꞉ ko꞉lo꞉, Ya꞉suwa꞉lo꞉ mela꞉no꞉ gilo꞉ amilo꞉ dimido꞉ a꞉ma꞉yo꞉ ene wiyo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ wabudabikiyo꞉, Ya꞉su eyo꞉ gili wiyo꞉lo꞉ wabuluma꞉kiyo꞉, niliyo꞉ ho꞉leno꞉ tambo gio꞉ Godemo꞉ dulugu sa꞉la꞉sen. Godeya꞉lo꞉ gililo꞉ man nafa dimidama꞉kilo꞉ ho꞉ido꞉ a꞉no꞉ ililima꞉ki, dulugu sa꞉la꞉sen. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ man nafa gililo꞉ dimidama꞉no꞉ asulan a꞉no꞉lia꞉, Godeya tilida꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉ ilikilo꞉ nanog dimidama꞉no꞉ a꞉no꞉lia꞉yo꞉, Godeya꞉ ene halaido꞉wa꞉yo꞉ gio꞉ asuwa꞉foma꞉ki, dulugu sa꞉la꞉sen.
<range>
Ni nao i, Alan Ya꞉su Kelisowo꞉ a꞉ma꞉la꞉ mia꞉nigab amio꞉, nio꞉ e o꞉lia꞉lo꞉ gasayakilo꞉ kegenema꞉no꞉ a꞉no꞉ ko꞉lo꞉, niyo꞉ gimo꞉wo꞉ sa꞉ma꞉nigo꞉l.
Kalu Alana꞉ ho꞉leno꞉ o꞉ma fa꞉la꞉dowo꞉ ko꞉m a꞉la꞉likiyo꞉, kalu nolba꞉yo꞉ wida꞉labele, mo dinali sa꞉la꞉labele, mo mo꞉fo꞉so꞉ nili iliga꞉fo꞉ka꞉ a꞉la꞉ sa꞉la꞉likilo꞉ agelab a꞉no꞉, gio꞉ dabulalega, iligakiyo꞉ kele asula꞉so꞉bo.
Kalu nolba꞉yo꞉ a꞉la꞉ dinali sa꞉lalikiyo꞉, gio꞉ tilida꞉da꞉so꞉bo. Mo꞉wo꞉ Alana꞉ ho꞉leno꞉ o꞉semo꞉fa꞉la꞉dowab amio꞉ kaluka꞉isaleya꞉lo꞉ Godemo꞉lo꞉ a꞉la꞉iyakilo꞉ gola ba꞉ba꞉no꞉ ho꞉len a꞉no꞉ fa꞉la꞉doma꞉ib. Ho꞉len a꞉namio꞉ ele saefa꞉lo꞉ gola ba꞉ba꞉no꞉ kalu imilig a꞉no꞉ kalaba fa꞉la꞉doma꞉ib. Kalu a꞉no꞉ deya꞉ mogagila꞉ma꞉ki da꞉fe alifo꞉lab.
Kalu a꞉no꞉ fa꞉la꞉dowalikiyo꞉, eyo꞉ Gode o꞉lia꞉ madali gode kaluka꞉isaleya꞉lo꞉ wabulu sa꞉la꞉lab o꞉lia꞉mo꞉wo꞉ gis dimidaki, enena꞉ma꞉la꞉yo꞉ kailaki, nol a꞉no꞉ wa꞉la꞉ sa꞉ma꞉ib. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ eyo꞉ Godeya꞉ malilo꞉ a usa ha꞉na꞉sa꞉ga꞉ silikiyo꞉, “Godeleyo꞉ neka꞉” a꞉la꞉sa꞉la꞉mela꞉ib.
Ne gi o꞉lia꞉ silikiyo꞉, to a꞉no꞉ wido꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ gio꞉ ga꞉lila꞉yele?
Ele saefa꞉lo꞉ gola ba꞉ba꞉no꞉ kalu a꞉no꞉ ho꞉lende imilaba fa꞉la꞉doma꞉kiyo꞉, o꞉go꞉ e kafolab, a꞉la꞉bo꞉ gio꞉ asulab.
Henfelo꞉ wenamio꞉ a꞉la꞉iyan man a꞉no꞉ nanogo꞉ wo꞉no꞉lebo꞉ dia꞉lab ko꞉sega, nolo꞉ e ka꞉la꞉lab Tif amio꞉ kafolab a꞉no꞉ Godeya꞉yo꞉ dila꞉ma꞉ib ko꞉lo꞉ ele saefo꞉lo꞉ gola ba꞉ba꞉no꞉ kalu a꞉no꞉ kalab amio꞉ a꞉na fa꞉la꞉doma꞉ib. E fa꞉la꞉dota꞉ga꞉ a꞉lalikiyo꞉, Alan Ya꞉suwo꞉ a꞉ma꞉la꞉ ya꞉ga꞉yo꞉, ene meho꞉ o꞉lia꞉ ene ho꞉len bumalab o꞉lia꞉ma꞉yo꞉ kalu a꞉no꞉ sanala꞉ma꞉ib.
<range>
Kalu a꞉no꞉, Seteneya꞉ ene halaido꞉ o꞉lia꞉ fa꞉la꞉doma꞉ib ko꞉lo꞉ halaido꞉ a꞉no꞉ widakiyo꞉, eyo꞉ madali dikidaki, ele ba꞉ba꞉no꞉ o꞉lia꞉ molo ha꞉na꞉no꞉wo꞉ o꞉lia꞉ ko꞉li ko꞉lilo꞉ dimidama꞉ib.
Kaluka꞉isale mogagila꞉ma꞉no꞉ doba꞉da꞉lo꞉ ha꞉na꞉lab a꞉no꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ dikidaki, kalu a꞉ma꞉yo꞉ man mogago꞉ ko꞉li ko꞉lilo꞉ dimidama꞉ib. Kaluka꞉isale i a꞉no꞉ to hendeleyo꞉ asuluma꞉no꞉wo꞉ gola ba꞉dabiki, Godeya꞉yo꞉ iyo꞉ mo꞉gasiliab ko꞉lo꞉ iyo꞉ mogagila꞉ma꞉no꞉ doba꞉da꞉lo꞉ ha꞉na꞉lab.
A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ kaluka꞉isale i a꞉no꞉ madali to sa꞉lab a꞉no꞉ hendele a꞉nako꞉ tilidabuma꞉kiyo꞉, Godeya꞉yo꞉ iyo꞉ a꞉naka ta꞉fa꞉ib.
A꞉la꞉go꞉ko꞉lo꞉ iyo꞉ to hendele a꞉no꞉ mo꞉tilida꞉daki, man mogago꞉le a꞉no꞉ sagala꞉li dimida꞉i ha꞉na꞉laliki, Godeya꞉yo꞉ iyo꞉ mo꞉walila꞉sa꞉ga꞉, falasila꞉ma꞉ib.
Ko꞉sega nao i, Godeya꞉yo꞉ gio꞉ mada alan asulo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ niliyo꞉ gi a꞉no꞉ asulakiyo꞉, Godemo꞉wo꞉ mada o꞉m a꞉la꞉sa꞉la꞉ mela꞉niki. Mo꞉wo꞉ Gio꞉ to hendele a꞉no꞉ tilida꞉dabiki, Godeya꞉ Mamaya꞉yo꞉ gio꞉ malilo꞉ melea꞉ki ta꞉takiyo꞉, Godeya꞉yo꞉ a꞉na a꞉ma꞉la꞉ gasili ko꞉lo꞉, a꞉la꞉dimidama꞉no꞉ a꞉laki, Godeya꞉lo꞉ taminde amilo꞉ gi ko꞉lo꞉ da꞉feyo꞉.
A꞉no꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ fa꞉la꞉doma꞉kiyo꞉, nio꞉ to nafayo꞉ gimo꞉ wida꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Godeya꞉yo꞉ gio꞉ a꞉na ho꞉ido꞉. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ Gode eyo꞉ Alan Ya꞉su Keliso E wabudab o꞉leaumbo꞉, gi wiyo꞉lo꞉ wabulu sama꞉ki, Godeya꞉yo꞉ gio꞉ a꞉na ho꞉leli.
A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ ni nao i, nililo꞉ towa꞉lo꞉ wido꞉ a꞉namio꞉lo꞉, mo꞉fo꞉s tamin amilo꞉ sa꞉sa꞉liga꞉fo꞉ a꞉no꞉lo꞉, giliyo꞉ mada dinafa tilida꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉, halale ta꞉li dofo꞉lubi.
Nili Alan Ya꞉su Keliso o꞉lia꞉ Do Gode o꞉lia꞉ma꞉yo꞉ nio꞉ alan asula꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Ene kanulo꞉ a꞉ma꞉yo꞉ nio꞉ ha꞉sa dofo꞉melea꞉ki ta꞉takiyo꞉, tilidabu a꞉no꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ halale alitaki, sagale yasilima꞉ki ta꞉fo꞉.
Eyo꞉ gili asulo꞉wo꞉ halale alitakiyo꞉, to nafa gililo꞉ sa꞉la꞉lab o꞉lia꞉ man nafa dimida꞉lab a꞉no꞉lia꞉yo꞉, ego꞉le mada doma꞉ki, niyo꞉ gio꞉ emo꞉wo꞉ dulugu so꞉lo꞉l.
To nowo꞉ edaki sa꞉ma꞉nigo꞉l. Nao i giliyo꞉ nio꞉ asuwa꞉foma꞉ki, Godemo꞉ dulugu sa꞉la꞉lubi. Alana꞉ to nafa a꞉no꞉ hen we tambo amio꞉ bo꞉bo꞉ge da꞉da꞉i ha꞉nakiyo꞉, gilo꞉ sagala꞉likilo꞉ dabu o꞉leaum dabuma꞉ki, Godemo꞉wo꞉ dulugu sa꞉la꞉lubi.
A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ kalu nolo꞉ Alan amio꞉ mo꞉tilidabu ko꞉lo꞉ mogago꞉lo꞉ dimida꞉lab kaluwa꞉ dagi amilo꞉ a꞉lab a꞉no꞉ nio꞉ ga꞉li mesea꞉ki, giliyo꞉ Godemo꞉ dulugu sa꞉la꞉lubi.
Ko꞉sega Alan e gio꞉ mada mo꞉ga꞉lila꞉sen ko꞉lo꞉, gimo꞉wo꞉ halaido꞉ dimiaki, man mogago꞉lo꞉ dimida꞉lab a꞉ma꞉yo꞉ mogagilabena꞉ki, dinafa tilidoma꞉ib.
A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ gio꞉ Alana tilida꞉daki, nililo꞉ gimo꞉lo꞉ sio꞉ a꞉no꞉ giliyo꞉ dimida꞉lab ko꞉lo꞉ tifamio꞉lo꞉ a꞉no꞉ko꞉ dimida꞉li ha꞉na꞉mela꞉ib a꞉la꞉bo꞉ nio꞉ hendele tili asulo꞉.
Keliso elo꞉ halale kagayab o꞉leaum giliyo꞉lo꞉ hida꞉yo꞉ diab amio꞉ halale kagama꞉no꞉ man o꞉lia꞉ Godeya꞉ ene ha꞉fo꞉ disa꞉lan man a꞉no꞉lia꞉yo꞉, Alan eyo꞉ gimo꞉wo꞉ tili walama꞉ki, nio꞉ Godemo꞉ dulugu so꞉lo꞉l.
Nao i, nili Alan Ya꞉su Kelisowa꞉ wiya ilikiyo꞉, niliyo꞉ halaido꞉ we ko꞉lo꞉ gimo꞉ salito꞉l. Kalu abeyo꞉ to nililo꞉ widabikilo꞉ gililo꞉ dabu a꞉no꞉ mo꞉kuduha꞉naki, ba madali bo꞉sulakilo꞉ sab i o꞉lia꞉yo꞉ uayo꞉ dowa꞉so꞉bo.
To a꞉no꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ fanda sa꞉ma꞉nigo꞉l. Nio꞉ gi o꞉lia꞉ silikilo꞉ man dimida꞉len a꞉no꞉ gio꞉ asulo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ giliyo꞉lo꞉ man o꞉leo꞉ngo꞉ ka kudu ha꞉na꞉bi. Nio꞉ gi o꞉lia꞉ silikiyo꞉ mo꞉bo꞉sulaki, ma꞉no꞉wo꞉ mo꞉kililiakiyo꞉, ba madaliyo꞉ mo꞉dia꞉sa꞉ga꞉ na꞉sen. A꞉la꞉do꞉ mo꞉dimidakiyo꞉, ni tili doma꞉no꞉wo꞉ gio꞉ kele asulabena꞉kiyo꞉, niliyo꞉ ho꞉lenowo꞉lo꞉ nuluwo꞉lo꞉ nanogo꞉ halaido꞉ dimida꞉len.
<range>
Nio꞉ gimo꞉wo꞉ ma꞉no꞉wo꞉ madali ka dimina a꞉la꞉ sa꞉ma꞉no꞉wo꞉ o꞉li ko꞉sega, a꞉la꞉bo꞉ mo꞉dimidaki, man nafa tifamilo꞉ gililo꞉ kudu ha꞉na꞉kilo꞉ dimidama꞉no꞉, a꞉no꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ widakigo꞉
Hendele, nio꞉ gi o꞉lia꞉ silikiyo꞉, ele we gimo꞉wo꞉ wido꞉. “Kalu abeyo꞉ nanogo꞉ mo꞉dialega, e ma꞉no꞉wo꞉ mo꞉ma꞉ib.”
A꞉la꞉wido꞉ ko꞉sega, o꞉go꞉ gi us amio꞉ nolo꞉ bo꞉sulaki ba madali sabka꞉, a꞉la꞉dabu. Iyo꞉ inin nanogo꞉ mo꞉diaki, kalu nolba꞉lo꞉ dimidab a꞉no꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ ka꞉ma꞉no꞉ a꞉laki nenela꞉sen.
Nio꞉ Alan Ya꞉su Kelisowa꞉ wi amio꞉, to halaido꞉wo꞉ kalu i o꞉ngo꞉mo꞉wo꞉ sa꞉ma꞉nigo꞉l. Gio꞉ ha꞉sa siliki, ma꞉no꞉wo꞉ ma꞉nikiyo꞉, go꞉no꞉no꞉ nanogo꞉ dimida꞉lubi.
Ni nao i, gio꞉ man digalo꞉ dimidama꞉no꞉wo꞉ mo꞉beakiyo꞉ dowa꞉so꞉bo.
Kalu abeyo꞉ to nililo꞉ sa꞉sa꞉liga꞉fo꞉ we mo꞉kuduha꞉nalega, gio꞉ kalu a꞉no꞉ sahele alitakiyo꞉, e sendoloma꞉ki, e o꞉lia꞉ dowa꞉so꞉bo.
Ko꞉sega kalu a꞉no꞉ gi o꞉lia꞉yo꞉ gis dowab a꞉la꞉bo꞉ asula꞉so꞉bo. Gili gaole o꞉ngo꞉ dowab ko꞉lo꞉ giliyo꞉ asulo꞉ nafale dimiaki, emo꞉wo꞉ hagugo꞉ towo꞉ sa꞉la꞉lubi.
Alan e, ha꞉salo꞉ dowan mo꞉wo꞉ e ko꞉lo꞉, ene ha꞉salo꞉ dowan man a꞉no꞉ ho꞉leno꞉ tambo a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ kelego꞉ tambo fa꞉la꞉dowab a꞉namio꞉lo꞉, man a꞉no꞉ gi o꞉lia꞉ dofo꞉ melea꞉ki, so꞉lo꞉l. Alan e gio꞉ tambo amio꞉ dofo꞉mela꞉ib.
Ne Fol ko꞉lo꞉, sagalo꞉ to we no꞉no꞉n dagileya꞉ sa꞉sa꞉ido꞉. Mo꞉fo꞉s nilo꞉ tambo sa꞉sa꞉lo꞉ a꞉namio꞉, na꞉no꞉lo꞉b a꞉la꞉ bo꞉ba꞉kiyo꞉, niyo꞉ a꞉la꞉dimida꞉sen.
Nili Alan, Ya꞉su Kelisowa꞉ ene kanulan man a꞉no꞉ gi o꞉lia꞉ tambo dowa꞉biyo꞉.
Ne Fol, Ya꞉su Keliso elo꞉ iliga꞉felo꞉ kalu nowo꞉ ne. Gode nilo꞉ asuwa꞉takilo꞉ gasili a꞉no꞉lia꞉, nililo꞉ tilida꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉lo꞉ yasiso꞉l Ya꞉su Keliso, a꞉la꞉ma꞉yo꞉ ne da꞉feyo꞉.
Timoti, ge hendele tilidabu ko꞉lo꞉ ni so꞉wale o꞉ngo꞉ fa꞉la꞉dowo꞉. A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ niyo꞉ mo꞉fo꞉s we gemo꞉ sa꞉sa꞉liga꞉to꞉l. Do Gode o꞉lia꞉ nili Misa꞉ Ya꞉su Keliso o꞉lia꞉ma꞉yo꞉ ini kanulo꞉ o꞉lia꞉ 21nofolan o꞉lia꞉ ha꞉salo꞉ mesa꞉no꞉ man a꞉no꞉lia꞉yo꞉ gi o꞉lia꞉ dofo꞉melea꞉ki, to we a꞉na sa꞉sa꞉lo꞉l.
Ne Masedonia hen ha꞉nakiyo꞉, ge Efesa꞉s a꞉naka o꞉melea꞉ki, gemo꞉wo꞉ towo꞉ salifogane ko꞉lo꞉ o꞉go꞉ niyo꞉ to a꞉no꞉ wa꞉ka sa꞉ma꞉nigo꞉l. Ge Efesa꞉s a꞉na silikiyo꞉, kalu nolba꞉lo꞉ Godeya꞉ man kaluka꞉isalemo꞉lo꞉ hala wida꞉lab a꞉no꞉ ta꞉foma꞉ki, giyo꞉ towo꞉ halaido꞉ sa꞉la꞉lubi.
Iliyo꞉ kandayo꞉ malola꞉sen o꞉lia꞉ e ma꞉mu i mio꞉ agela꞉sen a꞉no꞉lia꞉yo꞉ nenela꞉sa꞉ga꞉ widalikiyo꞉, ho꞉leno꞉ waleso꞉boka꞉ a꞉la꞉liki, imo꞉wo꞉ halale sa꞉la꞉lubi. Mo꞉wo꞉ i a꞉ma꞉yo꞉ a꞉no꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ malola꞉lalikiyo꞉, gadiaki kega꞉mela꞉ib ko꞉lo꞉, Godeya꞉ nanog diab a꞉no꞉ mo꞉asuwa꞉fa꞉ib. Kaluwa꞉yo꞉ tilida꞉daliki, Godeya꞉ ene nanogo꞉ a꞉na fa꞉la꞉doma꞉ib.
Nilo꞉ gemo꞉lo꞉ dimidama꞉kilo꞉ to so꞉lo꞉lo꞉ we. Kaluka꞉isaleyo꞉ egelebo꞉ ha꞉fo꞉ disa꞉ma꞉no꞉ man a꞉no꞉ wida꞉bi. Man a꞉no꞉ fa꞉la꞉doma꞉kiyo꞉, asugo꞉ go꞉go꞉do꞉ dowa꞉sa꞉ga꞉, hala dimido꞉ mo꞉asulaki, a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ tilidabu hendele dowalikiyo꞉, ha꞉fo꞉ disa꞉lan man a꞉no꞉, a꞉na a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ fa꞉la꞉doma꞉ib.
Kalu nolo꞉ man wida꞉lab a꞉no꞉ ta꞉fo꞉ ha꞉nakiyo꞉, madali to sa꞉la꞉lab.
Iyo꞉ Mosesa꞉ elelo꞉ widan kalu doma꞉no꞉ asulaki wida꞉lab ko꞉sega, to inido꞉ o꞉lia꞉ to ililo꞉ halale widab o꞉lia꞉yo꞉ inino꞉ mo꞉wo꞉ mo꞉fanda asulo꞉
Ko꞉sega kaluka꞉isaleyo꞉ Mosesa꞉ ele difa꞉ a꞉no꞉ digalo꞉le widalega, nio꞉ ele a꞉no꞉ nafa dowab a꞉la꞉asulo꞉l.
A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ ele a꞉no꞉, digalo꞉ kalu a꞉lab a꞉no꞉ bo꞉fo꞉melea꞉kiyo꞉, mo꞉saefa꞉. Ko꞉sega kalu ele difa꞉lo꞉ o꞉go꞉sa꞉lab a꞉no꞉lia꞉yo꞉, a꞉la꞉iyabo꞉, Godeyo꞉ gola ba꞉dabo꞉, mogago꞉lo꞉ dimida꞉seno꞉, Godeya꞉lo꞉ asulab aumbo꞉ mo꞉kuduha꞉na꞉sen a꞉no꞉, henfelo꞉ mando꞉ kuduha꞉na꞉labo꞉, iya anolo꞉ sanasowabo꞉, kalu noldo꞉ sanasowa꞉labo꞉, uwo꞉lo꞉ dia꞉labo꞉, da꞉lo꞉ dimia꞉labo꞉, kalu nolo꞉ afale tilili ha꞉na꞉sa꞉ga꞉lo꞉ madali nanog dian kalu ta꞉felabo꞉, dolole sa꞉lakilo꞉ dikili sa꞉labo꞉, mo꞉walilab amio꞉ towa꞉lo꞉ a꞉ a꞉la꞉sa꞉lano꞉, kaluka꞉isaleyo꞉ man digalo꞉wo꞉ mo꞉kuduha꞉na꞉lab a꞉no꞉, ele saefa꞉ we i a꞉ma꞉no꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ da꞉lab.
<range>
Man digalo꞉ a꞉no꞉, Godeya꞉ to nafale a꞉no꞉lia꞉yo꞉ imilo꞉ dowo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉, Godeya꞉ to nafa a꞉no꞉ nemo꞉ walama꞉ki wido꞉. To nafa a꞉no꞉, Gode Alan, kaluka꞉isaleya꞉lo꞉ wabulu sa꞉la꞉lab a꞉na a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ fa꞉la꞉dowo꞉.
Ya꞉su Keliso, nili Alana꞉yo꞉, nemo꞉wo꞉ halaido꞉wo꞉ dimia꞉sa꞉ga꞉, Eyo꞉ ne dibebea꞉sa꞉ga꞉, niyo꞉ nanogo꞉ o꞉li ditandalema꞉ib a꞉la꞉asulaki, ene nanog dima꞉ki dafe alifa꞉ ko꞉lo꞉, niyo꞉ emo꞉wo꞉ mada o꞉m a꞉la꞉so꞉lo꞉l.
Tamin amio꞉ ne Ya꞉suwa꞉ wiyo꞉ dio꞉ge sa꞉laki, e o꞉lia꞉yo꞉ gis dowa꞉liki, e niyo꞉ mogagela꞉len. Ko꞉sega ne e mo꞉fanda asulaki, semo꞉ tilidabu iliki, a꞉na dimido꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ eyo꞉ ne nofolo꞉ alifa꞉.
Nili Alan, Ya꞉su Kelisowa꞉yo꞉, ene kanulan man a꞉no꞉ ne amio꞉ mada modo꞉ ko꞉go꞉laki, ene tili dabu o꞉lia꞉ ha꞉fo꞉ disa꞉lan man a꞉no꞉ nemo꞉ dimi.
To we hendele sa꞉ma꞉nigo꞉l ko꞉lo꞉ gio꞉ tilida꞉da꞉bi. “Ya꞉su Kelisowo꞉ mogago꞉lo꞉ dimida꞉lab kaluka꞉isale a꞉no꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ gasilia꞉niki, henfelo꞉ wena mio꞉” niyo꞉ a꞉la꞉sa꞉sa꞉lo꞉l. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ ne mada mogago꞉lelo꞉ dimida꞉len kaluwo꞉ ne.
Ko꞉sega Godeya꞉yo꞉ ne nofola꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, Ya꞉su Kelisowa꞉yo꞉ ha꞉salo꞉ doma꞉no꞉ man a꞉no꞉ nemo꞉ ko꞉le wido꞉ ko꞉lo꞉, kaluka꞉isaleyo꞉ tambo a꞉no꞉ asula꞉sa꞉ga꞉, iyo꞉lo꞉ Ya꞉su Keliso amio꞉ tilida꞉daki, ko꞉ngo꞉ mela꞉no꞉ dima꞉kiyo꞉, mogago꞉le kalu nemo꞉ ko꞉le wido꞉.
Gode mada o꞉m, ko꞉ngo꞉ mela꞉no꞉ Misa꞉yo꞉ E, mo꞉sowano꞉ E, siya꞉lo꞉ mo꞉ba꞉dano꞉ E, Godeyo꞉ imilise E ko꞉lo꞉ a꞉lab. A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ kaluka꞉isaleya꞉yo꞉ E mada nafale a꞉la꞉liki, Ene wiyo꞉ ho꞉leno꞉ tambo wabulu sa꞉la꞉i ha꞉na꞉mela꞉ib. Hendele.
Ni so꞉wa Timoti, tamin amilo꞉ sa꞉s misa꞉ kaluwa꞉lo꞉ gemo꞉lo꞉ dinali sio꞉ a꞉no꞉, niyo꞉lo꞉ o꞉go꞉ to o꞉ngo꞉ wala sa꞉ma꞉nigo꞉l. To a꞉no꞉ ge asulufo꞉liki kudu ha꞉naki, ge halaledo꞉ buban kaluwo꞉ o꞉ngo꞉ dota꞉ga꞉, nanogo꞉ a꞉na halale dimida꞉bi.
Go꞉no꞉n tilidabuwo꞉ halale ta꞉li siliki, man digalo꞉ o꞉lia꞉ man mogago꞉ o꞉lia꞉yo꞉ dinafa aloba꞉daki, nanogo꞉ a꞉na dimida꞉bi. Mo꞉wo꞉ kalu nolba꞉yo꞉ a꞉la꞉bo꞉ mo꞉dimido꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ inin tilidabuwo꞉, ho꞉n ko꞉su ko꞉lo꞉ u nowa basayakilo꞉ mogagab o꞉ngo꞉ dowa꞉lab.
Kalu a꞉la꞉ nowo꞉, Himeneus o꞉lia꞉ Alegsanda o꞉lia꞉yo꞉ o꞉li o꞉ngo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ a꞉la꞉ma꞉yo꞉ Godeya꞉ wiyo꞉ mo꞉mogagima꞉no꞉ a꞉la꞉asulaki, niyo꞉ a꞉la꞉yo꞉ Seteneya꞉ dagiya difa꞉.
Tamin amio꞉, gio꞉ Godemo꞉wo꞉ dulugu sa꞉la꞉lubi. Kaluka꞉isaleyo꞉ tambo asuwa꞉takiyo꞉, halale alifoma꞉ki, Godemo꞉ to sa꞉la꞉bi. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ Godeya꞉lo꞉ asuwa꞉ta꞉lab a꞉no꞉, mada o꞉m a꞉la꞉sa꞉la꞉bi.
Nio꞉ sagala꞉li ha꞉sa silikiyo꞉, Godeyo꞉ wabuda꞉liki, Elo꞉ asulab aumb mesea꞉ki, gamani misa꞉ kalu o꞉lia꞉ gamani bo꞉fo꞉lowan kalu nolo꞉lo꞉, Godemo꞉ dulugu sa꞉la꞉bi.
A꞉la꞉do꞉ gab a꞉no꞉ mada nafale ko꞉lo꞉ Gode nilo꞉ gasili o꞉mo꞉wo꞉ sagale alifa꞉ib.
Mo꞉wo꞉ Gode eyo꞉ kaluka꞉isale tambo a꞉ma꞉la꞉ gasilia꞉no꞉ asulab. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ kaluka꞉isaleyo꞉ tambo to hendeleyo꞉ mada tili asuluma꞉ki asulab.
Mo꞉wo꞉ Godeyo꞉ imilig ko꞉lo꞉lab, a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ Gode o꞉lia꞉ kaluka꞉isale o꞉lia꞉ us amilo꞉ a꞉lab kaluleyo꞉, Ya꞉su Keliso imilig e ko꞉lo꞉lab.
Kaluka꞉isaleyo꞉ tambo ga꞉li mesea꞉ki, su dimian aumbo꞉ Ya꞉su eyo꞉ eneno꞉ boba dimi. Man a꞉no꞉ ene ho꞉lendeya fa꞉la꞉dowaki, Godeya꞉yo꞉ kaluka꞉isale tambo a꞉ma꞉la꞉ gasilia꞉no꞉ a꞉la꞉li wido꞉.
A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ Godeya꞉ to walama꞉kiyo꞉, ne Ya꞉suwa꞉lo꞉ iliga꞉felo꞉ kalu nowo꞉ ne da꞉fea꞉sa꞉ga꞉ ta꞉fo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉, niyo꞉ Yu kaluka꞉isalema sab o꞉mo꞉wo꞉ tilidabu hendeleyo꞉ walama꞉kilo꞉ da꞉feyo꞉ kaluwo꞉ ne. Niyo꞉ to we mo꞉dikidaki, hendele so꞉lo꞉l.
A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ nilo꞉ asulab o꞉m. Hen tambo amio꞉ kaluwo꞉ ene dagi dulugufo꞉liki, ene mela꞉no꞉wo꞉ Godemo꞉ dimia꞉sa꞉ga꞉, gadiano꞉ aundo꞉ma a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ to kegano꞉ aundo꞉ma iliki, Godemo꞉wo꞉ towo꞉ a꞉na sa꞉la꞉bi.
A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ ka꞉isale iyo꞉ so꞉g sa꞉ga꞉lakiyo꞉, eneno꞉ mo꞉fo꞉fo꞉doloma꞉no꞉ momadaki, e amio꞉ ego꞉leyo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ kama꞉ki, niyo꞉ a꞉la꞉asulab. Iyo꞉ kalu sendeakiyo꞉ misa꞉ fo꞉no꞉ mela꞉so꞉bo, a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ do꞉mo꞉ amio꞉ so꞉g mole alana꞉lo꞉ dian o꞉ngo꞉wo꞉ o꞉lia꞉ momadan ko꞉li ko꞉lilo꞉ go꞉l amio꞉ dimido꞉ a꞉no꞉ ka꞉la꞉so꞉bo.
Ko꞉sega ka꞉isale abeyo꞉ ne Godeyo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ wabuda꞉sen a꞉la꞉likiyo꞉, man nafale dimidab a꞉no꞉, momado꞉ ililo꞉wo꞉ o꞉m.
Iyo꞉ towo꞉ mo꞉tolaki ha꞉ga iliki, Godeya꞉ towo꞉ a꞉na da꞉da꞉lubi.
Ka꞉isale iliyo꞉ kaluwo꞉ mo꞉wa꞉la꞉sa꞉dakiyo꞉, Godeya꞉ towo꞉ imo꞉wo꞉ mo꞉walama꞉ki, niyo꞉ a꞉la꞉asulab. Iyo꞉ hela꞉ta꞉ga꞉ mesea꞉ki asulab.
Mo꞉wo꞉ Godeya꞉yo꞉ Adam e tamindeya dimida꞉sa꞉ga꞉yo꞉, Ifo tifa dimido꞉.
A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ Adam eyo꞉ dikili sio꞉wo꞉ mo꞉tilidabu. If eyo꞉ dikili sa꞉lab a꞉no꞉ tilida꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉, ele difa꞉yo꞉ e mogaso꞉.
Ko꞉sega ka꞉isale iyo꞉ so꞉wayo꞉ o꞉li sa꞉la꞉lian ko꞉lo꞉, iyo꞉ kelego꞉wo꞉ tambo i amio꞉ egaki, iyo꞉ Ya꞉su amio꞉ tilidabu iliki, kaluka꞉isale nolbo꞉wo꞉ ha꞉fo꞉ disa꞉laki, man digalo꞉ kudu ha꞉na꞉lalega, Godeya꞉yo꞉ iyo꞉ a꞉ma꞉la꞉ gasilia꞉ib.
To we hendele sa꞉ma꞉nigo꞉l. Kalu abeyo꞉ e sa꞉sdo꞉ bo꞉fo꞉lowan kalu doma꞉no꞉ asulalega, e nanog nafale a꞉no꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ dia꞉no꞉ asulab.
Sa꞉sdo꞉ bo꞉fo꞉lowan kaluwa꞉lo꞉ man dimidano꞉ we. Eyo꞉ mano꞉ digalo꞉le kudu ha꞉naki, kalu nolba꞉yo꞉ e hala dimidab a꞉la꞉bo꞉ mo꞉asula꞉sen. E gayo꞉ imilig di. E ha꞉sa dowan. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ enena꞉ma꞉la꞉yo꞉ dinafa tilidowan. E mageso꞉ kaluwo꞉ dinafa tilidowan. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ eyo꞉ Godeya꞉ mano꞉ nafale widan.
E aluna꞉ ho꞉n nakiyo꞉, mo꞉no꞉nolan kaluwo꞉ dowan. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ nol o꞉lia꞉yo꞉ mo꞉buban. E ha꞉sa dowaki, towa꞉yo꞉ mo꞉kegan. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ e moleyo꞉ mo꞉meselan.
Kalu a꞉no꞉ ene so꞉lo꞉wo꞉ dinafa tilidowaki, elo꞉ sa꞉lab aumbo꞉ ene so꞉wayo꞉ tilida꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉ kudu hamana꞉ki, bo꞉fo꞉lowan.
Kalu abeyo꞉ ene ga o꞉lia꞉ ene so꞉wa o꞉lia꞉yo꞉ dinafayo꞉ mo꞉tilidowalega, eyo꞉ Godeya꞉ ene kaluka꞉isaleyo꞉ waga tilidoma꞉ibele?
Keliso ho꞉gi dowab a꞉ma꞉yo꞉ sa꞉sdo꞉ bo꞉fo꞉lowan kaluwo꞉ mo꞉dowan. Mo꞉wo꞉ enena꞉ma꞉la꞉yo꞉ e nafale a꞉la꞉ asulalikiyo꞉, Godeya꞉yo꞉ e mo꞉walilakiyo꞉, Setene ko꞉lo꞉ mo꞉walilo꞉wo꞉ auma꞉ib.
A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ sa꞉sdo꞉ bo꞉fo꞉lowan kalu e Seteneya꞉ dafa amio꞉ walalaliki, e sendelowabena꞉kiyo꞉, ha꞉la꞉ kaluka꞉isaleya꞉ siwa꞉l amio꞉ e digalo꞉le kalu a꞉la꞉do꞉ sa꞉lab a꞉ma꞉ dowan.
Nilo꞉ tamin amilo꞉ so꞉lo꞉l o꞉leaum, digon iyo꞉lo꞉ man nafale dimidaki, wiyo꞉ nafa dia꞉no꞉ a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ mela꞉no꞉ ko꞉lo꞉lab. Iyo꞉ towa꞉yo꞉ mo꞉a꞉la꞉sa꞉lan. Iyo꞉ aluna꞉ ho꞉no꞉ modo꞉wo꞉ mo꞉na꞉sen a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ iyo꞉ moleyo꞉ alan asulakiyo꞉, kalu nolo꞉ dikidakiyo꞉, mo꞉afale dia꞉sen.
Asulo꞉ ililo꞉wo꞉ go꞉go꞉do꞉ dowaki, tilidabu a꞉namio꞉ to hendelelo꞉b a꞉la꞉do꞉ asulab a꞉no꞉ iliyo꞉ tili asula꞉sen.
Tamin amio꞉ ili mano꞉ alobana ba꞉ba꞉ amio꞉, kalu nolba꞉yo꞉ elo꞉ hala dimido꞉wo꞉ mo꞉sa꞉lalega, e digon nanogo꞉ dimidama꞉ki, ta꞉ta꞉bi.
A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ ga ililo꞉wo꞉lo꞉, mano꞉ imilig o꞉leo꞉ngo꞉ka dowaki, iyo꞉ man nafale dimidaki, wiyo꞉ nafa dia꞉no꞉ a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ mela꞉no꞉ ko꞉lo꞉lab. Iyo꞉ nolo꞉ mo꞉sada꞉dan. Ko꞉sega iyo꞉ ha꞉sa dowaki, ini nanogo꞉ tambo o꞉li tilidowa꞉sen o꞉leo꞉ngo꞉ma꞉ doma꞉ib.
Digon kalu e, gayo꞉ imilig dowaki, ene so꞉wa o꞉lia꞉ so꞉lo꞉ o꞉lia꞉yo꞉ dinafalo꞉ bo꞉fo꞉lab kalu a꞉ma꞉ dowan.
A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ sa꞉s nanogdo꞉ diab kalu i a꞉no꞉, nanogo꞉ nafale dia꞉liki, ili wiyo꞉ mada nafaleyo꞉ a꞉na doma꞉ib. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ Ya꞉su Kelisowa tilidabu a꞉la꞉likilo꞉ kalab amio꞉ halale sa꞉ma꞉no꞉ a꞉no꞉ mo꞉tagima꞉ib.
Ne gelo꞉ amio꞉ bo꞉bo꞉ge mia꞉no꞉ asulab ko꞉sega, ne bo꞉ibo꞉ mo꞉yalega, giyo꞉ Godeya꞉ so꞉lo꞉wa꞉lo꞉ man kudu ha꞉nan a꞉no꞉ asuluma꞉ki, niyo꞉ mo꞉fo꞉s we ko꞉le sa꞉sa꞉liga꞉to꞉l. Godeya꞉ so꞉lo꞉ a꞉la꞉do꞉ sa꞉lab a꞉ma꞉ ha꞉go꞉ we. Sa꞉so꞉ Gode mela꞉no꞉lo꞉ a꞉lab a꞉ma꞉no꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ sa꞉s a꞉no꞉ aiko꞉ o꞉ngo꞉ iliki, to hendelelo꞉ halalelo꞉ ta꞉lisabo꞉ o꞉m.
<range>
Godeya꞉ ene to man nimo꞉lo꞉ kalab amilo꞉ wido꞉ a꞉no꞉ mada alan fa꞉la꞉dowo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ to a꞉no꞉ mada hendele dowo꞉. To a꞉no꞉ we. E kalule fa꞉la꞉dowabiki, kaluka꞉isaleya꞉yo꞉ e ba꞉ba꞉. Man elo꞉wo꞉ digalo꞉le a꞉la꞉bo꞉ Godeya꞉ Mamaya꞉ wido꞉. Ma꞉mula꞉ kaluwa꞉yo꞉lo꞉ e ba꞉ba꞉. Widan kaluwa꞉yo꞉ ene mano꞉ so꞉lo꞉ ko꞉li ko꞉lilo꞉mo꞉wo꞉ wida꞉le ane ko꞉lo꞉, Henfelo꞉ tambo amio꞉ kaluka꞉isale nolo꞉ e tilidabu. E wabudaki, Hebene tililia꞉ fa꞉la꞉ ane.
Godeya꞉ Mamaya꞉yo꞉ fanda widakilo꞉ to sio꞉wo꞉ we. Elema꞉no꞉ ho꞉leno꞉ ko꞉na꞉ma dowalikiyo꞉, kalu nolo꞉ ene tilidabuwo꞉ ta꞉ta꞉ga꞉, mama mogago꞉wa꞉lo꞉ yo꞉ido꞉ to sa꞉lab a꞉no꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ tilida꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉, mama mogago꞉wa꞉lo꞉ mano꞉ widab a꞉no꞉ kudu ha꞉na꞉ib.
Man a꞉no꞉ madalilo꞉ dikidan kaluwa꞉ wida꞉sen ko꞉lo꞉ ili asulo꞉ nafalo꞉ mia꞉sen a꞉no꞉ sana sowo꞉ o꞉ngo꞉ dowaki, we mogago꞉ dimido꞉ a꞉la꞉bo꞉ mo꞉asulakigab.
Kalu i a꞉ma꞉ widakiyo꞉, gayo꞉ dia꞉so꞉bo a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ ma꞉no꞉ nolo꞉ na꞉so꞉boka꞉ a꞉la꞉liki wida꞉lab. Ko꞉sega Godeya꞉lo꞉ ma꞉no꞉ dimido꞉ a꞉no꞉, kaluka꞉isale to hendelelo꞉ asulakilo꞉ tilida꞉dab a꞉ma꞉yo꞉ mada o꞉m a꞉la꞉bo꞉ sa꞉la꞉li maya꞉ki, dimido꞉.
Godeya꞉lo꞉ kelego꞉ dimido꞉wo꞉ tambo nafa ko꞉lo꞉ gio꞉ kelego꞉ a꞉no꞉ mada o꞉m a꞉la꞉sa꞉la꞉liki, kelego꞉ imilig noma꞉yo꞉ mo꞉ka꞉laki, tambowo꞉ o꞉li dia꞉ib.
Mo꞉wo꞉ gililo꞉ Godemo꞉lo꞉ dulugu sio꞉ o꞉lia꞉ Godeya꞉lo꞉ to sio꞉ o꞉lia꞉ma꞉yo꞉ ma꞉no꞉ a꞉no꞉ Godeya꞉ siwa꞉l amio꞉ o꞉lika maya꞉ki ta꞉fo꞉.
Giyo꞉ to nilo꞉ sa꞉sa꞉lo꞉ a꞉no꞉ gao i nolbo꞉wo꞉ dinafa widalega, ge Ya꞉su Kelisowa꞉ nanogdo꞉ dian kalu nafale dowakigab. A꞉la꞉dimidalikiyo꞉, nililo꞉ tilidabuwa꞉ man we o꞉lia꞉ to nafa widab amilo꞉ gilo꞉ da꞉da꞉sa꞉ga꞉lo꞉ kudu ane a꞉ma꞉yo꞉, ge halaido꞉ dowakigab.
Giyo꞉ kandayo꞉ malola꞉sen, ha꞉go꞉ aundo꞉ma dowab a꞉no꞉ kata꞉ta꞉bi. Ko꞉sega giyo꞉ Godeya꞉lo꞉ asulab aumb doma꞉nikiyo꞉, ho꞉leno꞉ tambo asulo꞉ diakiyo꞉, mano꞉ da꞉fea꞉lubi.
Do꞉mo꞉wo꞉ halaido꞉ doma꞉ki, do꞉mo꞉ da꞉feakilo꞉ dimidan a꞉ma꞉yo꞉ ge ha꞉lu asuwa꞉fa꞉ib. Ko꞉sega, Godeya꞉lo꞉ asulab aumb kudu ha꞉nab a꞉ma꞉yo꞉, ge alan asuwa꞉fa꞉ib. O꞉go꞉ mela꞉no꞉ nafale dimia꞉lab ko꞉lo꞉, tif amio꞉ mela꞉no꞉ mela꞉no꞉wo꞉ nafale dimia꞉ib.
To a꞉no꞉ hendele so꞉lo꞉l ko꞉lo꞉, gio꞉ tilida꞉da꞉bi.
Mela꞉no꞉ mela꞉no꞉ a꞉no꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ dia꞉nikiyo꞉, nio꞉ nanogo꞉ halaido꞉ dimida꞉len. Godeyo꞉ kaluka꞉isale tambolo꞉ o꞉li gasilia꞉ibo꞉ e ko꞉lo꞉ kaluka꞉isale abeyo꞉ e amilo꞉ tilida꞉dab a꞉no꞉ eyo꞉ mada gasilia꞉ib. A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ nio꞉ ha꞉sa iliki, asulo꞉wo꞉ tambo Gode mela꞉no꞉lo꞉ a꞉lab emo꞉ dimi.
To we giyo꞉ kaluka꞉isale imo꞉wo꞉ widakiyo꞉, iyo꞉ kudu ha꞉na꞉melea꞉ki wida꞉lubi.
Ge sa꞉lelo꞉biki, kaluka꞉isaleya꞉yo꞉ ge wa꞉la꞉ sa꞉ndabena꞉ki, ka꞉la꞉bi. Ko꞉sega iyo꞉ gi mano꞉ kudu hamana꞉kiyo꞉, gilo꞉ to sa꞉lano꞉lo꞉, man gilo꞉ dimidano꞉lo꞉, gilo꞉ ha꞉fo꞉ disa꞉lano꞉lo꞉, gilo꞉ tilidabuwo꞉lo꞉, a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ gi asulo꞉wo꞉ go꞉go꞉do꞉ dowan a꞉no꞉lo꞉, iliyo꞉ kudu mena꞉ki, giyo꞉ digale dimida꞉bi.
Ne o꞉semo꞉ yalikiyo꞉, kaluka꞉isalemo꞉wo꞉ Godeya꞉ towo꞉ agela꞉ mia꞉bi. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ ho꞉leno꞉ tambo ili kufa꞉ uso꞉ halale alitakiyo꞉, Godeya꞉ mano꞉ imo꞉wo꞉ wida꞉lubi.
Sa꞉s misa꞉ kaluwa꞉yo꞉ gi misa꞉ wa꞉la golofo꞉liki, iyo꞉lo꞉ dinali sa꞉lakilo꞉ boba dimi a꞉no꞉ ge di ko꞉lo꞉, o꞉go꞉ giyo꞉ gola ba꞉da꞉so꞉bo.
Kaluka꞉isale tambowa꞉yo꞉ gi tilidabuwo꞉ anayabo꞉lo꞉b a꞉la꞉asuluma꞉ki, ge to a꞉no꞉ asula꞉liki, nanog a꞉no꞉ halale dimida꞉lubi.
Go꞉no꞉n man dimidan o꞉lia꞉ to man wida꞉lab a꞉no꞉lia꞉yo꞉ dinafa tilidowaki, ge man a꞉no꞉leko꞉ kudu ha꞉na꞉lubi. Mo꞉wo꞉ giyo꞉ a꞉la꞉dimidalikiyo꞉, go꞉no꞉n gelo꞉ a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ kaluka꞉isale gi tolo꞉ da꞉dab a꞉no꞉lo꞉ tambo Godeya꞉ gasilia꞉ib.
To gilo꞉ma꞉yo꞉ kalu ko꞉go꞉do꞉ sab a꞉no꞉ mo꞉wa꞉la꞉sa꞉ndaki, giyo꞉ ha꞉sa iliki, go꞉lbo꞉lo꞉ sa꞉lan aumb, iyo꞉ halale doma꞉ki sa꞉la꞉bi. Kalu so꞉wa a꞉no꞉, gaomo꞉lo꞉ sa꞉lan aumb, halale doma꞉ki sa꞉la꞉bi.
Ka꞉isale ko꞉go꞉do꞉ a꞉no꞉, go꞉molo꞉ sa꞉lan aumb, sa꞉la꞉bi. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ ka꞉isale so꞉wa o꞉mo꞉ sa꞉lakiyo꞉, ge malilo꞉ iliki, gado꞉molo꞉ sa꞉lan aumb, sa꞉la꞉bi.
Ga sa꞉ba꞉lo꞉ biso꞉lo꞉ma dowab a꞉no꞉, dinafa tilidowa꞉bi.
Ko꞉sega ga sa꞉ba꞉lo꞉ abeyo꞉, ene so꞉wayo꞉ sabo꞉lalega, o꞉ ene unuwo꞉ sabo꞉lalega, so꞉wa a꞉ma꞉lo꞉wo꞉ ene tilidabuwo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ kudu ha꞉naki, iyo꞉ sa꞉ba꞉lo꞉ a꞉no꞉ bo꞉fo꞉lubi. A꞉la꞉dimidalikiyo꞉, inin nanog di amilo꞉ wa꞉l dian aumbo꞉, iliyo꞉ unuwo꞉ anowo꞉ iya o꞉lia꞉ a꞉kililian aumgab ko꞉lo꞉ a꞉la꞉dimidab man a꞉no꞉ Godeyo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ sagale alitab.
Ga sa꞉ba꞉lo꞉ e so꞉lo꞉lo꞉ma ena꞉li iliki, ene asulo꞉wo꞉ Godemo꞉ dimifo꞉liki, ho꞉len o꞉lia꞉ nulu o꞉lia꞉yo꞉ Godemo꞉wo꞉ asuwa꞉foma꞉ki, dulugu sa꞉la꞉lab.
Ko꞉sega ga sa꞉ba꞉lo꞉ abeyo꞉ enen a꞉ma꞉la꞉yo꞉ sagalema꞉no꞉ mano꞉ ko꞉li ko꞉lilo꞉ a꞉no꞉ka dimida꞉lalega, e sowo꞉ o꞉ngo꞉ ilikigab.
Kaluka꞉isaleyo꞉ hala dimidabena꞉kiyo꞉, giyo꞉ to wido꞉ a꞉no꞉ imo꞉wo꞉ dinafa sa꞉la꞉bi.
Ko꞉sega kalu abeyo꞉ ene so꞉lo꞉leyo꞉ a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ a elo꞉ ta꞉sen o꞉lia꞉yo꞉ mo꞉tilidowai kibo꞉bowo꞉, kalu we ene tilidabuwo꞉ kata꞉taki, ene mano꞉ mada mogago꞉le domabe. Ha꞉la꞉ kaluwa꞉yo꞉ man mogago꞉le wengo꞉wo꞉ mo꞉dimida꞉sen.
Ga sa꞉ba꞉lo꞉ sa꞉s bo꞉fo꞉melea꞉ki da꞉feakiyo꞉, ga sa꞉ba꞉lo꞉ we o꞉ngo꞉ma꞉yo꞉ o꞉li dia꞉bi. E donayo꞉ 60 a꞉la꞉fo꞉ gulula꞉sa꞉ga꞉, ina꞉ ha꞉ga iliki mo꞉ta꞉fo꞉gane a꞉no꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ o꞉li dia꞉bi.
Amisa꞉n kaluka꞉isaleya꞉ siwa꞉l amio꞉ ga sa꞉ba꞉lo꞉ a꞉ma꞉ mano꞉ nafale dimidabilo꞉ ba꞉ba꞉ a꞉no꞉ o꞉li dia꞉bi. Man nafa a꞉no꞉ we. Ene so꞉wayo꞉ dinafa bo꞉fo꞉lowan. Mageso꞉ kaluka꞉isaleyo꞉ eyo꞉ tilidowa꞉sen. Keliso kaluka꞉isaleya꞉ gib amio꞉ hena꞉ mu a꞉no꞉ dinafa halita꞉sen. Hida꞉yo꞉lo꞉ dowab amio꞉ asuwa꞉ta꞉sen. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ man nafa ko꞉li ko꞉lilo꞉ a꞉no꞉ eyo꞉ dimida꞉lowan. Ga a꞉no꞉ o꞉li dia꞉bi.
Ko꞉sega ga nafa amio꞉ sa꞉ba꞉lab a꞉no꞉ da꞉fea꞉so꞉bo. Mo꞉wo꞉ e kaluwa꞉ a꞉dima꞉ki asulakiyo꞉, asulo꞉ a꞉ma꞉yo꞉ Kelisowa꞉ nanog dimidama꞉no꞉ asulan a꞉no꞉ a꞉ma꞉ tininima꞉ib. A꞉la꞉galikiyo꞉, ene dinali sio꞉ a꞉no꞉ ta꞉tab ko꞉lo꞉, Godeya꞉yo꞉ ga sa꞉ba꞉lo꞉ a꞉no꞉ mo꞉walilima꞉ib.
<range>
A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ ga a꞉no꞉ da꞉fealega, iyo꞉ bo꞉sulaki, a nowa, a nowa a꞉la꞉ sia꞉liki, ho꞉leno꞉ walemela꞉ib. A꞉la꞉dimida꞉lalikiyo꞉, ililo꞉ mo꞉sa꞉ma꞉no꞉ dowo꞉ towo꞉ a꞉na sa꞉laki, madali yo꞉ido꞉ towo꞉ a꞉na sada꞉da꞉mela꞉ib.
A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ ga o꞉nafa amilo꞉ sa꞉ba꞉lab a꞉no꞉ e kaluwo꞉ ha꞉na꞉sa꞉ga꞉, so꞉wayo꞉ a꞉na sa꞉la꞉la꞉liki, ene so꞉lo꞉ a꞉no꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ tilidowa꞉bi, a꞉la꞉likiyo꞉ niyo꞉ emo꞉wo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉. Iyo꞉ a꞉la꞉dimidalikiyo꞉, nili gis kaluwa꞉yo꞉ sendeloma꞉no꞉ to a꞉no꞉ nimo꞉wo꞉ mo꞉sama꞉ki go꞉l.
Hendele. Ga sa꞉ba꞉lo꞉ nolo꞉ tog nafa a꞉no꞉ o꞉ma ta꞉ta꞉ga꞉, Seteneyo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ kudu ane ko꞉lo꞉ a꞉lab.
Keliso ga dowab a꞉ma꞉ ene so꞉lo꞉ us amio꞉ ga sa꞉ba꞉lo꞉ nowo꞉ dowalega, Keliso ga a꞉ma꞉yo꞉ e dinafa bo꞉fo꞉lubi. A꞉la꞉galikiyo꞉, sa꞉s e hida꞉yo꞉ alano꞉ mo꞉diaki, ga sa꞉ba꞉lo꞉ so꞉lo꞉lo꞉ma ena꞉lile dowab nol a꞉no꞉ sa꞉s iliyo꞉ e o꞉li bo꞉fo꞉mela꞉ib.
Giliyo꞉ misa꞉ kaluwo꞉, sa꞉sdo꞉ dinafalo꞉ bo꞉fo꞉len a꞉no꞉ e wabudaki, moleyo꞉ kililia꞉bi. Misa꞉ kaluwa꞉lo꞉ Godeya꞉ mano꞉ halale widakilo꞉ wala sa꞉lab i a꞉no꞉, digalo꞉le kililia꞉bi.
Godeya꞉ bugo꞉ amio꞉ towo꞉ a꞉la꞉sio꞉, “Giyo꞉ kaowo꞉ da꞉si fo basi a꞉lalikiyo꞉, elo꞉ ma꞉no꞉wo꞉ maya꞉ki, e mego꞉fo꞉ mela꞉so꞉bo.” A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ to sa꞉lano꞉ nowo꞉ we, “Nanogdo꞉ di kalu o꞉mo꞉wo꞉, wa꞉lo꞉ kililia꞉ib.”
Misa꞉ kaluwa꞉lo꞉ mogago꞉ dimido꞉ a꞉no꞉, kalu a꞉la꞉yo꞉ o꞉ otalena꞉lo꞉ to imiligo꞉ mo꞉dowalega, to a꞉no꞉ da꞉da꞉so꞉bo.
Ko꞉sega kalu man mogago꞉lo꞉ dimida꞉lab a꞉no꞉, kalu nolba꞉ siwa꞉l amio꞉ kalaba sa꞉laki, digala꞉bi. A꞉la꞉galikiyo꞉, kaluka꞉isale nolo꞉ a꞉no꞉ ba꞉dakiyo꞉, tagima꞉ib.
Gode o꞉lia꞉ Ya꞉su Keliso o꞉lia꞉ ma꞉mula꞉ kalu Godeya꞉lo꞉ da꞉feyo꞉ o꞉lia꞉ma꞉ siwa꞉l amio꞉, giyo꞉ to we kudu hamana꞉ki, niyo꞉ gemo꞉wo꞉ halale so꞉lo꞉l. A꞉no꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ dimidakiyo꞉, giyo꞉ kaluka꞉isale nolo꞉ mo꞉wa꞉la꞉sa꞉ndaki, tambomo꞉wo꞉ man imilo꞉ ka dimida꞉bi.
Giyo꞉ kalu imilig nowo꞉ Godeya꞉ nanog dima꞉ki da꞉feakiyo꞉, dagiyo꞉ misa꞉ wa꞉lamio꞉ golakiyo꞉, bo꞉ibo꞉ da꞉fea꞉so꞉bo. Kalu nolba꞉lo꞉ man mogago꞉ dimidab a꞉no꞉, ge i o꞉lia꞉yo꞉ mo꞉gasa dowaki, mano꞉ digalo꞉le kudu ha꞉na꞉bi.
Ge walafo꞉ modo꞉ fa꞉la꞉dowo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉, kufo꞉ asuwa꞉foma꞉kiyo꞉, ge ho꞉ndeyo꞉ nakiyo꞉, wain ho꞉n ha꞉luwo꞉lo꞉ na꞉bi.
Kalu nolo꞉ man mogago꞉wo꞉ nolba꞉ siwa꞉la dimido꞉ ko꞉lo꞉, kalu a꞉no꞉ semo꞉ mo꞉walilaki, mogago꞉ dimido꞉ a꞉ma꞉yo꞉ kalaba wala fo꞉lab. Ko꞉sega kalu nolo꞉ man mogago꞉ ililo꞉ dimido꞉wo꞉ wo꞉no꞉le da꞉lab ko꞉lo꞉, tif amio꞉ kalaba fa꞉la꞉doma꞉ib.
A꞉la꞉do꞉ gan aumbo꞉, man nafale dimidab nolo꞉ kalaba dowaki, tambo ba꞉da꞉sen. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ man nafale dimidab nolo꞉lo꞉ wo꞉no꞉le dimidab, ko꞉sega a꞉no꞉lo꞉ kalaba fa꞉la꞉doma꞉ib.
Keliso kaluka꞉isale abeyo꞉ madali nanog dian kalu dowab a꞉ma꞉yo꞉ inin misa꞉ kaluwa꞉ ha꞉g amio꞉ ha꞉sa dowa꞉bi. A꞉la꞉galikiyo꞉, Gode o꞉lia꞉ nililo꞉ man ko꞉lo꞉ wido꞉ a꞉no꞉lia꞉ mo꞉mogagi sa꞉ma꞉ib.
Madali nanog dian kalu, gili misa꞉ kaluwo꞉ Keliso dofo꞉lalega, e gao o꞉ngo꞉ dowo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉, gio꞉ “e ha꞉g amio꞉ mo꞉doma꞉no꞉” a꞉la꞉bo꞉ asula꞉so꞉bo. A꞉la꞉do꞉ mo꞉gakiyo꞉, gio꞉ ini nanogo꞉ mada nafa, halale dimida꞉bi. Mo꞉wo꞉ kalu i o꞉mo꞉wo꞉ Godeya꞉yo꞉ ha꞉fo꞉wo꞉ disa꞉la꞉sen a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉, nanog halaido꞉ gililo꞉ dimido꞉ a꞉ma꞉yo꞉, Keliso kalu nolo꞉ asuwa꞉fa꞉ib. To we kaluka꞉isalemo꞉wo꞉ wida꞉bi.
Kalu abeyo꞉ mano꞉ ko꞉li ko꞉lilo꞉ widaki, Alan Ya꞉su Kelisowa꞉ to man digalo꞉ widab a꞉no꞉lia꞉ mo꞉ imilo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ widalega, kalu i a꞉no꞉ asugdo꞉ma iliki, inin wiyo꞉ mada kailaki gab. Kalu i a꞉no꞉ no꞉nolo꞉ dofo꞉liki, to ililo꞉ a꞉ma꞉yo꞉ kegema꞉no꞉wo꞉ ili mo꞉mo꞉da sa꞉la꞉mela꞉ib. To ililo꞉ kego꞉ a꞉ma꞉yo꞉ man ko꞉lilo꞉wo꞉ a꞉na mo꞉modama꞉ib. Man a꞉no꞉ we, meselano꞉, kaluka꞉isaleyo꞉ aloba꞉dano꞉, mogagi sa꞉lakilo꞉ sada꞉dano꞉, bulu kedakilo꞉ mo꞉dimidab aundo꞉ to sa꞉lano꞉, a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ to ko꞉li ko꞉lilo꞉ kegano꞉ a꞉na fa꞉la꞉doma꞉ib. Kalu i wema꞉ asulo꞉wo꞉ mogagila꞉fo꞉liki, to hendeleyo꞉ i amio꞉ mo꞉a꞉lab. Iyo꞉ Gode elo꞉ asulab aumb doma꞉no꞉ a꞉namio꞉, mole alan dia꞉no꞉ togo꞉ a꞉na dowab a꞉la꞉asulo꞉.
<range>
<range>
Ko꞉sega Gode elo꞉ asulab aumb kuduha꞉naki, ha꞉sa dowan man o꞉lia꞉ sagalan man o꞉lia꞉yo꞉ ge amio꞉ ililo꞉ aumbo꞉ dowalikiyo꞉, ge kelego꞉ nafaleyo꞉ di o꞉ngo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉lab.
Nio꞉ henfelo꞉ wenamilo꞉ sa꞉la꞉liab amio꞉ kelego꞉ imilig nowo꞉ mo꞉dia꞉ handalowo꞉. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ henfelo꞉ we ta꞉fo꞉ ha꞉nakiyo꞉, kelego꞉ imilig nowo꞉ mo꞉dia꞉ha꞉na꞉no꞉.
A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ ni amio꞉ ma꞉n o꞉lia꞉ so꞉g sa꞉ga꞉lan o꞉lia꞉ o꞉li dowo꞉lalega, nio꞉ o꞉li da꞉lab a꞉la꞉asuluma꞉niki.
Ko꞉sega, kalu abeyo꞉ mole alando꞉ dia꞉no꞉ asulab i a꞉no꞉, man mogago꞉ a꞉ma꞉yo꞉ iyo꞉ susululaliki, iyo꞉ dafa o꞉ngo꞉wa walalelab. Iyo꞉ babale dowaki, kelego꞉ nolo꞉ modo꞉ mesela꞉sen ko꞉lo꞉, man a꞉ma꞉yo꞉ inina꞉ma꞉la꞉ mogagilab.
Mole alando꞉ dia꞉no꞉ asulan a꞉no꞉, man mogago꞉ ko꞉li ko꞉lilo꞉ dimidama꞉no꞉ a꞉ma꞉ tefo꞉ o꞉m. Kaluka꞉isale nolo꞉ moleyo꞉ mada alan asula꞉sa꞉ga꞉, ili tilidabuwo꞉ gola dowaki, ha꞉na꞉no꞉ ane ko꞉lo꞉ kalu i a꞉no꞉ inino꞉ da꞉ya꞉lo꞉ olan o꞉ngo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ hida꞉yo꞉wo꞉ alan di.
Ko꞉sega ge Godeya꞉no꞉le dowo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ mogago꞉ ko꞉li ko꞉lilo꞉ a꞉ma꞉ anibamio꞉ mo꞉ege dowakiyo꞉, ge digalo꞉ mano꞉ a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ Gode Elo꞉ asulab aumb dimidano꞉, tilidabu mano꞉, ha꞉fo꞉ disa꞉lan mano꞉, halale kagama꞉no꞉ mano꞉, ha꞉sa dowan mano꞉ we ko꞉lo꞉, ge a꞉no꞉ kudu ha꞉na꞉lubi.
Ya꞉suwa tilida꞉daki, nanog dimidakiyo꞉, giyo꞉ halale nai ha꞉na꞉la꞉ga꞉ tinia꞉bi. Tamin amio꞉ ge kaluka꞉isaleya꞉ siwa꞉la kagayaki, tilidabu gilo꞉wo꞉ imo꞉ widakiyo꞉, Godeya꞉ ge mela꞉no꞉ mela꞉no꞉wo꞉ dima꞉ki ho꞉leli ko꞉lo꞉ ge o꞉go꞉ a꞉naka nai ha꞉na꞉la꞉ga꞉, mela꞉no꞉ mela꞉no꞉ a꞉no꞉ halale ta꞉lima.
Godeya꞉yo꞉ kelego꞉ tambo mela꞉no꞉wo꞉ dimiab a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ Ya꞉su Kelisowo꞉ Pontius Pailada꞉ siwa꞉la kagayaki, ene tilidabuwo꞉ kalaba fanda sio꞉ ko꞉lo꞉, niyo꞉ Gode o꞉lia꞉ Yesu o꞉lia꞉ma꞉ siwa꞉l amio꞉ ge to we kudu hamana꞉ki gemo꞉ halale sa꞉ma꞉nigo꞉l.
Gemo꞉lo꞉ wido꞉ a꞉no꞉ tambo dinafa kudu ha꞉na꞉la꞉ga꞉, Ya꞉su Keliso Alan elo꞉ a꞉ma꞉la꞉ mia꞉nigab a꞉no꞉ yasila꞉likiyo꞉, digale kudu ha꞉na꞉lubi.
Godeya꞉yo꞉ enedo꞉ ho꞉lende da꞉fe alifa꞉ a꞉namio꞉, Eyo꞉ Ya꞉suwo꞉ a꞉ma꞉la꞉ iliga꞉fa꞉ib. Iwalu Godeyo꞉ ena꞉li e, Kelego꞉ tambowo꞉ e bo꞉fo꞉lab. Kalu Alana꞉, Alandeyo꞉ E, Misa꞉ dowo꞉wa꞉, Misa꞉ Alandeyo꞉ E.
Gode imilise e mo꞉sowan. E ho꞉lendeya iliki, kalu imilig nowo꞉ e anib amio꞉ mo꞉kagama꞉ ha꞉na꞉ib. E kalu imilig noma꞉yo꞉ mo꞉ba꞉ba꞉ ko꞉lo꞉, tifamio꞉lo꞉ e mo꞉ba꞉ba꞉ib. Niliyo꞉ e ho꞉leno꞉ tambo wabudaki, Ene halaido꞉wo꞉ mela꞉no꞉ mela꞉no꞉ doma꞉ib. Hendele o꞉m.
Henfelo꞉ wenamio꞉ moleyo꞉ modo꞉lo꞉ da꞉lab kalu a꞉no꞉ mo꞉kaila꞉ma꞉ki, giyo꞉ imo꞉wo꞉ wida꞉bi. Ko꞉sega iyo꞉ kelego꞉ bo꞉bo꞉gelo꞉ mogagima꞉no꞉ a꞉namida꞉yo꞉ mo꞉tili asulaki, Godeyo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ tili asuluma꞉ki wida꞉bi. Mo꞉wo꞉ Godeya꞉yo꞉ nio꞉ sagalema꞉kiyo꞉, kelego꞉ nafale ko꞉li ko꞉lilo꞉ dimia꞉sen.
I amio꞉ man nafaleyo꞉ wa꞉litaki, iliyo꞉ nafale dimidan man a꞉no꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ modo꞉ dimida꞉ melea꞉ki, giyo꞉ wida꞉bi. Inin kelego꞉wo꞉ mo꞉kanulu ta꞉liaki, nolbo꞉wo꞉ sagala꞉liki dimia꞉ melea꞉kiyo꞉, giyo꞉ imo꞉wo꞉ wida꞉bi.
Iliyo꞉ a꞉la꞉dimidalikiyo꞉, a dia꞉nikilo꞉ aiko꞉ halaido꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ gelan aumbo꞉, man nafa dimidan a꞉no꞉ tifamio꞉lo꞉ kelego꞉ fa꞉la꞉doma꞉ib a꞉no꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ dimidai takigab. Iliyo꞉ a꞉la꞉dimidalega, mela꞉no꞉ hendele a꞉no꞉ mela꞉no꞉le dia꞉ib.
Timoti, ge Godeya꞉lo꞉ to hendele gemo꞉lo꞉ bo꞉fo꞉melea꞉kilo꞉ dimi a꞉no꞉ dinafa tili dowa꞉bi. Ge Godeya꞉ toma, madali tolo꞉ malola꞉sen a꞉no꞉ kadeta꞉bi. Kalu nolba꞉yo꞉ to a꞉no꞉ da꞉dakiyo꞉, “Hendele” a꞉la꞉ asulab ko꞉sega to a꞉no꞉ hendelema ko꞉lo꞉ da꞉da꞉so꞉bo.
Kalu nolba꞉yo꞉ to a꞉no꞉ tili asulakiyo꞉, tilidabu hendele a꞉no꞉ iyo꞉ ta꞉ta꞉ga꞉ ha꞉nab ko꞉lo꞉ giyo꞉ to a꞉no꞉ da꞉da꞉so꞉bo. Godeya꞉ kanulan man a꞉no꞉ gi o꞉lia꞉ dowa꞉biyo꞉.
Ne Fol, Ya꞉su Kelisowa꞉lo꞉ iliga꞉felo꞉ kaluwo꞉ ne. Kaluka꞉isaleyo꞉ Ya꞉su amio꞉ tilida꞉dab o꞉mo꞉wo꞉ mela꞉no꞉wo꞉ dimia꞉no꞉ a꞉la꞉liki, Godeya꞉ dinali sio꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ ne to a꞉no꞉ walama꞉ki, ne a꞉na da꞉fea꞉sa꞉ga꞉ iliga꞉fo꞉.
Timoti ge, ni so꞉wale o꞉ngo꞉ dowo꞉. Mo꞉fo꞉s we gemo꞉ iliga꞉to꞉l. Do Gode o꞉lia꞉ nili Alan Ya꞉su Keliso o꞉lia꞉ma꞉ kanulan mano꞉, nofolano꞉ a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ ha꞉sa dowano꞉ gelo꞉ dima꞉ki, Godemo꞉ dulugu so꞉lo꞉l.
Ne ma꞉mu iya꞉lo꞉ Gode kudu ha꞉na꞉sen aumbo꞉, niyo꞉lo꞉ asugo꞉ go꞉go꞉do꞉ dowaki, Godeya꞉ ene nanog dimida꞉likiyo꞉, ho꞉lenowo꞉lo꞉ nuluwo꞉lo꞉ niyo꞉ ge asula꞉likiyo꞉, Godemo꞉ mada o꞉m a꞉la꞉ sa꞉la꞉sen.
Gilo꞉ ya꞉lakilo꞉ si ho꞉n ane a꞉no꞉ ne asula꞉liki, ge galima꞉no꞉wo꞉ alan asula꞉sen. Mo꞉wo꞉ niyo꞉ ge ba꞉dakiyo꞉, mada alan sagalema꞉no꞉.
A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ gilo꞉ tilidabu hendeleyo꞉ ne asulakiyo꞉, tilidabu a꞉no꞉ tamina gu Lois dia꞉ go꞉ Yunes dia꞉ amio꞉ elen ko꞉lo꞉, o꞉go꞉ ge amio꞉lo꞉ a꞉lab, niyo꞉ a꞉la꞉ asulo꞉l.
A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ ni dagiya꞉ golab amio꞉, Godeya꞉yo꞉ boba kelego꞉wo꞉ gemo꞉ dimi ko꞉lo꞉, o꞉go꞉ de ko꞉lo꞉ dalifa꞉nigab amilo꞉ folan aumbo꞉, boba kelego꞉ a꞉no꞉ digidalitakiyo꞉, ge nanogo꞉ halale dimida꞉bi.
Gode eyo꞉ tagilan man a꞉no꞉ nimo꞉wo꞉ mo꞉dimi ko꞉sega, nili mamayo꞉ halaido꞉ dofo꞉liki, ha꞉fo꞉ disa꞉ma꞉no꞉ man o꞉lia꞉ nili asulo꞉wo꞉ dinafa tilidoma꞉no꞉ man o꞉lia꞉ a꞉no꞉ nimo꞉wo꞉ dimi.
A꞉la꞉fo꞉ko꞉lo꞉ gio꞉ Alan Ya꞉suwa꞉ wi ko꞉lo꞉ wala sa꞉ma꞉no꞉wo꞉ sendelowa꞉so꞉bo. A꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ Ya꞉suwa꞉ wi amilo꞉ dibolo to꞉lolo꞉ kalu ne amio꞉ ge sendelowa꞉so꞉bo. Ko꞉sega giyo꞉ Godeya꞉ halaido꞉wa dowaki, nilo꞉ to nafa wido꞉ amilo꞉ hida꞉yo꞉ dio꞉l we aumbo꞉ giyo꞉lo꞉ dia꞉niki, ne kudu ya꞉bi.
Gode eyo꞉ nio꞉ a꞉ma꞉la꞉ gasiliaki, nio꞉ mela꞉no꞉ malilo꞉wa mesea꞉ki, da꞉fe alifa꞉. A꞉no꞉ niliyo꞉ elo꞉ dimido꞉ amima ko꞉sega, eyo꞉ nimo꞉wo꞉ ha꞉fo꞉ disa꞉laki, enedo꞉ asulab aumb da꞉feyo꞉. Henfelo꞉ we o꞉fa꞉la꞉doma꞉no꞉ amio꞉, Godeya꞉yo꞉ Ya꞉suwa꞉lo꞉ dimidama꞉no꞉ a꞉no꞉ asula꞉sa꞉ga꞉, nimo꞉wo꞉ ha꞉fo꞉wo꞉ tamina disa꞉.
Ko꞉sega o꞉go꞉ ha꞉fo꞉ disa꞉lan a꞉no꞉ fanda asuluma꞉kiyo꞉, nilo꞉ gasilia꞉no꞉, Ya꞉su Keliso, e mio꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ sowan man a꞉no꞉ e bidilaki, to nafayo꞉ nilo꞉wa dia꞉mio꞉. To nafa a꞉ma꞉yo꞉ mela꞉no꞉ mela꞉no꞉ a꞉no꞉ nimo꞉ dima꞉ki, fanda wido꞉.
To nafa a꞉no꞉ wala sama꞉ki, Godeya꞉yo꞉ ne Ya꞉suwa꞉lo꞉ iliga꞉felo꞉ kalu a꞉la꞉ta꞉ga꞉ to nafalo꞉ walama꞉no꞉ kalu da꞉feyo꞉.
A꞉la꞉do꞉ dimido꞉ amio꞉ ne o꞉go꞉ hida꞉yo꞉ ba꞉da꞉li so꞉l. Ko꞉sega ne mo꞉sendelowaki, halale kagafo꞉lo꞉l. Mo꞉wo꞉ kalu nilo꞉ tilida꞉sa꞉ga꞉lo꞉ o꞉lo꞉l we, ne asulo꞉ ko꞉lo꞉, nanog nemo꞉lo꞉ dimi a꞉no꞉, Ya꞉suwa꞉ ene tilidofo꞉ ha꞉na꞉la꞉ga꞉, henfelo꞉ welo꞉ edabami a꞉na ta꞉fa꞉ib, niyo꞉ a꞉la꞉ asulo꞉l.
Digalo꞉ to nilo꞉ gemo꞉lo꞉ wido꞉ a꞉no꞉, giyo꞉ to a꞉no꞉ kaluka꞉isalemo꞉wo꞉ widakiyo꞉, Ya꞉suwa꞉ ene tilidabu o꞉lia꞉ ene ha꞉fo꞉ disa꞉lan man a꞉no꞉lia꞉yo꞉ oga꞉dita꞉ga꞉, to hendele a꞉no꞉ ko꞉lo꞉ halale ta꞉li dofo꞉lubi.
Godeya꞉ Mamayo꞉ ge o꞉lia꞉ iliki, asuwa꞉ta꞉lab ko꞉lo꞉ to nafale ko꞉lo꞉ gemo꞉lo꞉ bo꞉fo꞉melea꞉kilo꞉ dimi a꞉no꞉, giyo꞉ dinafa bo꞉fo꞉lubi.
